nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtya naraṃ caiva narottamam
dvaipāyanauṣṭhapuṭaniḥsṛtam aprameyaṃ puṇyaṃ pavitram atha pāpaharaṃ śubhaṃ ca
pārāśaryāya śāntāya namo nārāyaṇāya te
kṛtābhiṣekaṃ tanayam rājñaḥ pārīkṣitasya ha
draṣṭum abhyāyayuḥ prītyā śaunakādyā maharṣayaḥ
tān āgatān sa rājarṣiḥ pādyārghyādibhir arcitān
sukhopaviṣṭān viśrāntān kṛtasaṃpraśnasatkathān
tatkathābhiḥ kṛtāhlādaḥ praṇipatya kṛtāñjaliḥ
śatānīko 'tha papraccha nārāyaṇakathāṃ parām
yam āśritya jagannātham mama pūrvapitāmahāḥ
vipakṣāpahṛtaṃ rājyam avāpuḥ puruṣottamāḥ
parīkṣit prāṇasaṃyogaṃ devadevena lambhitaḥ
śrutaṃ subahuśo mayā stutasyāśeṣajanmanaḥ
tasya devasya kaḥ śaktaḥ pravaktuṃ vā vibhūtayaḥ
śrotum ārādhanaṃ yena nistareyaṃ bhavārṇavam
ārādhitaḥ samastānāṃ kleśānāṃ hānido hariḥ
śakyaḥ samārādhayituṃ tan naḥ śaṃsata sattamāḥ
vidyānām api sā vidyā śrutānām api tac chrutam
rahasyānāṃ rahasyaṃ tad yena viṣṇuḥ prasīdati
mantrāṇāṃ paramo mantro vratānāṃ tan mahāvratam
upoṣitaṃ hi tac chreṣṭhaṃ yena tuṣyati keśavaḥ
yad eva pulakodbhāsi viṣṇor nāmābhikīrtanāt
sā hānis tan mahac chidraṃ sā cāndhajaḍamūkatā
yan muhūrtaṃ kṣaṇaṃ vāpi vāsudevo na cintyate
nūnaṃ tat kaṇṭhaśālūkam athavā pratijihvikā
rogo vānyo na sā jihvā yā na vakti harer guṇān
dharmārthakāmasaṃprāptau puruṣāṇāṃ viceṣṭitam
janmany aviphalā saikā yā govindāśrayā kriyā
durgasaṃsārakāntāram apāram abhidhāvatām
ekaḥ kṛṣṇanamaskāro muktitīrasya deśikaḥ
evam ādiguṇo bhogaḥ kṛṣṇasyādbhutakarmaṇaḥ
śruto me bahuśo siddhaiḥ gīyamānas tathāparaiḥ
nārāyaṇam aśeṣasya jagato hṛdy avasthitam
śaṃkaraṃ jagataḥ prāṇaṃ smṛtamātrāghahāriṇam
tan mamādya muniśreṣṭhāḥ prasādayitum icchataḥ
sarve ca te muniśreṣṭhā bhṛguśreṣṭhaṃ ca śaunakam
bhaktyā ca devadevasya pravaṇīkṛtamānasaḥ
kṛtvottarīyaparyaṅkaṃ śithilaṃ bhagavān atha
pratyuvāca mahābhāgaḥ śaunakas taṃ mahīpatim
yat pṛcchasi mahīpāla kṛṣṇasyārādhanaṃ prati
vratopavāsajapyādi tad ihaikamanāḥ śṛṇu
tatkṣobhakatvād brahmāṇḍa sṛṣṭihetur nirañjanaḥ
pradhānapuruṣatvaṃ ca tathaiveśvaralīlayā
tataḥ sthitau pālayitā viṣṇutvaṃ jagataḥ kṣaye
pravakṣyāmi yathā pūrvaṃ matpitrā kathitaṃ mama
tasyāpi kila tatpitrā tasmai cāha kilośanāḥ
tenāpi bhṛgum ārādhya prāptam ārādhanaṃ hareḥ
sakāśād brahmaṇaḥ prāptaṃ bhṛguṇāpi mahātmanā
marīcimiśraiś ca purā param etan maharṣibhiḥ
prāptaṃ sakāśād devasya brahmaṇo vyaktajanmanaḥ
yogaṃ brahmā paraṃ prāha maharṣīṇāṃ yadā prabhuḥ
viṣayā durjayā nRṇām indriyākarṣaṇāḥ prabho
vṛttayaś cetasaś cāpi capalā cātidurdharāḥ
rāgādayaḥ kathaṃ jetuṃ śakyā varṣaśatair api
alpāyuṣaś ca puruṣā brahman kṛtayuge 'py amī
duḥkhāmbumagnāḥ puruṣāḥ prāpya brahma mahāplavam
evam uktas tadā brahmā kriyāyogaṃ mahātmanām
teṣām ṛṣīṇām ācaṣṭa narāṇāṃ hitakāmyayā
ārādhayata viśveśam nārāyaṇam atandritāḥ
bāhyālambanasāpekṣās tam ajaṃ jagataḥ patim
ijyāpūjānamaskāra śuśrūṣābhir aharniśam
vratopavāsair vividhair brāhmaṇānāṃ ca tarpaṇaiḥ
tais taiś cābhimataiḥ kāmair ye ca cetasi tuṣṭidāḥ
tanniṣṭhās tadgatadhiyas tatkarmāṇas tadāśrayāḥ
saṃnyasyadhvaṃ sa vaḥ kartā samastāvaraṇakṣayam
paraḥ parāṇāṃ paramaḥ sa ekaḥ puruṣottamaḥ
tam ārādhya jagannāthaṃ mokṣakāraṇam avyaktam
iti te brahmaṇaḥ śrutvā rahasyam ṛṣisattamāḥ
narāṇām upakārāya yogaśāstrāṇi cakrire
kriyāyogaparāṇīha muktikāryāṇy anekaśaḥ
ārādhyate jagannātho yadanuṣṭhānatatparaiḥ
paramātmā hṛṣīkeśaḥ sarveśaḥ sarvabhāvanaḥ
tāni te nṛpaśārdūla sarvapāpaharāṇy aham
saṃsārārṇavamagnānāṃ viṣayākrāntacetasām
uttāram icchatāṃ tasmād bhṛśaṃ yan nāntarair api
viṣṇupotaṃ vinā nānyat kiṃcid asti parāyaṇam
uttiṣṭhaṃś cintaya hariṃ vrajaṃś cintaya keśavam
janmamṛtyujarāgrāhaṃ saṃsārāmbhas tariṣyasi
anantam īḍyaṃ puruṣaṃ purāṇaṃ jagadvidhātāram ajaṃ janitryam
samāśritā ye harim īśitāraṃ teṣāṃ bhavo nāsti hi muktibhājām
śrūyatāṃ kuruśārdūla saṃvādo 'yam anuttamaḥ
ambarīṣasya rājarṣeḥ saha devena cakriṇā
ambarīṣo mahīpālaḥ pālayann eva medinīm
tutoṣa bhagavān viṣṇuḥ sarvalokapatiḥ prabhuḥ
nāham ārādhayāmi tvāṃ tava baddho 'yam añjaliḥ
varārthināṃ tvaṃ varadaḥ prayacchābhimatān varān
varārthāya tvayānyaiś ca kriyate nṛpate tapaḥ
viṣṇor ārādhanārthāya viddhi māṃ tvaṃ kṛtodyamam
pālayanti mamaivājñām ādityādyāḥ sadā surāḥ
ādityā vasavo rudrā nāsatyau marutāṃ gaṇāḥ
prajānāṃ patayaḥ sādhyā viśvedevā maharṣayaḥ
matto hi ko 'nyo varadaḥ pratigṛhṇīṣva vāñchitam
tvayāpi prāptam aiśvaryaṃ yatas taṃ toṣayāmy aham
saptodare śayā lokās tam īśaṃ toṣayāmy aham
nimeṣo brahmaṇo rātrir unmeṣo yasya vāsaraḥ
tam īḍyam īśam ajaraṃ praṇato 'smi janārdanam
yo hartā jagato devaḥ kartā pālāyitā ca yaḥ
trayasyāsya ca yo yonis taṃ viṣṇuṃ toṣayāmy aham
hiraṇyakaśipuḥ pūrvaṃ hiraṇyākṣaś ca te ripuḥ
balināpahṛtaṃ śakra dattaṃ yena purā tava
trailokyarājyaṃ taṃ baddhvā taṃ namāmi janārdanam
tapas tapsye jagannāthaṃ draṣṭuṃ nārāyaṇaṃ harim
śrūyate kila govinde bhaktim udvahatāṃ nṛṇām
saṃsārārṇāvabhītānāṃ tridaśāḥ paripanthinaḥ
tāpaso 'haṃ kva niḥsaṅgaḥ kva ca kopas tavedṛśaḥ
sa tvaṃ prahara vā mā vā mayi vajraṃ puraṃdara
nāham utsṛjya govindam anyam ārādhayāmi bhoḥ
na cāpi vajraṃ vajrī vā tvaṃ ca nānye surāsurāḥ
śaktā nihantum īśāne hṛdayasthe janārdane
kiṃ ca no bahunoktena nāhaṃ vakṣyāmy ataḥ paraṃ
cacāra maunam āsthāya tenātuṣyata keśavaḥ
saṃdarśayām āsa tataḥ svaṃ vapuḥ kaiṭabhārdanaḥ
caturbhujam udārāṅgaṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharam
kirīṭasragdharaṃ spaṣṭaṃ nīlotpaladalacchavim
airāvataś ca garuḍas tatkṣaṇāt samadṛśyata
pratyuvāca ca bhūpālaḥ praṇipatya kṛtāñjaliḥ
jayāspaṣṭaprakāśāṇḍa bṛhanmūrte jayākṣara
jaya vijñātasiddhānta māyāmohaka keśava
nṛsiṃha jaya devāri vakṣaḥsthalavidāraṇa
devānām aribhītānām ārtināśana vāmana
namo 'stv avyapadeśyāya namaḥ sūkṣmasvarūpiṇe
viśeṣair aviśeṣyāya tasmai tubhyaṃ namo namaḥ
puruṣākhyaṃ tato rūpaṃ nirguṇaṃ guṇabhoktṛ ca
prakṛteḥ parataḥ sūkṣmaṃ tan namasyāmi te hare
avyaktādiviśeṣāntam atisūkṣmatamaṃ mahat
prākṛtaṃ tava tad rūpaṃ tasmai deva namāmy aham
prasīda viṣṇo govinda śaṅkhacakragadādhara
dharādharāravindākṣa vāsudeva maheśvara
ambarīṣaṃ pṛthivīśaṃ jagat saṃnādayan girā
varaṃ vṛṇīṣva dharmajña yat te manasi vartate
eṣa eva varaḥ ślāghyo yad dṛṣṭo 'si jagatpate
vetti tāṃ bhagavān eva hṛdisthaḥ sarvadehinām
tvatprasādān mameśāna rājyam avyāhataṃ bhuvi
kośadaṇḍau tathātīva śarīrārogyam uttamam
striyo 'nnapānasāmarthyā hāniḥ svalpāpi nāsti me
saṃtatir nibhṛtā bhṛtyā sānurāgāś ca me janāḥ
jñātaṃ mayā hi govinde nāprasanne vibhūtayaḥ
punarāvṛttiduḥkhānāṃ trāsād udvignamānasaḥ
sukhāni tāni naivānte yeṣāṃ duḥkhaṃ na tat sukham
yad ante duḥkham āgāmi kiṃpākasyaiva bhakṣaṇam
jñānadānena yenemāṃ vāgurān nistaremahi
upadiṣṭe tato yoge praṇipatyācyutaṃ nṛpaḥ
punaḥ prāha mahābāhur vinayāvanataḥ sthitaḥ
viṣayā durjayāḥ puṃbhir indriyākarṣiṇaḥ sadā
indriyāṇāṃ jayaṃ teṣu kaḥ śaktānāṃ kariṣyati
ahaṃ mameti cākhyāti durjayaṃ cañcalaṃ manaḥ
rāgādayaḥ kathaṃ jetuṃ śakyā janmāntarair api
rāgādibhir amartyatvaṃ prāptuṃ prakṣīṇakalmaṣaḥ
yady evaṃ muktikāmas tvaṃ naranātha śṛṇuṣva tat
kriyāyogaṃ samastānāṃ kleśānāṃ hānikārakam
mām evaiṣyasi yuktvaivam ātmānaṃ matparāyaṇaḥ
madbhāvanā madyajanā madbhaktā matparāyaṇāḥ
mama pūjāparāś caiva mayi yānti layaṃ narāḥ
sarvabhūteṣu māṃ paśya samavasthitam īśvaram
kartāsi kena vairatvaṃ evaṃ doṣān prahāsyasi
jaṅgamājaṅgame jñāte mayy ātmani tathā tava
rāgalobhādināśena bhavitrī kṛtakṛtyatā
mayy anāsādavad bhūpa kuru madrūpiṇīṃ tanum
suvarṇarajatādyais tvaṃ śailamṛddārulekhajām
tasyāṃ cittaṃ samāveśya tyājayānyān vyapāśrayān
pūjitā saiva te bhaktyā dhyātā caivopakāriṇī
gacchaṃs tiṣṭhan svapan bhuñjaṃs tām evāgre ca pṛṣṭhataḥ
vāsobhir bhūṣaṇair bhakṣyair gītavādyair manoharaiḥ
yac ca yac ca nṛpeṣṭaṃ te kiṃcid bhojyādi tena tām
bhaktinamro naraśreṣṭha prīṇayārcāṃ kṛtāṃ mama
rāgeṇākṛṣyate ceto gandharvābhimukhaṃ yadi
mayi buddhiṃ samāveśya gāyethā mama tāṃ kathām
śrotavyā prītiyuktena avatāreṣu yā kathā
evaṃ mayy arpitamanāś cetaso ye vyapāśrayāḥ
akṣīṇarāgadoṣo 'pi matkriyā paramaḥ param
rājyaṃ kuru naraśreṣṭha nivedya pṛthivīṃ mama
maddhitāya jagannātha kriyāyogāśritaṃ mama
matprasādād avikalaṃ sa ca vetsyaty aśeṣataḥ
vasiṣṭhaṃ paripapraccha viṣṇor ārādhanaṃ prati
kriyāyogāśritaṃ sarvaṃ vyākhyāsyati bhavān kila
sa tvāṃ pṛcchāmy ahaṃ sarvaṃ kriyāyogena keśavam
saṃtoṣayitum īśānaṃ yathā śakṣyāmi tad vada
devaprasādād akhilā mamāpi smṛtir āgatā
jñānam etad aśeṣaṃ te kathayāmi nibodha tat
nārāyaṇe mahāprajñaḥ sarvalokaparāyaṇe
sa papraccha bhṛguśreṣṭhaṃ śukram ātmapurohitam
bhagavan nṛsiṃharūpasya viṣṇos tātaṃ jighāṃsataḥ
dṛṣṭaṃ dehe mayā sarvaṃ trailokyaṃ bhūrbhuvādikam
vasavo 'ṣṭau tathādityā dvādaśāhaḥkṣapā mahī
aśvinau marutaḥ sādhyā viśvedevās tatha rṣayaḥ
varṣācalās tathā nadyaḥ sapta sapta kulācalāḥ
samudrāḥ sapta ṛtavaḥ kāntārāṇi vanāni ca
satiryagūrdhvapātālaṃ tasya dṛṣṭaṃ tanau mayā
so 'haṃ tam ajaraṃ devaṃ duṣṭadaityanivarhaṇam
ārādhayitum icchāmi bhagavaṃs tvadanujñayā
tan mamopadiśādya tvaṃ mahad ārādhanaṃ hareḥ
na hy abhāgavatair viṣṇur jñātuṃ stotuṃ ca tattvataḥ
draṣṭuṃ vā śakyate martyaiḥ praveṣṭuṃ kuta eva hi
nākṣīṇe jāyate puṃsāṃ govindābhimukhī matiḥ
pradveṣaṃ yāti govinde dvijān vedāṃś ca nindati
yo naras taṃ vijānīyād asurāṃśasamudbhavam
pāṣaṇḍeṣu ratiḥ puṃsāṃ hetuvādānukūlatā
jāyate viṣṇumāyāmbhaḥ patitānāṃ durātmanām
yadā pāpakṣayaḥ puṃsāṃ tadā vedadvijātiṣu
viṣṇau ca yajñapuruṣe śraddhā bhavati te yathā
yadā svalpāvaśeṣas tu narāṇāṃ pāpasaṃcayaḥ
bhrāmyatām atra saṃsāre narāṇāṃ karmadurgame
sa tvaṃ bhāgavato bhūtvā sarvapāpaharaṃ harim
ārādhaya paraṃ bhaktyā prītim eṣyati keśavaḥ
kiṃlakṣaṇā bhāgavatā bhavanti puruṣā guro
karmaṇā manasā vācā prāṇināṃ yo na hiṃsakaḥ
yo brāhmaṇāṃś ca vedāṃś ca nityam envānumaṃsyati
sarvān devān hariṃ vetti sarvalokāṃś ca keśavam
tebhyaś ca nānyam ātmānaṃ daitya bhāgavato hi saḥ
devaṃ manuṣyam anyaṃ vā paśupakṣipipīlikān
tarupāṣāṇakaṣṭhādi bhūmyambhogaganaṃ diśaḥ
ātmānaṃ vāpi deveśān nātiriktaṃ janārdanāt
yo bhajeta vijānīṣva taṃ vai bhāgavataṃ naram
karmaṇā manasā vācā sa tu bhāgavato naraḥ
bhāvena niṣpādayati jñeyo bhāgavatas tu saḥ
nārayo yasya na snigdhā na codāsī na vṛttayaḥ
paśyataḥ sarvam evedaṃ viṣṇuṃ bhāgavato hi saḥ
sutapteneha tapasā yajñair vā bahudakṣiṇaiḥ
tāṃ gatiṃ na narā yānti yāṃ vai bhāgavatā gatāḥ
arvāṅ nirīkṣyate yajñī kimu ye yogapāragāḥ
yajñaniṣpattaye vedā yajño yajñapateḥ kṛte
tattoṣaṇāya bhāvena tasmād bhāgavato bhava
yena sarvātmanā viṣṇau bhaktyā bhāvo niveśitaḥ
daityeśvara kṛtārthatvāc ślāghyo bhāgavato hi saḥ
bhagavān bhaktibhāvena yena viṣṇur upāsitaḥ
yaḥ kārayati devārcāṃ hṛdayālambanaṃ hareḥ
sa naro viṣṇusālokyam upaiti dhūtakalmaṣaḥ
yaś ca devālayaṃ bhaktyā viṣṇoḥ kārayati svayam
sa saptapuruṣāṃl lokān viṣṇor nayati mānavaḥ
yāvanty abdāni devārcā hares tiṣṭhati mandire
tāvadvarṣasahasrāṇi viṣṇuloke sa modate
devārcā lakṣaṇopetā tadgṛhaṃ satataṃ divi
niṣkāmaṃ ca mano yasya sa yāty akṣarasātmyatām
puṣpāṇy atisugandhīni manojñāni ca yaḥ pumān
prayacchati hṛṣīkeśe tadbhāvagatamānasaḥ
dhūpāṃś ca vividhāṃs tāṃs tān gandhāḍhyaṃ cānulepanam
dīpāvalyupahārāṃś ca yac cābhīṣṭam athātmanaḥ
naraḥ so 'nudinaṃ yajñaṃ karoty ārādhanaṃ hareḥ
yajñeśo bhagavān viṣṇur makhair api hi toṣyate
bahūpakaraṇā yajñā nānāsaṃbhāravistarāḥ
bhaktyā ca puruṣaiḥ pūjā kṛtā dūrvāṅkurair api
yāni puṣpāṇi hṛdyāni dhūpagandhānulepanam
dayitaṃ bhūṣaṇaṃ yac ca ye ca kauśeyavāsasī
yāni cābhyavahārāṇi bhakṣyāṇi ca phalāni ca
ādyantaṃ yajñapuruṣaṃ yathāśaktyā prasādaya
kṣīreṇa snāpayed īśam acyutaṃ jagataḥ patim
dadhikṣīrahradān puṇyāṃs tato lokān madhucyutaḥ
prayāsyasy asuraśreṣṭha nirvṛtiṃ cāpi śāśvatīm
stotrair gītais tathā vādyair brāhmaṇānāṃ ca tarpaṇaiḥ
manasaś caikatāyogād ārādhaya janārdanam
ārādhya taṃ videhānāṃ puruṣāḥ saptasaptatiḥ
haihayāḥ pañcapañcāśad amṛtatvam upāgatāḥ
toṣayādyo hi tuṣṭo 'sau viṣṇur dvandvapraśāntidaḥ
upavāsair hṛṣīkeśaḥ kathaṃ tuṣyati bhārgava
parihārāṃs tathācakṣva ye tyājyāś copavāsinām
yad yat kāryaṃ yathā caiva keśavārādhane naraiḥ
smṛtaḥ saṃpūjito dhūpa puṣpādyair dayitair hariḥ
bhoginām upakārāya kiṃ punaś copavāsinām
upāvṛttas tu pāpebhyo yas tu vāso guṇaiḥ saha
ekarātraṃ dvirātraṃ vā trirātram athavāparam
upavāsī hariṃ yas tu bhaktyā dhyāyati mānavaḥ
yaṃ ca kāmam abhidhyāyan keśavārpitamānasaḥ
brāhmaṇaiḥ kṣatriyair vaiśyaiḥ śūdraiḥ strībhis tathā mune
anārādhya jagannāthaṃ sarvadhātāram acyutam
sa kathaṃ pāpapaṅkāṅkī naro yāsyati sadgatim
tadārādhaya sarveśaṃ jagaddhātāram acyutam
puṣpaiḥ sugandhair hṛdyaiś ca dhūpaiḥ sāgarucandanaiḥ
vāsobhir bhūṣaṇair bhakṣyair upavāsaparāyaṇaḥ
tadārādhaya govindaṃ yac ceṣṭaṃ tava cetasi
puṣpāṇi yadi te na syuḥ śastaṃ pādapapallavaiḥ
sugandhipuṣpadīpādyair yaḥ kuryāt keśavālaye
pūjitas tuṣṭim atulāṃ bhaktyāyāty ekacetasām
yaḥ sadāyatane viṣṇoḥ kurute mārjanakriyām
sa pāṃsubhūmer dehāc ca sarvapāpaṃ vyapohati
yāvantyaḥ pāṃsukaṇikā mārjyante keśavālaye
gocarmamātraṃ saṃmārjya hanti tat keśavālaye
yaś copalepanaṃ kuryād viṣṇor āyatane naraḥ
mṛdā dhātuvikārair vā varṇakair gomayena vā
udakābhyukṣaṇaṃ viṣṇor yaḥ karoti tathā gṛhe
so 'pi gacchati yatrāste bhagavān yādasāṃ patiḥ
samāpnoti naro dattvā dīpakaṃ keśavālaye
yas tu saṃvatsaraṃ pūrṇaṃ tilapātraprado naraḥ
vidhunvan hanti vātena dātur ajñānataḥ kṛtam
pāpaṃ ketur gṛhe viṣṇor divārātram asaṃśayam
gītavādyādibhir devaṃ ya upāste janārdanam
prāpnoti viṣṇvāyatane puṇyākhyānakathākaraḥ
upoṣitaḥ pūjito vā dṛṣṭo vā namito 'pi vā
vedavādakriyāyajña snānatīrthaphalaṃ param
aṣṭāṅgapraṇipātena praṇipatya hariṃ labhet
pragamya hṛdā śirasā pādapadme mahītale
niṣkalmaṣo bhavet sadyo na nāṭī pādapāṃsunā
ekasya kṛṣṇasya krājataḥ praṇāmo daśāśvamedhāvabhṛthena tulyaḥ
daśāśvamedhaiḥ punar eti janma kṛṣṇapraṇāmī na punarbhavāya
evaṃ deveśvaro bhaktyā yena viṣṇur upāsitaḥ
sa prāpnoti gatiṃ ślāghyāṃ yāṃ yām icchati cetasā
śakraḥ kratuśateneśam ārādhya garuḍadhvajam
tasyāpi yajñapuruṣo viṣṇuḥ pūjyo dvijottama
vaikhānasānām ārādhyas tapobhir madhusūdanaḥ
dhyeyaḥ parivrājakānāṃ vāsudevo mahātmanām
evaṃ sarvāśramāṇāṃ hi vāsudevaḥ parāyaṇam
sarveṣāṃ caiva varṇānāṃ tam ārādhyāpnuyād gatim
śṛṇuṣva gadataḥ kāmyām upavāsāṃs tathāparān
tat tam āśritya yān kāmān kurvītepsitam ātmanaḥ
ekādaśyāṃ śuklapakṣe phālgune māsi yo naraḥ
japet kṛṣṇeti devasya nāma bhaktyā punaḥpunaḥ
devārcane cāṣṭaśataṃ kṛtvaitat tu japec chuciḥ
pāṣaṇḍapatitāṃś caiva tathaivāntyāvasāyinaḥ
nālapeta tathā kṛṣṇam arcayec chraddhayānvitaḥ
idaṃ codāharet kṛṣṇe manaḥ saṃdhāya tatparaḥ
kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇa kṛpālus tvam agatīnāṃ gatir bhava
saṃsārāntarnimagnānāṃ prasīda madhusūdana
evaṃ prasādyopāvāsaṃ kṛtvā niyatamānasaḥ
pūrvāhna eva cānyedyur gavyaṃ saṃprāsya vai sakṛt
snāto 'rcayitvā kṛṣṇeti punar nāma prakīrtayet
vāridhārātrayaṃ caiva vikṣiped devapādayoḥ
martyaloke gatiṃ śreṣṭhāṃ dālbhya prāpnoti vai naraḥ
utkrāntikāle kṛṣṇasya smaraṇaṃ ca tathāpnute
āṣāḍhe śrāvaṇe caiva māse bhādrapade tathā
upoṣya saṃpūjya tathā keśaveti ca kīrtayet
gomūtraprāśanāt pūrvaṃ svargalokagatiṃ vrajet
ārādhitasya jagatām īśvarasyāvyāyātmanaḥ
utkrāntikāle smaraṇaṃ keśavasya tathāpnuyāt
kṣīrasya prāśanaṃ yas tu vidhiṃ cemaṃ yathoditam
kārttikādi yathānyāyaṃ kuryān māsacatuṣṭayam
sa yāti viṣṇusālokyaṃ viṣṇuṃ smarati ca kṣaye
pratimāsaṃ dvijātibhyo dadyād dānaṃ yathecchayā
cāturmāsye ca saṃpūrṇe puṇyaṃ śravaṇakīrtanam
kathāṃ vā vāsudevasya tadgītīr vāpi kārayet
evam etāṃ gatiṃ śreṣṭhāṃ devanāmānukīrtanāt
kathitaṃ pāraṇaṃ yat te kārṣṇaṃ māsacatuṣṭayam
ādhipatyaṃ tathā bhogāṃs tena prāpnoti mānuṣān
dvitīyena tathā bhogān aindrān prāpnoti mānavaḥ
viṣṇor lokaṃ tṛtīyena pāraṇena tathāpnuyāt
vidhānaṃ dvijaśārdūla kṛṣṇatuṣṭipradaṃ nṛṇām
sugatidvādaśīm etāṃ śraddadhānas tu yo naraḥ
upoṣya ca tathā nārī prāpnoti trividhāṃ gatim
eṣā dhanyā pāpaharā tithir nityam upāsitā
ārādhanāya śiṣṭaiṣā devadevasya cakriṇaḥ
pāṣaṇḍapatitāṃś caiva tathaivāntyāvasāyinaḥ
nāstikān bhinnavṛttīṃś ca pāpinaś cāpy anālapan
nārāyaṇe gatamanāḥ puruṣo niyatendriyaḥ
rātriṃ ca lakṣmīṃ saṃcintya samyag arghyena pūjayet
niṣpāditaṃ bhaved ekam pāraṇaṃ dālbhya bhaktitaḥ
dvitīyaṃ cāpi vakṣyāmi pāraṇaṃ dvijasattama
āṣāḍhe śrāvaṇe māsi prāpte bhādrapade tathā
tathaivāśvayuje 'bhyarcya śrīdharaṃ ca śriyā saha
dvitīyam etad ākhyātaṃ tṛtīyaṃ pāraṇaṃ śṛṇu
kārttikādiṣu māseṣu tathaivābhyarcya keśavam
bhūtyā samanvitaṃ dadyāc śaśāṅkāyārhanaṃ niśi
bhuñjīta ca tathā proktaṃ tṛtīyam iti pāraṇam
pratipūjāsu dadyāc ca brāhmaṇebhyaś ca dakṣiṇām
pratimāsaṃ ca vakṣyāmi prāśanaṃ kāyaśodhanam
caturaḥ prathamān māsān pañcagavyam udāhṛtam
kuśodakaṃ tathaivānyad uktaṃ māsacatuṣṭayam
sūryāṃśutaptaṃ tadvac ca jalaṃ māsacatuṣṭayam
gītavādyādikaṃ pāṭhyaṃ tathā kṛṣṇasya vā kathān
kāriyīta ca devasya pāraṇe pāraṇe gate
evaṃ saṃpūjya vidhivat sapatnīkaṃ janārdanam
nāpnotīṣtaviyogādīn pumān yoṣid athāpi vā
saśrīkaṃ śrīdharaṃ bhaktyā tṛtīye bhūtikeśavau
tāvanti janmāny asukhaṃ nāpnotīṣṭaviyogajam
nāriṃ prāpnoti na vyādhiṃ narakaṃ ca na paśyati
pratimāsaṃ tu nāmāni kṛṣṇasyaitāni dvādaśa
kṛtopavāsaḥ susnātaḥ pūjayitvā janārdanam
tato viprāya vai dadyād udakumbhaṃ sadakṣiṇaṃ
yad vai māsagataṃ nāma tatprītiś cāpi saṃvadet
saṃvatsarānte 'py athavā pratimāsaṃ dvijān budhaḥ
keśavaṃ mārgaśīrṣe tu pauṣe nārāyaṇaṃ tathā
mādhavaṃ māghamāse tu govindaṃ phālgune tathā
jyeṣṭhe trivikramaṃ devam āṣāḍhe vāmanaṃ tathā
śrāvaṇe śrīdharaṃ caiva hṛṣīkeśeti cāparam
nāma bhādrapade māsi gīyate puṇyakāṅkṣibhiḥ
padmanābhaṃ cāśvayuje dāmodaram ataḥ param
iha vai svasthatāṃ prāpya maraṇe smaraṇaṃ tataḥ
tato mānuṣyam āsādya nirātaṅko gatajvaraḥ
upavāsavratānīha keśavārādhanaṃ prati
mamācakṣva mahābhāga paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi me
kāmān yān yān naro bhakto manasecchati keśavāt
vratopavāsanāt prītas tāṃs tān viṣṇuḥ prayacchati
mārgaśīrṣaṃ tu yo māsam ekabhaktena yaḥ kṣapet
kurvan vai viṣṇuśuśrūṣāṃ sa deśe jāyate śubhe
pauṣamāsaṃ tathā dālbhya ekabhaktena yaḥ kṣapet
śuśrūṣaṇaparaḥ śaurer na rogī sa ca jāyate
māghamāsaṃ dvijaśreṣṭha ekabhaktena yaḥ kṣapet
viṣṇuśuśrūṣaṇaparaḥ sa kule jāyate satām
kṣapayed ekabhaktena śuśrūṣur yaś ca phālgunam
saubhāgyaṃ svajanānāṃ sa sarveṣām eti sonnatim
suvarṇamaṇimuktāḍhyaṃ sa gārhasthyam avāpnuyāt
naro vā yadi vā nārī jñātīnāṃ śreṣṭhatāṃ vrajet
kṛṣṇārpitamanā jyeṣṭham ekabhaktena yaḥ kṣapet
aiśvaryam atulaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ pumān strī vābhijāyate
āṣāḍham ekabhaktena yo nayed viṣṇutanmanāḥ
kṣapayed ekabhaktena śrāvaṇaṃ viṣṇutatparaḥ
dhanadhānyahiraṇyāḍhye kule sa jñātivardhanaḥ
ekāhāro bhādrapadaṃ yaś ca kṛṣṇaparāyaṇaḥ
nayaṃś cāśvayujaṃ viṣṇuṃ pūjayed ekabhojanaḥ
dhanavān vāhanāḍhyaś ca bahuputraś ca jāyate
kārttike caikadā bhuṅkte yaś ca viṣṇuparo naraḥ
śūraś ca kṛtavidyaś ca bahuputraś ca jāyate
ahiṃsaḥ sarvabhūteṣu vāsudevaparāyaṇaḥ
namo 'stu vāsudevāyety ahaś cāṣṭaśataṃ japet
tatkṣayād iha cāgatya māhātmyaṃ pratipadyate
brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vaiśyaḥ strī śūdro vā yathoditān
upavāsān imān kurvan phalāny etāny avāpnuyāt
jayaṃ śaraṇam abhyetya na janaiḥ śocyate janaḥ
prāpnoti śāśvataṃ sthānaṃ tataḥ pūjyataro hi saḥ
parāparaṃ sukṛtavatāṃ parāṃ gatiṃ svayaṃbhuvaṃ prabhavan nidhānam avyayam
śṛṇu dālbhya paraṃ kāmyaṃ vrataṃ saṃtatidaṃ nṛṇām
yam upoṣya na vicchedaḥ pitṛpiṇḍasya jāyate
kṛṣṇāṣṭamyāṃ caitramāse snāto niyatamānasaḥ
kṛṣṇam abhyarcya pūjāṃ ca devakyāḥ kurute tu yaḥ
nirāhāro japan nāma kṛṣṇasya jagataḥ pateḥ
upaviṣṭo japasnāna kṣutapraskhalitādiṣu
pūjāyāṃ cāpi kṛṣṇasya sapta vārān prakīrtayet
pāṣaṇḍino vikarmasthān nālapec caiva nāstikān
prabhāte tu punaḥ snāto dattvā viprāya dakṣiṇām
bhuñjīta kṛtapūjas tu kṛṣṇasyaiva jagatpateḥ
vaiśākhajyeṣṭhayoś caiva pāraṇaṃ hi trimāsikam
āṣāḍhe śrāvaṇe caiva māse bhādrapade tathā
upoṣite dvitīyaṃ vai pāraṇaṃ pūrvavat tu tat
tathaivāśvayujaṃ cādiṃ kṛtvā māsatrayaṃ budhaḥ
upoṣya snāpayed devaṃ haviṣā pāraṇe gate
caturthe pāraṇe pūrṇe ghṛtena snāpayed dharim
evaṃ kṛtopavāsasya puruṣasya tathā striyaḥ
kṛṣṇāṣṭamīm imāṃ yas tu naro yoṣid athāpi vā
upoṣyatīha sāhlādaṃ nṛloke prāpya nirvṛttim
ity etat kathitaṃ dālbhya mayā kṛṣṇāṣṭaṃīvratam
prāvṛṭkāle tu niyamāñ śṛṇu kāmyān imān mama
prāvṛṭkāle yadā śete vāsudevaḥ payonidhau
bhogibhoge nijāṃ māyāṃ yoganidrāṃ ca mānayan
viśiṣṭā na pravartante tadā yajñādikāḥ kriyāḥ
devānāṃ sā bhaved rātrir dakṣiṇāyanasaṃjñitā
adhaḥśāyī brahmacārī keśavārpitamānasaḥ
namo namo 'stu kṛṣṇāya keśavāya namo namaḥ
iti prātas tathā sāyaṃ japed devakriyāparaḥ
śamayaty atiduṣpāraṃ duritaṃ janmasaṃcitam
madhu māṃsaṃ ca yo māsāñ caturas tān nirasyati
arogī dhanadhānyāḍhyaḥ kulasaṃtatimān naraḥ
samastamandirāṇāṃ ca yaḥ supte madhusūdane
śastaṃ tv anantaraṃ puṃsāṃ tataś caivekabhojanam
tailābhaṅgaṃ ca yo māsāṃś caturas tān nirasyati
so 'py aṅgalāvaṇyaguṇam ārogyaṃ ca naro labhet
yas tv etāni samastāni māsān etān naraś caret
sa viṣṇulokam āsādya viṣṇor anucaro bhavet
caturbhiḥ pāraṇaṃ māsair niṣpādyaṃ haritatparaiḥ
brāhmaṇān bhojayed dadyāt tatas tebhyaś ca dakṣiṇām
devadevasya suptasya dvādaśīṃ śṛṇu cāparām
māsi proṣṭhapade śukle dvādaśyāṃ jalaśāyinam
praṇamyānantam abhyarcya puṣpadhūpādibhiḥ śuciḥ
pāṣaṇḍādibhir ālāpam akurvan niyatātmavān
viprāya dakṣiṇāṃ dattvā naktaṃ bhuṅkte tu yo naraḥ
tiṣṭhan vrajan svapaṃś caiva kṣutapraskhalitādiṣu
anantanāmasmaraṇaṃ kurvann uccāraṇaṃ tathā
anenaiva vidhānena māsān dvādaśa vai kramāt
gītavādyena hṛdyena prīṇayan vyuṣṭim aśnute
anantaṃ gītavādyena yataḥ phalam udāhṛtam
evaṃ yaḥ puruṣaḥ kuryād anantārādhanaṃ śuciḥ
evaṃ dālbhya hṛṣīkeśo narair bhaktyā yathāvidhi
phalaṃ dadāty asulabhaṃ salilenāpi pūjitaḥ
rāgādyapetaṃ hṛdayaṃ vāg duṣṭā nānṛtādinā
hiṃsādirahitaḥ kāyaḥ keśavārādhanatrayam
rāgādidūṣite citte nāspadī madhusūdanaḥ
na yogyā keśavastutyai vāg duṣṭā cānṛtādinā
tamaso nāśanāyālaṃ nendor lekhā ghanāvṛtā
hiṃsādidūṣitaḥ kāyaḥ keśavārādhane kutaḥ
sarvasvam api kṛṣṇāya yo dadyāt kuṭilāśayaḥ
rāgādyapetaṃ hṛdayaṃ kuru tvaṃ keśavārpitam
ārādhanavidhiḥ sarvo bhūyaḥ pṛcchāmi tad vada
mātāmahaṃ kāṇvam udāravīryaṃ maharṣim abhyarcya kulaprasūtim
yathāvad ācaṣṭa tato mahātmā sa rājavaryāya yathā kuleṣu
saṃpūjya viṣṇuṃ vidhinopavāsī sraggandhadhūpānnavaropahāraiḥ
gṛhṇīta māsaṃ pratimāsapūjām dānādiyuktaṃ vratam abdam ekam
ghṛtaṃ tilān vrīhiyavaṃ hiraṇyaṃ yavānnam ambhaḥkarakānnapānam
chattraṃ payo 'nnaṃ guḍaphāṇitāḍhyaṃ srakcandanaṃ vastram anukrameṇa
aśnīta yāny ātmaviśuddhihetoḥ saṃprāśanānīha nibodha tāni
gomūtram ambho ghṛtam āmaśākaṃ dūrvā dadhi vrīhiyavāṃs tilāṃś ca
sūryāṃśutaptaṃ jalam ambu dārbhaṃ kṣīraṃ ca māsakramaśopayuñjyāt
kuruṣva viṣṇuṃ bhagavantam īśam ārādhya kāmān akhilān upaiti
yadā ca śukladvādaśyāṃ nakṣatraṃ śravaṇaṃ bhavet
tadā sā tu mahāpuṇyā dvādaśī vijayā smṛtā
tasyāṃ snātaḥ sarvatīrthaiḥ snāto bhavati mānavaḥ
saṃpūjya varṣapūjāyāḥ sakalaṃ phalam aśnute
yat kṣemam api vai tasyāṃ sahasraṃ śrāvaṇe tu tat
anyasyām eva tithyāṃ śubhāyāṃ śrāvaṇaṃ yadā
rohiṇyāś ca yadā kṛṣṇa pakṣe 'ṣṭamyāṃ dvijottama
jayantī nāma sā proktā sarvapāpaharā tithiḥ
saptajanmakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ svalpaṃ vā yadi vā bahu
homajapyādidānānāṃ phalaṃ ca śatasaṃmitam
upavāsaś ca tatrokto mahāpātakanāśanaḥ
ekadaśyāṃ śuklapakṣe yadā rkṣaṃ vai punarvasuḥ
nāmnā sātijayākhyātā tithīnām uttamā tithiḥ
yo dadāti tilaprasthaṃ tṛṣkālaṃ vatsaraṃ naraḥ
upavāsaṃ ca tasyāṃ yaḥ karoty etat samaṃ smṛtam
pratyakṣatāṃ prayāty alpaṃ tadānantaphalaṃ smṛtam
sagareṇa kakutsthena duṃdhumāreṇa gādhinā
tasyām ārādhitaḥ kṛṣṇo dattavān nikhilāṃ bhuvam
kapilāṃ vipramukhyāya dadāty anudinaṃ hi yaḥ
snāpyamānaṃ ca paśyati ye ghṛtenottarāyaṇe
te yānti viṣṇusālokyaṃ sarvapāpavivarjitāḥ
maitreyī brāhmaṇī pūrvaṃ yājñavalkyam apṛcchata
praṇipatya mahābhāgaṃ yogeśvaram akalmaṣam
pāpapraśamanāyālaṃ yat puṇyasyopavṛṃhakam
kāni dānāni śastāni snānāni ca yatavrata
praśastās tithayaḥ kāś ca prāśanāni ca śaṃsa me
sarvadānāni śastāni yāny uddiśya janārdanam
kriyante śradhayā samyag upavāsavratāḥ sadā
manorathānāṃ saṃprāpti kārakaṃ pāpanāśanam
śrūyatāṃ mama dharmajñe vratānām uttamaṃ vratam
yat kṛtvā na jaḍo nāndho badhiro na ca duḥkhitaḥ
na caiveṣṭaviyogārtiṃ kaścit prāpnoti mānavaḥ
viṣṇuvratam idaṃ khyātaṃ bhāṣitaṃ viṣṇunā svayam
pauṣaśukladvitīyādi kṛtvā dinacatuṣṭayam
ṣaṇmāsapāraṇaprāyaṃ gṛhṇīyāt paramaṃ vratam
pūrvaṃ siddhārthakaiḥ snānaṃ tataḥ kṛṣṇatilaiḥ smṛtam
vacayā ca tṛtīye 'hni sarvauṣadhyā tataḥ param
nāmnā kṛṣṇācyutākhyena tathānantena pūjayet
śaśicandraśaśāṅkendu saṃjñāni brahmavādini
naktaṃ bhuñjīta matimān yāvat tiṣṭhati candramāḥ
evaṃ sarveṣu māseṣu jyeṣṭhānteṣu yaśasvini
kartavyaṃ vai vrataśreṣṭhaṃ dvitīyādicaturdinam
viprāya dakṣiṇāṃ dadyāt pañcamyāṃ ca svaśaktitaḥ
evaṃ samāpayen māsaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ prathamapāraṇam
pāraṇante ca devasya prīṇanaṃ bhaktitaḥ śubhe
yathāśaktyā tu kartavyaṃ vittaśāṭhyaṃ vivarjayet
āṣāḍhādidvitīyaṃ tu ṣaṇmāsena tapodhane
pāraṇaṃ vai samākhyātaṃ vratasyāsya śubhapradam
tathānyaiḥ pṛthivīpālair upavāsavidhānataḥ
caritaṃ munimukhyaiś ca ṛcīkacyavanādibhiḥ
surambhayā sukaikeyyā śāṇḍilyā dhūmrapiṅgayā
sudeṣṇayāthavā riṇyā matimatyā kṛtāśayā
sāvitryā paurṇamāsyā ca vairiṇyā ca subhadrayā
brāhmaṇakṣatriyaviśām iti strībhir anuṣṭhitam
prathame pādapūjā syād dvitīye nābhipūjanam
tṛtīye vakṣasaḥ pūjā caturthe śiraso hareḥ
etac cīrtvā samastebhyaḥ pāpebhyaḥ śraddhayānvitaḥ
vratam etan mahābhāge taṃ tu pūrayate nṛṇām
māghe snātasya yat puṇyaṃ prayāge pāpanāśanam
sakalaṃ tad avāpnoti śrutvā viṣṇuvrataṃ tv idam
sākṣād bhagavatā proktaṃ paramaṃ pāpanāśanam
śuklapakṣe tu pauṣasya saṃprāptidvādaśīṃ śṛṇu
pāṣaṇḍādibhir ālāpam akurvan viṣṇutatparaḥ
pauṣādipāraṇaṃ māsaiḥ ṣaḍbhir jyeṣṭhāntakaṃ smṛtam
prathame puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ nāma devasya gīyate
dvitīye mādhavākhyaṃ tu viśvarūpaṃ tu phālgune
ṣaṣṭhe jayeti devasya guhyaṃ nāma prakīrtyate
pūrveṣu ṣaṭsu māseṣu snānaprāśanayos tilāḥ
āṣāḍhādiṣu māseṣu pañcagavyam udāhṛtam
snāne ca prāśane caiva praśastaṃ pāpanāśanam
pratimāsaṃ ca devasya kṛtvā pūjāṃ yathāvidhi
viprāya dakṣiṇāṃ dadyāc śraddadhānaḥ svaśaktitaḥ
pāraṇānte ca devasya prīṇanaṃ bhaktipūrvakam
ekādaśyām uṣitvaivaṃ dvādaśyām athavā dine
etām uṣitvā dharmajñe prīṇanaṃ devatatparaḥ
tato lokeṣu vikhyātā saṃprāptidvādaśīti vai
kṛtābhilaṣitā hy eṣā prārabdhā dharmatatparaiḥ
pūrayaty akhilān kāmān saṃśrutā ca dine dine
tasminn eva dine puṇye govindadvādaśīṃ śṛṇu
yasyāṃ samyag anuṣṭhānāt prāpnoty abhimataṃ phalam
pauṣamāse site pakṣe dvādaśyāṃ samupoṣitaḥ
saṃyak saṃpūjya govindaṃ nāmnā devam adhokṣajam
puṣpadhūpopahārādyair upavāsaiḥ samāhitaḥ
viprāya dakṣiṇāṃ dadyād yathāśakti tapodhane
pāṣaṇḍādivikarmasthair ālāpaṃ ca vivarjayet
gomūtraṃ gomayaṃ vāpi dadhi kṣīram athāpi vā
godehataḥ samutpannaṃ saṃprāśnītātmaśuddhaye
tenaiva nāmnā saṃstūya dattvā viprāya dakṣiṇām
evam evākhilān māsān upoṣya prayataḥ śuciḥ
dadyād gavāhnikaṃ bhaktyā pratimāsaṃ svaśaktitaḥ
dattvā paragave bhūyaḥ śṛṇu yat phalam aśnute
suvarṇaśṛṅgāḥ pañca gāḥ ṣaṣṭhaṃ ca vṛṣabhaṃ naraḥ
govindadvādaśīm etām upoṣya divi tārakāḥ
vidyotamānā dṛśyante lokair adyāpi śobhane
upavāsavratānāṃ tu vaikalyaṃ yan mahāmune
dānakarmakṛtaṃ tasya vipāko vada yādṛśaḥ
yajñānām upavāsānāṃ vratānāṃ ca yatavrate
vaikalyāt phalavaikalyaṃ yādṛśaṃ tac chṛṇuṣva me
upavāsādinā rājyaṃ saṃprāpyaṃ te tathā vasu
bhraṣṭaiśvaryā nirdhanāś ca bhavanti puruṣāḥ punaḥ
kāṇāḥ kuṇṭhāś ca bhūyas te bhavanty andhāś ca mānavāḥ
upavāsān naraḥ patnīṃ nārī prāpya tathā patim
ye dravye saty adātāras tathānyenāhitāgnayaḥ
kule ca sati duḥśīlā dauṣkulāḥ śīlinaś ca ye
vastrānulepanair hīnā bhūṣaṇaiś cātirūpiṇaḥ
virūparūpāś ca tathā prasādhanaguṇānvitāḥ
guṇino 'pi hi doṣeṇa saṃyuktāḥ saṃbhavanti te
akhaṇḍadvādaśīm etām aśeṣeṣv eva karmasu
vaikalyapraśamāyālaṃ śṛṇuṣva gadato mama
mārgaśīrṣe site pakṣe dvādaśyāṃ niyataḥ śuciḥ
pañcagavyajalasnātaḥ pañcagavyakṛtāśanaḥ
yavavrīhibhṛtaṃ pātraṃ dadyād viprāya bhaktitaḥ
sapta janmāni yat kiṃcid mayā khaṇḍavrataṃ kṛtam
tathākhilāny akhaṇḍāni vratāni mama santu vai
evam evānumāsaṃ vai cāturmāsyavidhiḥ smṛtaḥ
prīṇanaṃ ca hareḥ kuryāt pārite pāraṇe tataḥ
caitrādiṣu ca māseṣu caturṣv anyaṃ tu pāraṇam
tatrāpi saktupātrāṇi dadyāc chraddhāsamanvitaḥ
śrāvaṇādiṣu māseṣu kārttikānteṣu pāraṇam
yatnāt tu ghṛtapātrāṇi dadyād viprāya bhaktitaḥ
evaṃ samyag yathānyāyam akhaṇḍadvādaśīṃ naraḥ
karoty avikalaṃ sarvam akhaṇḍadvādaśīvratam
akhaṇḍadvādaśī samyag upoṣyā phalakāṃkṣibhiḥ
evaṃ purā yājñavalkyaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ patnyā mahāmuniḥ
ācaṣṭa puṇyaphaladam upavāsavidhiṃ param
tathā tvam api viprarṣe keśavārādhane rataḥ
punaś caitan mahābhāga śrūyatāṃ gadato mama
proktaṃ nareṇa devānāṃ tithimāhātmyam uttamam
vijayātijayā caiva jayantī pāpanāśanī
tathottarāyaṇaṃ śastaṃ sarvadā keśavārcane
sakṛd evārcite kṛṣṇe tad etāsv api labhyate
vijayātijayā caiva jayantī pāpanāśanī
yatra saṃpūjitaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ sarvapāpaṃ vyapohati
ekādaśyāṃ site pakṣe puṣyarkṣaṃ yatra sattama
tithau bhavati sā proktā viṣṇunā pāpanāśanī
tasyāṃ saṃpūjya govindaṃ jagatām īśvareśvaram
saptajanmakṛtāt pāpān mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ
yaś copavāsaṃ kurute tasyāṃ snāto dvijottama
dānaṃ yad dīyate kiṃcit samuddiśya janārdanam
ekā ṛg devapurato japtā śraddhāvatā tathā
japtam ekaṃ muniśreṣṭha dadāty atra na saṃśayaḥ
yataḥ pāpam aśeṣaṃ vai nāśayaty atra keśavaḥ
puṣyarkṣaikādaśī brahmaṃs tenoktā pāpanāśanī
tathānyad api dharmajña śrūyatāṃ gadato mama
padadvayaṃ jagaddhātur devadevasya śārṅgiṇaḥ
saṃvatsaraḥ pādapīṭhaṃ tatra nyastaṃ padadvayam
vāsudevena viprendra bhūtānāṃ hitakāmyayā
vāmam asya padaṃ brahman uttarāyaṇasaṃjñitam
devādyaiḥ sakalair vandyaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ dakṣiṇāyanam
karoty ārādhanaṃ tasya toṣam āyāti keśavaḥ
katham ārādhanaṃ tasya devadevasya śārṅgiṇaḥ
ghṛtakṣīrādinā devaṃ snāpayed dharaṇīdharam
cāruvastropahāraiś ca puṣpadhūpānulepanaiḥ
samabhyarcya tataḥ samyag brāhmaṇānāṃ ca tarpaṇaiḥ
padadvayavrataṃ samyag gṛhṇīyād viṣṇutatparaḥ
snāto nārāyaṇaṃ vakṣye bhuñjan nārāyaṇaṃ tathā
bhuṅktvā nārāyaṇaṃ cāhaṃ gacchan nārāyaṇaṃ tataḥ
nārāyaṇasyānudinaṃ kariṣye nāmakīrtanam
yāvad adyadināt prāptaṃ kramaśo dakṣiṇāyanam
tāvan nārāyaṇaṃ vakṣye sarvam evottarāyaṇam
yāvaj jīvavadhaṃ kiṃcid jñānato 'jñānato 'pi vā
kariṣye 'haṃ tathā caiva kīrtayiṣyāmi taṃ prabhum
yadā tadānṛtaṃ kiṃcid atha vakṣyāmi durvacaḥ
ajñānād athavā jñānāt kīrtayiṣyāmi taṃ prabhum
ṣaṇmāsam eṣa me jāpo nārāyaṇamayaḥ paraḥ
taṃ smaran maraṇe yāti yāṃ gatiṃ sāstu me gatiḥ
tan mayā vāsudevāya svayam ātmā niveditaḥ
yam ante saṃsmaran yāti sa me viṣṇuḥ parā gatiḥ
yadā prātas tadā sāyaṃ madhyāhne vā mriye hy aham
ṣaṇmāsābhyantare nyāsaḥ kṛto vratamayo mayā
nārāyaṇa yathā nānyaṃ tvatto yāmi mṛte gatim
evam uccārya ṣaṇmāsa pāraṇaṃ pravaraṃ vratam
tāvan niṣpādayed yāvat saṃprāptaṃ dakṣiṇāyanam
tataś ca prīṇanaṃ kuryād yathāśaktyā jagadguroḥ
bhojayed brāhmaṇān samyag dadyāt tebhyaś ca dakṣiṇām
evaṃ vratam idaṃ dālbhya yaḥ pārayati mānavaḥ
nārī vā sarvapāpebhyaḥ ṣaṇmāsād vipra mucyate
ṣaṇmāsābhyantare cāsya maraṇaṃ yadi jāyate
bhagavān ujjagau viṣṇuḥ purā gārgyāya pṛcchate
phālgunāmalapakṣasya ekādaśyām upoṣitaḥ
snātvā samyak tam abhyarcya dadyād viprāya dakṣiṇām
praṇipatya jagannātham iti vāṇīm udīrayet
pātālasaṃsthā vasudhā yaṃ prasādya manorathān
yam abhyarcyāditiḥ prāptā sakalāṃś ca manorathān
putrāṃś caivepsitān devaḥ pradadātu manorathān
manorathān avāpāgryān sa dadātu manorathān
evam abhyarcya pūjāṃ ca niṣpādya haraye tataḥ
phālgunaṃ caitravaiśākhau jyeṣṭhamāsaṃ ca pārthiva
caturbhiḥ pāraṇaṃ māsair ebhir niṣpāditaṃ bhavet
dahec ca guggulaṃ prāśya gośṛṅgakṣālanaṃ jalam
tataś ca śrūyatām anyad āṣāḍhādau tu yā kriyā
jātīpuṣpāṇi dhūpaś ca śastaḥ sarjaraso nṛpa
prāśya darbhodakaṃ cātra śālyannaṃ ca nivedanam
svayaṃ tad eva cāśnīyāc śeṣaṃ pūrvavad ācaret
kārttikādiṣu māseṣu gomūtraṃ kāyaśodhanam
sugandhaṃ cecchayā dhūpaṃ pūjābhṛṅgārakeṇa ca
kāsāraṃ cātra naivedyam aśnīyāt tac ca vai svayam
pratimāsaṃ ca viprāya dātavyā dakṣiṇā tathā
prīṇanaṃ cecchayā viṣṇoḥ pāraṇe pāraṇe gate
yathāśakti yathāprīti vittaśāṭhyaṃ vivarjayet
sadbhāvenaiva govindaḥ pūjitaḥ prīyate yataḥ
pāraṇānte yathāśaktyā snāpitaḥ pūjito hariḥ
prīṇitaś cepsitān kāmān dadāty avyāhatān nṛpa
eṣā dhanyā pāpaharā dvādaśī phalam icchatām
yathābhilaṣitān kāmān dadāti manujeśvara
pūrayaty akhilān bhaktyā yataś caiṣā manorathān
manorathadvādaśīyaṃ tato lokeṣu viśrutā
upoṣyaitāṃ tribhuvanaṃ prāptam indreṇa vai purā
adityā cepsitāḥ putrā dhanaṃ cośanasā nṛpa
rājarṣibhis tathā vipraiḥ strībhiḥ śūdraiś ca bhūpate
yaṃ yaṃ kāmam abhidhyāyed vratam etad upoṣitaḥ
taṃ tam āpnoty asaṃdigdhaṃ viṣṇor ārādhanodyataḥ
rogābhibhūtaś cārogyaṃ kanyā prāpnoti satpatim
sarvān kāmān avāpnoti mṛtaḥ svarge ca modate
nāputro nādhano neṣṭa viyogī na ca nirguṇaḥ
ya eva vratasaṃcīrṇo viṣṇuloke mahīyate
svargaloke sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ manujādhipa
bhogān abhimatān bhuktvā svargaloke 'bhikāṅkṣitān
iha puṇyavatāṃ nRṇāṃ dhanināṃ sādhuśīlinām
gṛheṣu jāyate rājan sarvavyādhivivarjitaḥ
aśokapūrṇimāṃ cānyāṃ śṛṇuśva vadato mama
yām upoṣya naraḥ śokaṃ nāpnoti strī tathāpi vā
phālgunāmalapakṣasya pūrṇimāsyāṃ nareśvara
mṛjjalena naraḥ snātvā dattvā śirasi vai mṛdam
mṛtprāśanaṃ tathā kṛtvā kṛtvā ca sthaṇḍilaṃ mṛdā
puṣpaiḥ patrais tathābhyarcya bhūdharaṃ nānyamānasaḥ
dharaṇīṃ ca tathā devīm aśokety abhidhīyate
yathā viśokāṃ dharaṇīṃ kṛtavāṃs tvaṃ janārdanaḥ
tathā māṃ sarvapāpebhyo mocayāśeṣadhāriṇi
yathā samastabhūtānāṃ dhāraṇaṃ tvayy avasthitam
tathā viśokaṃ kuru māṃ sakalecchāvibhūtibhiḥ
dhyātamātre yathā viṣṇau svāsthyaṃ yātāsi medini
tathā manaḥ svasthatāṃ me kuru tvaṃ bhūtadhāriṇi
anenaiva prakāreṇa catvāraḥ phālgunādayaḥ
upoṣyā nṛpate māsāḥ prathamaṃ tat tu pāraṇam
āṣāḍhādiṣu māseṣu tadvat snānaṃ mṛdambunā
tad eva prāśanaṃ pūjā tathaivendos tathārhaṇam
caturṣv anyeṣu caivoktaṃ tathā vai kārttikādiṣu
pāraṇaṃ tritayaṃ caiva cāturmāsikam ucyate
prathamaṃ dharaṇī nāma stutyai māsacatuṣṭayam
dvitīye medinī vācyā tṛtīye ca vasuṃdharā
pāraṇe pāraṇe vastra pūjayā pūjayen nṛpa
dharaṇīṃ devadevaṃ ca ghṛtasnānena keśavam
vastrābhāve tu sūtreṇa pūjayed dharaṇīṃ tathā
ghṛtābhāve tathā kṣīraṃ śastaṃ vā salilaṃ hareḥ
pātālamūlagatayā cīrṇam etan mahāvratam
dharaṇyā keśavaprītyai tataḥ prāptā samunnatiḥ
devena coktā dharaṇī varāhavapuṣā tadā
vratenānena kalyāṇi praṇato yaḥ kariṣyati
vratam etad upāśritya pāraṇaṃ ca yathāvidhi
tathaiva kurute pūjāṃ bhaktyā mama śubho janaḥ
viśokaḥ sarvakalyāṇa bhājano matimāñ janaḥ
sarvatra pūjyaḥ satataṃ sarveṣām aparājitaḥ
tathā tvam api kalyāṇi bhaviṣyasi na saṃśayaḥ
evam etan mahāpuṇyaṃ sarvapāpopaśāntidam
viśokākhyaṃ vrataṃ dhanyaṃ tat kuruṣva mahīpate
strīṇāṃ dharmaṃ dvijaśreṣṭha upavāsaṃ bhavan mama
kaumārake gṛhasthāyā vidhavāyāś ca sattama
dharmaṃ prabrūhy aśeṣeṇa bhagavan prītikārakam
upakārāya ca strīṇāṃ triṣu lokeṣv anuttamam
praśnam etat purā devī śailarājasutā patim
kumārikābhir deveśa gṛhasthābhiś ca keśavaḥ
sādhu sādhvi tvayā pṛṣṭam etan nārāyaṇāśritam
upavāsādi yat tattvaṃ śrūyatām asya yo vidhiḥ
yogyaṃ patiṃ samāsādya nārī dharmam avāpnute
duḥśīle 'pi hi kāmārte nārī prāpnoti bhartari
anārādhya jagannāthaṃ sarvalokeśvaraṃ harim
katham āpnoti vai nārī patiṃ śīlaguṇānvitam
kartavyaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ tasya śrūyatāṃ varavarṇini
yac cīrtvā sarvanārīṇāṃ śreṣṭham āpnoty asaṃśayam
anujñāṃ prāpya pitṛto mātṛtaś ca kumārikā
triṣūttareṣu svṛkṣeṣu patikāmā kumārikā
atibālye ca yat kiṃcit tayā pāpam anuṣṭhitam
tad eva prāpnuyād bhadre nārāyaṇaparāyaṇā
ṣaṇmāsaṃ prīṇanaṃ kāryaṃ bhaktyā śaktyā ca vai hareḥ
pāraṇānte mahābhage tathā brāhmaṇatarpaṇam
gārhasthye 'vasthitā nārī bhaktyā saṃpūjayet patim
sa eva devatā tasyāḥ pūjyaḥ pūjyataraś ca saḥ
toṣam āyāti sarvātmā paramātmā janārdanaḥ
naiva tasyāḥ pṛthag yajño na śrāddhaṃ nāpy upoṣitam
bhartṛśuśrūṣaṇenaiva prāpnoti strī yathepsitam
tenaiva sāpy anujñātā tasya śuśrūṣaṇād anu
ghṛtakṣīrābhiṣekaiś ca brāhmaṇānāṃ ca tarpaṇaiḥ
gītavādyais tathā hṛdyair upavāsaiś ca bhāmini
evam ārādhya govindam anujñātā yathāvidhi
patinā sakalān kāmān avāpnoti na saṃśayaḥ
patinā tv ananujñātā kiṃcit puṇyaṃ karoti yā
viphalaṃ tad aśeṣaṃ vai tasyāḥ śailavarātmaje
nānujñātā tu yā nārī patinārcati keśavam
yā tu bhartṛparā nārī nārāyaṇam atandritā
bhaktyā saṃpūjayed devaṃ toṣam āyāti keśavaḥ
yā tu bhartrā parityaktā tathā yā mṛtabhartṛkā
pāṣaṇḍānugato vāpi yasyā bhartā maheśvara
prāyo dadāti nānujñāṃ viṣṇor ārādhane tadā
katham ārādhanaṃ kāryaṃ viṣṇos tad vada śaṃkara
yā tu bhartrā parityaktā sā saṃpūjya nijaṃ patim
na nindākaraṇī tasya śreyo'bhidhyāyinī tathā
ārādhayej jagannāthaṃ sarvadhātāram acyutam
kṛtopavāsā puṣpādi nivedya sakalaṃ tataḥ
svayaṃ yathābhilaṣitaṃ prārthayet taṃ varaṃ tataḥ
evaṃ bhartṛparityaktā yoṣid ārādhanaṃ hareḥ
kurvāṇā sakalān kāmān avāpnoti na saṃśayaḥ
tasya puṇyasya saṃpūrṇam ardhaṃ prāpnoti sā śubhe
yat tu sā kurute puṇyaṃ vinā doṣeṇa yojjhitā
kurvītārādhanaṃ nārī upavāsādinā hareḥ
etat tavoktaṃ yat pṛṣṭaṃ tvayāhaṃ girinandini
vidhavānām ato dharmaṃ śrūyatāṃ viṣṇutuṣṭidam
snātā pratidinaṃ dadyāt svabhartṛsalilāñjalim
kuryād yānudinaṃ bhaktyā devānām api pūjanam
pūrtadharmāśritaṃ cānyat kuryān nityam atandritā
nityakarma ṛte cāsyā neṣṭaṃ karma vidhīyate
viṣṇor ārādhanaṃ caiva kuryān nityam upoṣitā
upavāsāṃś ca vividhān kuryāc chāstroditān śubhe
lokāntarasthaṃ bhartāram ātmānaṃ ca varānane
tārayaty ubhayaṃ nārī yetthaṃ dharmaparāyaṇā
putraiśvaryasthitā nārī upavāsādinā harim
śubhāṃl lokāṃs tathā bhartur ātmanaś ca yathepsitān
sakalaṃ pūrayaty astaṃ pāpaṃ nayati cākhilam
ātmanaś caiva bhartuś ca nārī paramikāṃ gatim
dadāty ārādhya govindaṃ saputrā vidhavā ca yā
keśavārādhanaṃ kāryaṃ lokadvayaphalapradam
ye narā mṛtapatnikās tair apy etad aśeṣataḥ
viṣṇor ārādhanaṃ kāryaṃ tīrthasthair athavā gṛhe
brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vaiśyaḥ strī śūdraś ca varānane
anārādhya hṛṣīkeśaṃ nāpnoti paramāṃ gatim
aiśvaryaṃ saṃtatiṃ śreṣṭhām ārogyaṃ dravyasaṃpadam
dadāti bhagavān viṣṇur gatim agryāṃ sutoṣitaḥ
evaṃ śailasutā proktā svayaṃ devena śaṃbhunā
ārādhanīyo nātuṣṭe viṣṇau saṃprāpyate gatiḥ
na durgatiṃ rauravādīn narakāṃś ca na gacchati
yam ārādhyeśvaraṃ vandyaṃ kas taṃ viṣṇuṃ na pūjayet
tasmād amuṣmikān kleśān narake yāś ca yātanāḥ
bhagavan yātanā ghorāḥ śrūyante narakeṣu yāḥ
śṛṇu dālbhyātighorāṇāṃ yātanānāṃ mayoditam
aṅgārapūrṇamadhyo 'sau jvālāmālāpariṣkṛtaḥ
satyahānyānṛtī yāti tatra pāparatir naraḥ
rauravād dviguṇaś caiva mahārauvarasaṃjñitaḥ
taptatāmrapuṭāṅgāra jvalatpāvakasaṃvṛtaḥ
nāścaryaṃ dvijaśārdūla varṣalakṣayutāni ca
kālasūtreṇa cchidyante cakrārūḍhāś ca mānavāḥ
kālāṅgulisthena sadā āpādatalamastakāt
tatrāpi vañcakā yānti ye caivotkocajīvinaḥ
devavedadvijātīnāṃ ye nindāṃ kurvate sadā
saṃśṛṇvanti ca ye mūḍhā ye ca matsariṇo 'dhamāḥ
karambhavālukākumbha saṃjñaṃ ca narakaṃ śṛṇu
hṛtaṃ yaiś ca jalaṃ te 'pi tasmin yānti narādhamāḥ
gonipāneṣu vighnāni mūḍhā ye cāpi kurvate
andhe tamasi duṣpāre śītārtiparikampitāḥ
bhrāmyante mānavā gātraiḥ samastaiḥ sphuṭitāsthibhiḥ
govadhaḥ strīvadhaḥ pāpaiḥ kṛtaṃ yaiś ca gavānṛtam
utpāṭyate tathā jihvā saṃdaṃśair bhṛśadāruṇaiḥ
ākriśakānāṃ duṣṭānāṃ sadaivābaddhabhāṣiṇām
paradāraparadravya hiṃsakāḥ puruṣādhamāḥ
āyasīṃ ca śilāṃ taptām aśeṣāṅgais tathā narāḥ
paradāraratā evaṃ samāliṅganti pāpinaḥ
sarvāṅgair vikṛtair raktam udgiranto 'tipīḍitāḥ
yantreṣv anyeṣu pīḍyante jantupīḍākarā narāḥ
vṛkaiḥ saṃbhakṣyate pṛṣṭhaṃ narāṇāṃ pāpakāriṇām
janasya pṛṣṭhamāṃsaṃ yair bhakṣitaṃ pāpakāribhiḥ
sadbhāvapravaṇā yais tu bhagnā viśrambhino janāḥ
ayomukhaiḥ khagair bhagnāḥ khaṇḍakhaṇḍaṃ tathāparaiḥ
vrajanti pāpakarmāṇaḥ śvaśṛgālais tathāparaiḥ
sūṣāyām api dhāsyante jvaladagnicayāvṛtāḥ
pāṣāṇapeṣyaṃ piṣyante tathānye pāpakarmiṇaḥ
devatātithibhṛtyāṇām adattvā bhuñjate tu ye
mṛṣāgatās tathāivaikyaṃ trapuṣā sīsakena ca
prayānti puruṣās tailaiḥ kvāthyante 'nye punaḥ punaḥ
varṇadharmaparityāge naikyaṃ ye puruṣā gatāḥ
te 'pi pāpasamācārā varṇasaṃkarakāriṇaḥ
svarūpaṃ nārakasyāgneḥ śṛṇuṣva kathayāmi te
śastradhārās tathaivaitā mṛṇālaprastaraṃ naraḥ
himakhaṇḍacayāchanno nivātaṃ manyate naraḥ
vimukto nārakāc chītāt prakāśaṃ tamasas tamaḥ
protā gudeṣu bhinnāṅgā ārtā rāvavirāviṇaḥ
śūleṣu loheṣv apare triśūleṣu tathāpare
yājyopādhyāyadāmpatya suhṛnmitrasutādiṣu
kṛto bhedo durācārair yair alīkoktibhāṣibhiḥ
āyasāḥ kaṇṭakās tīkṣṇā narake kūṭaśālmalau
teṣu protā durātmānaḥ paradārabhujo narāḥ
kṛmikīṭajalaukādi tīkṣṇadaṃṣṭrāsyavikṣatāḥ
bhrāmyante cāndhatāmisre vṛthāmāṃsāśino hi ye
etāṃś cānyāṃś ca narakāñ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
karmāntaraṃ jano bhuṅkte pariṇāmāṃś ca cetasaḥ
yādṛk karma manuṣyāṇāṃ tādṛg viṣayarūpavat
pariṇāmaṃ mano yāti śubhāśubhamayaṃ dvija
atīvabhīṣaṇān itthaṃ śastrāgnibhayadān naraḥ
aho 'tikaṣṭapāpānāṃ vipāko narakasthitaiḥ
puṇyasya karmaṇaḥ pākaḥ puṇya eva dvijottama
tathaiva pākaḥ pāpānāṃ puruṣair narakasthitaiḥ
bhujyate tāvad akhilaṃ yāvat pāpaṃ kṣayaṃ gatam
yadā tu pāpasya jayaḥ kṣīyate sukṛtaṃ tadā
śubhasya karmaṇo vṛddhau kṣayam āyāty aśobhanam
jayāya dvādaśī śastā nRṇāṃ sukṛtakarmaṇām
yām upoṣya dvijaśreṣṭha na yāti narakaṃ naraḥ
phālgunāmalapakṣasya ekādaśyām upoṣitaḥ
dvādaśyāṃ tu dvijaśreṣṭha pūjayen madhusūdanam
ekādaśyāṃ samuddiṣṭaṃ viṣṇor nāmānukīrtanam
pūjāyāṃ vāsudevasya kurvīta susamāhitaḥ
namo nārāyaṇāyeti vācyaṃ ca svapatā niśi
krodhaḥ prapañca īrṣyā ca dambho lobhaś ca varjitaḥ
asāratāṃ ca loke 'smin saṃsāre bhāvayen matim
tathaiva kuryād dvādaśyāṃ nāmnām uccāraṇaṃ dvija
kāmaṃ krodhaṃ ca lobhaṃ ca dambham īrṣyāṃ ca varjayet
mānadrohādidoṣāṃś ca sarvān dhanamadodbhūtān
bhāvayed viṣṇubhaktāṃś ca saṃsārāsāratāṃ tathā
evaṃ bhāvitacittena prāṇināṃ hitam icchatā
yavapātrāṇi pūrvaṃ tu dadyān māsacatuṣṭayam
āṣāḍhādidvitīyaṃ tu pāraṇaṃ yan mahāmate
tatrāpi ghṛtapātrāṇi dadyāc chraddhāsamanvitaḥ
kārttikādiṣu māseṣu māghanteṣu tathā tilān
viprāya dadyāt pātrashtān pratimāsam upoṣitaḥ
nāmatrayam aśeṣeṣu māsi māsi dinadvayam
tathaivoccārayed dadyād dvādaśyāṃ ca yavādikam
praṇamya ca hṛṣīkeśaṃ kṛtapūjaḥ prasādayet
nārāyaṇa tvāṃ praṇato 'smy acintya jayo 'stu me śāśvatapuṇyarāśeḥ
nārāyaṇoṃ bhūtim upaitu puṇyam prayātu cāśeṣam aghaṃ vināśam
viṣṇo puṇyodbhavo me 'stu vāsudevāstu me śubham
nārāyaṇāstu dharmo me jahi pāpam aśeṣataḥ
puṇyaṃ vivṛddhim āyātu yātu pāpaṃ tu saṃkṣayam
ākāśādiṣu śabdādau śrotrādau mahadādiṣu
prayātu sukṛtasyāstu mamānudivasaṃ jayaḥ
pāpasya hāniḥ puṇyaṃ ca vṛddhim abhyety anuttamām
bhuñjīta kṛtakṛtyas tu pāraṇe pāraṇe gate
pāraṇānte ca devasya prīṇanaṃ śaktito dvija
kurvītākhilapāṣaṇḍair ālāpaṃ ca vivarjayet
dvādaśī narakaṃ mṛtyo yām upoṣya na paśyati
nāgnayo na ca śastrāṇi na ca lohamūkhāḥ khagāḥ
nāmoccāraṇamātreṇa viṣṇoḥ kṣīṇo 'ghasaṃcayaḥ
na yāti narakaṃ martyaḥ saṃkṣīṇāśeṣapātakaḥ
tasmāt pāṣaṇḍisaṃsargam akurvan dvādaśīm imām
upoṣya puṇyopacayī na yāti narakaṃ naraḥ
pāṣaṇḍibhir asaṃsparśam asaṃbhāṣaṇam eva ca
viṣṇor ārādhanaparair naraiḥ kāryam upoṣitaiḥ
kiṃ brūhi lakṣaṇaṃ teṣāṃ yādṛśān varjayed vratī
kathaṃcid yadi saṃlāpa darśanasparśanādikam
upoṣitānāṃ pāṣaṇḍair narāṇāṃ vipra jāyate
kiṃ tatra vada kartavyaṃ yenākhaṇḍaṃ vrataṃ bhavet
śrutismṛtyuditaṃ dharmaṃ varṇāśramavibhāgajam
vikarmābhiratā mūḍhā yuktiprāgalbhyadurmadāḥ
pāṣaṇḍinas te duḥśīlā narakārhā narādhamāḥ
tāṃs tu pāṣaṇḍinaḥ pāpān vikarmasthāṃś ca mānavān
vaiḍālavratikāṃś caiva nityam eva tu nālapet
saṃbhāṣyaitāñ śuciṣadaṃ cintayed acyutaṃ budhaḥ
idaṃ codāharet samyak kṛtvā tatpravaṇaṃ manaḥ
śārīram antaḥkaraṇopaghātaṃ vācaś ca viṣṇur bhagavān aśeṣam
śamaṃ nayatv astu mameha śarma pāpād anante hṛdi saṃniviṣṭe
antaḥśuddhiṃ bahiḥśuddhiṃ śuddho 'ntar mama yo 'cyutaḥ
bāhyopaghātād anagho boddhā ca bhagavān ajaḥ
śuddhiṃ nayatv anantātmā viṣṇuś cetasi saṃsthitaḥ
etat saṃbhāṣya japtavyaṃ pāṣaṇḍibhir upoṣitaiḥ
namaḥ śuciṣadety uktvā sūryaṃ paśyeta vīkṣitaiḥ
śrūyate ca purā martyāḥ svecchayā svargagāminaḥ
yajñādhyayanadāneṣu vartamānaiś ca mānavaiḥ
daiteyāś ca parābhāvam atuṣṭāv asurā yayuḥ
tataś ca ṣaṇḍo markaś ca daityendrāṇāṃ purohitau
cakratuḥ karma devānāṃ vināśāyātibhīṣaṇam
tatrotpanno 'tikṛṣṇāṅgas tamaḥprāyo 'tidāruṇaḥ
dambhādhāraḥ śāṭhyasāro nidrāprakṛtir ulvaṇaḥ
mahāmoha iti khyātaḥ kṛtyarūpo vibhīṣaṇaḥ
vedadevadvijātīnām ekāṃśena sa nindanam
vikarmaṇy apareṇāpi saṃyojayati mānavān
jñānabuddhyā tathājñānaṃ gṛhṇāty ajñānamohitaḥ
evaṃ sa tu mahāmohaḥ ṣaṇḍamarkopapāditaḥ
tanmohitānām acirād viveko yāti saṃkṣayam
kṣīṇajñānā vikarmāṇi kurvanty aharaho dvija
dharmabuddhyā tataḥ pāpaṃ kurvanty ajñānadurmadāḥ
jñānāvalepas tatraiva tatas teṣāṃ prajāyate
suhṛdbhir vāryamāṇās te paṇḍitaiś ca dayālubhiḥ
prayacchanty uttaraṃ ṃūḍhāḥ kūṭayuktisamanvitam
pāṣaṇḍino durācārāḥ parānnaguṇavādinaḥ
asaṃskṛtānnabhoktāro vrātyāḥ saṃskāravarjitāḥ
pāṣaṇḍāḥ pāpasaṃkalpā dāmbhikāḥ śaṭhabuddhayaḥ
varṇasaṃkarakartāro māyāvyājopajīvinaḥ
niḥśaucā vakramatayo nānyadastītivādinaḥ
evaṃvidhās te sanmārgād vedaproktād bahiḥsthitāḥ
kriyākalāpaṃ nindanta ṛgyajuḥsāmasaṃjñitam
ātmānaṃ ca parāṃś caiva kurvanti narakasthitān
teṣāṃ darśanasaṃbhāṣa sparśanāni naraiḥ sadā
parityājyāni dṛṣṭe ca proktaḥ saṃbhāṣaṇe ca yaḥ
saṃsparśe ca budhaḥ snātvā śuciḥ śuciṣadaṃ smaret
bhavaty ataḥ sadaivaiṣām ālāpasparśanaṃ tyajet
puṇyakāmo mahābhāgaḥ kiṃ punar yad upoṣitaḥ
pāṣaṇḍinām aśeṣāṇām aprītir vedakarmaṇi
te hy adhogāminaḥ proktā āsuraṃ bhāvam āśritāḥ
abhīṣṭād anyato vāpi padād yena na vicyutim
prāpnoti puruṣo brahman nārī vāpuṇyasaṃkṣayāt
satyam etan mahābhāga duḥkhaṃ prāptasya saṃkṣayaḥ
tad etac chrūyatāṃ dālbhya yathā neṣṭāt paricyutiḥ
sargāder jāyate samyag upavāsavatāṃ satām
dvādaśarkṣāṇi viprarṣe pratimāsaṃ tu yāni vai
tannāmāny acyutaṃ teṣu samyak saṃpūjayed budhaḥ
āditaḥ kṛttikāṃ kṛtvā kārttike munipuṅgava
naivedyaṃ kṛsaraṃ pūrvam annaṃ māsacatuṣṭayam
nivedayet kārttikādi saṃyāvaṃ ca tataḥ param
āṣāḍhādau ca devāya pāyasaṃ vai nivedayet
naivedyaṃ svayam aśnīyān naktaṃ saṃpūjite 'cyute
praṇamya prārthayed vidvāñ śuciḥ snāto yathāvidhi
aiśvaryavittādi sadākṣayaṃ me 'kṣayā ca me saṃtatir acyutāstu
tathācyutaṃ me kuru vāñchitaṃ yan mayā padaṃ pāpaharāprameya
yathāvan muniśārdūla cyutiṃ nāpnoti mānavaḥ
atrāpi śrūyate siddhā kācit svarge mahāvratā
nārī tapodhanā bhūtvā prakhyātā śāmbharāyaṇī
samastasaṃdehaharā sadā svargaukasāṃ hi sā
pūrvendrā parataḥ pūrve ye babhūvuḥ sureśvarāḥ
teṣāṃ caritam icchāmi śrotum āṅgirasāṃ vara
prāha dharmabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ paramarṣir bṛhaspatiḥ
nāhaṃ cirantanān vedmi devarāja sureśvarān
ātmanaḥ samakālīnaṃ mām avaihi sureśvara
praṣṭavyo 'tra mahābhāga kṛtādivasatir divi
bṛhaspatiś ciraṃ dhyātvā punar āha śacīpatim
tapasvinīṃ mahābhāgāṃ smṛtvāsau śāmbharāyaṇīm
na devā na ca gandharvā na cānye cirasaṃsthitāḥ
cirantanānāṃ cariteṣv abhijñā tridaśeśvara
ekaiva cirakālajñā dharmajñā śakra kevalam
jānāty akhiladevendra caritaṃ śāmbharāyaṇī
yayau yatra mahābhāgā tāpasī śāmbharāyaṇī
sā tau dṛṣṭvā samāyātau devarājabṛhaspatī
yad vāṃ kāryaṃ mahābhāgau sakalaṃ tad ihocyatām
āvām abhyāgatau praṣṭuṃ tvām atrātivivekinīm
yac ca kāryaṃ mahābhāge tat pṛṣṭā kathayeha nau
tadākhyāhi mahābhāge devendrasya kutūhalāt
yadi śakyaṃ mayā kartuṃ tat kariṣye vimṛṣyatu
tasmāt pūrvataro yaś ca tasyāpi prathamāś ca ye
teṣāṃ pūrvatarā ye ca vedmi tān akhilān aham
teṣāṃ ca caritaṃ kṛtsnaṃ jānāmy āṅgirasāṃ vara
manvantarāṇy anekāni sṛṣṭiṃ ca tridivaukasām
saptarṣīn subahūn deva manūnāṃ ca sutān nṛpa
tat pṛccha tvaṃ vadāmy eṣā pūrvendracaritaṃ mune
evam ukte tatas tābhyāṃ pṛṣṭā sā śāmbharāyaṇī
yathāvad ācaṣṭa tayoḥ pūrvendracaritaṃ dvija
tayor jagāda caritaṃ yathāvac chāmbharāyaṇī
tataḥ kautūhalaparo devarāṭ tāṃ tapasvinīm
uvāca jānāsi kathaṃ tvam etac chāmbharāyaṇi
sarva eva hi devendrāḥ svargasthā ye manīṣiṇaḥ
kiṃ kṛtaṃ vada dharmajñe tvayā yeneyam akṣayā
caritaṃ ca mayā teṣāṃ śrutaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ tathaiva ca
pratyuvāca mahābhāgā yathāvac chāmbharāyaṇī
māsarkṣeṣv acyuto devaḥ pratimāsaṃ sureśvara
yathoktavratayā samyak sapta varṣāṇi pūjitaḥ
tasyeyaṃ karmaṇo vyuṣṭir acyutārādhanasya me
svargaṃ dravyamayaiśvaryaṃ saṃtatiṃ vāpi yo 'cyutām
naro vāñchati tenetthaṃ toṣaṇīyo 'cyutaḥ prabhuḥ
svargavāsākṣayatvaṃ ca māsarkṣācyutapūjanāt
dharmārthakāmamokṣāṃs tu vāñchatāṃ vibudhādhipa
viṣṇor ārādhanān nānyat paramaṃ siddhikāraṇam
tasyās tad vacanaṃ śrutvā devarājabṛhaspatī
tāṃ tathety ūcatuḥ sādhvīṃ ceratuś cāpi tad vratam
māsarkṣācyutapūjāyāṃ bhavethās tanmanāḥ sadā
duṣṭagrahopaghātaiś ca sarvakālam upadrutāḥ
ābhicārukakṛtyābhiḥ sparṣarogaiś ca dāruṇaiḥ
sadā saṃpīḍyamānās te tiṣṭhanti munisattama
te narā muniśārdūla graharogādibhāginaḥ
viṣagrahajvarāṇāṃ te manuṣyā dālbhya bhājanāḥ
ārogyaṃ paramām ṛddhiṃ manasā yad yad icchati
kṛtyāsparśabhayaṃ vāpi toṣite madhusūdane
sarvaduṣṭaśamas tasya saumyās tasya sadā grahāḥ
devānām apradhṛṣyo 'sau tuṣṭo yasya janārdanaḥ
yaḥ samaḥ sarvabhūteṣu yathātmani tathāpare
upavādādinā tena toṣyate madhusūdanaḥ
toṣite tatra jāyante narāḥ pūṛṇamanorathāḥ
na teṣāṃ śatravo naiva sparśarogābhicārukāḥ
graharogādikaṃ vāpi pāpakāryaṃ na jāyate
avyāhatāni kṛṣṇasya cakrādīny ātmayudhāni tam
rakṣanti sakalāpadbhyo yena viṣṇur upāsitaḥ
anārādhitagovindā ye narā duḥkhabhāginaḥ
teṣāṃ duḥkhābhibhūtānāṃ kartavyaṃ yad dayālubhiḥ
paśyadbhiḥ sarvabhūtasthaṃ vāsudevaṃ mahāmune
samadṛṣṭibhir īśeśaṃ tan mama brūhy aśeṣataḥ
kuśamūlasthito brahmā kuśamadhye janārdanaḥ
kuśāgre śaṃkaraṃ vidyāt trayo devā vyavasthitāḥ
gṛhītvā ca sa mūlāgrān kuśāñ śuddhān upaspṛśet
mārjayet sarvagātrāṇi kuśāgrair dālbhya śāntikṛt
śarīre yasya tiṣṭhanti kuśasthajalabindavaḥ
naśyanti tasya pāpāni garuḍenaiva pannagāḥ
viṣṇubhaktā viśeṣeṇa cidgatamānasaḥ
rogagrahaviṣārtānāṃ kuryāc chāntim imāṃ śubhām
nārasiṃhaṃ samabhyarcya śucau deśe kuśāsane
vārāhaṃ nārasiṃhaṃ ca vāmanaṃ viṣṇum eva ca
dhyātvā samāhito bhūtvā dikṣu nāmāni vinyāset
pūrve nārāyaṇaḥ pātu vārijākṣas tu dakṣiṇe
īśānyām avatād viṣṇur āgneyyāṃ ca janārdanaḥ
nairṛtyāṃ padmanābhaś ca vāyavyāṃ caiva mādhavaḥ
etābhyo daśadigbhyas tu sarvataḥ pātu keśavaḥ
aṅguṣṭhāgre tu govindaṃ tarjanyāṃs tu mahīdharam
madhyamāyāṃ hṛṣīkeśam anāmikyāṃ trivikramam
kaṇiṣṭhāyāṃ nyased viṣṇuṃ karamadhye tu mādhavam
evaṃ nyāsaṃ purā kṛtvā paścād aṅgeṣu vinyaset
śikhāyāṃ keśavaṃ nyasya mūrdhni nārāyaṇaṃ nyaset
trivikramaṃ kapālasthaṃ vāmanaṃ karṇamūlayoḥ
uttaroṣṭhe hṛṣīkeśaṃ padmanābhaṃ tathādhare
jihvāyāṃ vāsudevaṃ ca tālvake garuḍadhvajam
vāmabhuje mahābhāgaṃ rāghavaṃ hṛdi vinyaset
kare tu dakṣiṇe vipra tataḥ saṃkarṣaṇaṃ nyaset
pṛṣṭhe kṣitidharaṃ vidyād acyutaṃ skandhayor api
mādhavaṃ bāhu kukṣau tu dakṣiṇe yogaśāyinam
svayaṃbhuvaṃ meḍhramadhye ūrubhyāṃ tu gadādharam
gulpayor narasiṃhaṃ ca pādapṛṣṭhe 'mitaujasam
śrīdharaṃ cāṅgulīṣu syāt padmākṣaṃ sarvasandhiṣu
romakūpe guḍākeśaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ raktāsthimajjāsu
evaṃ nyāsavidhiṃ kṛtvā sākṣān nārāyaṇo bhavet
tanur viṣṇumayī tasya yāvat kiṃcin na bhāṣate
evaṃ nyāsaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā yat kāryaṃ śṛṇu tad dvija
vanamālāṃ tu vinyasya sarvadevābhipūjitām
gadāṃ vakṣaḥsthale caiva cakraṃ caiva tu pṛṣṭhataḥ
śrīvatsāṅgaṃ śiro nyasya pañcāṅgakavacaṃ nyaset
oṃ apāmārjanako nyāsaḥ sarvavyādhivināśanaḥ
viṣṇur ūrdhvam adho rakṣed vaikuṇṭho vidiśo diśaḥ
pātu māṃ sarvato rāmo dhanvī cakrī ca keśavaḥ
homārambheṣu sarveṣu trisaṃdhyāsu ca nityaśaḥ
āyur ārogyam aiśvaryaṃ jñānaṃ vittaṃ phalaṃ bhavet
atha dhyānaṃ pravakṣyāmi sarvapāpapraṇāśanam
vārāharūpiṇaṃ devaṃ saṃsmaraty aparājitam
bṛhattanuṃ bṛhadgātraṃ bṛhaddaṃṣṭrasuśobhanam
samastavedavedāṅgaṃ yuktāṅgaṃ bhūṣaṇair yutam
uddhṛtya bhūmiṃ pātālād hastābhyām upagṛhṇatām
āliṅgya bhūmiṃ śirasi mūrdhni jighrantam āsthitam
pītāmbaradharaṃ devaṃ śuklamālyānulepanam
trayastriṃśakoṭidevaiḥ stūyamānaṃ mudāniśam
itthaṃ dhyātvā mahātmānaṃ japen nityaṃ mahātmanaḥ
suvarṇamaṇḍapāntasthaṃ padmaṃ dhyāyet sakesaram
sakarṇikadalair iṣṭair aṣṭabhiḥ pariśobhitam
taḍitsamaśaṭāśobhi kaṇṭhanālopaśobhitam
śrīvatsāṅkitavakṣaḥsthaṃ tīkṣṇadaṃṣṭraṃ trilocanam
javākusumasaṃkāśaṃ raktahastatalānvitam
kaṭisūtreṇa haimena nūpureṇa virājitam
vanamālādiśobhāḍhyaṃ muktāhāropaśobhitam
anekasūryasaṃkāśaṃ mukuṭāṭopamastakam
śaṅkhacakragṛhītābhyām udbāhubhyāṃ virājitam
prātaḥ sūryasamaprakhya kuṇḍalābhyāṃ virājitam
atiraktauṣṭhavadanaṃ vyāttāsyam atibhīṣaṇam
vāmāṅkasthaṃ śivabhakta śāntidāṃ sunitambinīm
arhaṇīyāṃ sujātoruṃ sunāsāṃ śubhalakṣaṇām
subhrūṃ sukeśīṃ suśroṇīṃ suśubhāṃ sudvijānanām
supratiṣṭhāṃ suvadanāṃ caturhastāṃ vicintayet
dukūle caiva cārvaṅgīṃ hāriṇīṃ sarvakāmadām
taptakañcanasaṃkāśāṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitām
gṛhītapadmayugalaṃ udbāhubhyāṃ tathānyayoḥ
gṛhītamātulaṅgākhyaṃ jāmbunadakarān tathā
evaṃ devīṃ nṛsiṃhasya vāmāṅkopari saṃsmaret
sulalitadadhikhaṇḍaṃ pāṇinā dakṣiṇena
kalaśam amṛtapūrṇaṃ savyahaste dadhānaṃ
tadatisakaladuḥkhaṃ vāmanaṃ bhāvayed yaḥ
bhīmākṣasphuradaṭṭahāsavilasāddaṃṣṭrāgradīptānanaḥ
dorbhiś cakradharau gadābjamukulau trāsāṃś ca pāśāṅkuśau
manobhūtānīndriyāṇi guṇāḥ sattvaṃ rajas tamaḥ
trailokyasyeśvaraṃ sarvam ahaṃkāre pratiṣṭhitāḥ
oṃ namaḥ paramārthāya puruṣāya mahātmane
arūpabahurūpāya vyāpine paramātmane
niṣkalmaṣāya śuddhāya sarvapāpaharāya ca
varāhanarasiṃhāya vāmanāya mahātmane
trivikramāya rāmāya vaikuṇṭhāya narāya ca
nārāyaṇāya devāya anantāya mahātmane
garuḍadhvajāya kṛṣṇāya pītāmbaradharāya ca
yogīśvarāya siddhāya guhyāya paramātmane
janārdanāya kṛṣṇāya upendraśrīdharāya ca
bhaktapriyāya vidhaye viṣvaksenāya śārṅgine
cakrahastāya śūlāya tarjanyapatrāya dhīmate
ādityāya upendrāya bhūtānāṃ jīvanāya ca
viṣūvṛcchravase tasmai kṣīrāmbunichiśāyine
adhokṣajāya bhadrāya śrīdharāyādimūrtaye
viśveśadvāramūrtiś ca mṛtyurāyohito 'sti saḥ
nānārāgāṃś ca dakṣāṃś ca vikaṭāya mahābhītī
nārāyaṇāya viśvāya viśveśāyāmbarāya ca
dāmodarāya devāya anantāya mahātmane
hayagrīveśa sarveśa hṛṣīkeśa harāśubham
harāmukasya duritaṃ duṣkṛtaṃ durupoṣitam
parāpadhyānasahitaṃ prayuktaṃ cābhicāruka
oṃ namo vāsudevāya namaḥ kṣṛṇāya śārṅgiṇe
namaḥ puṣkaranetrāya keśavāyādicakriṇe
mahāhavaripuskandha ghṛṣṭacakrāya cakriṇe
daṃṣṭroddhṛtakṣitidhṛte trayīmūrtimate namaḥ
mahāyajñavarāhāya śeṣabhogoruśāyine
kāśyapāyātihrasvāya ṛgyajuḥsāmabhūṣita
tubhyaṃ vāmanarūpāya sṛjate gāṃ namo namaḥ
varāhāśeṣaduṣṭāni sarvapāpaharāṇi vai
bhañja bhañja ninādena duṣṭāny asyārtināśana
ṛgyajuḥsāmagarbhābhir vāgbhir vāmanarūpadhṛk
ekāhikaṃ dvyāhikaṃ ca tathā tridivasaṃ jvaram
doṣotthaṃ saṃnipātotthaṃ tathaivāgantukaṃ jvaram
śamaṃ nayāśu govinda chittvā cchittvā tu vedanām
netraduḥkhaṃ śiroduḥkhaṃ duḥkhaṃ codarasaṃbhavam
anucchvāsam atiśvāsaṃ paritāpaṃ savepathuṃ
gudaghrāṇāṃhrirogāṃś ca kuṣṭharogaṃ tathā kṣayam
kāmalādīṃs tathā rogān pramehāṃś cātidāruṇān
bhagaṃdarātisārāṃś ca mukharogaṃ savalgulim
aśmarīmūtrakṛcchrāṃś ca rogān anyāṃś ca dāruṇān
kaphodbhavāś ca ye kecid ye cānye sāṃnipātikāḥ
āgantavaś ca ye rogā lūtāvisphoṭakādayaḥ
te sarve praśamaṃ yāntu vāsudevāpamārjitāḥ
vilayaṃ yāntu te sarve viṣṇor uccāraṇena ca
kṣayaṃ gacchantu cāśeṣās te cakrābhihatā hareḥ
acyutānantagovinda nāmoccāraṇabhīṣitāḥ
naśyantu sakalā rogāḥ satyaṃ satyaṃ vadāmy aham
sthāvaraṃ jaṅgamaṃ vāpi kṛtrimaṃ vāpi yad viṣam
śamaṃ nayatu tat sarvaṃ kīrtito 'sya janārdanaḥ
grahān pretagrahāṃś caiva tathā vai ḍākinīgrahān
vetālāṃś ca piśācāṃś ca gandharvān yakṣarākṣasān
śakunīpūtanādyāṃś ca tathā vaināyakagrahān
mukhamaṇḍinikāṃ krūrāṃ revatīṃ vṛddharevatīm
vṛddhikākhyān grahāṃś cogrāṃs tathā mātṛgrahān api
bālasya viṣṇoḥ caritaṃ hantu bālagrahān imān
vṛddhānāṃ ye grahāḥ kecid ye ca bālagrahāḥ kvacit
narasiṃhasya te dṛṣṭyā dagdhā ye cāpi yauvane
saṭākarālavadano narasiṃho mahāravaḥ
grahān aśeṣān niḥśeṣān karotu jagato hitam
narasiṃha mahāsiṃha jvālāmālojjvalānana
grahān aśeṣān sarveśa khāda khādāgnilocana
ye rogā ye mahotpātā yad viṣaṃ ye mahāgrahāḥ
yāni ca krūrabhūtāni grahapīḍāś ca dāruṇāḥ
śastrakṣateṣu ye doṣā jvālāgardabhakādayaḥ
yāni cāryāṇi bhūtāni prāṇipīḍākarāṇi vai
tāni sarvāṇi sarvātman paramātmañ janārdana
kiṃcid rūpaṃ samāsthāya vāsudeva vināśaya
kṣiptvā sudarśanaṃ cakraṃ jvālāmālāvibhīṣaṇam
jvalatpāvakasaṃkāśa sūryakoṭisamaprabha
trailokyarakṣakartṛ tvaṃ tvaṃ duṣṭadānavadāraṇa
chindhi vātaṃ ca dhūtaṃ ca chindhi ghoraṃ mahāviṣam
rujadāghaṃ ca śūlaṃ ca nimiṣajvālagardabham
sarvaduṣṭāni rakṣāṃsi kṣapayātivibhīṣaṇa
hāṃ hāṃ hūṃ hūṃ phaṭkāreṇa ṭhadvayena hatadviṣaḥ
sudarśanasya mantreṇa grahā yānti diśo diśaḥ
sarvaduṣṭāni rakṣāṃsi kṣayaṃ yānti vibhīṣayā
prācyāṃ pratīcyāṃ ca diśi dakṣiṇottaratas tathā
rakṣāṃ karotu sarvātmā narasiṃhaḥ svagarjitaiḥ
bhūmyantarikṣe ca tathā pṛṣṭhataḥ pārśvato 'grataḥ
rakṣāṃ karotu bhagavān bahurūpī janārdanaḥ
yathā viṣṇuṛ jagat sarvaṃ sadevāsuramānavam
yathā viṣṇau smṛte samyak saṃkṣayaṃ yāti pātakam
paramātmā yathā viṣṇur vedānteṣv abhidhīyate
yathā yajñeṣvaro viṣṇur vedeṣv api tu gīyate
yathā yajñeśvaro viṣṇur yajñānte api gīyate
śāntir astu śivaṃ cāstu praśāmyatv asukhaṃ ca yat
vāsudevaśarīrotthaiḥ kuśair nirmārjitaṃ mayā
apāmārjati govindo naro nārāyaṇas tathā
tavāstu sarvaduḥkhānāṃ praśamo vacanād dhareḥ
idaṃ śāstraṃ paṭhed yas tu saptāhan niyataḥ śuciḥ
śāntiṃ samastarogās te grahāḥ sarve viṣāni ca
bhūtāni ca prayāntv īśe saṃsmṛte madhusūdane
apamārjanakaṃ śastaṃ viṣṇunāmābhimantritam
ete kuśā viṣṇuśarīrasaṃbhavā janārdano 'haṃ svayaṃ eva cāgataḥ
hataṃ mayā duṣṭam aśeṣam asya svastho bhavaty eṣa vaco yathā hareḥ
śāntir astu śivaṃ cāstu duṣṭam asya praśāmyatu
yad asya duritaṃ kiṃcit tat kṣiptaṃ lavaṇārṇave
svāsthyam asya sadaivāstu hṛṣīkeśasya kīrtanāt
etad rogādipīḍāsu jantūnāṃ hitam icchatā
anena sarvaduṣṭāni praśamaṃ yānty asaṃśayam
sarvāparādhaśamanam apāmārjanakaṃ param
vināśāya ca rogāṇām avamṛtyukṣayāya ca
vyāghrāpasmārakuṣṭhādi piśācoragarākṣasāḥ
paṭhatāṃ śṛṇvatāṃ nityaṃ viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati
surūpatā manuṣyāṇāṃ strīṇāṃ ca dvijasattama
surūpāṇāṃ sugātrāṇāṃ suveṣāṇāṃ tathā mune
nyūnaṃ tathādhikaṃ vāpi kiṃcid aṅgaṃ prajāyate
kāṇāḥ kubjāś ca jāyante truṭitaśravaṇās tathā
narāṇāṃ yoṣitāṃ caiva samastāṅgsurūpatā
lāvaṇyagativākyāni sati rūpe mahāmate
prayānti cārutāṃ rūpaṃ tenoktaḥ paramo guṇaḥ
vākyalāvaṇyasaṃskāra vilāsalalitā gatiḥ
viḍambanā kurūpāṇāṃ strīpuṃsām abhijāyate
rūpakāraṇabhūtāya yateta matimāṃs tataḥ
karmaṇā tan mamācakṣva karma yac cārurūpadam
samyak pṛṣṭaṃ tvayā hīdam upavāsāśritaṃ dvija
kathayāmi yathā proktaṃ vasiṣṭhena mahātmanā
vasiṣṭham ṛṣim āsīnaṃ saptarṣipravaraṃ patim
tasyāḥ sa paripṛcchantyā jagāda munisattamaḥ
śrūyatāṃ mama yat pṛṣṭas tvayāhaṃ brahmavādini
surūpatā nṛṇāṃ yena yoṣitāṃ copajāyate
rūpādikā guṇāḥ kena prāpyante 'nyena karmaṇā
tasmād ārādhanīyo vai viṣṇur eva yaśasvini
yas tu vāñchati dharmajñe rūpaṃ sarvāṅgaśobhanam
nakṣatrapuruṣas tena saṃpūjyaḥ puruṣottamaḥ
nakṣatrāṅgaṃ yathāhāraḥ samupoṣyati yo harim
surūpair akhilāṅgaiś ca rūpavān abhijāyate
yoṣitā ca paraṃ rūpam icchantyā jagataḥ patiḥ
sa evārādhanīyo 'tra nakṣatrāṅgo janārdanaḥ
nakṣatrarūpī bhagavān pūjyate puruṣottamaḥ
caitramāsaṃ samārabhya viṣṇoḥ pādādipūjanam
yathā kurvīta rūpārthī tan niśāmaya tattvataḥ
nakṣatram ekam ekaṃ vai snātaḥ samyag upoṣitaḥ
nakṣatrapuruṣasyāṅgaṃ pūjayet sādhvī cakriṇaḥ
mūle pādau tathā jaṅghe rohiṇīṣv arcayec chubhe
jānunī cāśvinīyoga āṣāḍhe corusaṃjñite
phālgunīdvitaye guhyaṃ kṛttikāsu tathā kaṭim
pārśve bhadrapadāyugme dve kukṣī revatīṣu ca
anurādha uraḥ pṛṣṭhaṃ śraviṣṭhāsv abhipūjayet
punarvasāv aṅgulīṃś ca āśleṣāsu tathā nakhān
jyeṣṭhāyāṃ pūjayed grīvaṃ śravaṇe śravaṇe tathā
puṣye mukhaṃ tathā svātau daśanān abhipūjayet
hanvau śatabhiṣāyoge maghāyoge ca nāsikām
mṛgottamāṅge nayane pūjayed bhaktitaḥ śubhe
citrāyoge lalāṭaṃ ca bharaṇyāṃ ca tathā śiraḥ
saṃpūjanīyā vidvadbhiś cādrāsu ca śiroruhāḥ
nakṣatrayogeṣv eteṣu pūjito jagataḥ patiḥ
nakṣatrapuruṣākhyo 'yaṃ yathāvat puruṣottamaḥ
pāpāpahāraṃ kurute samyac chraddhāvatāṃ satām
aṅgopāṅgāni caivāsya pāpādīni yaśasvini
surūpāny abhijāyante sapta janmāntarāṇi vai
sarvāṇi caiva bhadrāṇi śarīrārogyam uttamam
saṃtatiṃ manasaḥ prītiṃ rūpaṃ cātīvaśobhanam
vāṅmādhūryaṃ tathā kāntiṃ yac cānyad abhivāñchitam
dadāti nakṣatrapumān pūjitaś ca janārdanaḥ
upoṣya samyag eteṣu krameṇa rkṣeṣu śobhane
saṃpūjanīyo bhagavān nakṣatrāṅgo janārdanaḥ
gandhapuṣpādisaṃyuktaṃ pūjayitvā yadāvidhi
jānubhyāṃ dharaṇīṃ gatvā idaṃ codāharet tataḥ
api sarvam etaṃ protaṃ sūtre maṇigaṇā iva
ekapuruṣa mahāpuruṣa ṛkṣapuruṣa namo 'stu te
nakṣatrajñāya viprāya dadyād dānaṃ ca śaktitaḥ
pārite ca punar dadyāt strīpūṃsāṃ cāruhāsini
strī vā sādhvī sadā viṣṇor ārādhanaparāyaṇā
sarvakāmān avāpnoti samārādhya janārdanam
nRṇāṃ strīṇāṃ ca viprarṣe nānyac chokasya kāraṇam
aputraḥ sarvaduḥkhānāṃ hetubhūto mato mama
śastaṃ praśāntaṃ balinaṃ parāṃ nirvṛtim āgatāḥ
śāstrajñaṃ dharmatattvajñaṃ dīnānāthajanāśrayam
devānukūlatāyuktaṃ yuktaṃ samyag guṇena ca
yenedṛglakṣaṇaḥ putraḥ prāpyate bhuvi mānavaiḥ
atrāpi śrūyatāṃ vṛttaṃ yat pūrvam abhavan mune
kṛtavīryo mahīpālo haihayānām abhūt purā
tasya śīladhanā nāma babhūva varavarṇinī
patnī sahasrapravarā mahiṣī śīlamaṇḍanā
sā tv aputrā mahābhāgā maitreyīṃ paryapṛcchata
guṇavatputralābhāya kṛtāsanaparigrahām
tayā ca pṛṣṭā vai samyag maitreyī brahmavādinī
kathayām āsa paramaṃ nāmnānantavrataṃ vratam
sarvakāmaphalāvāpti kārakaṃ pāpanāśanam
tasyāḥ sā putralābhāya rājaputrās tapasvinī
yo 'yam icchen naraḥ kāmaṃ nārī vā varavarṇini
sa taṃ samārādhya vibhuṃ samāpnoti janārdanam
mārgaśīrṣe mṛgaśiro bhīru yasmin dine bhavet
tasmin saṃprāśya gomūtraṃ snāto niyatamānasaḥ
anantaḥ sarvakāmānām anantaṃ bhagavān phalam
yathābhilaṣitāvāptiṃ kurvan mā kṣayam etu ca
ity uccāryābhipūjyainaṃ yathāvad vidhinā naraḥ
samāhitamanā bhūtvā praṇipātapuraḥsaram
viprāya dakṣiṇāṃ dadyād anantaḥ prīyatām iti
vāmām abhyarcayet kṛtvā gomūtraprāśanaṃ budhaḥ
anantaḥ sarvakāmānām iti coccārayed budhaḥ
bhuñjīta ca tathā vipraṃ vācayitvā yathāvidhi
caturṣv eteṣu gomūtra prāśanaṃ nṛpanandini
brāhmaṇāya tathā dadyāt tilān kanakam eva ca
tathaiva prāśanaṃ cātra pañcagavyam udāhṛtam
vipre vācanake dadyād yāvan māsacatuṣṭayam
vaiśākhe ca viśākhāsu bāhuṃ saṃpūjya dakṣiṇam
kaṭipūjāṃ ca jyeṣṭhāsu jyeṣṭhamūle śubhavrate
āṣāḍhāsu tathāṣāḍhe kuryāt pādārcanaṃ śubhe
padadvayaṃ ca śravaṇe śrāvaṇe subhru pūjayet
ghṛtaṃ viprāya dātavyaṃ prāśanīyaṃ tathā dadhi
kārttikānteṣu māseṣu prāśanaṃ dānam eva ca
tadvad āśvayuje pūjyaṃ hṛdayaṃ cāśvinīṣu vai
kuryāt samāhitamanāḥ snānaprāśanaśaucavān
anantaśirasaḥ pūjāṃ kārttike kṛttikāsu ca
ghṛtenānantam uddiśya pūrvamāsacatuṣṭayam
kurvīta homaṃ caitrādau śālinā kulanandini
kṣīreṇa śrāvaṇādau tu homaṃ māsacatuṣṭayam
śastaṃ tu sarvamāseṣu haviṣyānnaṃ ca bhojanam
evaṃ dvādaśabhir māsaiḥ pāraṇaṃ tritayaṃ śubhe
putrārthibhir vittakāmair bhṛtyadārān abhīpsubhiḥ
anantavratasaṃjñaṃ vai sarvapāpapraṇāśanam
iti śīladhanā śrutvā maitreyīvacanaṃ śubham
viṣṇus tutoṣa tuṣṭe ca viṣṇau sā suṣuve sutam
tasya vai jātamātrasya pravavāv anilaḥ śivaḥ
devadundubhayo neduḥ puṣpavṛṣṭiḥ papāta ca
prajagur divi gandharvā nanṛtuś cāpsarogaṇāḥ
kṛtavīryasutatvāc ca kārtavīryo babhūva saḥ
tenāpi bhagavān viṣṇur dattātreyasvarūpavān
ārādhito 'timahatā tapasā dālbhya bhūbhṛtā
purānusmaraṇaṃ jñānaṃ bhītānāṃ cārtināśanam
tam āha devadeveśaḥ puṇḍarīkanibhekṣaṇaḥ
yaś ca prabhāte rātrau ca tvāṃ naraḥ kīrtayiṣyati
anaṣṭadravyatā caiva tava nāmābhikīrtanaiḥ
sa cāpi varam āsādya prasannād garuḍadhvajāt
pālayām āsa bhūpālaḥ saptadvīpāṃ vasuṃdharām
teneṣṭaṃ vividhair yajñaiḥ samāptavaradakṣiṇaiḥ
jitvārivargam akhilaṃ dharmataḥ pālitāḥ prajāḥ
anantavratamāhātmyād āsādya tanayaṃ ca tam
yac cīrtvā rājapatnī sā kārtavīryam asūyata
yaś caitac chṛṇuyāj janma kārtavīryasya mānavaḥ
strī vā duḥkham apatyotthaṃ sapta janmāni nāśnute
rūpasaṃpat samākhyātā strīpuṃsāṃ jāyate śubhā
samupoṣya jagannāthaṃ nakṣatrapuruṣaṃ harim
vāso'tiśobhanaṃ cāru vastrādyābharaṇojjvalam
gṛhaṃ sarvaguṇopetam aśeṣopaskarānvitam
karmaṇā yena viprarṣe toṣito madhusūdanaḥ
yan māṃ pṛcchasi dālbhya tvaṃ gṛhopaskarabhūṣaṇam
narāṇāṃ jāyate yena tat sarvaṃ kathayāmi te
nandā bhadrā jayā riktā pūrṇā ca dvijasattama
tithayo vai samākhyātāḥ pratipatkramasaṃjñayā
pañcamī daśamī caiva tathā pañcadaśī tithiḥ
pūrṇā etāḥ samākhyātāṣ tithayo munisattama
mṛdā dhātuvikārair vā varṇakair gomayena vā
pravātāvātaguṇavad varṣāsv atimanoramam
anuliptaṃ śubhākāraṃ sugṛhaṃ labhate mune
pūrṇaṃ dhānyahiraṇyādyair maṇimuktāphalojjvalam
pratyāsannajalābhogaṃ gṛham āpnoti śobhanam
sāmnatasvajanānāṃ yat sarveṣām uttamottamam
yenānulipte tiṣṭhanti viṣṇvāyatanabhūtale
brāhmaṇakṣatriyaviśaḥ śūdrāḥ sādhvyas tathā striyaḥ
tasya pūṇyaphalaṃ dālbhya śrūyatāṃ yat prajāyate
apsarogaṇasaṃkīrṇaṃ muktāhāragaṇojjvalam
śreṣṭhaṃ sarvavimānānāṃ svarge dhiṣṇyam avāpnute
tasmin vimāne sa naraḥ strī vā tiṣṭhati sattama
gandharvāpsarasāṃ saṃbhaiḥ pūjyamānaḥ sa tiṣṭhati
liptaṃ ca yāvato hastān viṣṇor āyatanaṃ dvija
pūjyamānaḥ suragaṇaiḥ śītoṣṇādivivarjitaḥ
manojñagātro viprendras tiṣṭhaty astāghasaṃhatiḥ
cyutas tasmād ihāgamya viśiṣṭe jāyate kule
na tatra tāvad dāridryaṃ nopasargā na vā kaliḥ
na cāpi mṛtaniṣkrāntir yāvaj jīvaty asau dvija
viṣṇuḥ samastabhūtāni sasarjaitāni yāni vai
teṣāṃ madhye jagaddhātur atīveṣṭā vasuṃdharā
prayāti paramaṃ toṣaṃ vaiṣṇavīyaṃ mahī yataḥ
dharaṇīpitaraṃ viṣṇum idaṃ vākyam udīrayet
tvaṃ mahī jagatāṃ nātha sarvanātha namo 'stu te
śuśrūṣitaḥ prasīdeśa bhuvo lepanakarmaṇā
ity uccārya kṣitau kṣiptvā prathamaṃ dhāranītale
puṣpāṇi vā dvijaśreṣṭha yaḥ karoty anulepanam
nāpnoti sā ca vaidhavyaṃ gṛhabhaṅgaṃ kadācana
kṛtvopalepanaṃ bhūyaḥ praṇipatya janārdanam
snāto viṣṇuṃ samabhyarcya idaṃ vākyam udīrayet
kṛtaṃ tena samastaṃ me nāśam abhyetu pātakam
evaṃ saṃpūjya bhuñjīyād aparāhne dvijottama
tatkṣayāt svargeloke tu jāto gṛhavaraṃ yathā
sarvābharaṇasaṃpūrṇaṃ sarvopaskaradhānyavat
gomahiṣyādisaṃbhogaṃ gṛham āpnoti mānavaḥ
saptadvīpavatīṃ kṛtsnāṃ yathendras tridivaṃ tathā
alpopalepanād yasya māndhātā sakalāṃ mahīm
dīpaṃ prayacchati naro viṣṇor āyatane hi yaḥ
sadakṣiṇasya yajñasya phalaṃ prāpnoty asaṃśayam
kārttike tu viśeṣeṇa kaumude māsi dīpakam
dālbhyānyad api vakṣyāmi purāvṛttam idaṃ śṛṇu
vidarbharāṭ citraratho babhūvāstraviśāradaḥ
tasya putraśataṃ rājño jajñe pañcadaśottaram
ekaiva kanyā dālbhyāsīl lalitā nāmanāmataḥ
sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpūrṇā bhrātRṇāṃ pitur eva ca
tasya tasyāticārvaṅgī babhūveṣṭā dvijottama
tāṃ dadau kāśirājāya sa pitā cāruvarmane
upayeme ca tāṃ subhrūṃ cāruvarmā mahīpatiḥ
śatāny anyāni bhāryāṇāṃ trīṇy āsaṃś cāruvarmaṇaḥ
tāsāṃ madhye 'gramahiṣī lalitā tasya cābhavat
viṣṇor āyatane tasyāḥ sahasraṃ dvijasattama
dīpānāṃ vai prajajvāla divārātram atandritam
tasyā dyutiparābhūtās tasyā lāvaṇyanirjitāḥ
kautūhalaparāḥ sarvā yat pṛcchāmas tad ucyatām
nāhaṃ matsariṇī bhadrā na ca rāgādidūṣitā
bhavatyo mama sarvāsāṃ bhavatīnām ahaṃ tathā
apṛthagbhartṛsāmanyā devalokābhikāmukāḥ
pūrvaṃ yūyam ahaṃ caiva bhavatīnāṃ sadharmiṇī
na tathā puṣpadhūpeṣu na tathā dvijapūjane
prayatnaṃ tava paśyāmo viṣṇor āyatane śubhe
yathāhani tathā rātrau yathā rātrau tathāhani
vyājahāra sapatnīs tā na kiṃcid api bhāminī
punaḥ punaś ca sā tābhir bahuṣo dālbhya coditā
dākṣiṇyasārā lalitā kathāyām āsa bhāminī
kautukaṃ bhavatīnāṃ ced atīvālpe 'pi vastuni
tad eṣā kathayāmy etad yad vṛttaṃ mama śobhanāḥ
tena cāyatanaṃ viṣṇoḥ kāritaṃ devikātaṭe
ahany ahani śuśrūṣāṃ puṣpadhūpopalepanaiḥ
āsīn nirvāṇabhūyiṣṭho devārcāpurato niśi
devatāyatane cāsaṃ tatrāham api mūṣikā
pradīpavartiharaṇe kṛtabuddhir varānanāḥ
gṛhītā ca mayā vartir vṛṣadaṃśo nanāda ca
naṣṭā cāhaṃ tadā tasya mārjārasya bhayāturā
vartiprāntena naśyantyā sa dīpaḥ prerito mayā
jajvāla pūrvavad dīptyā tasminn āyatane punaḥ
mṛtāhaṃ ca tato jātā vaidarbhī rājakanyakā
jātismarā kāntimatī bhavatīnāṃ samā guṇaiḥ
eṣa prabhāvo dīpasya kārttike māsi śobhanāḥ
dattasya viṣṇvāyatane yasyeyaṃ vyuṣṭir uttamā
asaṃkalpitam apy asya preraṇaṃ yat kṛtaṃ mayā
lobhābhibhūtā hartuṃ taṃ pradīpam aham āgatā
tato jātismṛtir janma mānuṣyaṃ śobhanaṃ vapuḥ
vaśyaḥ patiḥ pṛthivīśaḥ kiṃ punar dīpadāyinām
etasmāt kāraṇād dīpān aham etān aharniśam
bhavatīnām idaṃ satyaṃ mayoktaṃ keśavālaye
mūṣikatvād ahaṃ yena karmaṇā siddhim āgatā
viṣṇvāyatanadattasya jagāda lalitā yathā
dadāti kārttike yas tu viṣṇvāyatanadīpakam
jātismaratvaṃ prajñāṃ ca prākāśyaṃ sarvavastuṣu
avyāhatendriyatvaṃ ca saṃprāpnoti na saṃśayaḥ
śeṣakāle ca cakṣuṣmān medhāvī dīpado naraḥ
jāyate narakaṃ vāpi tamaḥsaṃjñaṃ na paśyati
ekādaśīṃ dvādaśīṃ vā pratipakṣaṃ ca yo naraḥ
dīpaṃ dadāti kṛṣṇāya tasyāpi śṛṇu yat phalam
suvarṇamaṇimuktāḍhyaṃ manojñam atiśobhanam
dīpamālākulaṃ divyaṃ vimānaṃ so 'dhirohati
tasmād āyatane viṣṇor dadyād dīpaṃ dvijottama
tāṃś ca dattān na hiṃseta na ca tailaviyojitān
kurvīta dīpahartā tu mūko 'ndho jāyate yataḥ
jāyate narakaṃ cāpi tapaḥsaṃjñaṃ sa paśyati
vikrośamānān kṣutkṣāmāñ jagāda yamakiṃkaraḥ
yadā pramādibhiḥ pūrvam ātmātyantam upekṣitaḥ
idānīṃ yātanābhogaḥ kiṃ vilāpaḥ kariṣyati
deho dināni svalpāni viṣayāś cātidurdharāḥ
etat ko na vijānāti yena yūyaṃ pramādinaḥ
tatrāpy ativimūḍhatvāt kiṃ bhogān abhidhāvati
bhavadbhir āgataṃ duḥkhaṃ vilāpapariṇāmikam
paritāpāya taj jātaṃ duḥkhaṃ karmavipākajam
svalpam āyur manuṣyāṇāṃ tadante paratantratā
yad abhūt paradāreṣu prītaye 'ṅgakucādikam
yātanāduḥkharūpāya narake ca tad āgatam
hā māta ityādi rutaṃ tad idānīṃ vilapyate
mṛtānāṃ svakṛtaṃ karma paścāttāpāya kevalam
muhūrtārdhasukhāsvāda lubdhānām akṛtātmanām
anekavarṣakoṭiṣu duḥkhadaṃ karma jāyate
hā mātas tāta tāteti bhavadbhiḥ kiṃ vilapyate
putradāragṛhakṣetra hitāya satatodyatāḥ
na vetti sūryacandrādīn kālam ātmānam eva ca
sākṣibhūtān aśeṣasya śubhasyehāśubhasya ca
janmāny anyāni jāyante putradārādidehinām
krandate mātaraṃ tātaṃ pīḍyamāno 'pi yat svayam
evam ākṛṣṭacittānāṃ viṣayāsvādatarṣulaiḥ
nRṇāṃ na jāyate buddhiḥ paramārthāvalokinī
tathā ca viṣayāsaktiṃ karoty avirataṃ manaḥ
ko 'tibhāro harer nāmni jihvāyāḥ parikīrtane
yeneyaṃ teṣu hasteṣu svātantrye sati dīpakaḥ
mahāphalo viṣṇugṛhe na datto narakāpahaḥ
na vo vilapite kiṃcid idānīṃ dṛśyate phalam
avaśyaṃpātinaḥ prāṇā bhoktā jīvo hy aharniśam
idānīṃ kiṃ vilāpena sahadhvaṃ yad upāgatam
kṛte 'pi pāpake karmaṇy ajñānād aghanāśanam
nārakās tadvacaḥ śrutvā tām ūcur atiduḥkhitāḥ
kṣutkṣāmakaṇṭhās tṛṣayā parisphuṭitatālukāḥ
dyūtodyotāya govinda gṛhād dīpaḥ purā hṛtaḥ
tenāsmin narake ghore kṣuttṛṣṇāparipīḍitāḥ
bhavantaḥ patitās tīvra śītavātavidāritāḥ
puṇyaṃ pāpaṃ ca kathitaṃ keśavāyatane dvija
viśeṣeṇa jagaddhātuḥ keśavasya niveśane
ye 'ndhā mūkā niḥśrutā nirvivekā hīnās tais taiḥ sādhanair vipravarya
tais tair dīpāḥ sādhulokapradattā devāgārād anyato vipraṇītāḥ
āhlādaṃ cakṣuṣaḥ prītiṃ karoti manasas tathā
keṣāṃcid darśanaṃ brahman manuṣyāṇām aharniśam
udvejanīyā bhūtānām animittaṃ tathāpare
manuṣyāṇām aśeṣaṃ vai tan mamācakṣva sattama
devabrāhmaṇavedeṣu yajñeṣu ca narādhamaiḥ
yair jugupsā kṛtā dālbhya manasāpy atimānibhiḥ
teṣāṃ saṃdarśanāt sarvo na sukhaṃ vindate dvija
sparśād udvijate lokaḥ kaṭu teṣāṃ ca darśanam
saṃbhāṣaṇaṃ ca nindā vai kṛtā vedadvijātike
tasmān na nindāṃ vedādau na jugupsāṃ ca paṇḍitaḥ
yajñādike caiva kṛtā dālbhya taddarśanaṃ nṛṇām
āhlādaś cakṣuṣaḥ prītir manaso nirvṛtiḥ parā
saṃbhāṣaṇe tathāhlādaḥ sarvalokasya jāyate
stutāḥ praśastāḥ saṃprītyā pūjitā bahumānataḥ
śreyaḥ paraṃ prayacchanti devā vedā makhā dvijāḥ
eta eva samākhyātāḥ stavādigrahaṇe guṇāh
nindāyāḥ śravaṇe doṣa eteṣām evam eva hi
tasmāt stavyāḥ praśaṃsyāś ca devā vedā dvijātayaḥ
yajñāś ca manasāpy eṣāṃ na nindām ācared budhaḥ
śṛṇu dālbhya mahāpuṇyāṃ dvādaśīṃ pāpanāśanīm
yām upoṣya paraṃ puṇyaṃ prāpnute śraddhayānvitaḥ
māghamāse tu saṃprāpta āṣāḍhārkṣaṃ bhaved yadi
mūlaṃ vā kṛṣṇapakṣasya dvādaśyāṃ niyatas tadā
gṛhṇīyāt puṇyaphaladaṃ vidhānaṃ tasya me śṛṇu
kṛṣṇanāmnā ca saṃstūya ekādaśyāṃ mahāmate
upoṣito dvitīye 'hni punaḥ saṃpūjya keśavam
saṃstūya nāmnā ca tataḥ kṛṣṇākhyena punaḥ punaḥ
dadyāt tilāṃs tu viprāya kṛṣṇo me prīyatām iti
snānaprāśanayoḥ śastās tathā kṛṣṇatilā mune
nāndho na badhiraś ceha na kuṣṭhī na jugupsitaḥ
bhavaty etām uṣitvā tu tilākhyāṃ dvādaśīṃ naraḥ
viṣṇoḥ prīṇanam atroktaṃ samāpte varṣapāraṇe
pūjāṃ ca kuryād viprāya bhūyo dadyāt tathā tilān
anena dālbhya vidhinā tiladānād asaṃśayam
mucyate pātakaiḥ sarvair nirāyāsena mānavaḥ
udbhṛtapulakaḥ sarvān nirāyāsena mānavaḥ
dānavidhis tathā śraddhā sarvapātakaśāntaye
nārthaḥ prabhūto nāyāsaḥ śārīro munisattama
viśeṣaḥ kṣetrabhedena kathyatāṃ yadi vidyate
viśeṣaḥ kathito nāmnāṃ viśeṣaphaladāyakaḥ
tathā kṣetraviśeṣeṇa bhedaṃ nāmakṛtaṃ vada
śṛṇu dālbhya yathākhyātam arjunāya mahātmane
praṇipātaprasannena viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā
kṛte bhārāvataraṇe nivṛtte bhārate raṇe
āgamya śibiraṃ viṣṇū rathasthaḥ prāha phālgunam
iṣudhīgāṇḍivaṃ caiva samādāya tvarānvitaḥ
avatīrya rathād vīra dūre tiṣṭḥa dhanaṃjaya
avarokṣyāmy ahaṃ paścād avatīrṇe tatas tvayi
evam uktas tathā cakre vākyaṃ pārtho gadādhṛtaḥ
avārohat tataḥ paścāt svayam eva janārdanaḥ
jajvāla sa rathaḥ sadyo bhasmībhūtaś ca tatkṣaṇāt
vahninā ca yathā kāṣṭhaṃ sadyo bhasmalavīkṛtam
tad adbhutaṃ mahad dṛṣṭvā pārthaḥ papraccha keśavam
hṛṣṭaromā dvijaśreṣṭha bhayavismayagadgadaḥ
āścaryaṃ puruṣavyāghra kim etan madhusūdana
vināgninā ratho 'yaṃ me dagdhas tṛṇacayo yathā
bhīṣmadroṇakṛpādīnāṃ karṇādīnāṃ ca phālguna
madadhiṣṭhitatvāt kaunteya na śīrṇo 'yaṃ tadābhavat
kaṃ bhavantam ahaṃ vidyām atimānuṣaceṣṭitam
pūrvam eva yathākhyātaṃ raṇārambhe tavārjuna
kālo 'smi lokanāśāya pravṛtto 'haṃ yathādhunā
tan mayā sādhitaṃ kāryaṃ tridaśānāṃ tathā bhuvaḥ
bhārāvataraṇārthāya mama janma mahītale
tuṣṭāva vāgbhir iṣṭābhir udbhūtapulakas tataḥ
namo 'stu te cakradharograrūpa namo 'stu te śārṅgadharāruṇākṣa
vācaḥ samuccārayataḥ skhalanti keśā hṛṣīkeśa samucchvasanti
kālo bhavān kālakarālakarmā yenaitad evaṃ kṣayam akṣayātman
kṣatraṃ samudbhūtaruṣā samastam nītaṃ bhuvo bhāravirecanāya
na me dṛg eṣā tava rūpam etad draṣṭuṃ samarthā kṣubhito 'smi cāntaḥ
smarāmi rūpaṃ tava viśvarūpaṃ yad darśitaṃ pūrvam abhūn mamaiva
yasmin mayā viśvam aśeṣam āsīd dṛṣṭaṃ sayakṣoragadevadaityam
sā me smṛtir darśanabhāṣanādi prakurvato nātha gatā praṇāśam
kartā bhavān kāraṇam apy aśeṣam kāryaṃ ca niṣkāraṇa kartṛrūpa
brahmā bhavān viśvasṛg ādikāle viśvasya rūpo 'si tathā visṛṣṭau
viṣṇuḥ sthitau pālanabaddhakakṣo rudro bhavān saṃharaṇe prajānām
yathā hi mūle viṭapī mahādrumaḥ pratiṣṭhitaskandhavarograśākhaḥ
muñcāmi yāvat paramāyudhāni vairiṣv anantāhavadurmadeṣu
dṛṣṭvā hi tāvat sahasā patanto nūnaṃ tavaivācyuta sa prabhāvaḥ
hatā hatās te bhavato dṛśaiva mayā punaḥ keśava śastrapūgaiḥ
kāh karṇabhīṣmapramukhān vijetuṃ yuṣmatprasādena vinā samarthaḥ
triśūlapāṇir mama yaḥ purastān niṣūdayan vairibalaṃ jagāma
jñātaṃ mayā sāṃpratam etad īśa tava prasādasya hi sā vibhūtiḥ
nāśāya nābhūt patito 'pi kāye tvatsaṃnidhānasya hi so 'nubhāvaḥ
bālye bhavān yāni cakāra deva karmāṇy asahyāni surāsurāṇām
tair eva jānīma na yat paraṃ tvāṃ doṣaḥ sa nirdoṣo manuṣyatāyāḥ
tālocchritāgraṃ gurubhārasāram āyāmavistāravad adyajātaḥ
pādāgravikṣepavibhinnabhāṇḍaṃ cikṣepa ko 'nyaḥ śakaṭaṃ yathā tvam
anyena kenācyuta pūtanāyāḥ prāṇaiḥ samaṃ pītam asṛgvimiśram
viṣānaloṣṇāmbunipātabhīmam āsphoṭya ko vā bhuvi manuṣo 'nyaḥ
nanarta pādābjanipīḍitasya phaṇaṃ samāruhya ca kāliyasya
pralambacāṇūramukhān nihatya kaṃsāsuraṃ yasya bibheti śakraḥ
tam aṣṭavarṣo nijaghāna ko 'nyo nirāyodho nātha manuṣyajanmā
bāṇārtham abhyudyatam ugraśūlaṃ nirjitya saṃkhye tripurārim ekaḥ
kaḥ pārijātaṃ surasundarīṇāṃ sadopabhogyaṃ vijitendrasainyaḥ
hatvā hayagrīvam udāravīryaṃ niśumbhaśumbhau narakaṃ ca ko 'nyaḥ
maitrī na yeṣāṃ vinayāya tāṃs tān sarvān bhavān saṃharate 'vyayātman
hitāya teṣāṃ kapilādirūpiṇā tvayānuśastā bahavo 'nujīvāḥ
yeṣāṃ na maitrī hṛdi te na neyā viśvopakārī vadha eva teṣām
itthaṃ bhavān duṣṭavadhena nūnaṃ viśvopakārāya vibho pravṛttaḥ
etāni cānyāni ca duṣkarāṇi dṛṣṭāni karmāṇi tathāpi satyam
manyāmahe tvāṃ jagataḥ prasūtiṃ kiṃ kurma māyā tava mohanīyam
prasīda kṛṣṇācyuta vāsudeva janārdanānanta nṛsiṃha viṣṇo
manuṣyasāmānyadhiyā yadīśa dṛṣṭo mayā tat kṣamasvādideva
prasīdeśa hṛṣīkeśa akṣauhiṇyā daśāṣṭa ca
tvayā grastā bhuvo bhūtyai hetubhūtā hi madvidhāḥ
evaṃ stutas tataḥ prāha prītimāṃs taṃ janārdanaḥ
pariṣvajya mahābāhuṃ samāśvāsya ca phālgunam
prvāca bhagavān devaḥ prahṛṣṭenāntarātmanā
yas tvāṃ vetti sa māṃ vetti yas tvām anu sa mām anu
abhedenātmanā vedmī tvām ahaṃ pāṇḍunandana
mamāṃśatvaṃ mahābāho jagataḥ pālanecchayā
bhuvo bhārāvatārārthaṃ pṛthak pārtha mayā kṛtam
devadaityoragā yakṣā gandharvāḥ kiṃnarāpsarāḥ
rākṣasāś ca piśācāś ca paśupakṣisarīsṛpāḥ
vṛkṣagulmādayaḥ śailāḥ sarvabhūtāni cārjuna
mamaivāṃśāni bhūtāni viddhi sarvāṇy ariṃdama
kṣetreṣu yeṣu yeṣu tvaṃ cintanīyo mayācyuta
cetasaḥ praṇidhānārthaṃ tan mamākhyātum arhasi
sarvagaḥ sarvabhūto 'haṃ na hi kiṃcid mayā vinā
puṣkare puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ gayāyāṃ ca gadādharam
lohadaṇḍe tathā viṣṇuṃ stuvaṃs tarati duṣkṛtam
kṣvāmācye kumāraṃ nepāle lokabhāvanam
rāghavaṃ citrakūṭe tu prabhāse daityasūdanam
mandodapāne vaikuṇṭhaṃ māhantre cācyutaṃ vibhum
vārāhaṃ kardamāle tu kāśmīre cakrapāṇinam
janārdanaṃ ca kubjāmre mathurāyāṃ ca keśavam
śālagrāme mahāyogiṃ hariṃ govardhanācale
piṇḍārake caturbāhuṃ śaṅkhoddhāre ca śaṅkhinam
vāmanaṃ ca kurukṣetre yamunāyāṃ trivikramam
viśveśvaraṃ tathā śoṇe kapilaṃ pūrvasāgare
vanamālaṃ ca kiṣkindhāyāṃ devaṃ raivatake dvija
kāśījale mahāyogaṃ devaṃ cāmitatejasam
vaiśākhayūpe ajitaṃ virajāyāṃ viprakṣayam
śvetadvīpapatiṃ cāpi gaṅgāsāgarasaṃgame
bhūdharaṃ devikānadyāṃ prayāge caiva mādhavam
naranārāyaṇākhyaṃ ca tathā badarikāśrame
dvārakāyāṃ tathā kṛṣṇaṃ stuvaṃs tarati durgatim
rāmaṃ nāma mahendrādrau hṛṣīkeśaṃ tathārbude
aśvatīrthe hayagrīvaṃ viśvarūpaṃ himācale
nṛsiṃhaṃ kṛtasauce ca vipāśāyāṃ dvijapriyam
naimiṣe yajñapuruṣaṃ jambūmārge tathācyutam
anantaṃ saindhavāraṇye daṇḍake śāṅgadhāriṇam
utpalāvartake śauriṃ narmadāyāṃ śriyaḥ patim
dāmodaraṃ raivatake nandāyāṃ jalaśāyinam
sahyādrau devadeveśaṃ vaikuṇṭhaṃ māgadhe vane
hṛdaye cāpi kaunteya paramātmānam ātmanaḥ
vaṭe vaṭe vaiśravaṇaṃ catvare catvare śivam
vāsudevaṃ ca sarvatra saṃsmarañ jyotiṣāṃ patim
arcayan praṇamaṃs tu tvaṃ saṃsmaraṃś ca dhanaṃjaya
eteṣv etāni nāmāni naraḥ pāpaiḥ pramucyate
sthāneṣv eteṣu mannāmnām eteṣāṃ prīṇanaṃ naraḥ
dvijānāṃ prīṇanaṃ kṛtvā svargaloke 'bhijāyate
nāmāny etāni kaunteya sthānāny etāni cātmavān
jayaṃ vai pañcapañcāśat trisandhyaṃ matparāyaṇaḥ
trīṇi janmāni yat pāpam avasthātritaye kṛtam
tat kṣālayaty asaṃdigdhaṃ jāyate ca satāṃ kule
dviṣkālaṃ vā japann eva divārātrau ca yat kṛtam
dhanyaṃ yaśasyam āyuṣyaṃ jayaṃ kuru kulodvaha
grahānukūlatāṃ caiva karoty āśu na saṃśayaḥ
upoṣito matparamaḥ sthāneṣv eteṣu mānavaḥ
kṛtāyatanavāsaś ca prāpnoty abhimataṃ phalam
utkrāntir apy aśeṣeṣu sthāneṣv eteṣu śasyate
anyasthānāc chataguṇam eteṣv anaśanādikam
yas tu matparamaḥ kālaṃ karoty eteṣu mānavaḥ
yan na tāpāya vai puṃsāṃ bhavaty āmuṣmikaṃ kṛtam
upavāsaprabhāvaṃ ca kṛṣṇārādhanakāṅkṣiṇaḥ
śrūyatāṃ dālbhya yat pṛṣṭāḥ kautukād bhavatā vayam
āmuṣmikaṃ na tāpāya yac ca tāpāya jāyate
upoṣitaprabhāvaṃ ca kṛṣṇārādhanakāṅkṣiṇaḥ
kathayāmi yathāvṛttaṃ pūrvam eva mahāmate
bhāryājāmātṛduhitṛ putrapautrasnuṣānvitaḥ
prabhūtabhṛtyavargaś ca bahuvyāpārakārakaḥ
cakārānudinaṃ so 'tha nyāyānyāyair dhanārjanam
na juhoty udite kāle na dadāty atitṛṣṇayā
nityanaimittikānāṃ ca hāniṃ cakre svakarmaṇām
tṛṣṇābhibhūto viprarṣe svavargabharaṇādhṛtaḥ
kālena gacchatā so 'tha mṛto vindhyāṭavītaṭe
yātanādehabhṛt preto grīṣmakāle 'bhavan mune
taṃ dadarśa mahābhāgo divyajñānasamanvitaḥ
bhāskarasyāṃśubhir dīptair dahyantam anivāraṇaiḥ
prataptavālukāmadhye tṛṣā cātyantapīḍitam
kṣutkṣāmakaṇṭhaṃ śuṣkāsyaṃ stabdhodvṛttavilocanam
niṣkrāntajihvam aṅgeṣu visphoṭaiḥ sarvataś citam
niśvāsāyāsakhedena viralāsyam anādaram
śrāntaṃ makṣikayākīrṇaṃ durdagdhaṃ cātidāruṇam
taṃ tādṛśam atho dṛṣṭvā gārdabheyo mahāmuniḥ
pipītaḥ prāha viprarṣiḥ kāruṇyastimitaṃ vacaḥ
jānann api tathā prāptaṃ tadanuṣṭhānajaṃ phalam
adhaḥ sūryāṃśubhis taptair bahubhir yānapāṃsubhiḥ
upary arkakarair ugrais tṛṣā cārtas tathā kṣudhā
yātanāstha uvācedaṃ kṛcchrād ucchvāsya mastakam
aśāśvate śāśvatadhīs tena dahyāmi durmatiḥ
dhanāpaṇagṛhakṣetra putradārahite rataḥ
nātmano 'haṃ hitārambhī tena dahyāmi durmatiḥ
idaṃ kariṣye kṛtvedaṃ kariṣyāmy aparaṃ tv idam
itīcchāśatasaro 'haṃ tena dahyāmi durmatiḥ
śītoṣṇavarṣābhibhavaṃ lobhāt soḍḥaṃ mayāśubham
pitṛdevamanuṣyāṇām adattvāpoṣitā hi ye
putrabhṛtyakalatreṣu mama tv ādṛtamānasaḥ
kṛtvā karmāṇy asādhūni dahyāmy eko 'tra durmatiḥ
na hi naḥ pūjitā gehān nirgatā dvijasattamāḥ
yan me na pūjitā devāḥ kuṭumbaṃ poṣītaṃ param
ekākī tena dahyāmi ye puṣṭās te 'nyato gatāḥ
nityanaimittikaṃ karma kṛte yeṣāṃ na ma kṛtam
dārāḥ putrāś ca bhṛtyāś ca pāpavyāptyā mayaidhitāḥ
putradārādibhṛtyārthe mayānyāyārthasaṃcayāḥ
kṛtās tenātra dahyāmi bhuñjate 'py anyato gatāḥ
nāntarduḥkhaṃ na vā bhānuḥ pāpam eva dvidhā sthitam
mama yenāham āhlādam āpnuyāṃ munisattama
alpakālikam uddhāraṃ tava paśyāmy asaṃśayam
prakṣīṇaprāyam etat te sukṛtaṃ cāsti te param
sukarmajayadāṃ bhadra dvādaśīṃ tvam upoṣitaḥ
alpair ahobhiḥ saṃkṣīṇaṃ navapātre yathā jalam
gataṃ pāpam ayaṃ tasyāḥ prabhāvo 'tyantadurlabhaḥ
śamaṃ pāpasya kurute jayaṃ sukṛtakarmaṇaḥ
satkarmajayadā hy eṣā tato vai dvādaśī smṛtā
tat tathā nātra saṃdeho mamatā pāpahetukī
pāpam atra kṛtaṃ pretya bhadra tāpāya jāyate
āhlādāya tathā puṇyam iha puṇyakṛtāṃ nṛṇām
vīrabhadraṃ samāśvāsya yayāv itthaṃ mahāmuniḥ
evaṃ dālbhya pare loke yad atrāsukṛtaṃ kṛtam
tat tāpāya sukhāyoktaṃ yad atraiva śubhaṃ kṛtam
tasmān nareṇa puṇyāya patitavyaṃ na pātake
upavāsāś ca kartavyāḥ sadaivātmahitaiṣiṇā
saṃsārāsāratāṃ jñātvā viṣayāṃś cātitarṣulān
kartavyaṃ yan mahābhāga puruṣeṇa tad ucyatām
saṃsārāsāratāṃ jñātvā viṣayāṃś cātitarṣulān
gṛddhis teṣv eva saṃtyājyā tattyāgo guṇavān nṛṇām
yeṣām abdasahasrāṇāṃ sahasrair api no naraḥ
yāvato vāñchate bhogān ahany ahani mānavaḥ
teṣāṃ sahasrabhāge 'pi dālbhya prāptiṃ na vindati
tṛptaye ye na saṃprāptāḥ prāpyante ye na vāñchitāḥ
buddhimān indriyārtheṣu teṣv asaṅgī sadā bhavet
yeṣāṃ tṛptir na bhogena tyāgaś caivopakārakaḥ
kṛcchracāndrāyaṇādīni narais tasmān mumukṣubhiḥ
niṣkāmair dālbhya kāryāṇi phalāya ca phalepsubhiḥ
dasrābhyāṃ saha saṃvādam ailasya ca mahātmanaḥ
ailaḥ purūravāḥ pūrvaṃ babhūva manujeśvaraḥ
cakame yaṃ mahābhāgam urvaśī surasundarī
saṃtyajya tridaśāvāsaṃ rūpaudāryaguṇānvitam
nāsatyadasrau rūpeṇa devānām adhikau tataḥ
urvaśīlobhanaṃ tasya rūpaṃ draṣṭuṃ samutsukau
pratiṣṭhānaṃ puraṃ tasya budhaputrasya dhīmataḥ
