draṣṭuṃ tavāśvinau prāptau rūpasaṃpadguṇaṃ ṇrpa
tadehy atra mahābhāga ihāsmān saṃpraveśaya
āścaryabhūtaṃ lokeṣu urvaśīlobhanaṃ vapuḥ
āvāṃ samāgatau tasmāt tvāṃ draṣṭuṃ manujottama
ācacakṣe ca tad rājñe nāsatyavacanaṃ dvija
tac chrutvā vacanaṃ rājā dvāstham āha muhūrtakam
vilambyatāṃ mahābhāgau tau brūhi vacanān mama
vyāyāmatailasaṃsarga malino na vibhūṣitaḥ
prasādhanaṃ ca kṛtvāhaṃ niṣkramāmi tvarānvitaḥ
samācaṣṭa tato dālbhya tau ca bhūyas tam ūcatuḥ
paśyāvas tava bhūyo 'pi tvāṃ drakṣyāvaḥ prasādhitam
ity ukto nirgatas tūrṇaṃ bhavanād avanīpatiḥ
sa praṇāmaṃ tayoḥ kṛtvā kiṃcin nataśirā nṛpaḥ
saptadvīpavatī pṛthvī putradārabalaṃ dhanam
ity udāhṛtam ākarṇya nṛpater aśvināv api
aṅgopāṅgādikaṃ sarvaṃ śanakais tāv apaśyatām
śirolalāṭabāhuṃ sa nayanādivilokanam
kṛtvā ca taṃ mahīpālam ūcatus tāv idaṃ surau
praviśya snāhi bhūpāla yathārthaiś ca vibhūṣaṇaiḥ
vibhūṣitaṃ tu bhūyas tvāṃ drakṣyāvo 'vāṃ nareśvara
snāto 'nuliptaḥ sragdhārī suvastraḥ suvibhūṣitaḥ
nāsatyadasrayoḥ pārśvam iyāya vasudhādhipaḥ
bhūyo 'pi tau yathā pūrvam aṅgopāṅgavilokanam
tau sahāsau samālakṣya sa tadā vasudhādhipaḥ
hāsasya kāraṇaṃ deva bhiṣajau tāv apṛcchata
pṛcchantaṃ na tato dālbhya nṛpatiṃ hāsyakāraṇam
yad ūcatur mahābhāgau tac chṛṇuṣva vadāmi te
śṛṇu bhūpāla sakalaṃ hāsakāraṇam āvayoḥ
yuṣmaddarśanasaṃbhūtaṃ kṣaṇāpacayahetukam
asnātasyābhavad bhūpa yādṛśī te surūpatā
sāṃprataṃ tādṛśī neyaṃ bhūṣitasyāpi bhūṣaṇaiḥ
snātaḥ sragdāmadhārī tvaṃ svanuliptaḥ subhūṣitaḥ
tathāpy asnāta eva prāc śobhano 'bhūn na sāṃpratam
kiṃtu tatkāraṇaṃ yena vyāyāmamalināmbaraḥ
śobhano 'ham abhūt pūrvam idānīṃ na vibhūṣitaḥ
divyena cakṣuṣā bhūpa kālasyāsya ca tasya ca
vayaḥpariṇatiṃ sūkṣmāṃ paśyāvo 'pacayapradām
yathā hi nāḍikā pūrṇā galaty avirataṃ nṛpa
nRṇāṃ pariṇatas tadvac śarīragrahaṇād anu
janmato 'nantaraṃ bālyaṃ paugaṇḍatvaṃ tataḥ param
yauvanaṃ madhyadehitvaṃ vārddhakaṃ ca jarā nṛṇām
sthūladṛṣṭyā tu paśyanti na tu te sūkṣmadarśinaḥ
nimeṣaśatabhāgasya sahasrāṃśaḥ kṣaṇo nṛpa
tasyāpy ayutabhāgāṃśo bhavaty apacayo nṛṇām
sūkṣmātisūkṣmāpacayī bhavaty eṣa pumān nṛpa
pariṇāmaṃ kramād yāti tṛptiṃ vāri pibann iva
pratikṣaṇāṃśayā vṛddhir bālatvaṃ hīyate tayā
kāntir yā nṛpa bālasya pogaṇḍasya hi sā kutaḥ
kāntyādisaṃpado hāniḥ paramā nṛpa vārddhake
tatrāpy anukṣaṇaṃ hānir hānir ā mṛtyuto nṛpa
evaṃ pratikṣaṇāṃśāṃśo nRṇām apacayapradaḥ
asmaddṛṣṭo bhavān yāvat praviṣṭo nijamandiram
tāvad dhānim anuprāptaḥ kimu yāmārdhasaṃsthitaḥ
yādṛśo 'dya bhavāṃs tādṛk tvaṃ na rūpī nareśvara
paraśvaḥ śastanaṃ naiva
evaṃ samastabhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca
pratikṣaṇāṃśāpacayaṃ prāpnuvanti mahītale
tasmān na kautukaṃ kāryaṃ bhavatā tu nareśvara
rājā purūravā bhūyaḥ śrutvā vākyam idaṃ tayoḥ
cintayitvā vacaḥ prāha saṃvegotkampimānasaḥ
ajñānatimirāndhānāṃ madvidhānāṃ bhavadvidhāḥ
pradīpabhūtāḥ saṃdeho vidyate nātra kaścana
sadāpacayadoṣeṇa duṣṭakāyaiḥ surottamau
yat kāryaṃ puruṣais tac ca kathyatāṃ hitakāmyayā
āsanaṃ śayanaṃ yānaṃ paridhānaṃ gṛhādikam
mūḍho 'dhruvaṃ dhruvamatiḥ kim ātmānaṃ na budhyate
bālyāt paugaṇḍatāṃ gatvā yaḥ punar yauvanaṃ gataḥ
bhuvaḥ śailaṃ samārūḍhaḥ samārūḍhas tato drumam
ārohaṇaṃ sa kim anyad ṛkṣabhītaḥ kariṣyati
bālyāt paugaṇḍatāṃ yāto yauvanād vṛddhatāṃ gataḥ
tasmād etan manuṣyeṇa vicāryātmahitaiṣiṇā
śreyasy āmuṣmike yatnaḥ kartavyo 'harniśaṃ nṛpa
śreyaḥ paraṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ kapilaḥ prāha pārthivaḥ
śreyaḥ paraṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ prāha pañcaśikho muniḥ
śreyaḥ paraṃ manuṣyāṇām aṅgāriṣṭho 'bravīn nṛpaḥ
adhyātmikādiduḥkhānām atyantādipratikriyā
śreyaḥ paraṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ janako hy āha mokṣavit
hāniṃ sarvavidhitsānām ātmanaḥ sukhahetukīm
śreyaḥ paraṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ devalo 'py āha tattvavit
etad eva paraṃ śreyo vijñānaṃ hitakāminām
kāmānusārī puruṣaḥ kāmān anu vinaśyati
aśreyasaṃ paraṃ caitad yad bhūpālātikāmitā
evaṃ vijñātatattvārthaḥ sanako yogināṃ varaḥ
narendra prāha viprāṇāṃ paramārthaparaṃparam
kriyākalāpaphaladam ṛgyajuḥsāmasaṃjñitam
amuṣmin madhyamaṃ śreyaḥ prāhuḥ sapta rṣayo nṛpa
tad āhur aparaṃ śreyo ṛcīkacyavanādayaḥ
dve karmaṇī naraśreṣṭha brahmaṇā samudāhṛte
karma svarūpato bhraṣṭam anākāṅkṣya phalaṃ kṛtam
sāmānyaṃ cāparaṃ śreyaḥ sarvavarṇāśrameṣu yat
tac chṛṇuṣva mahīpāla vadato mama tattvataḥ
satyaṃ vaktavyaṃ nityaṃ maitreṇa bhāvyaṃ kāryaṃ ca tyājyaṃ nityam āyāsakāri
loke 'muṣmin yad dhitaṃ ca tathāsmiṃs tasminn ātmā yojanīyo 'nudhīraiḥ
tīrthasnānaiḥ sopavāsair ajasraṃ pātre dānair homajāpaiś ca nityam
śuddhir neyo devatābhyarcanaiś ca śuddho 'py ātmā saṅgadoṣād aśuddhaḥ
śuddhaṃ vastraṃ saṅgadoṣād aśuddhaṃ bhūyaḥ śuddhiṃ śodhyamānaṃ paryāti
etaj jñātvā na pramādo manuṣyaiḥ śuddhe hy ātmany ātmavidbhir vidheyaḥ
samyak saṃpūjitau yātau nāka pṛṣṭham athāśvinau
niṣkāmo 'nudinaṃ yajñair iyāja puruṣottamam
bhogāsaṅgi mano dālbhya yadāsīt tasya bhūpateḥ
tatyājārtheṣu mamatām ahaṃkāraṃ tathātmani
samatāṃ sarvabhūteṣu saṃprāpa pṛthivīpatiḥ
madāvalepo pūpādau tasya syād iti kā kathā
evaṃ dālbhya manuṣyeṇa samatām anutiṣṭhatā
tasmān niḥsaṅgacittena śakyaś cintayituṃ hariḥ
prītidveṣādayas tyaktvā maharṣe yasya cetasā
kāryārambheṣu sarveṣu duḥsvapneṣu ca sattama
yenārambhāś ca sidhhyanti duḥsvapnaṃ copaśāmyati
amaṅgalānāṃ sarveṣāṃ pratighātaś ca jāyate
janārdanaṃ bhūtapatiṃ jagadguruṃ smaran manuṣyaḥ satataṃ mahāmune
duṣṭāny aśeṣāṇy apahanti sādhayaty aśeṣakāryāṇi tathā yadīcchati
śṛṇuṣva cānyad vadato mamākhilaṃ vadāmi yat te dvijavarya maṅgalam
sarvārthasiddhiṃ pradadāti yaḥ sadā nihanty aśeṣāṇi ca pātakāni
vyomāmbuvāyvagnimahīsvarūpair vistāravān yo 'ṇutaro 'ṇubhāgāt
sa sthūlasūkṣmaḥ satateśvareśvaro
yasmāt parastāt puruṣād anantād anādimadhyād akhilaṃ na kiṃcit
hiraṇyagarbhācyutarudrarūpī sṛjaty aśeṣaṃ paripāti hanti
guṇāśrayī yo bhagavān sa sarvadā
paraḥ surāṇāṃ paramo 'surāṇāṃ paro munīnāṃ paramo yatīnām
dhyāto yatīnām apakalmaṣair yo dadāti muktiṃ parameśvareśvaraḥ
manobhir ādyaḥ puruṣaḥ sa sarvadā
yenoddhṛteyaṃ dharaṇī rasātalād aśeṣasattvasthitikāraṇād idam
bibharti viśvaṃ jagataḥ sa mūlavān
pādeṣu vedā jaṭhare carācaraṃ romasv aśeṣā munayo mukhe makhāḥ
samastayajñāṅgamayaṃ vapur vibhor yasyāṅgam īśeśvarasaṃstutasya
yajñeśvaro yajñapumān sa sarvadā
pātālamūleśvarabhogisaṃhatau vinyasya pādau pṛthivīṃ ca bibhrataḥ
ekārṇavād yasya mahīyaso mahīm ādāya vegena samutpatiṣyataḥ
hato hiraṇyākṣamahāsuraḥ purā purāṇapuṃsā parameṇa yena
varāharūpaḥ sa patiḥ prajāpater
daṃṣṭrākarālaṃ surabhītināśanaṃ kṛtvā vapur divyanṛsiṃharūpiṇaṃ
daityendravakṣaḥsthaladāradāruṇaiḥ karoruhaiḥ śatrurujānukāribhiḥ
dantāntadīptidyutinirmalāṇi cakāra sarvāṇi diśaṃ mukhāni
yannāmasaṃkīrtanato mahābhayād vimokṣam āpnoti na saṃśayaṃ naraḥ
saṭākalāpabhramaṇānilahatāḥ sphuṭanti yasyāmbudharāḥ samantataḥ
sa divyasiṃhaḥ sphuritākulekṣaṇo
yadīkṣaṇajyotiṣi raśmimaṇḍalaṃ pralīnam eva na rarāja bhāsvataḥ
kutaḥ śaśāṅkasya sa siṃharūpadhṛṅ
dravanti daityāḥ praṇamanti devatā naśyanti rakṣāṃsy apayānti cārayaḥ
aśeṣadeveśanareśvareśvaraiḥ sadā stutaṃ yac caritaṃ mahādbhutam
ṛkkāritaṃ yo yajuṣātiśāntimat sāmadhvanidhvastasamastapātakam
yatpādavinyāsapavitratāṃ mahī yayau viyad ṛgyajuṣām udīraṇāt
sa vāmano divyaśarīradhṛk sadā
yasmin prayāte surabhūbhṛto 'dhvaraṃ nanāma khedād avaniḥ sasāgarā
samastadeveṣṭimayaṃ mahādyutir dadhāra yo rūpam atīndriyaṃ prabhuḥ
saṅghaiḥ surāṇāṃ divi bhūtale sthitais tathā manuṣyair gagane sa sarvadā
krāntvā dharitrīṃ gaganaṃ tathā divaṃ marutpater yaḥ pradadau triviṣṭapam
surāṃś ca yajñasya bhujaḥ sa sarvadā
rasātalād yena purā samāhṛtāḥ samastavedā varavājirūpiṇā
niḥkṣatriyāṃ yaś ca cakāra medinīm anekaśo bāhuvanaṃ tathāchinat
jaghāna cānyān rajanīcarān asau
cikṣepa bālaḥ śakaṭaṃ babhañja yo yamalārjunau kaṃsam ariṃ jaghāna
mamarda cāṇūramukhaṃ sa sarvadā
prātaḥ sahasrāṃśumarīcinirmalaṃ kareṇa bibhrad bhagavān sudarśanam
kaumodakīṃ cāpi gadām anuttamāṃ
himendukundasphaṭikābhrakomalaṃ mukhānilāpūritam īśvareśvaraḥ
sarveṣu kāleṣu samastadeśeṣv aśeṣakāryeṣu tatheśvareśvaraḥ
sarvaiḥ svarūpair bhagavān anādimān
sidhyanti kāryāṇi tathāsya sarvāṇy arthān avāpnoti tathā yatheṣṭam
prārambho drutam upayāti siddhim īśaḥ pāpāni kṣapayati cāsya vāsudevaḥ
vaidehaḥ paramapadaṃ prasādya viṣṇuṃ saṃprāptaḥ sakalaphalaprado hi viṣṇuḥ
sarvārambheṣu dālbhyaitad duḥsvapneṣu ca paṇḍitaḥ
śamaṃ prayānti duṣṭāni grahapīḍāś ca dāruṇāḥ
karoty akhilarūpaiś ca rakṣām akṣataśaktidhṛk
kurvīta kiṃ pumān sthānaṃ kaḥ pumān brahmaṇo balam
svakarmaṇā dhanaṃ labdhvā nityanaimittikāḥ kriyāḥ
kurvīta śuddhim āsthāya svecchayā ca tathā paraḥ
tyaktvā rāgādikān doṣān samaḥ sarvatra vai bhavet
sarvatra maitrīṃ kurvīta dadyād iṣṭāni cārthinām
kuryād dīneṣu karuṇāṃ duḥśīlān parivarjayet
muditāṃ dharmaśīleṣu bhāvanāṃ munisattama
niḥśeṣārthamalāpetāṃ
ekatra vā jagannāthe bhāvanāṃ puruṣottame
śuddhāṃ kurvīta paṇḍitaḥ
śarīrabāhyatāṃ śaśvad dhiṃsāṃ kurvīta na kvacit
nindāvamānam anyeṣāṃ yac cānyad upaghātakam
śarīravāṅmanaḥśuddhiṃ kurvīta ca sadātmanaḥ
bhūtānām upakāraś ca tapobhiś cātmakarṣaṇam
eṣa dharmaḥ samāsena dālbhyākhyāto mayā tava
adharmaś cāyam evokto viparīto manīṣibhiḥ
ete yatra guṇāḥ pūrvaṃ kathitā jñānasaṃyutāḥ
brahmaṇaḥ sāśrayaḥ śuddha upacārāt tad eva saḥ
nāmnāṃ bahutvaṃ lokānām upakārakaraṃ śṛṇu
sādhakaṃ puruṣavyāghra saumyakrūreṣu vastuṣu
vāsudevācyutānanta satyājyapuruṣottamaiḥ
dhanakṛd dharmakṛd dharmī dharmātmā viśvakṛc chuciḥ
śuciṣad viṣṇur abjākṣaḥ puṣkarākṣo hy adhokṣayaḥ
śuciśravāḥ śipiviṣṭo yajñeśo yajñabhāvanaḥ
nāmnām ity evam ādīnāṃ samuccāraṇato naraḥ
dharmaṃ mahāntam āpnoti pāpabandhakṣayaṃ tathā
tathārthaprāptaye brahman devanāmāni me śṛṇu
yeṣāṃ samuccāraṇato vittam āpnoti bhaktimān
śrīdaḥ śrīśaḥ śrīnivāsaḥ śrīdharaḥ śrīniketanaḥ
śriyaḥ patiḥ śrīparamaḥ śrīmāñ śrīvatsalāñcchanaḥ
nṛsiṃho duṣṭadāmano jayo viṣṇus trivikramaḥ
kāmyaḥ kāmapradaḥ kāntaḥ kāmapālas tathā hariḥ
ānando mādhavaś caiva kāmasaṃsiddhaye nṛpa
rāmaḥ paraśurāmaś ca nṛsiṃho viṣṇur eva ca
vikramaś caivam ādīni japyāny arijigīṣubhiḥ
keśavaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ puṣkarākṣaṃ tathā japet
netrabādhāsu sarvāsu hṛṣīkeśaṃ bhayeṣu ca
acyutaṃ cāmṛtaṃ caiva japed auṣadhakarmaṇi
cakriṇaṃ gadinaṃ caiva śārṅginaṃ khaḍginaṃ tathā
kṣemārthe prasavan rājan dikṣu prācyādiṣu smaret
ajitaṃ cādhikaṃ caiva sarvaṃ sarvaśvaraṃ tathā
saṃsmaret puruṣo bhaktyā vyavahāreṣu sarvadā
nārāyaṇaṃ sarvakālaṃ kṣutapraskhalitādiṣu
grahanakṣatrapīḍāsu devabādhāṭavīṣu ca
asyuvairinirodheṣu vyāghrasiṃhādisaṃkaṭe
taraty akhiladurgāṇi tāpārto jalaśāyinam
jvaraduṣṭaśiroroga viṣavīryaṃ praśāmyati
snāne devārcane home praṇipāte pradakṣiṇe
kurvīta tanmanā bhūtvā anantācyutakīrtanam
nārāyaṇaṃ śārṅgadharaṃ śrīdharaṃ puruṣottamam
vāmanaṃ khaḍginaṃ caiva duḥsvapneṣu ca saṃsmaret
ekārṇavāhiparyaṅka śāyinaṃ ca naraḥ smaret
vāyvagnīgṛhadāhāya pravṛddhāv upalakṣya ca
vidyārthī mohavibhrānti vegāghūrṇitamānasaḥ
manuṣyo muniśārdūla sadāśvaśirasaṃ smaret
śrīśaṃ sarvābhyudayike karmaṇi saṃprakīrtayet
ariṣṭānteṣv aśeṣeṣu viśokaṃ ca sadā japet
marutpratāpāgnijala bandhanādiṣu mṛtyuṣu
sarvārthasiddhim āpnoti nāmnām ekārthatā yataḥ
sarvāṇy etāni nāmāni parasya brahmaṇo 'nagha
yaṃ yaṃ kāmam abhidhyāyet taṃ tam āpnoty asaṃśayam
sarvān kāmān avāpnoti samārādhya jagadgurum
tanmayo vāñchitān kāmān yad avāpnoti mānavaḥ
vāṅmanaḥkāyikaṃ dveṣaṃ yac ca kurvan prayāty adhaḥ
svarūpaśaktiḥ sā tasya matibhedakṛtaṃ na tad
sa śākto nirguṇaḥ śuddho brahmabhūto jagadguruḥ
ekasvarūpam adhyātmaṃ puṇyāpuṇyavibhedibhiḥ
bhrāntijñānānvitair miśraṃ sitāsitaviceṣṭitaiḥ
tāpārtās tāpaśamanam atiprītyatiśītalam
kaphadoṣānvitair nāti prītiyuktair niraṃśubhiḥ
madhyasthabuddhyā caivānye nātiśītātitāpibhiḥ
mṛṣṭam etad itīty anyair matsyāḍhyam iti cāparaiḥ
nātivegātivegaṃ ca hṛṣṭodvignais tathāparaiḥ
kim eteneti caivānyaiḥ paradārābhilāṣibhiḥ
dālbhya saṃdṛśyate cānyair jantubhir bhāyakātaraiḥ
tad eva pūyaṃ paśyanti pretādyā hṛtipāpinaḥ
naite gaṅgāmbhaso bhedāḥ prītyaprītipradāyinaḥ
prāṇināṃ cetaso bhedād dālbhyaite karmayonayaḥ
viśeṣakāraṇābhāvād viśeṣābhāva eva hi
yogibhir dṛśyate śuddhaṃ rāgādyupaśamāmalaiḥ
rāgibhir viṣayākāraṃ tad eva brahma dṛśyate
ātmaputrasuhṛdbhartṛ
bhūtendriyāntaḥkaraṇa pradhānapuruṣātmakam
aparaṃ brahmaṇo rūpaṃ paraṃ dālbhya niśāmaya
aheyam akṣaraṃ śuddham asaṃbhūtinirañjanam
viṣṇvākhyaṃ paramaṃ brahma yad vai paśyanti sūrayaḥ
patnī nRṇāṃ muniśreṣṭha yoṣitas ca tathā naraḥ
upoṣītena yenāgryā patnyā ca rahito naraḥ
aśūnyaśayanā nāma dvitīyāṃ śṛṇu tāṃ mama
śete jagatpatiḥ kṛṣṇaḥ śriyā sārdhaṃ yadā dvija
aśūnyaśayanā nāma tadā grāhyā hi sā tithiḥ
kṛṣṇapakṣadvitīyāyāṃ śrāvaṇe dvijasattama
śrīvatsadhāriṇaṃ śrīśaṃ bhaktyābhyarcya śriyā saha
śrīvatsadhāriñ śrīkānta śrīdhāma śrīpate 'cyuta
gārhasthyaṃ mā praṇāśaṃ me yātu dharmārthakāmadam
agnayo mā praṇaśyantu mā praṇaśyantu devatāḥ
lakṣmyā na śūnyaṃ varada yathā te śayanaṃ sadā
śayyā mamāpy aśūnyāstu tathaiva madhusūdana
evaṃ prasādya pūjāṃ ca kṛtvā lakṣmyās tathā hareḥ
phalāni dadyāc chayyāyām abhīṣṭāni jagatpateḥ
naktaṃ praṇamyāyatane havir bhuñjīta vāgyataḥ
brāhmaṇāya dvitīye 'hni śaktyā dadyāc ca dakṣiṇām
aśūnyaśayanaś cāsau dharmakarmārthasādhakaḥ
bhavaty avyāhataiśvaryaḥ puruṣo nātra saṃśayaḥ
kathitaṃ bhavatā sarvaṃ yat pṛṣṭo 'si mayā dvija
saṃsārahetuṃ muktiṃ ca saṃsārān munisattama
saṃsārasyāsya tanmuktiḥ saṃkṣepāc chrūyatāṃ mama
kurvataḥ kṣīyate pūrvaṃ manyubandhaś ca neṣyate
apūrvasaṃbhavābhavāt kṣayaṃ yāty ādikarmaṇi
dālbhya saṃsāravicchedaḥ kāraṇābhāvasaṃbhavaḥ
bhavaty asaṃśayaṃ cānyac śrūyatām atra kāraṇam
saṃsārān mucyate dālbhya samāsād vadato mama
gṛhītakarmaṇā yena puṃsāṃ jātir dvijottama
tatprāyaścittabhūtaṃ vai śṛṇu karmakṣayāvaham
brāhmaṇakṣatriyaviśāṃ śūdrāntyānāṃ ca sattama
jātipradasya kṣayadaṃ tad evādyasya karmaṇaḥ
jñānakāraṇabhāvaṃ ca tad eva pratipadyate
pumāṃś cādhigatajñāno bhedaṃ nāpnoti sattama
brahmaṇā viṣṇusaṃjñena parameṇāvyayātmanā
etat te kathitaṃ dālbhya saṃsārasya samāsataḥ
kāraṇaṃ bhavamuktiś ca jāyate yogino yathā
ārādhayām āsa hariṃ lebhe kāmāṃś ca vāñchitān
ārādhya taṃ jagannāthaṃ na kaścid avasīdati
iti śukravacaḥ śrutvā prahlādo madhusūdanam
ārādhya prāptavān kṛtsnaṃ trailokaiśvaryam ūrjitam
anārādhyācyutaṃ devaṃ kaḥ kāmān prāpnute naraḥ
śrutvā babhūva satataṃ keśavārpitamānasaḥ
bhogān vā vilupān devāt tasmād ārādhayācyutam
dadāti vāñchitān kāmān sakāmair arcito hariḥ
muktiṃ dadāti govindo niṣkāmair abhipūjitaḥ
bhagavān avatīrṇo 'bhūn martyalokaṃ janārdanaḥ
bhārāvataraṇārthāya bhuvo bhūtapatir hariḥ
cakāra prītim atulāṃ sāmānyapuruṣo yathā
sārathyaṃ kṛtavāṃś caiva teṣāṃ sarveśvaro hariḥ
upakārī mahābhāgaḥ sa teṣāṃ sarvavastuṣu
keśavaḥ pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ sutānāṃ janako yathā
dhanyās te kṛtapuṇyāś ca mama pāṇḍusutā matāḥ
rājyahetor arīñ jaghnur akasmāt pāṇḍunandanāḥ
jātaṃ nirdhūtapāpe 'smin kule viṣṇuparigrahe
evaṃ devavaras teṣāṃ prasādasumukho hariḥ
pṛcchatāṃ kaccid ācaṣṭe kiṃcid guhyaṃ mahātmanām
guhyaṃ janārdanaṃ yāṃs tu dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
dharmārthakāmamokṣeṣu yad guhyaṃ madhusūdanaḥ
śaratalpagatād bhīṣmād dharmāñ śrutvā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
pṛṣṭavān yaj jagannāthaṃ tan me nigadataḥ śṛṇu
pañcamenāśvamedhena yadā snāto yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
tadā nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ praśnam etam apṛcchata
bhagavan vaiṣṇavā dharmāḥ kiṃphalāḥ kiṃparāyaṇāḥ
kiṃ kṛtyam adhikṛtyaite bhavatotpāditāḥ purā
śrotavyāś cen mayā dharmās tatas tān kathayākhilān
pavitrāś caiva ye dharmāḥ sarvapāpapraṇāśanāḥ
yāñ śrutvā brahmahā goghnaḥ pitṛghno gurutalpagaḥ
surāpo vā kṛtaghnaś ca mucyate sarvakilbiṣaiḥ
vasiṣṭhādyair mahābhāgair munibhir bhāvitātmabhiḥ
tato 'haṃ tava deveśa pādamūlam upāgataḥ
śrutā me mānavā dharmā vāsiṣṭhāś ca mahāmate
parāśarakṛtāś caiva tathātreyasya dhīmataḥ
jāpāleś ca mahābāho muner dvaipāyanasya ca
umāmaheśvarāś caiva jātidharmāś ca pāvanāḥ
guṇeś ca guṇabāhoś ca kāśyapeyās tathaiva ca
bahvāyanakṛtāś caiva śākuneyās tathaiva ca
agastyagītā maudgalyāḥ śāṇḍilyāḥ saurabhās tathā
bhṛgor aṅgirasaś caiva kaśyapoddālakās tathā
saumantūgrāyaṇāgrāś ca pailasya ca mahātmanaḥ
vaiśampāyanagītāś ca piśaṅgamakṛtāś ca ye
aindrāś ca vāruṇāś caiva kauberā vātsyapauṇakāḥ
āpastambāḥ śrutā dharmās tathā gopālakasya ca
bhṛgvaṅgiraḥkṛtāś caiva sauryā hārītakās tathā
yājñavalkyakṛtāś caiva tathā saptarṣayaś ca ye
etāś cānyāś ca vividhāḥ śrutā me dharmasaṃhitāḥ
bhagavañ śrotum icchāmi tava vaktrād viniḥsṛtān
bahumānāc ca prītyā ca dharmaputraṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
iṣṭas tvaṃ hi mahābāho sadā mama yudhiṣṭhira
paramārthaṃ tava brūyāṃ kiṃ punar dharmasaṃhitām
evam ukte tu kṛṣṇena ṛṣayo 'mitatejasaḥ
samājagmuḥ sabhāmadhye śrotukāmā harer giram
devagandharvaṛṣayo guhyakāś ca mahāyaśāḥ
vālakhilyā mahātmāno munayaḥ saṃmitavratāḥ
vaiṣṇavān akhilān dharmān yaḥ paṭhet pāpanāśanān
bhaveyur akṣayās tasya lokāḥ satpuṇyabhāginaḥ
kṛṣṇadṛṣṭihataṃ cāsya kilbiṣaṃ saṃpraṇaśyati
vaiṣṇavasya ca yajñasya phalaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ
kautūhalasamāviṣṭaḥ papracchedaṃ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
kīdṛśaṃ kiṃpramāṇaṃ vā kathaṃ vāntaṃ janārdana
taranti puruṣāḥ kṛṣṇa kenopāyena saṃśame
pratyuvāca mahātmānaṃ dharmaputraṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
sādhu sādhur ayaṃ praśnaḥ śrūyatāṃ bho yudhiṣṭhira
ṣaḍaśītisahasrāṇi yojanānāṃ narādhipa
tāmrapātram ivātaptaṃ śūlavyāmiśrakaṇṭakam
dvādaśādityasaṃkāśaṃ bhairavaṃ duratikramam
na tatra vṛkṣā na cchāyā pānīyaṃ ketanāni ca
yatra viśramate śrāntaḥ puruṣo 'dhvānako nṛpa
yāmyair dūtair nīyamāno yamasyājñākarair balāt
avaśyaṃ ca mahārāja sa gantavyo mahāpathaḥ
naraiḥ strībhis tathā tiryaiḥ pṛthivyāṃ jīvasaṃjñakaiḥ
ekaviṃśac ca narakā yamasya viṣaye smṛtāḥ
ye tu duṣkṛtakarmāṇas te patanti pṛthak pṛthak
kṣuradhārā mahāraudraḥ sūkaras tāla eva ca
kīṭādaḥ kṛmibhakṣaś ca śālmaliś ca mahādrumaḥ
tathā pūyavahaḥ pāpā rudhirāndho mahattamaḥ
agnijvālo mahānādaḥ saṃdāmśaḥ śunabhojanaḥ
tathā vaitaraṇī coṣṇā asipattravanaṃ tathā
viṣṇos tad vacanaṃ śrutvā papāta bhuvi pāṇḍavaḥ
sa saṃjñaś ca muhūrtena bhūyaḥ keśavam abravīt
bhītaś cāsmi mahābāho śrutvā mārgasya vistaram
kenopāyena taṃ mārgaṃ taranti puruṣāḥ sukham
brāhmaṇebhyaḥ pradānāni nānārūpāṇi pārthiva
upānahapradā yānti sukhaṃ chāyāsu cchattradāḥ
na teṣām aśubhaṃ kiṃcic śūlādi na ca kaṇṭakāḥ
aśvataryaḥ pradātāram upatiṣṭhanti taṃ naram
vitṛṣṇāś cāmbudātāras tarpitāś cānnadās tathā
auprāvṛtā vastradāś ca nagnā vai yānty avastradāḥ
hiraṇyadāḥ sukhaṃ yānti puruṣāḥ svābhyalaṃkṛtāḥ
gopradā yānti ca sukhaṃ vimuktāḥ sarvakilbiṣaiḥ
bhūmidāḥ sukham adhante sarvakāmaiḥ sutarpitāḥ
yānti caivāparikliṣṭā narāḥ śayyāsanapradāḥ
tataḥ sukhataraṃ yānti vimāneṣu gṛhapradāḥ
ārāmaropī cchāyāsu śītalāsu sukhaṃ vrajet
adattadānā gacchanti padbhyāṃ yānena yānadāḥ
dīpapradāḥ sukhaṃ yānti dīpayantaś ca tatpatham
vimānair haṃsayuktais tu yānti māsopavāsinaḥ
tato barhiṇayuktena ṣaḍrātram upavāsinaḥ
anantaraṃ ca yo 'śnīyāt tasya lokā yathā mama
panīyaṃ paralokeṣu pāvanaṃ paramaṃ smṛtam
pānīyasya pradānena tṛptir bhavati śāśvatī
pānīyasya guṇā divyāḥ pretaloke sukhāvahāḥ
tatra puṇyodakā nāma nadī teṣāṃ pravartate
ye ca duṣkṛtakarmāṇaḥ pūyaṃ teṣāṃ pravartate
eṣā nadī mahārāja sarvakāmadughā śubhā
adhvani khinnagātras tu dvijo yaḥ kṣuttṛṣṇānvitaḥ
pṛcchan sadānnadātāram abhyeti gṛham āśayā
taṃ pūjaya prayatnena so 'tithir brāhmaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ
pitaro devatāś caiva ṛṣayaś ca tapodhanāḥ
pūjitāḥ pūjite tasmin nirāśe tu nirāśakāḥ
tasmin dvije pūjite pūjitās te gate nirāśe pratiyānti nāśam
āgamiṣyati yat pātraṃ tat pātraṃ tārayiṣyati
kapilāyāṃ tu dattāyāṃ yat phalaṃ jyeṣṭhapuṣkare
tat phalaṃ pāṇḍavaśreṣṭha viprāṇāṃ pādaśaucane
dvijapādodakaklinnā yāvat tiṣṭhati medinī
devamālyāpanayanaṃ dvijocchiṣṭāpamārjanam
śrāntasaṃvāhanaṃ caiva dīnasya paripālanam
ekaikaṃ pāṇḍavaśreṣṭha gopradānād viśiṣyate
pādaśaucaṃ tathābhyaṅgaṃ dīpam annaṃ pratiśrayam
svāgatenāgnayaḥ prītā āsanena śatakratuḥ
pitaraḥ pādaśaucena annādyena prajāpatiḥ
yeṣāṃ taḍāgāni bahūdakāni prapāś ca kūpāś ca pratiśrayāś ca
savṛṣaṃ gośataṃ tena dattaṃ bhavati śāśvatam
śochayet kapilāṃ dattvā etad vai nātra saṃśayaḥ
prāsādā yatra sauvarṇā vasordhārā ca syandate
prayacchate yaḥ kapilāṃ savatsāṃ kāṃsyopadohāṃ kanakāgraśṛṅgīm
yān yān hi kāmān abhivāñchate 'sau tāṃs tān avāpnoty amalāṃś ca lokān
tāvad gauḥ pṛthivī jñeyā yāvad garbhaṃ na muñcati
tasmin kāle pradātavyā vidhinā yā mayoditā
antarikṣagato vatso yāvad yonyāṃ pradṛśyate
tāvad gauḥ pṛthivī jñeyā yāvad garbhaṃ na muñcati
yāvanti tasya romāṇi tāvadvarṣāṇi mānavaḥ
haṃsayuktena yānena yuktenāpsarasāṃ gaṇaiḥ
tiladhenuṃ pravakṣyāmi yaś cāsyā vidhir uttamaḥ
suvarṇanābhiṃ yaḥ kṛtvā sukhūraṃ kṛṣṇamārgaṇām
kutapaprastarasthāṃ tu tilāṃ kṛtvā prayatnataḥ
tilaiḥ prasthādi tāṃ dadyāt sarvaratnair alaṃkṛtām
caturantā bhaved dattā pṛthivī nātra saṃśayaḥ
kṛṣṇājine tilāṃ kṛtvā kṛṣṇāṃ vā yadi vetarām
yāvaj jīvakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tena dānena pūyate
rājateṣu tu pātreṣu koṇeṣu madhusarpiṣī
dhanaṃ prāpnoti puṇyena maunenājñāṃ prayacchati
ahiṃsayā paraṃ rūpam dīkṣayā kulajanma ca
phalamūlāśanād rājyaṃ svargaḥ parṇāśano bhavet

śākaṃ sādhayato rājyaṃ nākapṛṣṭham anāśanāt
sthaṇḍile ca śayānasya gṛhāṇi śayanāni ca

śayanāsanayānāni ye gatā hi tapovanam
rasānāṃ pratisaṃhārāt saubhāgyam abhijāyate
āmiṣapratiṣedhāt tu bhavaty āyuṣmatī prajā
kīrtir bhavati dānena ārogyaṃ cāpy ahiṃsayā
dvijaśuśrūṣayā rājyaṃ divyarūpam avāpnute

dīpālokapradānena cakṣuṣmāñ jāyate naraḥ
gandhamālyapradānena tuṣṭir bhavati puṣkalā
keśaśmaśrūn dhārayato hy agrā bhavati saṃtatiḥ
vākśaucaṃ manasaḥ śaucaṃ yac ca śaucaṃ jalāśrayam

tāmrāyasānāṃ bhaṇḍānāṃ dātā ratnādhipo bhavet
labhate tu paraṃ sthānaṃ balavān puṣyate sadā
dhānyaṃ krameṇārjitavittasaṃcayaṃ vipre suśīle te prayacchate yaḥ
vasuṃdharā tasya bhavet sutuṣṭā dhārā vasūnāṃ pratimuñcatīha
sa śrīsamṛddhaṃ bahuratnapūrṇaṃ labhaty adhiṣṭhānavaraṃ samṛddham
indhanāni ca yo dadyād dvijebhyaḥ śiśirāgame
kāyāgnidīptiṃ saubhāgyam aiśvaryaṃ cādhigacchati

svargīyam apy āha hiraṇyadānam tathā variṣṭhaṃ kanakapradānam
svādhyāyacāritraguṇānvitāya tasyāpi lokāḥ pravarā bhavanti
hiraṇyadānaṃ ca tathā viśiṣṭaṃ sa śakro lokaṃ labhate durāpam

rūpānvitāṃ dakṣavatīṃ manojñāṃ bhāryām ayatnopacitāṃ labhet saḥ
lavaṇasya tu dātāras tilānāṃ sarpiṣas tathā
svarge 'psarobhiḥ saha bhuktabhogas tataś cyutaḥ śīlavatīṃ sa bhāryām
rūpānvitāṃ dakṣavatīṃ suraktāṃ sukhena dharmeṇa tathāpi kāle
kīdṛgvidhāsv avasthāsu dattaṃ dānaṃ janārdana
avasthāṃ kṛṣṇa kathaya paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi me
vṛthājanmāni catvāri vṛthādānāni ṣoḍaśa
aputrāṇāṃ vṛthā janma ye ca dharmabahiṣkṛtāḥ
parapākaṃ ca ye 'śnanti paradāraratāś ca ye
pary asthānaṃ vṛthā dānaṃ sadoṣaṃ parikīrtitam
ārūḍhapatite caiva anyāyopārjitaṃ ca yat
vyarthaṃ cābrāhmaṇe dānaṃ patite taskare tathā
guroś cāprītijanake kṛtaghne grāmayājake
paricārake ca yad dattaṃ vṛthādānāni ṣoḍaśa
serṣyāmanyumanāś caiva dambhārthaṃ cārthakāraṇāt
yaḥ śuddhiḥ prayato bhūtvā prasannamānasendriyaḥ
deśe deśe ca pātre ca yo dadāti dvijātiṣu
trailokya kṛṣṇa bhūtānāṃ sarvalokātmako hy asi
nRṇāṃ yaduvaraśreṣṭha tuṣyase kena karmaṇā
brāhmaṇaiḥ pūjitair nityaṃ pūjito 'haṃ na saṃśayaḥ
viprāparā gatir mahyaṃ yas tān pūjayate nṛpa
tam ahaṃ tena rūpeṇa prapaśyāmi yudhiṣṭhira
kāṇāḥ kubjāś ca khañjāś ca daridrā vyādhitāś ca ye
nāvamanyed dvijān prājño mama rūpaṃ hitaṃ tathā
bahavo 'pi na jānante narā jñānabahiṣkṛtāḥ
yathāhaṃ dvijarūpeṇa carāmi pṛthivītale
ye kecit sāgarāntāyāṃ pṛthivyāṃ kīrtitā dvijāḥ
apreṣaṇe preṣayanto dāsatvaṃ kārayanti hi
mṛtāṃs tān karapattrena yamadūtā mahābalāḥ
nikṛntanti yathā kāṣṭhaṃ sūtramārgeṇa śilpinaḥ
ye caivāślakṣṇayā vācā tarjayanti narādhamāḥ
mṛtāṃs tān yamalokeṣu nihatya dharaṇītale
agnivarṇaiś ca saṃdaṃśair jihvām uddharate yamaḥ
pāpāś ca nārake vahnau dhāsyante yamakiṃkaraiḥ
ye tu viprān nirīkṣanti pāpāḥ pāpena cakṣuṣā
abrahmaṇyāḥ śruter bāhyā nityaṃ brahmadviṣo narāḥ
teṣāṃ ghorā mahākāyā vajratuṇḍā bhayānakāḥ
uddharanti muhūrtena cakṣuḥ kākā yamājñayā
yas tāḍayati viprāṃs tu kṣataṃ kuryāt saśoṇitam
asthibhaṅgaṃ ca yaḥ kuryāt prāṇair vāpi viyojayet
kīlair vinihataḥ pāpo mīrāyāṃ pacyate bhṛśam
subahūni sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ kleśabhāg bhavet
ravān muñcati durbuddhir na tasmai niṣkṛtiḥ smṛtā
tasmād viprā naraśreṣṭha namaskāryāś ca nityaśaḥ
annapānapradānais tu pūjārhāḥ satataṃ dvijāḥ
āmantrayitvā yo viprān gandhair mālyaiś ca mānavaḥ
sa māṃ prasādayec caiva sa ca māṃ paritoṣayet
tapodamānviteṣv eva nityaṃ pūjāṃ prayojayet
ye brāhmaṇāḥ so 'ham asaṃśayaṃ nṛpa teṣv arciteṣv arcito 'haṃ yathāvat
yaḥ pūjayed bhojayitvā dvijāgryān
saṃpūjayitvā paritoṣayec ca
tenaiva mām eva sadā pūjayanti na saṃśayaḥ
virūpāś ca surūpāś ca vijanān niṣkalān api
kṛpayā bhāvitātmāno ye 'rcayanti dvijottamān
anasūyā hitātmāno viprān ārādhate kvacit
asaṃśayaṃ sadā bhaktyā mām evārcayate hi saḥ
yaś candanaiḥ sāgarugandhamālyair abhyarcayed dārumayīṃ mamārcām
vipraprasādān madha eva cāhaṃ vipraprasādād asurāñ jayāmi
sāyaṃ prātaś ca yaḥ saṃdhyām upāste 'skannamānasaḥ
japan hi pāvanīṃ devīṃ gāyatrīṃ vedamātaram
sa tayā pāvito devyā brāhmaṇaḥ pūtakilbiṣaḥ
na sīdet pratigṛhṇānaḥ pṛthivīṃ tu sasāgarām
ye cānye dāruṇāḥ kecid grahāḥ sūryādayo divi
te cāsya saumyā jāyante śivāḥ śivatamāh sadā
yatratatragataṃ cainaṃ dāruṇāḥ piśitāśanāḥ
ghorarūpā mahākāyā na karṣanti dvijottamam
yāvantaś ca pṛthivyāṃ hi cīrṇavedavratā dvijāḥ
acīrṇavratavedā vā vikarmapatham āśritāḥ
teṣāṃ tu pāvanārthaṃ hi nityam eva yudhiṣṭhira
nāsti kiṃcin naravyāghra duṣkṛtaṃ brāhmaṇasya tu
pūrṇāhutiṃ vā prāpnoti juhute ca trayo 'ghnayaḥ
dahanti duṣkṛtaṃ tasya agnayo nātra saṃśayaḥ
purāṇaṃ mānavā dharmāḥ sāṅgo vedaś cikitsitam
ājñāsiddhāni catvāri na hantavyāni hetubhiḥ
hatvā hy etāni saṃmūḍhaḥ kalpaṃ tamasi pacyate
na brāhmaṇaṃ parīkṣeta śrāddhakāle hy upasthite
sumahān parivādo hi brāhmaṇānāṃ parīkṣaṇe
kāṇāḥ kuṇṭhāś ca ṣaṇḍāś ca daridrā vyādhitās tathā
sarve śrāddhe niyoktavyā miśritā vedapāragaiḥ
brāhmaṇo hi mahad bhūtaṃ janmanā saha jāyate
lokā lokeśvarāś cāpi sarve brāhmaṇapūjakāḥ
brāhmaṇāḥ kupitā hanyur bhasma kuryuś ca tejasā
lokān anyān sṛjeyuś ca lokapālāṃs tathāparān
brāhmaṇā hi mahātmāno virajāḥ svargasaṃkramāḥ
brāhmaṇānāṃ parīvādād asurāḥ salileśayāḥ
apeyaḥ sāgaro yais tu kṛtaḥ kopān mahātmabhiḥ
yeṣāṃ kopāgnir adyāpi daṇḍake nopaśāmyati
ete svargasya netāro bhūmidevāḥ sanātanāḥ
ebhiś cādhikṛtaḥ panthā devayānaḥ sa ucyate
te pūjyās te namaskāryās teṣu sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam
pramāṇaṃ sarvalokānāṃ niyatā brahmacāriṇaḥ
tān apāśritya tiṣṭhante trayo lokāḥ sanātanāḥ
gūḍhasvādhyāyatapaso brāhmaṇāḥ saṃśitavratāḥ
vidyāsnātā vratasnātā anapāśrityajīvinaḥ
āśīviṣā iva kruddhā upacaryā hi brāhmaṇāḥ
tapasā dīpyamānās te daheyuḥ sāgarān api
brāhmaṇeṣu ca tuṣṭeṣu tuṣyante sarvadevatāḥ
brāhmaṇānāṃ namaskāraiḥ sūryo divi virājate
brāhmaṇānāṃ parīvādāt pateyur api devatāḥ
dhuri ye nāvasīdanti praṇīte yajñavahnayaḥ
te gatiḥ sarvabhūtānām adhyātmagaticintakāḥ
ādimadhyāvasānānāṃ jñānānāṃ chinnasāmśayāḥ
parāparaviśeṣajñā netāraḥ paramāṃ gatim
avadhyā brāhmaṇās tasmāt pāpeṣv api ratāḥ sadā
yaś ca sarvam idaṃ hanyād brāhmaṇaṃ vāpi tatsamam
so 'gniḥ so 'rko mahātejā viṣaṃ bhavati kopitaḥ
bhūtānāṃ agrabhug vipro varṇaśreṣṭhaḥ pitā guruḥ
praṇītaś cāpraṇītaś ca yathāgnir daivataṃ mahat
evaṃ vidvān avidvān vā brāhmaṇo daivataṃ mahat
śmaśāneṣv api tejasvī pāvako naiva duṣyati
sarvathā brāhmaṇāḥ pūjyāḥ sarvathā daivataṃ mahat
śakro 'pi hi dvijendrāṇāṃ bibheti vibudhādhipaḥ
dānaṃ devāḥ praśaṃsanti iti dharmavido viduḥ
nānādānavidhiṃ tasmāc śṛṇuṣva susamāhitaḥ
hiraṇyadānaṃ godānaṃ pṛthivīdānam eva ca
yad yad iṣṭatamaṃ loke yac cāsti dayitaṃ gṛhe
suvarṇadānaṃ godānaṃ pṛthivīdānam eva ca
yad dadāsi viśiṣṭebhyo yac cāśnāsi dine dine
tat te vittam ahaṃ manye śeṣaṃ kasyāpi rakṣasi
tulyanāmāni śastāni trīṇi tulyaphalāni ca
nityaṃ deyāni rājendra gāvaḥ pṛthvī sarasvatī
deyāni yācamānebhyaḥ pānam annaṃ tathaiva ca
evaṃ dānaṃ samuddiṣṭaṃ vyuṣṭimat tārakaṃ param
eṣa te vihito yajñaḥ śraddhāpūtaḥ sadakṣiṇaḥ
viśiṣṭaḥ sa ca yajñeṣu dadatām anasūyayā
dānavidbhiḥ kṛtaḥ panthā yena yānti manīṣiṇaḥ
evaṃ dattvā brāhmaṇebhyo dātā phalam upāśnute
brāhmaṇāś caiva vidyante satyavanto bahuśrutāḥ
dattaṃ vā dāpitaṃ vāpi votsāhyam api vā kṛtam
utthāyotthāya dātavyaṃ brāhmaṇebhyo yudhiṣṭhira
āgamiṣyati yat pātraṃ tat pātraṃ tārayiṣyati
asaṃkīrṇaṃ ca yat pātraṃ tat pātraṃ tārayiṣyati
adhyāyaṃ tapaso vakṣye tan me nigadataḥ śṛṇu
tapasā prāpyate svargaṃ tapasā prāpyate yaśaḥ
āyuḥprakarṣaṃ bhogāṃś ca tapasā vindate naraḥ
jñānaṃ vijñānam āstikyaṃ saubhāgyaṃ rūpam uttamam
yat kāryaṃ kiṃcid āsthāya puruṣas tapyate tapaḥ
surāpaḥ pāradārī ca bhrūṇahā gurutalpagaḥ
api sarveśvaraḥ sthāṇur viṣṇuś caiva sanātanaḥ
brahmā hutāśanaḥ śakras tapasyanti sanātanāḥ
ṣaḍaśītisahasrāṇi munīnām ūrdhvaretasām
tapasā prāpyate rājyaṃ śakraḥ sarvasureśvaraḥ
tapasaiva prakāśete nakṣatrāṇi grahās tathā
viśvāmitraś ca tapasā brāhmaṇatvam upāgataḥ
ṛcam ekāṃ api paṭhan sa yāti paramāṃ gatim
tapo yaśaś ca puṇyaṃ ca pitṛdevarṣipūjanam
satyaṃ yajñas tathā vedā mantrā devī sarasvatī
satyena cāpaḥ kṣipati parjanyaḥ pṛthivītale
pāraṇaṃ sarvavedānāṃ sarvatīrthāvagahanah
satyaṃ ca vadato loke tat samaṃ syān na saṃśayaḥ
munayaḥ satyaprapathāḥ parāṃ siddhim ito gatāḥ
satyena devāḥ prīyante pitaro brāhmaṇās tathā
munayaḥ satyaniratās tasmāt satyaṃ viśiṣyate
apsarogaṇasaṃkīrṇair vimānair upayānti te
etat pramāṇaṃ yaḥ kuryāt sarvayajñaphalaṃ labhet
snātavyaṃ manasā yuktaiḥ snānaṃ tat paramaṃ smṛtam
ātmārthe ca parārthe vā putrārthe vāpi pārthiva
ye 'nṛtaṃ nābhibhāṣante te narāḥ svargagāminaḥ
yaḥ satyavādī puruṣo nānṛtaṃ paribhāṣate
saṃprāpya virajāṃl lokān uṣitvā śāśvatīḥ samāḥ
śucīnāṃ śrīmatāṃ gehe jāyate sumahāmatiḥ
ādityacandrāv analānilau ca dyaur bhūmir āpo hṛdayaṃ yamaś ca
satyaṃ vadaṃs tejasā dīpyamāno na hīyate dharmayaśo 'rthakāmaiḥ
eṣa vāṇīkṛto dharmo vaidiko dharmaniścaye
sarveṣām eva varṇānāṃ pravakṣyāmi yudhiṣṭhira
avāpnoti yathā kāmān upavāsaparāyaṇaḥ
upavāsā manuṣyāṇāṃ mayy evārpitacetasām
pañcamīṃ caiva ṣaṣṭhīṃ ca paurṇamāsīṃ ca pāṇḍava
upoṣya rūpavān dhanyaḥ subhagaś caiva jāyate
aṣṭamīṃ caiva kaunteya śuklapakṣe caturdaśīm
upoṣya vyādhirahito vīryavāṃś caiva jāyate
mārgaśīrṣaṃ tu yo māsaṃ nityam ekāśano bhavet
kṛṣibhāgī bhaved rājan bahuputraś ca jāyate
subhago darśanīyaś ca jñānabhāgī ca jāyate
strīṣu vallabhatāṃ yāti vaśyāś cāsya bhavanti tāḥ
strīṣu vallabhatāṃ yāti vaśyāś cāsya bhavanti tāḥ
naro vā yadi vā nārī jñātīnāṃ śreṣṭhatāṃ vrajet
jyeṣṭhamāsam apānīyam ekabhaktena yaḥ kṣapet
aiśvaryaṃ puruṣavyāghra strībhāgī copajāyate
āṣāḍhaṃ bharataśreṣṭha ekabhaktena yaḥ kṣapet
śūraś ca bahudhānyaś ca bahuputraś ca jāyate
śrāvaṇaṃ tu naravyāghra bhaktenaikena yaḥ kṣapet
māsaṃ bhādrapadaṃ rājann ekabhaktena yaḥ kṣapet
dhanāḍhyo vīryavāṃś caiva aiśvaryaṃ pratipadyate
yaḥ kṣaped ekabhaktena māsam āśvayujaṃ naraḥ
dhanavān vāhanāḍhyaś ca bahuputraś ca jāyate
kārttikaṃ tu naro māsaṃ nityam ekāśano bhavet
śūraś ca bahubhāryaś ca kīrtimāṃś caiva jāyate
ete māsā naraśreṣṭha ekabhaktena kīrtitāḥ
tithīnāṃ niyamāṃś caiva tāñ śṛṇuṣva narādhipa
pakṣe pakṣe caturthaṃ tu bhaktaṃ yaḥ kṣapayen naraḥ
kṛṣibhāgī yaśobhāgī tejasvī cāpi jāyate
pakṣe pakṣe trirātraṃ tu yaḥ kṣapen narapuṅgava
gaṇe ghoṣe pure grāme māhātmyaṃ pratipadyate
gaṇādhipatyaṃ labhate niḥsapatnam akaṇṭakam
yas tu sāyaṃ tathā kalyaṃ bhuṅkte naivāntarā pibet
ṣaḍbhir eva tu varṣais tu sidhyate nātra saṃśayaḥ
agniṣṭomasya yajñasya phalaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ
gavāmayasya yajñasya phalaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ
pūrṇaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu svargaloke mahīyate
ārto vā vyādhito vāpi gacched anaśanaṃ tu yaḥ
ārūḍhastrīśatākīrṇe viharan sukham edhate
gacched anaśanaṃ yas tu tasyāpi śṛṇu yat phalam
śataṃ varṣasahasrāṇāṃ svargaloke mahīyate
yāvanti romakūpāni tasya gātreṣu bhārata
nāsti vedāt paraṃ śāstraṃ nāsti mātṛsamo guruḥ
brāhmaṇebhyaḥ paraṃ nāsti divi ceha ca pāvanam
divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu viśvāmitreṇa dhīmatā
sarve hy ete divaṃ prāptāḥ kṣamāvanto bahuśrutāḥ
brāhmaṇatvaṃ suduṣprāpaṃ nisargād brāhmaṇo bhavet
kṣatriyo vāthavā vaiśyo nisargād eva jāyate
duṣkṛtena tu duṣṭātmā sthānād bhraśyati mānavaḥ
śreṣṭhaṃ sthānaṃ samāsādya tasmād rakṣeta paṇḍitaḥ
brāhmaṇyāt sa paribhraṣṭaḥ kṣatrayonyāṃ prasūyate
śūdrakarmāṇi kurvāṇaḥ śūdratvam upapadyate
sa tatra durgatiṃ prāpya sthānād bhraṣṭo yudhiṣṭhira
tasmāt prāpya śubhaṃ sthānaṃ pramādān na tu nāśayet
śūdrānnenāvaśeṣeṇa yo mriyej jaṭhare dvijaḥ
āhitāgnis tathā yajvā sa śūdragatibhāg bhavet
kṣatrānnenāvaśeṣeṇa kṣatratvam upapadyate
vaiśyānnenāvaśeṣeṇa vaiśyatvam upapadyate
tāṃ yoniṃ labhate vipro bhuktvānnaṃ yasya vai mṛtaḥ
brāhmaṇatvaṃ śubhaṃ prāpya durlabhaṃ yo 'vamanyate
karmaṇā yena medhāvī śūdro vaiśyo 'bhijāyate
śūdrakarma yathoddiṣṭaṃ śūdro bhūtvā samācaret
yathāvat paricaryāṃ tu triṣu varṇeṣu nityadā
kurute 'vimanā yas tu sa śūdro vaiśyatāṃ vrajet
kṣatriyatvaṃ yathā vaiśyas tad vakṣyāmy anupūrvaśaḥ
caukṣaḥ pāpajanadveṣṭā śeṣānnakṛtabhojanaḥ
sa vaiśyaḥ kṣatriyakule jāyate nātra saṃśayaḥ
kṣatriyo brahmayonyāṃ tu jāyate śṛṇu tad yathā
adhīte svargam anvicchaṃs tretāgniśaraṇaḥ sadā
ṛtukāle tu svāṃ bhāryām abhigacchan vidhānataḥ
śūdrāṇāṃ yācakānāṃ ca nityaṃ siddhim iti bruvan
gobrāhmaṇasya cārthāya raṇe cābhimukho hataḥ
tretāgnimantrapūtātmā kṣatriyo brāhmaṇo bhavet
vidhijñaḥ kṣatriyakule yājakaḥ sa tu jāyate
brāhmaṇatvaṃ suduṣprāpaṃ kṛcchreṇāsādyate naraiḥ
suvarṇaṃ paramaṃ dānaṃ suvarṇaṃ dakṣiṇā parā
daśa pūrvāparān vaṃśān ātmānaṃ ca viśāmyate
api pāpaśataṃ kṛtvā dattvā vipreṣu tārayet
agnir hi devatāḥ sarvāḥ suvarṇaṃ ca hutāśanaḥ
tasmāt suvarṇaṃ dadatā dattāḥ sarvāś ca devatāḥ
sarvavedapramāṇajñā vedaśrutinidarśanāt
suvarṇadaḥ svargaloke kāmān iṣṭān upāśnute
virajāmbarasaṃvītaḥ pariyāti yatas tataḥ
vimānenārkavarṇena bhāsvareṇa virājatā
apsarogaṇasaṃkīrṇe bhāsvatā svena tejasā
tasmāt svaśaktyā dātavyaṃ kāñcanaṃ mānavair bhuvi
lokāṃs tu sṛjatā pūrvaṃ gāvaḥ sṛṣṭāḥ svayaṃbhuvā
prītyarthaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ tasmāt tā mātaraḥ smṛtāḥ
tasmāt tā varṇayiṣyāmi dānaṃ cāsāṃ yathāvidhi
yādṛśī vidhinā yena dātavyā yādṛśāya ca
dvijāya poṣaṇārthaṃ tu homadhenukṛte na vai
prathamā gaurakapilā dvitīyā gaurapiṅgalā
tṛtīyā raktakapilā caturthī nīlapiṅgalā
pañcamī śuklapiṅgākṣī ṣaṣṭhī tu śuklapiṅgalā
saptamī citrapiṅgākṣī aṣṭamī babhrurohiṇī
navamī śvetapiṅgākṣī daśamī śvetapiṅgalā
tādṛśā ye 'py anaḍvāhaḥ kapilās te prakīrtitāḥ
brāhmaṇo vāhayet tāṃs tu nānyo varṇaḥ kadācana
dhenuṃ dattvā suvratāṃ sopadhānāṃ kalyāṇavatsāṃ ca payasvinīṃ ca
yāvanti romāṇi bhavanti dhenvā duhyeta kāmān nṛpa varṣāṇi tāvat
prayacchate yaḥ kapilāṃ savatsāṃ kāṃsyopadohāṃ kanakāgraśṛṅgīm
tais tair guṇaiḥ kāmdughā hi bhūtvā naraṃ pradātāram upaiti sā gauḥ
parāṃ vṛddhiṃ śriyaṃ prāpya svargaloke mahīyate
daśa cobhayataḥ pretya mātāmahapitāmahaiḥ
gacchet sukṛtināṃ lokān gāvo dattvā yathāvidhi
tasyāpi cākṣayā lokā bhavantīha paratra ca
yo dyūtena dhanaṃ jitvā krītvā gāvaḥ prayacchati
pratigṛhya tu yo dadyād gāvaḥ śuddhena cetasā
yaś cātmavikrayaṃ kṛtvā gāvo dadyād yathāvidhi
saṃgrāme yas tanuṃ tyaktvā gāvaḥ krītvā prayacchati
dehavikrayamūlyas tāḥ śāśvatāḥ kāmadohanāḥ
rūpānvitāḥ śīlavayopapannāḥ sarvāḥ praśastā hi sugandhavatyaḥ
yathā hi gaṅgā saritāṃ variṣṭhā tathārjunīnāṃ kapilā variṣṭhā
antarjātāḥ sukrayajñānalabdhāḥ prāṇāṃs tyaktvā sodakāḥ sodvahāś ca
kṛcchrotsṛṣṭāḥ poṣaṇāyābhyupetā dvārair etair goviśeṣā variṣṭhāḥ
tisro rātryaś cāpy upoṣyeha dātā tṛptā gā vai tarpitebhyaḥ prayacchet
loke jyeṣṭhā lokavṛttāntavṛttā vedair gītāḥ somaniṣyandabhūtāḥ
saumyāḥ puṇyāḥ kāmadāḥ prāṇadāś ca gāvo dattvā sarvadā santi santaḥ
na caivāsāṃ dānamātraṃ praśastaṃ pātraṃ kālo goviśeṣo vidhiś ca
dṛṣṭvā gāvaḥ pāvakādityabhūtāḥ svādhyāyāḍhye pātravarye viśiṣṭe
vaitānasthaṃ satyavākyaṃ kṛtajñaṃ goṣu kṣāntaṃ gośaraṇyaṃ suvṛttaṃ
śastaṃ pātraṃ gopradānasya bhūmes tathā suvarṇasya ca sarvakālam
bhikṣādānaṃ cādhikaṃ saṃpraśastaṃ pāthodānaṃ cānnadānaṃ tathā ca
bhikṣate bahubhṛtyāya śrotriyāyāhitāgnaye
dātavyā gauḥ prayatnena ekāpy atiphalā hi sā
tāṃ ced vikrīṇate rājan vacasā kaluṣīkṛtām
jīrṇāṃ caivopabhuktāṃ ca jaratkūpam ivāphalām
tamaḥ praviśate dātā dvijaṃ kleśena yojayan
duṣṭāḥ kṛśāś caiva pālayatīś ca naitādṛśā dānayogyā bhavanti
anaḍvāhaṃ suvrataṃ yo dadāti halasya voḍhāram anantavīryam
prayacchate yaḥ puruṣo dvijāya svādhyāyacāritraguṇānvitāya
balena yuktaṃ vṛṣabhaṃ tu nīlaṃ ṣaḍāṅgavaṃ prītikaraṃ surūpam
yuvānaṃ balinaṃ śyāmaṃ śatena saha yūthapam
gavendraṃ brāhmaṇendrāya bhūriśṛṅgam alaṃkṛtam
vṛṣabhaṃ ye prayacchanti śrotriyāyāhitāgnaye
aiśvarye te 'bhijāyante jāyamānāḥ punaḥ punaḥ
sadakṣiṇāṃ kāñcanarūpyaśṛṅgīṃ kāṃsyopadohāṃ kanakottarīyām
dhenuṃ tilānāṃ kanakottarīyām lokā vasūnām acalā bhavanti
tilālābhe tu yo dadyād ghṛtadhenuṃ yatavrataḥ
ghṛtālābhe tu yo dadyāj jaladhenuṃ yatavrataḥ
brāhmaṇāś caiva gāvaś ca kulam ekaṃ dvidhākṛtam
yāvanti tāsāṃ romāṇi tāvat svarge mahīyate
śṛṇu tvaṃ me gavāṃ lokā yādṛśā yatra vā sthitāḥ
manojñā ramaṇīyāś ca sarvakāmadughāḥ sadā
puṇyāḥ pāpaharāś caiva gavāṃ lokā na saṃśayaḥ
pramodante mahāsthāne narā vigatakalmaṣāḥ
evaṃ yair dattasatkārāḥ surabhyaś cārcitāḥ sadā
kāmarūpā mahātmānaḥ pūtā vigatakilbiṣāḥ
gandharvair upagīyante gośaraṇyā na saṃśayaḥ
brahmaṇyāḥ sādhuvṛttāś ca dayāvanto 'nukampinaḥ
ghṛṇinaḥ śubhakarmāṇo modante te 'maraiḥ saha
gobhiḥ pāpakṛtaṃ karma dṛḍham eva mayohyate
mātaraḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ prajāsaṃrakṣaṇe smṛtāḥ
brahmaṇā lokasāreṇa gāvaḥ pāpabhayāpahāḥ
kṛśāya tu viśeṣeṇa vṛttiglānāya sīdate
bhūdānena samaṃ dānaṃ na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati
iti dharmavidaḥ prāhus tan me nigadataḥ śṛṇu
ṣaṣṭiṃ varṣasahasrāṇi svarge vasati bhūmidaḥ
atidānaṃ tu sarveṣāṃ bhūmidānam ihocyate
acalā hy akṣayā bhūmiḥ sarvān kāmān prayacchati
bhūmidaḥ svargam āruhya śāśvatīr edhati samāḥ
yathā bhūmiḥ sadā devī dātāraṃ kurute patim
evaṃ sadakṣiṇā dattā kurute gaur janādhipam
api pāpakṛtaṃ prāpya pratigṛhṇīta bhūmidam
mahīṃ dadan pavitrī syāt puṇyā hi jagatī yataḥ
tad asyāḥ satataṃ prītyai kīrtanīyaṃ prayacchatā
yat kiṃcit kurute pāpaṃ puruṣo vṛttikarṣitaḥ
suvarṇaṃ rajataṃ tāmraṃ maṇimuktāvasūni ca
sarvān etān mahāprājña dadāti vasudhāṃ dadan
tapo yajñāḥ śrutaṃ śīlam alobhaḥ satyavāditā
bhartur niḥśreyase yuktās tyaktātmāno raṇe hatāḥ
phalakṛṣṭāṃ mahīṃ dattvā sodakāṃ saphalānvitām
sodakaṃ vāpi śaraṇaṃ prāpnoti mama saṃpadam
ratnopakīṛṇāṃ vasudhāṃ yo dadāti dvijātaye
ikṣubhiḥ saṃtatāṃ bhūmiṃ yavagodhūmaśāḍbalām
na bhūyo bhūmidānād dhi dānam anyad viśiṣyate
puṇyāṃ sarvarasāṃ bhūmiṃ yo dadāti nararṣabha
na tasya lokāḥ kṣīyante bhūmidasya mahātmanaḥ
yathā janitrī puṣṇāti kṣīreṇa svasutaṃ nṛpa
evaṃ sarvaguṇā bhūmir dātāram anupuṣyati
agniṣṭomādibhir yajñair iṣṭvā vipuladakṣiṇaiḥ
na tat phalaṃ avāpnoti yad dattvā vasudhāṃ nṛpa
mṛtyor hi kiṃkarā daṇḍā hy agnitāpāḥ sudāruṇāḥ
ghorāś ca vāruṇāḥ pāśā nopasarpanti bhūmidam
saṃtarpayanti dātāraṃ bhūmeḥ prabhavatāṃ vara
kṛśāya kṛśabhṛtyāya vṛttikṣīṇāya sīdate
bhūmiṃ vṛttikārīṃ dattvā sattrī bhavati mānavaḥ
siṃhāsanaṃ tathā cchattraṃ varāśvā varavāraṇāḥ
bhūmidānasya puṣpāṇi phalaṃ svargaṃ tathaiva ca
ādityā iva dīpyante tejasā divi mānavāḥ
ye prayacchanti vasudhāṃ brāhmaṇāyāhitāgnaye
yathā bījāni rohanti prakīrṇāni mahītale
tathā kāmādhirohanti bhūmidānaguṇārjitāḥ
āsphoṭayanti pitaraḥ pravalganti pitāmahāḥ
bhūmido naḥ kule jātaḥ sa naḥ saṃtārayiṣyati
śūlapāṇiś ca bhagavān abhinandanti bhūmidam
sa dātā sa ca vikrānto yo dadāti vasuṃdharām
dātāram anugṛhṇāti yathā dattena rocate
pūrvadattāṃ haran bhūmiṃ narakāyopapadyate
vindhyāṭavīṣv atoyāsu śuṣkakoṭaravāsinaḥ
kṛṣṇasarpā hi jāyante ye haranti vasuṃdharām
patanty aśrūṇi rudatāṃ dīnānām avasīdatām
brāhmaṇānāṃ hṛtaṃ kṣetraṃ hanyāt tripuruṣaṃ kulam
pūrvadattāṃ dvijātibhyo yatnād rakṣa yudhiṣṭhira
mahīṃ mahībhṛtāṃ śreṣṭha dānāc chreyo 'nupālanam
yatraiṣaḥ paṭhyate śrāddhe bhūmidānasya saṃstavaḥ
na tatra rakṣasāṃ bhāgo nāsurāṇāṃ kathaṃcana
akṣayaṃ tu bhavec chrāddhaṃ pitRṇāṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ
tasmād viśrāvayed enaṃ śrāddheṣu brāhmaṇān sadā
evam etad yathoddiṣṭaṃ pitRṇāṃ dattam akṣayam
bhūmidānaṃ mahārāja sarvapāpāpahaṃ śubham
agniṣṭomādibhir yajñair iṣṭvā vipuladakṣiṇaiḥ
iti yajñavidaḥ prāhur yajñakarmaviśāradāḥ
tasmāt tat te pravakṣyāmi yat phalaṃ śastrajīvinām
yaḥ śūro vadhyate yuddhe vimṛdan paravāhinīm
tasya dharmārthakāmāś ca yajñāś caivāptadakṣiṇāḥ
viṣṇukrāntaṃ sa yajata evaṃ yudhyan raṇājire
yas tu śastram anutsṛjya vīryavān vāhinīmukhe
rājānaṃ rājaputraṃ vā senāpatim athāpi vā
hanyāt kṣatreṇa yaḥ śūras tasya loko 'kṣayo dhruvaḥ
vīrāsanaṃ vīraśayyā vīrasthānasthitiḥ sthirā
gavārthe brāhmaṇārthe vā svāmyarthe tu kṛtaṃ ca yaiḥ
ūrdhvaṃ tiryak ca yaś cārvāk prāṇān saṃtyajate yudhi
yasya cihnīkṛtaṃ gātraṃ śaraśaktyṛṣṭitomaraiḥ
varāpsaraḥsahasrāṇi śūram āyodhane hatam
bhūyo gatiṃ pravakṣyāmi raṇe ye 'bhimukhā hatāḥ
śakyaṃ tv iha samṛddhais tu yaṣṭuṃ kratuśatair naraiḥ
yāṃ yajñasaṃghais tapasā ca viprāḥ svargaiṣiṇas tatra cayaiḥ prayānti
kṣaṇena tām eva gatiṃ prayānti mahāhave svāṃ tanuṃ saṃtyajantaḥ
sarvāṃś ca vedān saha ṣaḍbhir aṅgaiḥ sāṃkhyaṃ ca yogaṃ ca vane ca vāsam
etān guṇān eka evātiśete saṃgrāmadhāmny ātmatanuṃ tyajed yaḥ
imāṃ giraṃ citrapadāṃ śubhākṣarāṃ subhāṣitāṃ vṛtabhidāṃ divaukasām
eṣa puṇyatamaḥ svargyaḥ suyajñaḥ sarvatomukhaḥ
sarveṣām eva varṇānāṃ kṣatriyasya viśeṣataḥ
bhūyaś caiva pravakṣyāmi bhīṣmavākyam anuttamam
yādṛśāya prahartavyaṃ yādṛśaṃ parivarjayet
ātatāyinam āyāntam api vedāntagaṃ raṇe
jighāṃsantaṃ jighāṃsīyān na tena brahmahā bhavet
hatāśvaś ca na hantavyaḥ pānīyaṃ yaś ca yācate
bhagnadhanvācchinaguṇaḥ prāṇepsuḥ kṛpaṇaṃ bruvan
parṇaśākhātṛṇagrāhī tavāsmīti ca yo vadet
brāhmaṇo 'smīti yaś cāha bālo vṛddho napuṃsakaḥ
tasmād etān parihared yathoddiṣṭān raṇājire
amāṃsabhakṣaṇe rājan yo dharmaḥ kurupuṅgava
tan me śṛṇu yathātathyaṃ yaś cāsya vidhir uttamaḥ
māsi māsy aśvamedhena yo yajeta śataṃ samāḥ
na ca khādati yo māṃsaṃ samam etad yudhiṣṭhira
yo māṃsarasam āsvādya sarvamāṃsāni varjayet
caturvratam idaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ prāṇināṃ mṛtyubhīruṇām
tadā bhavati loke 'smin prāṇināṃ jīvitaiṣiṇām
viśvāsyaś copagamyaś ca na hi hiṃsārudir yadā
duṣṭarāṃs tarate maāṃ māṃsasya parivarjanāt
prāṇā yathātmano 'bhīṣṭā bhūtānām api te tathā
ahiṃsā paramo dharmaḥ satyam eva ca pāṇḍava
ahiṃsā caiva satyaṃ ca dharmo hi paramaḥ smṛtaḥ
na hi māṃsaṃ tṛṇāt kāṣṭhād upalād vāpi jāyate
jīvād utpadyate māṃsaṃ tasmād garhanti tad budhāḥ
lobhād vā buddhimohād vā yo māṃsāny atti mānavaḥ
bhakṣayitvā tu yo māṃsaṃ paścād api nivartate
idam anyat pravakṣyāmi purāṇam ṛṣinirmitam
yo dadyāt kāñcanaṃ meruṃ kṛtsnāṃ vāpi vasuṃdharām
abhakṣaṇaṃ ca māṃsasya na tu tulyaṃ yudhiṣṭhira
śrūyate ca purākalpe hy ṛṣīṇāṃ vrīhayaḥ paśuḥ
yajante yena vai yajñān ṛṣayaḥ puṇyakarmiṇaḥ
ṛṣibhiḥ saṃśayaṃ pṛṣṭo vasū rājā tataḥ purā
abhakṣyaṃ bhakṣyam iti vai māṃsam āha narādhipa
ākāśān medinīṃ prāptas tataḥ sa pṛthivīpatiḥ
kaumudaṃ tu viśeṣeṇa śuklapakṣe narādhipa
caturo vārṣikān māsān yo māṃsaṃ parivarjayet
catvāri bhadrāṇy āpnoti kīrtir āyur yaśo balam
atītya sarvaduḥkhāni sukhaṃ jīven nirāmayaḥ
yo hi varṣaśataṃ pūrṇaṃ tapas tapyet sudāruṇam
apy ekaṃ varjayen māsaṃ māṃsam etat samaṃ matam
yo varjayati māṃsāni māsaṃ pakṣam athāpi vā
sarvakālaṃ tu māṃsāni varjitāni maharṣibhiḥ
manvā kṣupeṇa śvetena tathaivekṣvākunāpi ca
bhṛguṇā nalarāmābhyāṃ dilīparaghupauravaiḥ
āyuṣā caiva gārgyeṇa janakaiś cakravartibhiḥ
dhundhumārāmbarīṣābhyāṃ nahuṣeṇa ca dhīmatā
gādhinā purukutsena kuruṇā puruṇā tathā
mucukundena māndhātrā sagareṇa mahātmanā
śibinā cāśvapatinā vīrasenādibhis tathā
saṃjayenātha bhīṣmeṇa puṣkareṇātha pāṇḍunā
suvarṇaṣṭhīvinā caiva duṣvantanṛgarohitaiḥ
etaiś cānyaiś ca bahubhiḥ sarvair māṃsaṃ na bhakṣitam
śaratkaumudikaṃ māsaṃ tataḥ svargaṃ gatā nṛpāḥ
brahmaloke ca pūjyante jvalamānāḥ śriyāvṛtāḥ
upāsyamānā gāndharvaiḥ strīsahasrasamanvitāḥ
tad evam uttamaṃ dharmam ahiṃsālakṣaṇaṃ śubhan
ye rakṣanti mahātmāno nākapṛṣṭhe vasanti te
madhu māṃsaṃ ca ye nityaṃ varjayantīha mānavāḥ
pravṛttau ca nivṛttau ca pramāṇam ṛṣisattamaiḥ
gobrāhmaṇahitārthāya cāturvarṇyahitāya ca
aśiṣṭanigrahārthāya śiṣṭānāṃ rakṣaṇāya ca
yudhiṣṭhirasya rājarṣer evaṃ nārāyaṇo 'bravīt
pañca rūpāṇi rājāno dhārayanty amitaujasaḥ
tān na hiṃsen na cākrośen nākṣipen nāpriyaṃ vadet
devā mānuṣarūpeṇa caranti pṛthivīm imām
indrāt prabhutvaṃ jvalanāt pratāpaṃ krauryaṃ yamād vaiśravaṇāt prabhāvam
sattvasthitiṃ rāmajanārdanābhām ādāya rājñaḥ kriyate śarīram
mahatī devatā hy eṣā nararūpeṇa tiṣṭhati
svayam indro naro bhūtvā pṛthivīm anuśāsati
na hi pālayituṃ śakto manuṣyaḥ pṛthivīm imām
yat prajāpālanaiḥ puṇyaṃ prāpnuvantīha pārthivāḥ
ṣaṣṭhaṃ labhati bhāgaṃ tu prajā dharmeṇa pālayan
grāmādhipatyaṃ nagarādhipatyaṃ deśādhipatyaṃ pṛthivīpatitvam
na prāpnuvantīha manuṣyamātrā ye devatānāṃ na bhavanti bhāgāḥ
evaṃvṛttās tu rājāno devabhāgā na mānuṣāḥ
nābhīto yajate kāṃścan nābhīto daṇḍam icchati
ya eva devā hantāras tāṃl loko 'rcayate bhṛśam
hantā śakraś ca rudraś ca hantā vaiśravaṇo yamaḥ
varuṇo vāyur ādityaḥ parjanyo 'gnir bṛhaspatiḥ
etān devān namasyanti pratāpapraṇatā janāḥ
na brahmāṇaṃ na dhātāraṃ na pūṣāṇaṃ kathaṃcana
na hi paśyāmi jīvantaṃ rājan kaṃcid ahiṃsayā
na hatvā lipyate rājā prajā dharmeṇa pālayan
yadi daṇḍo na vidyeta durvinītās tatho narāḥ
hanyuḥ paśūn manuṣyāṃś ca yājñiyāni haviṃṣi ca
tasmāt prāṇihite daṇḍe hiṃsādoṣo na bādhate
naivostrā na balīvardā nāśvāśvataragardabhāḥ
yuktā vaheyur yānāni daṇḍaś cen nodyato bhavet
satyaṃ kilaitad yad uvāca śakro daṇḍaḥ prajā rakṣati sādhuvṛttaḥ
yasyāgnayaḥ pratimāsasya bhītāḥ saṃtarjitā daṇḍabhayāj jvalanti
yatra śyāmo lohitākṣo daṇḍaś carati pāpahā
daṇḍanītau sunītāyāṃ sarve sidhyanty upakramāḥ
daṇḍaś cen na pravarteta vinaśyeyur imāḥ prajāḥ
kākādyāś ca purodāśaṃ śvā caivāvalihed dhaviḥ
cāturvarṇyavimokṣāya durvinītabhayāya ca
daṇḍasya hi bhayād bhītā narās tiṣṭhanti śāsane
ti 'pi bhogāya kalpante daṇḍenoparipīḍitāḥ
gurur ātmavatāṃ śāstā śāstā rājā durātmanāṃ
ihapracchannapāpānāṃ śāstā vaivasvato yamaḥ
pāpānām atha mūḍhānāṃ paradravyāpahāriṇām
paradāraratā ye ca ye ca pātakasaṃjñitāḥ
teṣāṃ tu śāsanārthāya mayaitat samudāhṛtam
brāhmaṇyaṃ duṣkaraṃ jñātvā tasya daṇḍaṃ nipātayet
karmānurūpo daṇḍaḥ syād gohiraṇyādiko bhavet
avadhyo brāhmaṇo rājan strī vṛddho bāla eva ca
yaś cared aśubhaṃ karma pāpaṃ rājavigarhitam
śiraso muṇḍanaṃ kṛtvā gomayenānulepayet
kharayānena nagaraṃ ḍiṇḍimena tu bhrāmayet
rājanirdiṣṭadaṇḍasya prāyaścittaṃ na vidyate
eṣa te kathito daṇḍo brāhmaṇasya yudhiṣṭhira
kṣatriyasya tu yo daṇḍas taṃ vakṣyāmy anupūrvaśaḥ
tasya daṇḍaṃ pravakṣyāmi tan me nigadataḥ śṛṇu
sarvasvaharaṇaṃ kṛtvā pararāṣṭrāya preśayet
rājyaṃ kāṅkṣeta yo mūḍho rājapatnīm athāpi vā
śarais tu rājā vidhyeta śakticakragadādibhiḥ
kṣatriyasya tu duṣṭasya daṇḍa eṣa vidhīyate
vaiśyasyāpi ca yo daṇḍas taṃ pravakṣyāmi bhārata
pātakeṣv eva krūreṣu yas tu vaiśyaḥ pravartate
śūlāyāṃ bhedanaṃ tasya vṛkṣaśākhāvalambanam
etad vaiśyasya nirdiṣṭaṃ śūdrasyāpy anupūrvaśaḥ
śūle śūdrasya yo duṣṭas tasyaikasya vadhaḥ smṛtaḥ
kuñjareṇābhimardeta mīnīyām atha pācayet
etac chūdrasya nirdiṣṭaṃ nānyo daṇḍo vidhīyate
naikasyārthe kulaṃ hanyān na rāṣṭraṃ na ca grāmakam
ekaṃ suśiṣṭitaṃ kṛtvā śeṣaṃ kośaṃ praveśayet
dhanalobhān na moktavyo rāgād vā śāsanaṃ vinā
yudhiṣṭhirasya rājarṣer evaṃ nārāyaṇo 'bravīt
samāsena yathānyāyaṃ daṇḍanītim anuttamām
uttamādhamakāryeṣu sameṣu viṣameṣu ca
rājadharmāṃs tu paśyeta viṣṇunā samudāhṛtān
etān dharmāñ jagannāthaḥ pāṇḍuputrāya pṛcchate
yādṛk sattvaṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ tādṛg ārādhya keśavam
muktikāmā narā muktiṃ svargaṃ devatvam īpsavaḥ
gandharvayakṣasiddhānāṃ vṛṇvanty anye salokatām
varṣeṣv abhīpsavo viṣṇuṃ pātāleṣu tathāpare
bhogān abhīpsavo viṣṇuṃ toṣayaṇti narādhipa
dharmopadeśād acalāṃ vahan bhaktiṃ janārdane
saśarīro gataḥ svargaṃ dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
tathaiva janakaḥ kṛṣṇe viniveśya svamānasam
avāpa paramāṃ siddhiṃ vasuḥ prāyāt tripiṣṭapam
avāpur atulān kāmāṃs te te saṃtoṣya keśavam
anārādhya jagannāthaṃ sarvapāpaharaṃ harim
sadgatiḥ kena saṃprāptā bhogāś cāpi manoramāḥ
viṣṇoḥ kāryamanuṣyasya darśanād utthitaḥ punaḥ
samaṃ vināśam āyāti devaḥ ko 'bhyadhikas tataḥ
rāṣṭrasya śaraṇaṃ rājā pitarau bālakasya ca
dharmaḥ samastamartyānāṃ sarvasya śaraṇaṃ hariḥ
śrutaṃ mayā yathā pūrvam āryako me yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
saśarīro gataḥ svargaṃ jitam ātmīyakarmabhiḥ
yat tv etad bhagavān āha sa yathā pāṇdupūrvajaḥ
uvāca śvapaco dvāḥsthaṃ praśrayāvanatasthitaḥ
śuddhasphaṭikasopānaṃ maṇikāñcanatoraṇam
aṣṭāśītisahasrāṇi brāhmaṇānāṃ dine dine
yudhiṣṭhiram ṛte bhūpaṃ bhuñjate kasya veśmani
duḥkhārtaḥ kāryavān rājaṃś caṇḍālo dvāri tiṣṭhati
kenāpi hetumātreṇa bhavantaṃ duṣṭam āgataḥ
kiṃ rūpaṃ kīdṛśaṃ śīlaṃ ko 'syārthaḥ kiṃ prayojanam
brūhi dvāḥstha yathāvan me naras tiṣṭhati kīdṛśaḥ
kākakokilakṛṣṇāṅgo bhagnanāsāruṇekṣaṇaḥ
yavamadhyaḥ kṛśagrīvo vakrapādo mahāhanuḥ
brūhi gaccha durācāraṃ caṇḍālaṃ pāpakarmiṇam
caṇḍālapatitau dṛṣṭvā naraḥ paśyeta bhāskaram
pratyuvāca pratīhāram īṣan manyupariplutaḥ
kiṃ devakāryeṇa narādhipasya kṛtvā hi manyuṃ viṣayasthitānām
tad devakāryaṃ sa ca yajñahomo yad aśrupātā na patanti rāṣṭre
ity uktaḥ satvaraṃ gatvā dharmarājaṃ tathā tathaṃ
kathayām āsa tat sarvaṃ cāṇḍālena yad īritam
suśobhanam idaṃ vākyaṃ na bhaved antyajātiṣu
cintayitvā tato rājā nirjagāma yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
ity etad vacanaṃ śrutvā nirjagāma yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
pratyuvāca ca caṇḍālam īṣan kopasamanvitaḥ
āvādhākāraṇaṃ sarvaṃ yathāvat kathayasva me
tad ahaṃ te pratijñāya caṇḍakarmakarakṣaṇam
apāsya devakāryārthaṃ praviśyāmy antaraṃ punaḥ
na bhuñjate brāhmaṇā me sarvāś codvijate janaḥ
prāṇihiṃsā ca no vṛttir deva puṣṇāti me 'nṛtam
anekajanmasāhasrīṃ prāpya saṃsārapaddhatim
mānuṣye kutsitāṃ jātim āpanno muṣito 'smi bhoḥ
tāṃ saṃprāpya vṛthājanmā muṣṭo 'smi kurusattama
duḥkhe duḥkhādhikān paśyet sukhe paśyet sukhādhikān
ātmānaṃ śokaharṣābhyāṃ śatrubhyām iva nārpayet
so 'ham icchāmi vijñātum atiduṣkṛtakarmakṛt
vaktum arhasi dharmajña kaḥ pāpiṣṭhataro mayā
adhvānam upari śrāntaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ gṛham āgatam
anarcayitvā yo bhuṅkte sa pāpiṣṭhataras tvayā
godhanasya tṛṣārtasya jalārthaṃ paridhāvataḥ
vivāhayitvā yaḥ kanyāṃ kulajāṃ śīlamaṇḍanām
vinā tyajati doṣeṇa sa pāpiṣṭhataras tvayā
āśākāras tv adātā yo dātuś ca pratiṣedhakaḥ
dattaṃ ca yaḥ kīrtayati sa pāpiṣṭhataras tvayā
brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vāpi vaiśyaḥ śūdro 'pi vā naraḥ
kṛtārtho 'haṃ gamiṣyāmi yaśodharmam avāpnuhi
tuṣṭo 'smy ahaṃ svayā yonyā mattaḥ proktās tvayādhamāḥ
devatānām ṛṣīṇāṃ ca pitRṇāṃ ca kṛtaṃ mayā
sāṃprataṃ deśakālo 'yaṃ tvam evātra bhavātithiḥ
caṇḍālo 'haṃ mahārāja patito lokavarjitaḥ
caṇḍālo bhava pāpo vā śatrur vā pitṛghātakaḥ
deśakālābhyupetaṃ tvāṃ bharaṇīyaṃ hi vedmy aham
daśasūnāsamaṃ cakraṃ daśacakrasamo dhvajaḥ
daśadhvajasamā veśyā daśaveśyāsamo nṛpaḥ
daśa sūnāsahasrāṇi kurute yo hi saunikaḥ
nānāgotrādicaraṇā bhuñjate brāhmaṇā mama
na te vadanti vāgduṣṭaṃ yathaitat kīrtitaṃ tvayā
lobhātmāno na jānīyur brāhmaṇā rājakilbiṣam
rājakilbiṣadagdhānāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ yudhiṣṭhira
chinnānām iva bījānāṃ punarjanma na vidyate
narendrabhavane bhuṅktvā viṣṭhāyāṃ jāyate kṛmiḥ
nindase sarvarājāno na cātmānaṃ praśaṃsasi
athavā nindyarūpeṇa pitā nas tvam ihāgataḥ
dhairyavān ātmano 'nindyo nāśvāsārthaṃ ca pṛcchasi
anindyo nindyarūpeṇa mahātmā tvaṃ hi me mataḥ
bhavān upendraḥ śakro vā śarvo vā tvaṃ pinākadhṛk
jñāto 'smi pṛthivīpāla tuṣṭaś ca tava darśanāt
nandantu bhūmibhāgās te yeṣu tvaṃ pṛthivīpatiḥ
kiṃ me rājyena bhos tāta viṣayair jīvitena vā
yo 'haṃ sūnāsahasrais tu daśabhiḥ pariveṣṭitaḥ
mā viṣādaṃ naraśreṣṭha samupaihi yudhiṣṭhira
yajñeśvaraṃ yajñamūrtiṃ tvaṃ ca viṣṇuṃ samāśritaḥ
yeṣāṃ na viṣaye viprā yajñair yajñapatiṃ harim
yeṣāṃ pāṣaṇḍasaṃkīrṇaṃ na rāṣṭraṃ brāhmaṇotkaṭam
te tu sūnāsahasrāṇāṃ daśānāṃ bhāgino nṛpāḥ
yeṣāṃ na yajñapuruṣaḥ kāraṇaṃ puruṣottamaḥ
te tu pāpasamācārāḥ sūnāpāpaughabhāginaḥ
iṣṭir vaiśvānarī pāpam upahaṃsyati te 'khilam
avaśyaṃ viṣaye kaścid brāhmaṇaḥ saṃśritavrataḥ
iṣṭiṃ vaiśvānarīṃ klptāṃ nirvaped abdaparyaye
tasya ṣaḍbhāgamātreṇa tvaṃ pāpaṃ nirdahiṣyasi
samyak śraddhāsamācārād aham ārādhitas tvayā
paraḥ parāṇām ādyo 'sau jñeyo dhyeyo janārdanaḥ
lobhādivyāptahṛdayo yat pāpaṃ kurute naraḥ
śamāyālaṃ jalaṃ vahnes tamaso bhāskarādayaḥ
kṣāntiḥ kaler aghaughasya nāmasaṃkīrtanaṃ hareḥ
yā kācin manaso vṛttiḥ sā bhavatv acyutāśrayā
yā yā jāyeta me buddhir yāvaj jīvāmy ahaṃ pitaḥ
sā sā chinattu saṃdehān kṛṣṇāptau paripanthinaḥ
yathā govindam ārādhya saśarīraḥ surālayam
evam etad aśeṣaṃ te matprasādād bhaviṣyati
nāsti govindabhaktānāṃ vāñchitaṃ bhuvi durlabham
ārādhya pāṇḍavo yātaḥ saśarīraḥ surālayam
bhūyaś ca śṛṇu rājendra janakena mahātmanā
yad gītaṃ vahatā bhaktiṃ jñānam āsādya keśave
sarvatra samadṛṣṭiṃ taṃ janakaṃ mithileśvaram
dvijarūpaṃ samāsthāya devadevo janārdanaḥ
pṛthivīṃ pṛthivīpālaḥ pālayitvā pitā tava
śabdādayo ye viśayās te vairāgyaphalā nṛpa
nītyā vihīnas tu bhavān kathaṃ rājyaṃ kariṣyati
sarvair nītiṃ samāsthāya yathā te prapitāmahaiḥ
kṛtaṃ rājyaṃ tathā bhūpa kuru mātijaḍo bhava
tava prajñā matā hy eṣā mama moho mahīpate
mamāpi śrūyatāṃ vākyaṃ bhavato yadi rocate
yadā sarvagato viṣṇuḥ paramātmā prajāpatiḥ
tadā mitrādimadhyastha saṃjñā keṣu nipātyatām
pitā mātā tathā bhrātā yadā nānyaj janārdanāt
pitṛmātṛmayīṃ saṃjñāṃ tadā kutra karomy aham
anekarūparūpo 'yaṃ viṣṇur evākhilaṃ jagat
viṣṇuḥ pitā me jagataḥ pratiṣṭhā viṣṇur mātā viṣṇur evāgrajo me
viṣṇur gatir viṣṇumayas tathāsmi viṣṇau sthito 'smy akṣagataś ca viṣṇuḥ
yo me mamatvopagataḥ sa viṣṇur yaś cāribhūto mama so 'pi viṣṇuḥ
divaṃ viyad bhūḥ kakubhaś ca viṣṇur bhūtāni viṣṇur bhuvanāni viṣṇuḥ
paśyāmi viṣṇuṃ na paraṃ tato 'nyac śṛṇomi viṣṇuṃ na paraṃ tato 'nyat
spṛśāmi viṣṇuṃ na paraṃ tato 'nyaj jighrāmi viṣṇuṃ na paraṃ tato 'nyat
rasāmi viṣṇuṃ na paraṃ tato 'nyan manye ca viṣṇuṃ na paraṃ tato 'nyat
budhyāmi viṣṇuṃ na paraṃ tato 'nyat sarvaṃ hi viṣṇur na paraṃ tato 'nyat
jighrāmi viṣṇuṃ na paraṃ tato 'nyac namāmi viṣṇuṃ na paraṃ tato 'nyat
viṣṇuḥ samastaṃ na paraṃ tato 'sti viṣṇuḥ samastaṃ na paraṃ ca devaḥ
viṣṇur laghīyān na paraṃ tato 'sti viṣṇur garīyān na paraṃ tato 'nyat
viṣṇuḥ sthārīyān na paraṃ tato 'sti
yathā na viṣṇuvyatiriktam anyac śṛṇomi paśyāmi tathā spṛśāmi
tvaṃ cāhaṃ anye ca śarīrabhedair vibhinnam īśasya hareḥ svarūpam
mūrtāmūrtiviśeṣaṃ tu paśyatas tanmayaṃ dvija
krodhaharṣādayo bhāvāḥ sthāsyanti hṛdaye katham
tathāpi mā ruṣaṃ kārṣīr acikitsyā hi mohitāḥ
bahurūpas tato rūpaṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharam
darśayām āsa suprīto janakāya janārdanaḥ
tatas taddarśanād bhūpaṃ śirasā praṇataṃ prabhuḥ
ādyaḥ prajāpatipatiḥ pratyuvācācyuto hariḥ
evaṃ bhaviṣyatīty uktvā gato 'ntardhānam īśvaraḥ
iti kṛṣṇe naravyāghra kurvan bhaktiṃ naraḥ sadā
mamāvatārān akhilāñ śrotum icchā pravartate
yathā yathā hi kṛṣṇasya katheyaṃ kathyate tvayā
manaḥprītir anāyāsād apuṇyacayasaṃkṣayaḥ
sa kuruṣvāmalamate prasādapravaṇaṃ manaḥ
avatārān sureśasya viṣṇor icchāmi veditum
nārāyaṇaṃ purākalpe pṛṣṭavān kamalodbhavaḥ
oṃkārapravaṇā vedā jagmus te ca rasātalam
kṛṣṇanābhihradodbhūta kamalodaraśāyini
bhogiśayyāśayaḥ kṛṣṇo dvitīyāṃ tanum ātmanaḥ
kṛtvā mīnamayīṃ sadyaḥ praviveśa rasātalam
madhukaiṭabhābhyāṃ ca punar bhogiśayyāgato hariḥ
hṛtān hayaśirā bhūtvā vedān āhṛtavān rasāt
āhṛteṣv atha vedeṣu devadevaṃ pitāmahaḥ
tuṣṭāva praṇato bhaktyā tasya cāvir babhau hariḥ
uvāca prakaṭībhūtaṃ praṇipatyābjasaṃbhavaḥ
namaḥ sūkṣmātisūkṣmāya namas tubhyaṃ trimūrtaye
so 'ham icchāmi taṃ jñātum ātmānaṃ prabhavāvyayam
tan māṃ bhakta iti jñātvā kathayātmānam acyuta
kathayāmi tavātmānam anākhyāgodaraṃ param
na vācāṃ viṣaye yo 'sāv aviśeṣaṇalakṣaṇaḥ
anākhyātasvarūpaṃ māṃ bhavāñ jñāsyati yogataḥ
majjijñāsā parā brahmaṃs tena jātā matis tava
evam uktas tato brahmā viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā
viṣṇoḥ svarūpaṃ jijñāsur yuyojātmānam ātmanā
sa dadarśātisūkṣmaṃ ca sūkṣmajyotiṣy ajaṃ vibhum
niyutārdhārdhamātreṇa vyāptāśeṣacarācaram
ātmānam indrarudrārka candrāśvivasumārutān
khādīny atha ca śabdādīn dadṛśe ca sa tanmayān
ye vyaktā ye tathāvyaktā bhāvā ye cāpi pauruṣāḥ
tāṃś ca tatrātisūkṣmo 'pi dṛṣṭavān akhilān vibhuḥ
jñātaṃ svarūpam ajñāta svarūpa bhagavaṃs tava
bhagavañ jñātam ajñātam anantāja namo 'stu te
paramaṃ cāvatāreṣu yad rūpaṃ tad vadasva me
keṣu keṣu mayā jñeyaḥ sthāneṣu tvam adhokṣaja
saṃbhūtayo mamācakṣva yā bhaviṣyanti te bhuvi
saṃbhūtayo yās tu bhavān kariṣyati vadasva tāḥ
tvaṃ kartā sarvabhūtānāṃ saṃhartā ceśvareśvaraḥ
tavāpi kartā nānyo 'sti svecchayā krīḍate bhavān
yan māṃ tvaṃ pṛcchasi brahman avatārāśritaṃ param
deveṣu nRṣu tiryakṣu sthāvareṣu careṣu ca
mamāvatārāḥ kāryārthaṃ jagataś copakāriṇaḥ
abhyutthānam adharmasya tadātmāṅgaṃ sṛjāmy aham
paritrāṇāya sādhūnāṃ vināśāya ca duṣkṛtāṃ
pūrvotpanneṣu bhūteṣu nṛdevādiṣu cāpy aham
praviśya ca tathā pūrvaṃ tanuṃ dharmabhṛtāṃ vara
devatve devikā ceṣṭā tiryaktve mama tāmasī
icchayā mānuṣatve ca vicarāmi nṛceṣṭayā
pratikṣaṇaṃ ca bhūteṣu sṛjāmi jagataḥ sthitim
caritaṃ mānuṣādīnāṃ tad vai jānīhi matkṛtam
yac ca pṛcchasi māṃ brahman kāḥ kāḥ saṃbhūtayas tava
tāḥ śṛṇuṣva samāsena yā bhaviṣyanti sāṃpratam
matsyena bhūtvā pātālāt tava vedāḥ samuddhṛtāḥ
madhukaiṭabhābhyāṃ ca hṛtā dattāśvaśirasā mayā
tvam apy atra mahābhāga madaṃśaḥ kamalodarāt
mannābhisaṃbhavāj jātaḥ prajāsṛṣṭikaraḥ paraḥ
ekārṇavaṃ ca yad idaṃ brahman paśyasy aśeṣataḥ
asmin vasumatīṃ devīṃ magnāṃ pātālam āgatām
vedapādo yūpadaṃṣṭraḥ kratudantaś citīmukhaḥ
agnijihvo darbharomā brahmaśīrṣo mahātapāḥ
ahorātrekṣaṇadharo vedāṅgaśrutibhūṣaṇaḥ
ājyanāsaḥ śruvastuṇḍaḥ sāmaghoṣasvaro mahān
prāgvaṃśakāyo dyutimān nānādīkṣābhir ācitaḥ
dakṣiṇāhṛdayo yogī mahāsattramayo mahān
upakarmeṣṭiruciraḥ pravargāvartabhūṣaṇaḥ
bhūtvā yajñavarāho 'ham iti brahman rasātalāt
pṛthivīm uddhariṣyāmi sthāpayaiṣyāmi ca sthitau
parvatānāṃ nadīnāṃ ca dvīpādīnāṃ ca yā sthitiḥ
tāṃ ca tadvat kariṣyāmi śailādīnām anukramāt
hiraṇyākṣaṃ ca durvṛttaṃ kaśyapasyātmasaṃbhavam
tenaiva ghātayiṣyāmi rūpeṇāhaṃ prajāpate
utpādya pṛthivīṃ samyak sthāpayitvā yathā purā
sṛṣṭiṃ tataḥ kariṣyāmi tvām āviśya prajāpatim
jānāsi kāpilaṃ rūpaṃ prathamaṃ pauruṣaṃ mama
sarvavidyāpraṇetāraṃ tvayā vedeṣu darśitam
tata utsṛjya rūpāṇi amarādivibhedataḥ
vyāpayiṣyāmi lokāṃs tu bhūlokādīm aśeṣataḥ
sṛṣṭaṃ jagad idaṃ deva mānuṣyādiviśeṣaṇam
nṛsiṃharūpaṃ kṛtvāhaṃ ghātayiṣyāmi taṃ ripum
kṣīrābdau kūrmarūpo 'haṃ devānāṃ kamalodbhava
mandaraṃ dhārayiṣyāmi pṛṣṭhenāmṛtamanthane
hariṣyati ca devānāṃ yajñabhāgān yadā baliḥ
tadāhaṃ vāmano bhūtvā gatvā tasya mahādhvaram
vañcayitvāsurapatiṃ kariṣyāmi tripiṣṭapam
baliṃ cāpi kariṣyāmi pātālatalavāsinam
dattātreyo bhaviṣyāmi nihaṃsyāmi tathāsurān
sattvānām upakārāya pradhānapuruṣāntaram
darśayiṣyāmi lokeṣu kāpilaṃ rūpam āsthitaḥ
kārtavīryādibhiś cānyaiś caturdaśabhir anvitāḥ
bhaviṣyanti madaṃśena tretāyāṃ cakravartinaḥ
tataś ca bhārgavo rāmo gṛhītaparaśur dvijaḥ
bhūtvā kṣatriyahīnāṃ ca kariṣyāmi vasuṃdharām
punaś ca rāghavo rāmo bhūtvā daśarathātmajaḥ
baddhvā mahodadhiṃ kartā rākṣasānāṃ kulakṣayam
uttīrya ca paraṃ pāraṃ laṅkām āsādya durjayām
nihatya rāvaṇaṃ vīraṃ varadānena darpitam
māyāvināṃ mahāvīryaṃ rakṣasāṃ vanaśāyinām
lakṣmaṇānucaro rāmaḥ kariṣyāmi kulakṣayam
aṣṭāviṃśatime prāpte dvāpare kaṃsam ucchritam
keśinaṃ dhenukaṃ caiva śakuniṃ pūtanāṃ tathā
ariṣṭaṃ ca haniṣyāmi muruṃ narakam eva ca
niśumbhaṃ sahayagrīvaṇ tathānyāṃś cāsureśvarān
haniṣyāmi sudurvṛttāṃl lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā
govardhanaṃ girivaraṃ dhārayiṣyāmi bāhunā
bhārākrāntām imām urvīṃ dhanaṃjayasahāyavān
ghātayitvākhilān bhūpāṃl laghvīṃ kartāsmi sattama
dvārakāṃ plāvayiṣyāmi utsrakṣyāmi manuṣyatām
dvitīyo yo mamāṃśas tu rāmo 'nantaḥ sa lāṅgalī
narāṇām atha nārīṇāṃ dayāṃ bhūteṣu darśayan
raktāmbarā hy āñjitākṣāḥ praśāntamanasas tataḥ
eḍūkacihnā pṛthivī na devagṛhabhūṣitā
śūdrāḥ śūdreṣu dāsyanti mayi buddhatvam āgate
narakārhāṇi karmāṇi kariṣyanti prajāpate
svādhyāyeṣv avasīdanto brāhmaṇāḥ śaucavarjitāḥ
na śroṣyanti pituḥ putrāḥ śvaśrūśvaśurayoḥ snuṣāḥ
na bhāryā bhartur īśasya na bhṛtyā vinayasthitāḥ
varṇasaṃkaratāṃ prāpte loke 'smin dasyutāṃ gate
brāhmaṇādiṣu varṇeṣu bhaviṣyaty adharottaram
mānuṣān bhakṣayiṣyanti mlecchāḥ pārthivarūpiṇaḥ
daśa pañca ca vai śākhāḥ pramāṇena bhaviṣyati
tato 'haṃ saṃbhaviṣyāmi brāhmaṇo haripiṅgalaḥ
kalkī viṣṇuyaśaḥputro yājñavalkyapurohitaḥ
mlecchān utsādayiṣyāmi gṛhītāstraḥ kuśāyudhaḥ
sthāpayiṣyāmi maryādāś cāturvarṇye yathoditāḥ
tathāśrameṣu sarveṣu brahmacārivratādikāḥ
sthāpayitvā tataḥ sarvāḥ prajāḥ saddharmavartmani
kalkirūpaṃ parityajya divam eṣyāmy ahaṃ punaḥ
tataḥ kṛtayugaṃ bhūyaḥ pūrvavat saṃpravartsyate
varṇāśramāś ca dharmeṣu dveṣu sthāsyanti sattama
mamāvatārāḥ śataśo ye bhavanti jagaddhitāḥ
saṃkarṣaṇātmajaś caiva kalpānte ca rasātalāt
samutpatsyet tadā rudraḥ kālāgnir iti yaḥ śrutaḥ
tataḥ kṣayaṃ kariṣyāmi jagat sthāvarajaṅgamam
tvadrūpī ca tato bhūtvā jagat srakṣyāmy ahaṃ punaḥ
aṃśāvataraṇaṃ sarvaṃ mattaḥ saṃkṣepataḥ śṛṇu
yad dṛśyaṃ yac ca vai spṛśyaṃ yad ghreyaṃ rasyate ca yat
yac chravyaṃ yac ca mantavyaṃ bodhavyaṃ cāham aṃśagaḥ
labhante 'bhimatān kāmān narās tāṃs tān yathepsitān
rahasyam idam ākhyātaṃ tavāpi kathitaṃ mayā
viṣṇuḥ sarvagato 'nantaḥ sarvaṃ tatra pratiṣṭhitam
etat pavitraṃ paṭhitaṃ tathā duḥsvapnanāśanam
jātismaratvaṃ prajñāṃ ca dadāti paṭhatāṃ nṛṇām
śrutāḥ saṃbhūtayaḥ sarvā gadatas tava suvrata
tad ahaṃ śrotum icchāmi nRṇāṃ duḥsvapnanāśanam
svapnā hi sumahābhāga dṛśyante ye śubhāśubhāḥ
idam eva mahārāja pṛṣṭavāṃs te pitāmahaḥ
bhīṣmaṃ dharmabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
devavrataṃ mahāprājñaṃ sarvaśāstraviśāradam
tad ahaṃ śrotum icchāmi brūhi me vadatāṃ vara
śṛṇu rājan mahābāho vartayiṣyāmi te 'khilam
atrāpy udāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanam
gajendramokṣaṇaṃ puṇyaṃ kṛṣṇasyākliṣṭakarmaṇaḥ
sarvaratnamayaḥ śrīmāṃs trikūṭo nāma parvataḥ
kṣīrodajalavīcyagrair dhautāmalaśilātalaḥ
utthitaḥ sāgaraṃ bhittvā devarṣigaṇasevitaḥ
apsarobhiḥ samākīrṇaḥ śrīmān prasravaṇākulaḥ
mṛgair dvīpair dvijaiś caiva vṛtaḥ sauvarṇarājataiḥ
puṃnāgaiḥ karṇikāraiś ca puṣpitair upaśobhitaḥ
śālais tālais tamālaiś ca kuṭajaiś cārjunais tathā
evaṃ bahuvidhair vṛkṣaiḥ sarvataḥ samalaṃkṛtaḥ
nānādhātūjjvalaiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ prasravadbhiḥ samantataḥ
mṛgaiḥ śākhāmṛgaiḥ siṃhair mātaṃgaiś ca sadāmadaiḥ
jīvaṃjīvakasaṃghuṣṭaṃ cakoraśikhināditam
tasyaikaṃ kāñcanaṃ śṛṅgaṃ sevate yad divādaraḥ
nānāpuṣpasamākīrṇaṃ nānāgandhasamākulam
dvitīyaṃ rājataṃ śṛṅgaṃ sevate yan niśākaraḥ
pāṇḍurāmbudasaṃkāśaṃ tuṣāracayasaṃnibham
tṛtīyaṃ brahmasadanaṃ prakṛṣṭaṃ śṛṅgam uttamam
na tat kṛtaghnāḥ paśyanti na nṛśaṃsā na nāstikāḥ
nātaptatapasaḥ śailaṃ taṃ vai paśyanti mānavāḥ
tasya sānumataḥ pṛṣṭhe saraḥ kāñcanapaṅkajam
kāraṇḍavasamākīrṇaṃ rājahaṃsopaśobhitam
utpalaiḥ śatapattraiś ca kāñcanaiḥ samalaṃkṛtam
pattrair maṇidalaprakhyaiḥ puṣpaiḥ kāñcanasaṃnibhaiḥ
gulmaiḥ kīcakaveṇūnāṃ samantāt parivāritam
tasmin sarasi duṣṭātmā virūpo 'ntarjalāśayaḥ
āsīd grāho gajendrāṇāṃ durādharṣo mahābalaḥ
ājagāmāsitābhrābhaḥ kareṇuparivāritaḥ
madasrāvī mahāraudraḥ pādacārīva parvataḥ
sa gajo 'ñjanasaṃkāśo madāc calitamānasaḥ
tṛṣitaḥ sa jalaṃ prāpya kusumākaraśītalam
gṛhītas tena raudreṇa grāheṇāvyaktamūrtinā
paśyantīnāṃ kareṇūnāṃ krośantīnāṃ ca dāruṇam
kriyate paṅkajavane grāheṇātibalīyasā
gajaś cākarṣate tīraṃ grāhaś cākarṣate jalam
vāruṇaiḥ saṃyataḥ pāśair niḥprayatnagatiḥ kṛtaḥ
veṣṭyamānaḥ sughorais tu pāśair nāgo dṛḍhais tathā
vyathitaḥ saṃnirutsāho gṛhīto ghorakarmaṇā
sa tu nāgavaraḥ śrīmān nārāyaṇaparāyaṇaḥ
tam eva paramaṃ devaṃ gataḥ sarvātmanā tadā
ekāgraṃ cintayām āsa viśuddhenāntarātmanā
ādyaṃ devaṃ mahātmānaṃ pūjayām āsa keśavam
navameghapratīkāśaṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharam
digbāhuṃ sarvamūrdhānaṃ bhūpādaṃ gaganodaram
ādityacandranayanaṃ samagraṃ lokasākṣiṇam
pragṛhya puṣkarāgreṇa kāñcanaṃ kamalottamam
anāśritāya devāya niḥspṛhāya namo namaḥ
nama ādyāya bījāya śivāya ca praśāntāya
ārṣeyāya pravartine niścalāya yaśasvine
anantarāya caikāya sanātanāya pūrvāya
avyaktāya namo namaḥ purāṇāya namo namaḥ
namo guhyāya gūḍhāya
guṇāyāguṇavartine
atarkyāyāprameyāya
viśveśvarāya devāya śivāya haraye namaḥ
nārāyaṇāya viśvāya devānāṃ paramātmane
namo namaḥ kāraṇavāmanāya nārāyaṇāyāmitavikramāya
śrīśārṅgacakrāsigadādharāya namo 'stu tasmai puruṣottamāya
pītāmbarāya madhukaiṭabhanāśanāya bhaktipriyāya varadīptasudarśanāya
viśvāya cārumukuṭāya namo 'kṣarāya
nānāvicitramukuṭāṅgadabhūṣaṇāya sarveśvarāya varadāya namo varāya
viśvātmane paramakāraṇakāraṇāya phullāravindavimalāyatalocanāya
lokāyanāya tridaśāyanāya brahmāyanāyātmabhavāyanāya
dharmāyanāyaikajalāyanāya mahāvarāhāya sadā nato 'smi
acintyam avyaktam anantarūpaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ kāraṇam ādidevam
yugāntaśeṣaṃ puruṣaṃ purāṇaṃ taṃ vāsudevaṃ śaraṇaṃ prapadye
kṣetrajñam ātmaprabhavaṃ vareṇyaṃ taṃ vāsudevaṃ śaraṇaṃ prapadye
vadanti yaṃ vai puruṣaṃ sanātanaṃ taṃ vāsudevaṃ śaraṇaṃ prapadye
tam īśvaraṃ tṛptam anopamair guṇaiḥ parāyaṇaṃ viṣṇum upaimi śāśvatam
kāryaṃ kriyākāraṇam aprameyaṃ hiraṇyanābhaṃ varapadmanābham
mahābalaṃ vedanidhiṃ surottamaṃ vrajāmi viṣṇuṃ śaraṇaṃ janārdanam
pītāmbaraṃ kāñcanabhakticitraṃ mālādharaṃ keśavam abhyupaimi
bhavodbhavaṃ vedavidāṃ variṣṭhaṃ yogātmānaṃ sāṃkhyavidāṃ variṣṭham
śrīvatsāṅkaṃ mahādevaṃ vedaguhyam anuttamam
prabhavaṃ sarvalokānāṃ nirguṇaṃ parameśvaram
prapadye muktasaṃgānāṃ yatīnāṃ paramāṃ gatim
bhagavantaṃ surādhyakṣam akṣaraṃ puṣkarekṣaṇam
śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ bhaktyā prapadye brāhmaṇapriyam
bhūtātmānaṃ mahātmānaṃ prapadye madhusūdanam
ādidevam ajaṃ śambhuṃ vyaktāvyaktaṃ janārdanam
kṣetrajñaṃ puruṣaṃ yajñaṃ triguṇātītam avyayam
nārāyaṇam aṇīyāṃsaṃ prapadye parameśvaram
vareṇyam anaghaṃ devam ṛṣayo vedapāragāḥ
namas te puṇḍarīkākṣa bhaktānām abhayaprada
subrahmaṇya namas te 'stu trāhi māṃ śaraṇāgatam
prītimān abhavad rājañ śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ
sāṃnidhyaṃ kalpayām āsa tasmin sarasi mādhavaḥ
grāhagrastaṃ gajaṃ taṃ ca saṃgṛhya salilāśayāt
ujjahārāprameyātmā tarasaivārisūdanaḥ
sthalasthaṃ dārayām āsa grāhaṃ cakreṇa mādhavaḥ
mokṣayām āsa ca gajaṃ pāśebhyaḥ śaraṇāgatam
gajatvam agamat kṛṣṇān mokṣaṃ prāpya divaṃ gataḥ
śāpād vimuktaḥ sadyaś ca gajo gandharvatāṃ gataḥ
grāho 'pi yakṣatāṃ yāto yaḥ kṛṣṇena nipātitaḥ
tasyāpi śāpamokṣo 'sau jaigīṣavyakṛto 'bhavat
prītimāṃs trāti govindaḥ sadyaḥ saṃsārasāgarāt
gandharvarāṭ tathā yakṣaḥ parāṃ nirvṛtim āgatau
dṛṣṭvā muktau gajagrahau bhagavān madhusūdanaḥ
yo grāhaṃ nāgarājaṃ ca māṃ caiva praṇidhānavān
smariṣyati saraś cedaṃ yuvayor mokṣaṇaṃ tathā
gulmaṃ kīcakaveṇūnāṃ taṃ ca śailavaraṃ tathā
aśvatthaṃ bhāskaraṃ gaṅgāṃ naimiṣāraṇyam eva ca
saṃsmariṣyanti ye martyāḥ samyak śroṣyanti vāpi ye
sarvapāpaiḥ pramokṣyante kalyāṇānāṃ ca bhāginaḥ
bhaviṣyanti tathā puṇyāṃ gatiṃ yāsyanti mānavāḥ
duḥsvapnaṃ ca nṛṇāṃ teṣāṃ susvapnaṃ ca bhaviṣyati
kaurmaṃ mātsyaṃ ca vārāhaṃ vāmanaṃ tārkṣyam eva ca
nārasiṃhaṃ tathā rūpaṃ sṛṣṭisaṃhārakārakam
etāni prātar utthāya saṃsmariṣyanti ye narāḥ
aspṛśad gajagandharvaṃ grāhayakṣaṃ ca taṃ tadā
tena spṛṣṭāv ubhau sadyo divyamālyāmbarānvitau
tato devapatiḥ kṛṣṇo mokṣayitvā gajottamam
ṛṣibhiḥ stūyamāno hi guhyair vedapadākṣaraiḥ
gataḥ sa bhagavān viṣṇur durvijñeyagatiḥ prabhuḥ
gajendramokṣaṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve cendrapurogamāḥ
brahmāṇam agrataḥ kṛtvā sarve prāñjalayo 'bhavan
vavandire mahātmānaṃ prabhuṃ nārāyaṇaṃ harim
vismayotphullanayanāḥ prajāpatipuraḥsarāḥ
ya idaṃ śṛṇuyān nityaṃ prātar utthāya mānavaḥ
prāpnuyāt paramāṃ siddhiṃ duḥsvapnas tasya naśyati
śraddhayā hi kuruśreṣṭha smṛtena kathitena ca
gajendramokṣaṇeneha dīrgham āyur avāpnuyāt
mayā te kathitaṃ divyaṃ pavitraṃ pāpanāśanam
kīrtayasva mahābāho mahāduḥsvapnanāśanam
kīrtyamānaṃ ca viprebhyaḥ śṛṇu bhaktyā yathoditam
gajendramokṣaṇaṃ śrutvā kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
bhīṣmād bhagīrathīputrāt pūjayām āsa keśavam
ye cāpi pāṇḍuputrasya samīpasthā dvijottamāḥ
te 'pi bhīṣmasya pārśvasthaṃ vāsudevaṃ praṇemire
varaṃ vareṇyaṃ varapadmanābhaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ brahmanidhiṃ sureśam
taṃ devaguhyaṃ puruṣaṃ purāṇaṃ vavandire brahmavidāṃ variṣṭham
etat puṇyaṃ mahārāja narāṇāṃ pāpakarmaṇām
bhaktimān puṇḍarīkākṣe gajo duḥkhād vimocitaḥ
mahāmate mahāprājña sarvaśāstraviśārada
śrīvatsāṅkaṃ jagadbījam anantaṃ lokabhāvanam
purā nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ nāradaḥ paryapṛcchata
kiṃ vā japyaṃ japen nityaṃ kalyam utthāya mānavaḥ
śrutvā tasya tu devarṣer vākyaṃ vākyaviśāradaḥ
provāca bhagavān viṣṇur nāradaṃ jagato gatiḥ
maraṇe yām anusmṛtya prāpnoti paramāṃ gatim
oṃkāram āditaḥ kṛtvā mām anusmṛtya manmanāḥ
avyaktaṃ śāśvataṃ devam anantaṃ puruṣottamam
purāṇaṃ paramaṃ viṣṇum adbhutaṃ lokabhāvanam
prapadye puṇḍarīkākṣam īśaṃ bhaktānukampinam
sraṣṭāraṃ sarvabhūtānām anantabalapauruṣam
padmanābhaṃ hṛṣīkeśaṃ papadye satyam avyayam
sahasraśirasaṃ devaṃ vaikuṇṭhaṃ tārkṣyavāhanam
nārāyaṇaṃ naraṃ haṃsaṃ yogātmānaṃ sanātanam
śaraṇyaṃ sarvalokānāṃ prapadye dhruvam īśvaram
carācaragurur devaḥ sa no viṣṇuḥ prasīdatu
yasmāj jātaḥ purā brahmā padmayoniḥ pitāmahaḥ
prasīdatu sa no viṣṇuḥ pitā mātā pitāmahaḥ
yaḥ purā pralaye prāpte naṣṭe loke carācare
ekas tiṣṭhati yogātmā sa no viṣṇuḥ prasīdatu
hūyate ca punar dvābhyāṃ sa no viṣṇuḥ prasīdatu
parjanyaḥ pṛthivī sasyaṃ kālo dharmaḥ kriyā phalam
guṇākaraḥ sa no babhrur vāsudevaḥ prasīdatu
ajeya khaṇḍaparaśo viśvamūrte vṛṣākape
trigarte pañcakālajña namas te jñānasāgara
avyaktād aṇḍam utpannam avyaktādyaḥ paraḥ prabhuḥ
yasmāt parataraṃ nāsti tam asmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ
niścayaṃ nādhigacchanti tam asmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ
jitendriyā mahātmāno jñānadhyānaparāyaṇāḥ
yaṃ prāpya na nivartante tam asmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ
ekāṃśena jagat sarvaṃ yo 'vaṣṭabhya vibhuḥ sthitaḥ
agrāhyo nirguṇaḥ śāstā tam asmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ
kṣetrajñam iti yaṃ prāhuḥ sa mahātmā prasīdatu
āsthitaḥ prakṛtiṃ bhuṅkte sa mahātmā prasīdatu
kṣetrajñaḥ pañcadhā bhuṅkte prakṛtiṃ bahubhir guṇaiḥ
manoguṇāṃś ca yo bhuṅkte sa mahātmā prasīdatu
sāṃkhyā yogāś ca ye cānye siddhāś caiva maharṣayaḥ
ye tu tvāṃ nābhijānanti saṃsāre saṃsaranti te
aśarīraṃ śarīrasthaṃ samaṃ sarveṣu dehiṣu
avyaktaṃ buddhyahaṃkārau mahābhūtendriyāṇi ca
tvayi tāni na teṣu tvaṃ teṣu tvaṃ tāni na tvayi
sraṣṭā bhoktāsi kūṭastho guṇānāṃ prabhur īśvaraḥ
bhaktānāṃ yad dhitaṃ deva tad dhyāya tridaśeśvara
ahaṃkāreṇa buddhyā vā tathā sattvādibhir guṇaiḥ
viṣayair indriyair vāpi mā me bhūyāt samāgamaḥ
pṛthivīṃ yātu me ghrāṇaṃ yātu me rasanā jalam
cakṣur hutāśanaṃ yātu sparśo me yātu mārutam
śabdo hy ākāśam abhyetu mano vaikārikaṃ tathā
pūrvadehakṛtā ye me vyādhayas te viśantu mām
ārdayantu ca duḥkhāni pravimuñcāmi yad ṛṇam
upatiṣṭhantu me rogā ye mayā pūrvasaṃcitāḥ
anṛṇo gantum icchāmi tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam
tasyāhaṃ na praṇaśyāmi sa ca me na praṇaśyati
imām anusmṛtiṃ nityaṃ vaiṣṇavīṃ pāpanāśanīm
api pāpasamācāraḥ so 'pi yāti parāṃ gatim
paurṇamāsyām amāvāsyāṃ dvādaśyāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ
śrāvayec chraddadhānaṃs tu ye cānye mām upāśritāḥ
tasya syur akṣayā lokāḥ śvapākasyāpi nārada
dhyāyanti ca yathānyāyaṃ te yānti paramāṃ gatim
aśvamedhasahasrāṇāṃ yaḥ sahasraṃ samācaret
iṣṭaṃ dattaṃ tapo 'dhītaṃ vratāni niyamāś ca ye
sarvam etad vināśāntaṃ jñānasyānto na vidyate
dānādīny antavantīha madbhakto nāntam aśnute
yo dadyād bhagavajjñānaṃ kuryād vā dharmadeśanām
kṛtsnāṃ vā pṛthivīṃ dadyān na tu tulyaṃ kathaṃcana
kāntāravanadurgeṣu kṛcchreṣv āpatsu saṃbhrame
dasyubhiḥ saṃniruddhaś ca nāmabhir māṃ prakīrtayet
varāho rakṣatu jale viṣameṣu ca vāmanaḥ
aṭavyāṃ nārasiṃhas tu sarvataḥ pātu keśavaḥ
rāmo rāmaś ca rāmaś ca trāyantāṃ dasyudoṣataḥ
janmāntarasahasrāṇi tapojñānasamādhibhiḥ
narāṇāṃ kṣīṇapāpānāṃ kṛṣṇe bhaktiḥ prajāyate
gatvā gatvā nivartane candrasūryādayo grahāḥ
adyāpi na nivartante dvādaśākṣaracintakāḥ
tasmān mām eva devarṣe dhyāyasvātandritaḥ sadā
cakāra keśave bhaktiṃ tasmāt tvaṃ kuru bhūpate
yaḥ paṭhet parayā bhaktyā sa gacched viṣṇusāmyatām
etat puṇyaṃ pāpaharaṃ dhanyaṃ duḥsvapnanāśanam
pāpaṃ praṇaśyate yena puṇyaṃ yena vivardhate
yaj japan sugatiṃ yāti śṛṇvaṃś ca mama tad vada
kaścid āsīd dvijadrogdhā piśunaḥ kṣatriyādhamaḥ
parapīḍārucir duṣṭaḥ svabhāvād eva nirghṛṇaḥ
paribhūtāḥ sadā tena pitṛdevadvijātayaḥ
paradāreṣu caivāsya babhūvābhirataṃ manaḥ
sa tv āyuṣi parikṣīṇe jajñe ghoro niśācaraḥ
tena vai karmadoṣeṇa svena pāpakṛtāṃ varaḥ
krūrair eva tato vṛttiṃ rākṣasatve viśeṣataḥ
cakāra karmabhiḥ pāpaḥ sarvaprāṇivihiṃsakaḥ
yad yat paśyati sattvaṃ sa tat tad ādāya rākṣasaḥ
evaṃ tasyātiduṣṭasya kurvataḥ prāṇināṃ vadham
jagāma sumahān kālaḥ pariṇāmaṃ tathā vayaḥ
ūrdhvabāhuṃ mahābhāgaṃ kṛtarakṣaṃ samantataḥ
taṃ dṛṣṭvā sa tu durbuddhir brāhmaṇaṃ rākṣasādhamaḥ
samabhyadhāvad vegena samādātuṃ cikhādiṣuḥ
tena rakṣā ca yā dikṣu brāhmaṇenābhavat kṛtā
tayā nirastaṃ tad rakṣo nipapātāvidūrataḥ
bhagavan kīdṛśīṃ rakṣāṃ sa cakāra dvijottamaḥ
tapaś cacāra vipro 'sau praviṣṭo viṣṇupañjaram
viṣṇupañjaram icchāmi śrotuṃ dharmabhṛtāṃ vara
tripuraṃ jaghnuṣaḥ pūrvaṃ brahmaṇā viṣṇupañjaraḥ
śaṃkarasya kuruśreṣṭha rakṣaṇāya nirūpitaḥ
vāgīśena tu śakrasya balaṃ hantuṃ prayāsyataḥ
viṣṇuḥ prācyāṃ sthitaś cakrī viṣṇur dakṣiṇato gadī
pratīcyāṃ śārṅgadhṛg viṣṇur viṣṇuḥ khaḍgī mamottare
hṛṣīkeśo vikoṇeṣu tacchidreṣu janārdanaḥ
asyāṃśumālā duḥprekṣā hantu pretaniśācarān
gadā ceyaṃ sahasrārcir udvamatpāvakolvaṇā
rakṣobhūtapiśācānāṃ ḍākiṇīnāṃ ca nāśanī
śārṅgavisphūrjitaṃ caiva vāsudevasya madripūn
tiryaṅmanuṣyakūṣmāṇḍa pretādīn hantv aśeṣataḥ
khaḍgadhārājvalajjyotsnā nirdhūtā ye samāhatāḥ
ye kūṣmāṇḍās tathā yakṣā ye daityā ye niśācarāḥ
pretā vināyakāḥ krūrā manuṣyā jambhakāḥ khagāḥ
siṃhādayo ye paśavo dandasūkāś ca pannagāḥ
sarve bhavantu te saumyāḥ kṛṣṇaśaṅkharavāhatāḥ
cittavṛttiharā ye me ye janāḥ smṛtihārakāḥ
balaujasāṃ ca hartāraś chāyāvibhraṃśakāś ca ye
ye copabhogahartāro ye ca lakṣaṇanāśakāḥ
kūṣmāṇḍās te praṇaśyantu viṣṇucakrarayāhatāḥ
pṛṣṭhe purastān mama dakṣiṇottare vikoṇagaś cāstu janārdano hariḥ
tad īḍyam īśānam anantam īśvaraṃ janārdanaṃ praṇipatito na sīdati
ṛtena tenācyutanāmakīrtanāt praṇāśam etu trividhaṃ mamāśubham
ity asāv ātmarakṣārthaṃ nyastavān viṣṇupañjaram
tenāsādhyaḥ sa duṣṭānāṃ babhūva nṛpa rakṣasām
etayārakṣayā rakṣo nirdhūtaṃ bhuvi pātitam
dṛṣṭvā ca kṛpayāviṣṭaḥ samāśvāsya niśācaram
papracchāgamane hetuṃ taṃ cācaṣṭa yathātatham
prasīda vipravarya tvaṃ nirviṇṇasyātipāpinaḥ
pāpapraśamanāyālam upadeśaṃ prayaccha me
bahūni pāpāni mayā kṛtāni bahavo hatāḥ
kṛtāḥ striyaś ca me bahvyo vidhavā hataputrikāḥ
anāgasāṃ ca sattvānām anekānāṃ kṣayaḥ kṛtaḥ
pāpasyāsya kṣayaṃ kartuṃ kuru me dharmadeśanām
sahasaiva samāyātā jijñāsā dharmavartmani
tvām attum āgataḥ kṣipto rakṣayā kṛtayā tvayā
kā sā rakṣā na tāṃ vedmi vedmi nāsyāḥ parāyaṇam
kiṃtv asyāḥ saṃgam āsādya nirvedaṃ prāpitaṃ param
sa kṛpāṃ kuru dharmajña mayy anukrośam āvaha
pratyuvāca mahābhāga vimṛśya suciraṃ tadā
yat tvam ātthopadeśārthaṃ nirviṇṇaḥ svena karmaṇā
yuktam etan na pāpānāṃ nivṛtter upakārakam
kariṣye yātudhānānāṃ na tv ahaṃ dharmadeśanām
tāṃs tvaṃ pṛccha dvijān saumya ye vai pravacane ratāḥ
evam uktvā yayau vipraś cintām āpa ca rākṣasaḥ
kathaṃ pāpāpanodaḥ syād ity asau vyākulendriyaḥ
na tadā khādate sattvān kṣudhā saṃpīḍito 'pi san
ṣaṣṭhe ṣaṣṭhe tadā kāle jantum ekam abhakṣayat
sa kadācit kṣudhāviṣṭaḥ paryaṭan vipine vane
dadarśātha phalāhāram agrataḥ kauśikaṃ dvijam
taṃ jagrāha ca bhakṣārthaṃ ṣaṣṭhe kāle bubhukṣitaḥ
guror arthe phalāhāram āgataṃ brahmacāriṇam
gṛhīto rakṣasā tena sa tadā munidārakaḥ
nirāśo jīvite prāha sāmapūrvaṃ niśācaram
ṣaṣṭhe kāle mamāhāraḥ kṣudhitasya tvam āgataḥ
niḥśūkasyātipāpasya nirghṛṇasya dvijadruhaḥ
yady avaśyaṃ tvayādhyāhaṃ bhakṣaṇīyo niśācara
mamātra niṣṭhāṃ prāptasya tat pāpāya niveditam
sa tvaṃ muhūrtamātraṃ mām atraiva pratipālaya
ṣaṣṭhe kāle na me brahman kaścid grahaṇam āgataḥ
eka evātra mokṣasya tava hetuḥ śṛṇuṣva tam
mayā nisargato brahmañ jātidoṣād viśeṣataḥ
ā bālyān mama pāpeṣu na puṇyeṣu rataṃ manaḥ
tatpāpasaṃcayān mokṣaṃ prāpnuyāṃ yena tad vada
yāni pāpāni karmāṇi bālatvāc caritāni me
duṣṭāṃ yonim imāṃ prāpya tanmuktiṃ kathaya dvija
tat kṣudhārtāt samārtas tvaṃ niyataṃ mokṣam āpsyasi
na caitat pāpaśīlo 'ham adya tvāṃ kṣutpipāsitaḥ
ṣaṣṭhe kāle nṛśaṃsātmā bhakṣayiṣyāmi nirghṛṇaḥ
vimṛśya suciraṃ vipraḥ śaraṇaṃ jātavedasam
jagāma jñānadānāya saṃśayaṃ paramaṃ gataḥ
yadi śuśrūṣito vahnir guroḥ śuśrūṣaṇād anu
vratāni vā sucīrṇāni saptārciḥ pātu māṃ tataḥ
yathāham avagacchāmi tathā māṃ pātu pāvakaḥ
yathā guruṃ na manasā karmaṇā vacasāpi vā
avajānāmy ahaṃ tena pātu satyena pāvakaḥ
saptārciṣā samādiṣṭā prādurāsīt sarasvatī
sā covāca dvijasutaṃ rākṣasagrahaṇākulam
mā bhair dvijasutāhaṃ tvāṃ mokṣayāmy atisaṃkaṭāt
adṛśyā rakṣasā tena proktvetthaṃ taṃ sarasvatī
adarśanam itā so 'pi dvijaḥ prāha niśācaram
śrūyatāṃ tava yac chreyas tathānyeṣāṃ ca pāpinām
prātar utthāya satataṃ madhyāhne 'hnaḥ kṣaye 'pi vā
ayaṃ śastaḥ sadā jāpaḥ sarvapāpopaśāntidaḥ
hariṃ kṛṣṇaṃ hṛṣīkeśaṃ vāsudevaṃ janārdanam
viśveśvaram ajaṃ viṣṇum aprameyaparākramam
praṇato 'smi prajāpālaṃ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
viṣṇum acyutam īśānam anantam aparājitam
praṇato 'smi mahātmānaṃ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
carācaraguruṃ nāthaṃ govindaṃ śeṣaśāyinam
praṇato 'smi gadāpāṇiṃ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
śaṅkhinaṃ cakriṇaṃ śāntaṃ śārṅgiṇaṃ sragdharaṃ param
praṇato 'smi patiṃ lakṣmyāḥ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
dāmodaram udārākṣaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣam avyayam
nārāyaṇaṃ naraṃ śauriṃ mādhavaṃ madhusūdanam
praṇato 'smi dharādhāraṃ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
keśavaṃ keśihantāraṃ kaṃsāriṣṭanisūdanam
śrīvatsavakṣasaṃ śrīśaṃ śrīdharaṃ śrīniketanam
praṇato 'smi śriyaḥ kāntaṃ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
yam īśaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ dhyāyanti yatayo 'kṣaram
vāsudevam anirdeśyaṃ tam asmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ
dhyāyanti vāsudevākhyaṃ tam asmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ
sarvagaṃ sarvabhūtaṃ ca sarvasyādhātam īśvaram
vāsudevaṃ paraṃ brahma tam asmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ
karmakṣaye 'kṣayaṃ devaṃ tam asmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ
na yoginaḥ prāpnuvanti tam asmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ
brahmā bhūtvā jagat sarvaṃ sadevāsuramānuṣam
yaḥ sṛjaty acyuto devas tam asmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ
sūtaṃ prabho purā jajñe tam asmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ
sraṣṭṛtve saṃsthitaṃ sṛṣṭau praṇato 'smi sanātanam
yaḥ pāti sṛṣṭaṃ ca vibhuḥ sthitāv asurasūdanaḥ
tam ādipuruṣaṃ viṣṇuṃ praṇato 'smi sanātanam
dhṛtā mahī hatā daityāḥ paritrātās tathāmarāḥ
yena taṃ viṣṇum ādyeśaṃ praṇato 'smi sanātanam
yajñair yajanti yaṃ viprā yajñeśaṃ yajñabhāvanam
taṃ yajñapuruṣaṃ viṣṇuṃ praṇato 'smi sanātanam
varṇāśramān sthitāv ādyo yaḥ sthāpayati vartmani
tam ādipuruṣaṃ viṣṇuṃ praṇato 'smi sanātanam
tam ādipuruṣaṃ viṣṇuṃ praṇato 'smi janārdanam
pātālavīthībhūrādīṃs tathā lokān bibharti yaḥ
tam antapuruṣaṃ viṣṇuṃ praṇato 'smi janārdanam
saṃbhakṣayitvā sakalaṃ yathā sṛṣṭam idaṃ jagat
surāsurāḥ pitṛgaṇā yakṣagandharvarākṣasāḥ
yasyāṃśabhūtā devasya sarvagaṃ taṃ namāmy aham
samastadevāḥ sakalā mānuṣāṇāṃ ca jātayaḥ
yasyāṃśabhūtā devasya sarvagaṃ taṃ namāmy aham
vṛkṣagulmādayo yasya tathā paśumṛgādayaḥ
ekāṃśabhūtā devasya sarvagaṃ taṃ namāmy aham
yathā sarveṣu bhūteṣu sthāvareṣu careṣu ca
viṣṇur eva tathā pāpaṃ mamāśeṣaṃ praṇaśyatu
yac ca jñānaparicchedyaṃ pāpaṃ naśyatu me tathā
pravṛttaṃ ca nivṛttaṃ ca karma viṣṇumayaṃ yathā
yan niśāyāṃ tathā prātar yac ca madhyāparāhṇayoḥ
saṃdhyayoś ca kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ karmaṇā manasā girā
tiṣṭhatā vrajatā yac ca śayyāsanagatena ca
kṛtaṃ yad aśubhaṃ karma kāyena manasā girā
ajñānato jñānato vā vāsudevasya kīrtanāt
tat sarvaṃ vilayaṃ yātu toyasthaṃ lavaṇaṃ yathā
paripīḍodbhavaṃ nindāṃ kurvato yan mahātmanām
yac ca bhojye tathā peye yac ca kaṇḍūyanādiṣu
tan nārāyaṇagovinda harikṛṣṇeśakīrtanāt
viṣṇave vāsudevāya haraye keśavāya ca
janārdanāya kṛṣṇāya namo bhūyo namo namaḥ
idaṃ sārasvataṃ stotram aśeṣāghavināśanam
paṭhatāṃ śṛṇvatāṃ caiva sarvapāpavināśanam
idaṃ yaḥ prātar utthāya praṇipatya janārdanam
yas tu saṃvatsaraṃ pūrṇaṃ sāyaṃ prātaḥ samāhitaḥ
japaty etan naraḥ puṇyaṃ kṛtvā manasi keśavam
śārīraṃ mānasaṃ vāgjaṃ jñānato 'jñānato 'pi vā
kṛtaṃ tena tu yat pāpaṃ sapta janmāntarāṇi vai
mahāpātakam alpaṃ vā tathā yac copapātakam
viprāya suviśiṣṭāya tilapātrāṇi ṣoḍaśa
aviplutamatiś cānte saṃprāpya smaraṇaṃ hareḥ
yathainaṃ paṭhati nityaṃ stavaṃ sārasvataṃ pumān
api pāpasamāyukto mokṣaṃ prāpnoty asāv api
rākṣasagrastasarvāṅgaṃ tathā mām eṣa muñcatu
etad bhadramukhākhyātaṃ tava pātakanāśanam
viṣṇoḥ sārasvataṃ stotraṃ yaj jagāda sarasvatī
hutāśanena prahitā mama jihvāgrasaṃsthitā
jagādemaṃ stavaṃ viṣṇoḥ sarvapāpapraśāntidam
tataḥ pāpāpanodaṃ tu stute prāpsyasi keśave
aharniśaṃ hṛṣīkeśaṃ stavenānena rākṣasa
stauhi bhaktiṃ parāṃ kṛtvā tataḥ pāpād vimokṣyase
stuto hi sarvapāpāni nāśayiṣyaty asaṃśayam
bhaktyā rākṣasaśārdūla sarvapāpaharo hariḥ
tataḥ praṇamya taṃ vipraṃ prasādya ca niśācaraḥ
śālagrāmaṃ mahārāja tadaiva tapase yayau
devakriyāratir bhūtvā tapas tepe sa rākṣasaḥ
tathā tvam api rājarṣe sarvapāpapraśāntidam
ārādhaya hṛṣīkeśaṃ japan sārasvataṃ stavam
brahmann asāre saṃsāre rogādivyāptamānasaḥ
śabdādilubdhaḥ puruṣaḥ kiṃ kurvan nāvasīdati
śokamohavinirmuktaṃ viṣṇuṃ dhyāyan na sīdati
aprāṇacitikaṃ brahma vedānteṣu prakāśitam
ādyaṃ puruṣam īśānaṃ viṣṇuṃ dhyāyan na sīdati
aśanādyair asaṃspṛṣṭaṃ sevitaṃ yogibhiḥ sadā
sarvadoṣavinirmuktaṃ viṣṇuṃ dhyāyan na sīdati
niṣkalaṃ śāśvataṃ devaṃ viṣṇuṃ dhyāyan na sīdati
abhayaṃ satyasaṃkalpaṃ viṣṇuṃ dhyāyan na sīdati
amṛtaṃ sādhanaṃ sādhyaṃ yaṃ paśyanti manīṣiṇaḥ
jñeyākhyaṃ paramātmānaṃ viṣṇuṃ dhyāyan na sīdati
atulaṃ sukhadharmāṇaṃ vyomadehaṃ sanātanam
dharmādharmavinirmuktaṃ viṣṇuṃ dhyāyan na sīdati
vyāsādyair munibhiḥ sarvair dhyānayogaparāyaṇaiḥ
arcitaṃ bhāvakusumair viṣṇuṃ dhyāyan na sīdati
viṣṇvaṣṭakam idaṃ puṇyaṃ yogināṃ prītivardhanam
yaḥ paṭhet parayā prītyā sa gacched viṣṇusātmyatām
etat puṇyaṃ pāpaharaṃ dhanyaṃ duḥsvapnanāśanam
paṭhatāṃ śṛṇvatāṃ caiva viṣṇor māhātmyam uttamam
kurvan bhaktiṃ hṛṣīkeśe mānavo bhṛgunandana
nirvāṇaṃ samavāpnoti yādṛśaṃ tad vadasva me
tasyāpi karmābhiratā duḥkhabhājaḥ kathaṃ narāḥ
kaiś ca dānair jagatsvāmī svāmī nārāyaṇo nṛṇām
upakārāya bhaktānāṃ jāyate sa mahāmune
tvadyukto 'yam anupraśno mahārāja śṛṇuṣva tam
yathā pṛṣṭam idaṃ samyak kathyamānaṃ yathākhilam
pṛthivīṃ ratnasaṃpūrṇāṃ yaḥ kṛṣṇāya prayacchati
śrūyate ca purākhyāto rājoparicaro vasuḥ
iyāja subahūn yajñāñ śraddhāpūtena cetasā
sa vipraśāpād rājarṣiḥ kasmiṃścit kāraṇāntare
ākāśacārī sahasā praviveśa rasātalam
devānām eṣa yajñāṃśair yajvī pakṣavivardhanaḥ
cedirāḍ iti daityānāṃ matir āsīd rasātale
iti saṃmantrya te daityāś cedirājajighāṃsavaḥ
tatsamīpam anuprāptā gṛhītavividhāyudhāḥ
sa cāpi vasur āsīnaḥ keśavārpitamānasaḥ
jajāpa mantram oṃkāraṃ praṇavaṃ dvādaśākṣaram
