dadarśa ca sa viśveśaṃ dhyānāvasthitamānasaḥ
prāg īśam akṣaraṃ dhyānaṃ jñānaṃ jñeyaṃ jagadgurum
saṃcintya vāsudevākhyam anirdeśyaṃ parāyaṇam
brahmaviṣṇuśivānāṃ ca svarūpaiḥ saṃsthitaṃ tridhā
sthāvarānteṣu bhūteṣu sarveṣv eva samāsthitam
dikṣv ambaradharābhūbhṛt toyavāyvanalādiṣu
dṛśyādṛśyeṣu caiveśaṃ cintayām āsa pārthivaḥ
sarvaṃ ca tanmayaṃ dṛṣṭvā virarāma samādhitaḥ
indriyāṇīndriyārtheṣu pūrvavat sa narādhipaḥ
tān sa dṛṣṭvā gṛhītārghya ekaikasyaiva pārthivaḥ
pādyapūrveṇa vidhinā pūjayām āsa bhaktimān
prasādaṃ kuru bhadraṃ vo bhagavāñ jagataḥ patiḥ
vāsudevo bhavān prāpto mamānugrahakāmyayā
pūjayām āsa pādyādi nivedya vacasā tathā
te 'pi taṃ cedirājānaṃ papracchur asurās tadā
kva vāsudevo 'tra vayaṃ prāptā dākṣāyaṇīsutāḥ
praṇāmanamro rājendra sarvadarśī mahāmatiḥ
brahmādiṣu tṛṇānteṣu sa evaiko jagadguruḥ
ahaṃ bhavanto devādyā manuṣyāḥ paśavaś ca ye
tenaiva māyā vitatā vaiṣṇavī bhinnadarśanī
tayā svāṅgeṣu devo 'sau pradarśayati sarvaśaḥ
tataḥ purohitaṃ sarve kāvyaṃ nītiviśāradam
asmatpakṣakṣayāyaiṣa devānāṃ pakṣavardhanaḥ
svagocaram ariḥ prāptaḥ śatrupakṣopakārakaḥ
tasmāt pragṛhya divyāni sarvāstrāṇy amarārdanāḥ
kṛtaṃ na śakito hantuṃ niryatno 'pi hi pārthivaḥ
tapaso vā muniśreṣṭha vistarāt tad vadasva naḥ
sāsya rakṣā parā manye ko hinasty acyutāśrayam
kīrtitaḥ saṃsmṛto dhyātaḥ pūjitaḥ saṃstutas tathā
aihikāmuṣmikīṃ rakṣāṃ karoti bhagavān hariḥ
śarīrārogyam arthāṃś ca bhogāṃś caivānuṣaṅgikān
yad idaṃ cedirājānaṃ hantum icchatha dānavāḥ
tad asya keśavāc cittam upāyenāpanīyatām
tatas te tadvacaḥ śrutvā dānavāḥ kurupuṅgava
dadṛśus te mahātmānaṃ praṇataṃ cedipuṅgavam
kṛtapūjaṃ jagaddhātur vāsudevasya pārthivam
saṃstutāv udyataṃ śāntaṃ sarvatra samadarśinam
kṛṣṇārpitamanovṛttiṃ jānubhyām avaniṃgatam
tataḥ saṃśṛṇvatāṃ teṣāṃ tuṣṭāva madhusūdanam
tannāmasmaraṇodbhūta pulakaś cedipuṅgavaḥ
jagāda yaṃ sa rājarṣiḥ stavaṃ kṛṣṇasya śaunaka
śṛṇvatāṃ dānavendrāṇāṃ tan me pāpaharaṃ vada
śṛṇu yad devadevasya viṣṇor adbhutakarmaṇaḥ
stotraṃ jagāda rājāsau rasātalatalaṃ gataḥ
avṛddhikṣayam īśānam acyutaṃ parataḥ param
kalpanākṛtanāmānam anirdeśyam ajaṃ vibhum
mūlahetum ahetuṃ tvāṃ vāsudevaṃ namāmy aham
paramārthaparair īśaś cintyate yaḥ prajākaraiḥ
taṃ vāsudevam īśeśaṃ namāmy adya guṇaṃ param
jñeyaṃ jñātāram ajaraṃ bhoktāraṃ prakṛteḥ prabhum
puruṣasvarūpiṇaṃ devaṃ nato 'smi puruṣaṃ param
pradhānādiviśeṣānta svarūpam ajam avyayam
sthūlasūkṣmamayaṃ sarvaṃ vyāpinaṃ taṃ namāmy aham
sraṣṭā pālayitā cānte yaś ca saṃhārakārakaḥ
trayīmayaṃ taṃ triguṇaṃ nato 'smi puruṣottamam
vyaktarūpī ca taṃ devaṃ nato 'haṃ viṣṇum avyayam
tavāgnir āsaṃ vasudhāṅghriyugmaṃ nabhaḥ śiraś candraravī ca netre
namo hṛṣīkeśa tavāprameya namaś ca tubhyaṃ paramārthasāra
viṣṇo namas te 'stu parāpareśa kṛṣṇācyutānanta jagannivāsa
saṃhṛtya viśvaṃ jalaśāyine namo namaś ca te kaiṭabhasūdanāya
rudrāya cānte kṣayahetave te nato 'smi saṃhārakarāya viṣṇo
jitaṃ jitākṣāmalacittadṛśya carācarādhāra dharādhareḍya
yajñāśrayo yajñapumān aśeṣa deveśa martyāsurayajñabhoktaḥ
tvam īḍyamāno 'bhimataṃ dadāsi dharādhareśācyuta vāsudeva
kṛṣṇācyuta hṛṣīkeśa sarvabhūteśa keśava
mahātmaṃs trāhi māṃ bhaktaṃ vāsudeva prasīda me
iti stotrāvasāne taṃ cedirājaṃ tato 'surāḥ
jahasuḥ satalākṣepaṃ procuś ca dvijarūpiṇaḥ
prājñaḥ kila prajāpālaś cedirāṭ saṃśruto bhuvi
tas asya jñānam akhilaṃ viparītārtham īdṛśam
kva vāsudevaḥ kva bhavān imām antyāṃ daśāṃ gataḥ
yo bhavān vipraśāpena rasātalatalāśrayaḥ
bhaviṣyati smṛto devas trātā kila tavācyutaḥ
yo 'nyatras trāṇakāmo vā yajñabhāgam abhīpsate
yadā tvaṃ bhagavadbhakto vipraśāpān nipātitaḥ
śāpaṃ dadatsu vipreṣu paritrāṇaparo bhavet
na vayaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ nānantaṃ nācyutaṃ harim
saṃśritā na ca sīdāmaḥ svapauruṣam upāśritāḥ
tadāśrayasva svaṃ vīryaṃ parityajya vimūḍhatām
ity udīritam ākarṇya sa teṣāṃ cedipuṅgavaḥ
ajñānapaṭalacchannān hṛdayena śuśoca tān
yena sarveśvare viṣṇāv eteṣām āvṛtā matiḥ
prakāśaṃ ca sa tān āha dānavān prītipūrvakam
pāpatas tatparitrāṇaṃ cikīrṣur vasudhādhipaḥ
saṃsārābdhau manuṣyāṇām ekaḥ poto janārdanaḥ
sukhaduḥkhamayo nRṇāṃ vipākaḥ karmaṇāṃ ca yaḥ
parīkṣāṃ ca jagannāthaḥ karoty adṛḍhacetasām
narāṇām arthavidhvaṃsa nikāśeṣu janārdanaḥ
alpayatnena cāyānti vimuktiṃ keśavāśrayāt
yadā janārdane bhaktiṃ vahan sīdati mānavaḥ
nirviṇṇacetāḥ śaithilyaṃ manasaḥ kurute tadā
devānāṃ mahatī śaṅkā bhaktiyuktā janārdane
satyaṃ śatena vighnānāṃ sahasreṇa tathā tapaḥ
svaṃ cāpi karma puruṣaḥ śubhāśubham upāgatam
maryādāṃ ca kṛtāṃ tena yo bhinatti sa mānavaḥ
brāhmaṇā devadevena mukhāt sṛṣṭā mahātmanā
devānām api saṃpūjya bhūmidevā dvijottamāḥ
anuvṛttiḥ sadā kāryā teṣāṃ varṇair anuvrataiḥ
te pūjyās te namaskāryās toṣaṇīyāś ca yatnataḥ
teṣu tuṣṭeṣv aśeṣāṇāṃ devānāṃ prītir uttamā
teṣāṃ mayā yad ajñānāj jñānād vā kṛtam apriyam
tenāpi tuṣṭa evāhaṃ viṣṇor aṃśā dvijottamāḥ
kriyāvān mama poto 'yaṃ bhūtalād yo rasātale
rasātalatalottāraṃ na hi vāñchāmy ahaṃ dvijāḥ
saṃsāragartād uttāraṃ vṛṇomy ārādhanād dhareḥ
yathāhaṃ nābhivāñchāmi bhogān ārādhya keśavam
yathā na mātā na pitā nātmā na suhṛdaḥ sutāḥ
kṛṣṇālāpāt priyatarās tathā māṃ pātu keśavaḥ
yathā viṣṇumayaṃ sarvam etat paśyāmy ahaṃ jagat
tathā mama manodoṣān aśeṣān sa vyapohatu
jātā viṣṇuvilomeṣu bhavatsv api dayā mama
yathā nāhaṃ bhavaddveṣān na saṃharṣād bravīmy aham
evam uccārite teṣāṃ daityānāṃ tatkṣaṇāt tathā
svarūpadhāriṇaś cainaṃ praṇamyāsurapuṅgavāḥ
pratyūcuḥ pārthivaṃ viṣṇu bhaktaṃ sadbrahmacāriṇam
saṃsāre tvatsamaiḥ saṅgaḥ puṇyabhājāṃ pravartate
vayaṃ svajātidoṣeṇa devapakṣavirodhinaḥ
viṣṇudhyānamahārakṣā kakṣāntaragataḥ prabho
vaiphalyam atipuṇyeṣu viṣṇuśuśrūṣaṇā nṛṇām
diṣṭyā krodhābhibhūtānām asmākaṃ tvannivarhaṇe
matir jātā yataḥ prāptā tvatsaṅgād durlabhā matiḥ
kuruṣva ca prasādaṃ tvaṃ praṇatānāṃ nareśvara
śatrāv api kṛpāśīlaṃ yan no duṣṭam abhūn manaḥ
diśāṃ vaimalyaṃ vimalaṃ cakṣuṣaś copapāditam
bhavatā duṣṭatāṃ etām āsurīm apamārjatā
duṣṭāḥ sma varṣapūgāni yad yātāni vṛthaiva naḥ
viṣayākṣiptacittānāṃ kṛṣṇe bhaktim akurvatām
karmabhūmau manuṣyāṇāṃ tad eva viphalaṃ dinam
yad acyutakathālāpa dhyānārcārahitaṃ gatam
ity uktvā te 'surā bhūyaḥ prasādya ca tathā vasum
viṣṇau bhaktiparā yātās tīvrasaṃyogino 'layan
sa cāpi cedirāṭ tasmād devadevena cakriṇā
pātālād uddhṛtaḥ paścāt saṃsāragahanād api
ity etat sarvam ākhyātaṃ yan māṃ tvaṃ paripṛcchasi
dṛḍhā janārdane bhaktir yadaivāvyabhicāriṇī
ity etad asuraiḥ sārdhaṃ saṃvādaṃ yaḥ purā vasoḥ
praṇipatyāham etaṃ tvāṃ yat pṛcchāmi tad ucyatām
yair upāyaiḥ pradānair vā narāṇām amarārcitaḥ
prītimān puṇḍarīkākṣo bhavaty ācakṣva tan mama
vidharmeṣu na vartante prītimāṃs teṣu keśavaḥ
brahmacārigṛhasthādyā na cyavanty āśramāc ca ye
svadharmato haris teṣāṃ prītimān eva sarvadā
tyaktagrāmyādisaṃgāś ca teṣu prītiḥ parā hareḥ
dātāro nāpahartāraḥ parasvānām amāyinaḥ
ye narās teṣu govindaḥ putreṣv iva sadā hitaḥ
yeṣāṃ narāṇāṃ na matir jihvā vāsatyam ujjhati
te priyā vāsudevasya ye ca dvijaparāyaṇāḥ
karmaṇā manasā vācā ye na hiṃsānuvartinaḥ
te narā vāsudevasya priyāḥ pāṇḍukulodvaha
brahmādyaṃ sthāvarāntaṃ ca bhūtagrāmaṃ janārdanāt
ye ca paśyanty abhedena te viṣṇoḥ satataṃ priyāḥ
devavedadvijātīnāṃ nindāyāṃ ye na mānavāḥ
prītibhājo bhavantīṣṭās te sadā śārṅgadhanvinaḥ
priyāṇām atha sarveṣāṃ devadevasya sa priyaḥ
tasmāt priyatvaṃ kṛṣṇasya vāñchatā nijadharmajaiḥ
guṇair ātmā sadā yojyo na dūre guṇino hariḥ
yeṣāṃ na gṛddhiḥ pārakye dāre dravye ca cetasaḥ
hiṃsāyāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ te kṛṣṇenāvalokitāḥ
vedāḥ pramāṇaṃ smṛtayo yeṣāṃ sanmārgasevinām
paropakārasaktānāṃ te kṛṣṇenāvalokitāḥ
kalikalmaṣadoṣeṇa yeṣāṃ nopahatā matiḥ
pāṣaṇḍānugatā naiva te kṛṣṇenāvalokitāḥ
na vivitsāsamudbhūtas te kṛṣṇenāvalokitāḥ
svapantaḥ saṃsthitā yāntas tiṣṭhantaś ca janārdanam
ye cintayanty avirataṃ te kṛṣṇenāvalokitāḥ
yathātmani tathāpatye yeṣāṃ adrohiṇī matiḥ
samastasattvajāteṣu te kṛṣṇenāvalokitāḥ
ye kurvanti narā viddhi te kṛṣṇenāvalokitāḥ
devān pitRṃs tathāpannān atithīñ jāmayo 'dhvagān
taṃ vijānīhi bhartavyaṃ devadevasya śārṅginaḥ
kurvann ālakṣyatām eti keśavenāvalokitaḥ
nātmasaṃstavam anyeṣāṃ na nindāṃ cārthalipsayā
karoti puruṣavyāghra yasya nārāyaṇo hṛdi
sarvabhūtadayāṃ satyam akrodhaṃ dharmaśīlatām
narāṇāṃ jāyate rājan govinde hṛdayasthite
kṣamāṃ karoti kruddheṣu dayāṃ mūḍheṣu mānavaḥ
tadā kuruvaraśreṣṭha naraḥ kṛṣṇena vīkṣitaḥ
putradāragṛhakṣetra dravyāder mamatāṃ naraḥ
nāyāsyati jagannāthe hṛṣīkeśe parāṅmukhe
kalau kṛtayugaṃ teṣāṃ kleśās teṣāṃ sukhādhikāḥ
yeṣāṃ śarīragrahaṇe hariśuśrūṣaṇe matiḥ
yadā necchati pāpāni yadā puṇyāni vāñchati
jñeyas tadā manuṣyeṇa hṛdaye 'sya hariḥ sthitaḥ
paramārthe matiḥ puṃsām asāre tu bhavārṇave
śraddadhāno dayāśīlaḥ samaloṣṭāśmakāñcanaḥ
parārthe mānavaḥ kṛṣṇe prasanne nṛpa jāyate
vahato 'pi sadā kṛṣṇe bhaktim avyabhicāriṇīm
pāṇiṣv asamadṛgbuddheḥ sulabho naiva keśavaḥ
kāmalobhāśritaṃ yeṣāṃ cittaṃ krodhādidūṣitam
teṣāṃ janmasahasre 'pi na matiḥ keśavāśrayā
heyāṃ kṛṣṇāśrayāṃ vṛttiṃ manyante hetusaṃśritāḥ
aviyopahatajñānā ye 'jñāne jñānamāninaḥ
vedavādavirodhena kūṭayuktim apāśritāḥ
mānuṣaṃ taṃ manuṣyatve manyamānāḥ kubuddhayaḥ
karmāṇi ye 'sya nindanti na teṣāṃ niṣkṛtir nṛṇām
tiryaktvaṃ cāpare viṣṇuṃ māyayā tasya mohitāḥ
devatvam api kṛṣṇasya yasya nindā mahātmanaḥ
stutiṃ tasya kathaṃ śaktāḥ kartum īśasya mānavāḥ
vyāpitvaṃ śāśvatatvaṃ ca janmabhāvavivarjitam
sarveśvareśvaraḥ kṛṣṇaḥ procyate yadi paṇḍitaḥ
nindāpi tasya na nṛbhiḥ kartum īśasya śakyate
yadā kāṇāś ca kūṇṭhāś ca mūḍho durbuddhir āturaḥ
sraṣṭā pālayitā hartā jagato 'sya jagac ca saḥ
yaṣṭā yājayitā yājyaḥ sa eva bhagavān hariḥ
dātā dānaṃ tathādātā kartā kāryaṃ tathā kriyāḥ
hantā ghātayitā hiṃsyo hāryaṃ hartā ca yaḥ svayam
sarvakāraṇabhūtasya tasyeśasya mahātmanaḥ
kaḥ karoti stutiṃ viṣṇor nindāṃ vā pṛthivīpate
śakyate sarvabhūtatvāc cokṣācokṣasvarūpiṇā
stuteḥ pādād yato nānyad utkṛṣṭam upalabhyate
tasyāpy uccāraṇeneśo na stotuṃ śakyate hariḥ
yato 'taḥ sarvabhūtasya kā nindā tasya kā stutiḥ
yena sarvātmanā tatra hṛdayaṃ saṃniveśitam
kuru viṣṇuṃ ca hṛdaye sarvavyāpinam īśvaram
viṣṇor evaṃ priyatvaṃ tvam āśu yāsyasi pārthiva
tam īśvareśvaraṃ viṣṇuṃ hṛdaye saṃniveśaya
tam īśvareśvaraṃ viṣṇuṃ hṛdaye kuru pārthiva
eṣa śāstrārthasadbhāvaḥ kim uktair bahuvistaraiḥ
taṃ taṃ cintaya govindaṃ manasaḥ sthairyakāraṇāt
yathāgnisaṃgāt kanakam apadoṣaṃ prajāyate
saṃśliṣṭaṃ vāsudevena manuṣyāṇāṃ tathā manaḥ
bhūyaś ca śṛṇu rājendra yaj jagāda janārdanaḥ
nāgaparyaṅkaśayane pṛṣṭaḥ kṣīrābdhikanyayā
purā śayānaṃ govindaṃ prāvṛṭkāle mahodadhau
śeṣabhogimahābhoge vīcyambukaṇaśītale
śrīvatsavkṣasaṃ lakṣmīḥ karasaṃvāhanādṛtā
ananyāsaktadṛṣṭiṃ ca kim apy ekāgramānasam
papraccha puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ puṇḍarīkakarā harim
sṛṣṭaṃ jagad idaṃ sarvaṃ bahuśaś copasaṃhṛtam
devān manuṣyān gandharvān yakṣavidyādharāsurān
sṛṣṭvā sṛṣṭān nirghṛṇatvād upasaṃharate bhavān
kaścid eteṣu bhūteṣu devādiṣu tavācyuta
tathāpi guṇagṛhyo 'haṃ pratyekahṛdayasthitaḥ
puṇyāpuṇyakṛtau teṣu prītidveṣau śubhe mama
dveṣānubhāvenāpuṇyaṃ phaladaṃ teṣu bhāmini
śrūyatāṃ ca mahābhāge nareṣu śubhacāriṣu
satataṃ yeṣu me prītis tathāprītir varānane
pralayotpattitattvajñā ātmajñānaparāś ca ye
ete svakarmaṇā bhadre mama prītipathaṃ gatāḥ
vāṅmanaḥkāyikīṃ hiṃsāṃ ye na kurvanti kutracit
svakīyadravyasaṃtuṣṭā nivṛttāś cauryakarmaṇaḥ
satyaśīladayāyuktā narā mama sadā priyāḥ
mātṛsvasṛsutātulyān paradārāṃś ca ye narāḥ
manyante te ca me lakṣmi dṛḍhaṃ priyatamāḥ sadā
na kāmān na ca saṃrambhān na dveṣād ye ca bhāmini
viśvāsyāḥ sarvabhūtānām ahiṃsrāś ca dayālavaḥ
tyaktānṛtakathā devi manuṣyā dayitā mama
dharmalabdhāṃs tu ye bhogān bhuñjate nātikīkaṭāḥ
yeṣāṃ matir manuṣyāṇāṃ te 'tīva dayitā mama
dharmalabdheṣu dāreṣu ṛtukālābhigāminaḥ
pararandhreṣu jātyandhāḥ paradāreṣv apuṃsakāḥ
parāpavāde ye mūkā dayitās te narā mama
parāpavādaṃ nindāṃ ca paramarmāvaghaṭṭanam
satyāṃ ślakṣṇāṃ nirābādhāṃ madhurāṃ prītidāyinīm
ye vācam īrayanti sma te manuṣyā mama priyāḥ
sākṣād devam ivāyāntaṃ yā patiṃ nityam arcati
pādaśaucādibhir nārī tasyā nāhaṃ sudurlabhaḥ
pūrṇacandram ivodyataṃ bhartāraṃ yā gṛhāgatam
hṛṣṭā paśyati tāṃ viddhi dayitāṃ yoṣitaṃ mama
śrutismṛtyuditaṃ dharmaṃ manasāpi na ye narāḥ
brahmarūpadharasyāsyān mama vedā viniḥsṛtāḥ
manvādirūpiṇaś caiva samastāḥ smṛtayaḥ smṛtāḥ
śrutiḥ smṛtir mamaivājñā tām ullaṅghya yajec chubhe
sarvasvenāpi māṃ devi nāpnoty ājñāvighātakṛt
etad devi mayākhyātaṃ yat pṛṣṭo 'ham iha tvayā
priyāṇāṃ mama sarveṣāṃ śṛṇu yo 'titaraṃ priyaḥ
brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vaiśyaḥ śūdraś ca varavarṇini
vāṅmanaḥkarmabhiḥ śānto dayitaḥ satataṃ mama
evaṃ śrīr devadevena prāg uktā harimedhasā
tavāpi hi naraśreṣṭha yathāvat kathitaṃ mayā
yaḥ śṛṇoti sa pāpebhyaḥ samastebhyaḥ pramucyate
samyagārādhanāyālaṃ kriyāyogaṃ bravīhi me
yat phalaṃ keśavasyārcāṃ pratiṣṭhāpya labhen naraḥ
yac ca devakulaṃ viṣṇoḥ kārayitvā phalaṃ labhet
yad dīpadhūpapuṣpāṇāṃ gandhānāṃ ca nivedane
dhvajādidāne yat puṇyaṃ yat puṇyaṃ gītavādite
tathā pavitrapaṭhane jayaśabdādyudīraṇe
saṃmārjanādau yat puṇyaṃ namaskāre pradakṣiṇe
śīrṇasphuṭitasaṃskāra karaṇe cāpi yat phalam
teṣāṃ phalaṃ ca yat kṛtsnaṃ tan mamācakṣva vistarāt
saṃkṣepāt pūrvam evaitad bhavataḥ kathitaṃ mayā
vistareṇa mahārāja śrūyatāṃ bruvato mama
aditir nāma devānāṃ mātā paramaduścaram
tapaś cacāra varṣāṇāṃ sahasraṃ pṛthivīpate
ārādhanāya kṛṣṇasya vāgyatā vāyubhojanā
daityair nirākṛtān dṛṣṭvā tanayān kurunandana
vṛthāputrāham asmīti nirvedāt praṇatā harim
tuṣṭāva vāgbhir iṣṭābhiḥ paramārthāvabodhinī
devadaityanṛpaśvāpa vyomavāyvādirūpiṇam
śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ viṣṇuṃ praṇatā bhaktavatsalam
namaḥ smṛtārtināśāya namaḥ puṣkaramāline
namaḥ paramakalyāṇa kalyāṇāyādivedhase
namaḥ paṅkajanetrāya namaḥ paṅkajanābhaye
namaḥ paṅkajasaṃbhūti saṃbhavāyātmayonaye
śriyaḥ kāntāya dāntāya dāntadṛśyāya cakriṇe
namaḥ śaṅkhāsihastāya namaḥ kanakaretase
tathātmajñānavijñāna yogacittātmayogine
nirguṇāya viśeṣāya haraye brahmarūpiṇe
jagat pratiṣṭhitaṃ yatra jagatā yo na dṛśyate
namaḥ sthūlātisūkṣmāya tasmai devāya śaṅkhine
ādyaḥ prajāpatipatir yaḥ pitRṇāṃ paraḥ patiḥ
patiḥ surāṇāṃ yas tasmai namaḥ kṛṣṇāya vedhase
yaś cintyamāno manasā sadyaḥ pāpaṃ vyapohati
yaṃ praviśyākhilādhāram īśānam ajam avyayam
taṃ yajñapuruṣaṃ viṣṇuṃ namāmi prabhum īśvaram
yas tasmai vedavedyāya viṣṇave jiṣṇave namaḥ
yato viśvaṃ samudbhūtaṃ yasmiṃś ca layam eṣyati
māyāṃ nālaṃ samuttartuṃ tam upendraṃ namāmy aham
yam ārādhya viśuddhena manasā karmaṇā girā
viṣādatoṣaroṣādyair yo 'jasraṃ sukhaduḥkhajaiḥ
viśvaṃ viśvapatiṃ viṣṇuṃ taṃ namāmi prajāpatim
rātrijaṃ sūryarūpī ca tam upendraṃ namāmy aham
kapilādisvarūpastho yaś cājñānamayaṃ tamaḥ
yasyākṣiṇī candrasūryau sarvalokaśubhāśubham
nānṛtaṃ tam ajaṃ viṣṇuṃ namāmi prabhavāvyayam
satyena tena sakalāḥ pūryantāṃ me manorathāḥ
adṛśyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ tasyāḥ saṃdarśane sthitaḥ
tāṃs tān prāpsyasi dharmajñe matprasādād asaṃśayam
śṛṇuṣva ca mahābhāge varaṃ yas te hṛdi sthitaḥ
taṃ prayacchāmi niyataṃ mātra kāryā vicāraṇā
hṛtarājyo hṛtaś cāsya yajñabhāgo mahāsuraiḥ
hṛtaṃ rājyaṃ na duḥkhāya mama putrasya keśava
sapatnād āyatibhraṃśo bādhāṃ naḥ kurute hṛdi
svāṃśena caiva te garbhe saṃbhaviṣyāmi kaśyapāt
tān ahaṃ nihaniṣyāmi nirvṛtā bhava nandini
nāhaṃ tvām udareṇeśa voḍhuṃ śakṣyāmi keśava
yasmin pratiṣṭhitaṃ viśvaṃ yo viśvaṃ svayam īśvara
tad ahaṃ nodareṇa tvāṃ voḍhuṃ śakṣyāmi durdharam
pratiṣṭhitaṃ na māṃ śaktā voḍhuṃ sendrā divaukasaḥ
kintv ahaṃ sakalāṃl lokān sadevāsuramānuṣān
jaṅgamājaṅgamaṃ sarvaṃ tvāṃ ca devi sakāśyapām
dākṣāyaṇi prasādaṃ te karomy anyaiḥ sudurlabham
tejasas tasya hāniṃ ca kariṣye mā vyathāṃ kṛtāḥ
evam uktvā tataḥ sadyo gato 'ntardhānam īśvaraḥ
garbhasthite tataḥ kṛṣṇe cacāla sakalā kṣitiḥ
cakampire mahāśailā jagmuḥ kṣobham athābdhayaḥ
tatas tataḥ kṣitiḥ khedān nanāma vasudhādhipa
babhūva tejaso hānir yathoktaṃ parameṣṭhinā
nistejaso 'surān dṛṣṭvā samastān asureśvaraḥ
duriṣṭaṃ kiṃ nu daityānāṃ kiṃ kṛtyā vairinirmitā
nāśāyaiṣāṃ samudbhūtā yena nistejaso 'surāḥ
ity āsuravaras tena pṛṣṭaḥ pautreṇa pārthiva
ciraṃ dhyātvā jagādedam asurendraṃ tadā balim
sadyaḥ samudrāḥ kṣubhitā daityā nistejasaḥ kṛtāḥ
sūryādayo yathā pūrvaṃ tathā gacchanti na grahāḥ
devānāṃ ca parā lakṣmīḥ kāraṇair anumīyate
mahad etan mahābāho kāraṇaṃ dānaveśvara
ity uktvā dānavapatiṃ prahrādaḥ so 'surottamaḥ
sa dhyānapathagaṃ kṛtvā prahrādaḥ svaṃ mano 'suraḥ
sa dadarśodare 'dityāḥ prahrādo vāmanākṛtim
sādhyān viśve tathādityān gandharvoragarākṣasān
jambhaṃ kujambhaṃ narakaṃ bāṇam anyāṃs tathāsurān
ātmānam urvīgaganaṃ vāyum ambho hutāśanam
samudrādridrumasarit sarāṃsi paśavo mṛgān
vayomanuṣyān akhilāṃs tathaiva ca sarīsṛpān
samastalokasraṣṭāraṃ brahmāṇaṃ bhavam eva ca
grahanakṣatratārāś ca dakṣādyāṃś ca prajāpatīn
saṃpaśyan vismayāviṣṭaḥ prakṛtisthaḥ kṣaṇāt punaḥ
prahrādaḥ prāha daityendraṃ baliṃ vairocaniṃ tadā
vatsa jñātaṃ mayā sarvaṃ yadarthaṃ bhavatām iyam
tejaso hānir utpannā tac chṛṇu tvam aśeṣataḥ
parāparāṇāṃ paramaḥ paraḥ paravatām api
prabhuḥ pramāṇaṃ mānānāṃ saptalokaguror guruḥ
sthitiṃ kartuṃ jagannāthaḥ so 'dityā garbhatāṃ gataḥ
prabhuḥ prabhūṇām paramaḥ parāṇām anādimadhyo bhagavān anantaḥ
trailokyam aṃśena sanātham eṣa kartuṃ mahātmāditijo 'vatīrṇaḥ
jānanti daityādhipa yat svarūpaṃ sa vāsudevaḥ kalayāvatīrṇaḥ
yo 'sau kalāṃśena nṛsiṃharūpī jaghāna pūrvaṃ pitaram aśeṣaḥ
yaḥ sarvayogīśamanonivāsaḥ sa vāsudevaḥ kalayāvatīrṇaḥ
yam akṣaraṃ vedavido viditvā viśanti taṃ jñānavidhūtapāpāḥ
vijñāyate sarvapitāmahādyais taṃ vāsudevaṃ praṇamāmy acintyam
rūpasya cakṣur grahaṇe tvag eṣā sparśagrahītrī rasanā rasasya
śrotraṃ ca śabdagrahaṇe narāṇāṃ ghrāṇaṃ ca gandhagrahaṇe niyuktam
na ghrāṇacakṣuḥśravaṇādibhir yaḥ sarveśvaro veditum avyayātmā
śakyas tam īḍyaṃ manasaiva devaṃ grāhyaṃ nato 'haṃ harim īśitāram
yenaikadaṃṣṭrāgrasamuddhṛteyaṃ dharācalā dhārayatīha sarvam
grastvā sa śete sakalaṃ jagad yas tam īḍyam īśaṃ praṇato 'smi viṣṇum
aṃśāvatīrṇena ca yena garbhe hṛtāni tejāṃsi mahāsurāṇām
namāmi taṃ devam anantam īśam aśeṣasaṃsārataroḥ kuṭhāram
devo jagadyonir ayaṃ mahātmā sa ṣoḍaśāṃśena mahāsurendra
surendramātur jaṭharaṃ praviṣṭo hṛtāni vas tena bale vapūṃṣi
santi me śataśo daityā vāsudevabalādhikāḥ
vipracittiḥ śibiḥ śaṅkur ayaḥśaṅkus tathaiva ca
ayaḥśirā aśvaśirā bhaṅgakāro mahāhanuḥ
pratāpī praghasaḥ śaṃbhuḥ kurkurākṣaś ca durjayaḥ
mahābalā mahāvīryā bhūbhāradharaṇakṣamāḥ
yeṣām ekaikaśaḥ kṛṣṇo na vīryārdhena saṃmitaḥ
dhig dhig ity āha sa baliṃ vaikuṇṭhākṣepavādinam
vināśam upayāsyanti manye daiteyadānavāḥ
yeṣāṃ tvam īdṛśo rājā durbuddhir avivekavān
devadevaṃ mahābhāgaṃ vāsudevam ajaṃ vibhum
tvām ṛte pāpasaṃkalpaṃ ko 'nya evaṃ vadiṣyati
ya ete bhavatā proktāḥ samastā daityadānavāḥ
sabrahmakās tathā devāḥ sthāvarāntāś ca bhūtayaḥ
tvaṃ cāhaṃ ca jagac cedaṃ sādridrumanadīnadam
samudradvīpalokāś ca yac ceṅgaṃ yac ca neṅgati
ekāṃśāṃśakalājanma kas tam evaṃ pravakṣyati
ṛte vināśābhimukhaṃ tvām ekam avivekinam
durbuddhim ajitātmānaṃ vṛddhānāṃ śāsanātigam
yasya tvam īdṛśaḥ putro devadevāvamanyakaḥ
tiṣṭhatv anekasaṃsāra saṃhṛtāghavināśanī
kṛṣṇe bhaktir ahaṃ tāvad avekṣyo bhavato na kim
na me priyataraḥ kṛṣṇād api deho 'yam ātmanaḥ
iti jānāty ayaṃ loko bhavāṃś ca ditijādhamaḥ
mamāpi sarvajagatāṃ gurur nārāyaṇo guruḥ
nindāṃ karoṣi tasmiṃs tvaṃ kṛṣṇe guruguror gurau
yasmāt tasmād ihaiśvaryād acirād bhraṃśam eṣyasi
mā devo mā jagannātho bale māsau janārdanaḥ
nāpekṣitā vayaṃ yasmāt tasmāc chāpaṃ dadāmi te
yathā me śirasaś chedād idaṃ gurutaraṃ bale
yathā na kṛṣṇād aparaṃ paritrāṇaṃ bhavārṇave
prasādayām āsa guruṃ praṇipatya puṇaḥ punaḥ
rājyabhraṃśaṃ vasubhraṃśaṃ saṃprāpsyāmīti na tv aham
viṣaṇṇo 'smi yathā tāta tavaivāvinaye kṛte
saṃsāre durlabhās tāta guravo ye bhavadvidhāḥ
tvatkopahetuduṣṭo 'haṃ paritapye na śāpataḥ
yadi mohena me jñānaṃ nākṣiptaṃ syān mahāsura
tat kathaṃ sarvagaṃ jñānan hariṃ kaṃcic chāpāmy aham
bhāvyam etena nūnaṃ te tasmāt tvaṃ mā viṣīdathāḥ
bhavethā bhaktimān īśaḥ sa te trātā bhaviṣyati
śāpaṃ prāpya ca māṃ vīra saṃsmarethāḥ smṛtas tvayā
tathā tathā yatiṣyāmi śreyasā yokṣyate yathā
ajāyata sa govindo bhagavān vāmanākṛtiḥ
avatīrṇe jagannāthe tasmin sarvam aśīśamat
yad āsuram abhūd duḥkhaṃ devānām adites tathā
vavur vātāḥ sukhasparśā nīrajaskam abhūn nabhaḥ
dharme ca sarvabhūtānāṃ tadā matir ajāyata
nodvegaś cāpy abhūd dehe manujānāṃ janeśvara
tathā hi sarvabhūtānāṃ bhūmyambaradivaukasām
taṃ jātamātraṃ bhagavān brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ
jātakarmādikāḥ kṛtvā kriyās tuṣṭāva pārthiva
paramārthārtha sarvajña jñāna jñeyātmaniḥsṛta
jayāśeṣajagatsākṣiñ jaya kartar jagadguroḥ
jayākhila jayāśeṣa jayākhilahṛdi sthita
mumukṣubhir anirdeśya svayaṃdṛṣṭa jayeśvara
yogibhir muktiphalada damādiguṇabhūṣaṇaiḥ
jaya sthūlātisūkṣma tvaṃ jayātīndriya sendriya
jaya svamāyāyogastha śeṣabhogaśayākṣara
jayaikadaṃṣṭrāprāntānta nṛkesariñ jayārāti
vakṣaḥsthalavidāraṇa sāṃprataṃ jaya viśvātman
māyāvāmana keśava
tvayy eṣā jagatām īśa saṃsthitā dharmapaddhatiḥ
na tvām ahaṃ na ceśāno nendrādyās tridaśā hare
jñātum īśā na munayaḥ sanakādyā na yoginaḥ
kas tvāṃ vetsyati sarveśaṃ tvatprasādaṃ vinā naraḥ
tad īśvareśvareśāna vibho vardhasva bhāvana
prabhāvāyāsya viśvasya viśvātman pṛthulocana
evaṃ stuto hṛṣīkeśaḥ sa tadā vāmanākṛtiḥ
bhūyaś cāhaṃ stuto 'dityā tasyāś cāpi pratiśrutam
yathā śakrāya dāsyāmi trailokyaṃ hatakaṇṭakam
so 'haṃ tathā kariṣyāmi yathendro jagataḥ patiḥ
tataḥ kṛṣṇājinaṃ brahmā hṛṣīkeśāya dattavān
āṣāḍham adadad daṇḍaṃ marīcir brahmaṇaḥ sutaḥ
kamaṇḍaluṃ vasiṣṭhaś ca kauśyaṃ vedam athāṅgirāḥ
akṣasūtraṃ ca pulahaḥ pulastyaḥ sitavāsasī
upatasthuś ca taṃ vedāḥ praṇavasvarabhūṣaṇāḥ
śāstrāṇy aśeṣāṇi tathā sāṃkhyayogoktayaś ca yāḥ
sa vāmano jaṭī daṇḍī chattrī dhṛtakamaṇḍaluḥ
dadāti bhūmir vivaraṃ tatra tatrātipīḍitā
sābdhidvīpavatīṃ sarvāṃ cālayām āsa medinīm
tataḥ saṃśayam āpannāḥ sarve daiteyadānavāḥ
saparvatavanām urvīṃ dṛṣṭvā saṃkṣubhitāṃ baliḥ
papracchośanasaṃ śukraṃ praṇipatya kṛtāñjaliḥ
ācārya kṣobham āyāti sābdhibhūbhṛddharā mahī
kasmāc ca nāsurān bhāgān pratigṛhṇanti vahnayaḥ
iti pṛṣṭo 'tha balinā kāvyo vedavidāṃ varaḥ
uvāca daityādhipatiṃ ciraṃ dhyātvā mahāmatiḥ
avatīrṇo jagadyoniḥ kaśyapasya gṛhe hariḥ
vāmaneneha rūpeṇa paramātmā sanātanaḥ
sa nūnaṃ yajñam āyāti tava dānavapuṅgava
tatpadanyāsavikṣobhād iyaṃ pracalitā mahī
kampante girayaś cāmī kṣubhitā makarālayāḥ
nainaṃ bhūtapatiṃ bhūmiḥ samarthā voḍhum īśvaram
anenaiva dhṛtā bhūmir āpo 'gniḥ pavano nabhaḥ
dhārayaty akhilān deva manuṣyādīn mahāsura
iyam asya jagaddhātur māyā kṛṣṇasya gahvarī
dhāryadhārakabhāvena yayā saṃpiṇḍitaṃ jagat
tatsaṃnidhānād asurā na bhāgārhāḥ suradviṣaḥ
bhuñjate cāsurān bhāgān amī te na tavāgnayaḥ
śukrasya vacanaṃ śrutvā hṛṣṭaromābravīd baliḥ
yaṃ yoginaḥ sadodyuktāḥ paramātmānam avyayam
tam adhvareśvaraṃ viṣṇuṃ mattaḥ ko 'nya upaiṣyati
sarveśvareśvare viṣṇau mamādhvaram upāgate
yan mayā cārya kartavyaṃ tan mamādeṣṭum arhasi
yajñabhāgabhujo devā vedaprāmāṇyato 'sura
tvayā tu dānavā daityā yajñabhāgabhujaḥ kṛtāḥ
nisṛṣṭeś cāyam ante ca svayam atti prajāḥ prabhuḥ
tvayānubandhī bhavitā nūnaṃ viṣṇuḥ sthitau sthitaḥ
pratijñā naiva voḍhavyā vācyaṃ sāma tathāphalam
nālaṃ dātuṃ dhanaṃ devety evaṃ vācyaṃ tu yācataḥ
kṛṣṇasya devabhūtyarthaṃ pravṛttasya mahāsura
brahman katham ahaṃ brūyām anyenāpi hi yācitaḥ
nāstīti kimu devena saṃsārāghaughahāriṇā
yadartham upahārāḍhyā damaśaucaguṇānvitaiḥ
yajñāḥ kriyante deveśaḥ sa māṃ dehīti vakṣyati
tat sādhu sukṛtaṃ karma tapaḥ sucaritaṃ ca naḥ
yan mayā dattam īśeśaḥ svayam ādāsyate hariḥ
nāstīty ahaṃ guro vakṣye tam apy āgatam īśvaram
yajñe 'smin yadi yajñeśo yācate māṃ janārdanaḥ
nāstīti yan mayā noktam anyeṣām api yācatām
ślāghya eva hi dhīrāṇāṃ dānād āpatsamāgamaḥ
nābādhākāri yad dānaṃ tad aṅgamalavat katham
madrājye nāsukhī kaścin na daridro na cāturaḥ
hṛṣṭatuṣṭaḥ sugandhī ca tṛptaḥ sarvasukhānvitaḥ
janaḥ sarvo mahābhāga kimutāhaṃ sadā sukhī
etad viśiṣṭapātrotthaṃ dānabījaphalaṃ mama
viditaṃ bhṛguśārdūla mayaitat tvatprasādataḥ
janārdane mahāpātre kiṃ na prāptaṃ tato mayā
matto dānam avāpyeśo yadi puṣṇāti devatāḥ
upabhogānvayaguṇaṃ dānaṃ ślāghyataraṃ tataḥ
matprasādaparo nūnaṃ yajñenārādhito hariḥ
tenābhyeti na saṃdeho darśanād upakārakṛt
māṃ nihantum ato 'pi syād vadhaḥ ślāghyataro 'cyutāt
sa māṃ yācitum abhyeti nānugraham ṛte hariḥ
yaḥ sṛjaty ātmabhūḥ sarvaṃ cetasaivāpahanti ca
sa māṃ hantuṃ hṛṣīkeśaḥ kathaṃ yatnaṃ kariṣyati
taṃ dṛṣṭvā yajñavāṭāntaḥ praviṣṭam asurāḥ prabhum
jagmuḥ prabhāvataḥ kṣobhaṃ tejasā tasya niṣprabhāḥ
tataḥ saṃkṣobham āpanno na kaścit kiṃcid uktavān
pratyeko devadeveśaṃ pūjayām āsa cetasā
athāsurapatiṃ prahvaṃ dṛṣṭvā munivarāṃś ca tān
devadevapatiḥ sākṣād viṣṇur vāmanarūpadhṛk
tuṣṭāva yajñaṃ vahniṃś ca yajamānam atha rtvijaḥ
tataḥ prasannam akhilaṃ vāmanaṃ prati tatkṣaṇāt
yajñavāṭasthitaṃ vīraṃ sādhu sādhv ity udīrayan
sa cārgham ādāya baliḥ prodbhūtapulakas tadā
pūjayām āsa govindaṃ prāha cedaṃ vaco 'suraḥ
suvarṇaratnasaṃghātaṃ gajāśvam amitaṃ tathā
striyo vastrāṇy alaṃkārān gāvo grāmāṃś ca puṣkalān
sarvasvaṃ sakalām urvīṃ bhavato vā yad īpsitam
tad dadāmi vṛṇuṣva tvaṃ mamārthī satataṃ priyaḥ
prāha sasmitagambhīraṃ bhagavān vāmanākṛtiḥ
mamāgniśaraṇārthāya dehi rājan padatrayam
śataṃ śatasahasraṃ vā padānāṃ mārgatāṃ bhavān
etāvatā daityapate kṛtakṛtyo 'smi mārgatām
anyeṣām arthināṃ vittam icchayā dāsyate bhavān
pāṇau tu patite toye vāmano bhūtabhāvanaḥ
sarvadevamayaṃ rūpaṃ darśayām āsa tatkṣaṇāt
candrasūryau ca nayane dyauḥ śiraś caraṇau kṣitiḥ
pādāṅgulyaḥ piśācāś ca hastāṅgulyaś ca guhyakāḥ
viśvedevāś ca jānusthā jaṅghe sādhyāḥ surottamāḥ
yakṣā nakheṣu saṃbhūtā rekhāsv apsarasaḥ sthitāḥ
dṛṣṭir dhiṣṇāny aśeṣāṇi keśāḥ sūryāṃśavaḥ prabho
tārakā romakūpāṇi romāṇi ca maharṣayaḥ
bāhavo vidiśas tasya diśaḥ śrotraṃ mahātmanaḥ
aśvinau śravaṇau tasya nāsā vāyur mahābalaḥ
prasādaś candramā devo mano dharmaḥ samāśritaḥ
satyam asyābhavad vāṇī jihvā devī sarasvatī
grīvāditir devamātā vidyās tadvalayas tathā
svargadvāram abhūn maitraṃ tvaṣṭā pūṣā ca vai bhruvau
mukhaṃ vaiśvānaraś cāsya vṛṣaṇau tu prajāpatiḥ
hṛdayaṃ ca paraṃ brahma puṃstvaṃ vai kaśyapo muniḥ
pṛṣṭhe 'sya vasavo devā marutaḥ sarvasaṃdhiṣu
sarvasūktāni daśanā jyotīṃṣi vimalaprabhāḥ
vakṣaḥsthale tathā rudro dhairye cāsya mahārṇavaḥ
udare cāsya gandharvā marutaś ca mahābalāḥ
lakṣmīr medhā dhṛtiḥ kāntiḥ sarvavidyāś ca vai kaṭiḥ
sarvajyotīṃṣi yānīha tapaś ca paramaṃ mahat
stanau kukṣau ca vedāś ca jānū cāsya mahāmakhāḥ
iṣṭayaḥ paśubandhāś ca dvijānāṃ ceṣṭitāni ca
tasya devamayaṃ rūpaṃ dṛṣṭvā viṣṇor mahābalāḥ
kṛtvā rūpaṃ mahākāyaṃ sa jahārāśu medinīm
paraṃ vikramamāṇasya jānumūle prabhākarau
viṣṇor āstām mahīpāla devapālanakarmaṇi
jitvā lokatrayaṃ kṛtsnaṃ hatvā cāsurapuṅgavān
sutalaṃ nāma pātālam adhastād vasudhātalāt
baler dattaṃ bhagavatā viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā
atha daityeśvaraṃ prāha viṣṇuḥ sarveśvareśvaraḥ
yat tvayā salilaṃ dattaṃ gṛhītaṃ pāṇinā mayā
sāṃprataṃ devarājāya trailokyam akhilaṃ mayā
dattaṃ caturyugānāṃ vai sādhikā hy ekasaptatiḥ
tenāhaṃ parayā bhaktyā pūrvam ārādhito bale
sutalaṃ nāma pātālaṃ tam āsādya manoramam
vasāsura mamādeśaṃ yathāvat paripālayan
sugandhidhūpasaṃbādhe varābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ
upabhuñjan mahābhogān vividhān dānaveśvara
mamājñayā kālam imaṃ tiṣṭha strīśatasaṃvṛtaḥ
yadā ca devaviprāṇāṃ viruddhāny ācariṣyasi
bandhiṣyanti tathā pāśā vāruṇās tvām asaṃśayam
etad viditvā bhavatā mayājñaptam aśeṣataḥ
ity evam ukto devena viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā
baliḥ prāha mahārāja praṇipatya kṛtāñjaliḥ
tatrāsato me pātāle bhagavan bhavadājñayā
āpyāyito yena deva smareyaṃ tvām ahaṃ sadā
dānāny avidhidattāni śrāddhāny aśrotriyāṇi ca
hutāny aśraddhayā yāni tāni dāsyanti te phalam
adakṣiṇās tathā yajñāḥ kriyāś cāvidhinā kṛtāḥ
baler varam idaṃ dattvā śakrāya trividaṃ tathā
vyāpinā tena rūpeṇa jagāmādarśanaṃ hariḥ
siṣeva ca parān kāmān baliḥ pātālam āśritaḥ
baliprahrādasaṃvādaṃ mantritaṃ baliśukrayoḥ
baliviṣṇvoś ca kathitaṃ yaḥ smariṣyati mānavaḥ
nādhayo vyādhayo vāsya na ca mohākulaṃ manaḥ
bhaviṣyati kuruśreṣṭha puṃsas tasya kadācana
cyutarājyo nijaṃ rājyam iṣṭaprāptiṃ viyogavān
avāpnoti mahābhāga naraḥ śrutvā kathām imām
kāmopabhogasaṃprāptyā mudaṃ prāpa parāṃ vibhuḥ
alaṃbuṣā miśrakeśī puṇḍarīkātha vāmanā
ghṛtācī menakā rambhā nanṛtus tasya saṃnidhau
tuṣṭuvuś ca mahābhāga baliṃ siddhāḥ sacāraṇāḥ
tasmin saṃgītagītā tu vīṇāveṇuravākule
śarkārasavamādhvikāṃ puṣpāsavaphalāsavam
divyāḥ prasannāś ca surās tadarhāṇi madhūni ca
parāvadaṃśān madhurāṃl lavaṇāṃs tiktakāṇ kaṭūn
kaṣāyāṃś ca mahārāja sumṛṣṭāny aparāṇi ca
prāsādāḥ kāñcanāḥ sarve suvarṇamaṇimaṇḍitāḥ
sphāṭikāmalasopānā muktāhāraśatojjvalāḥ
teṣu sarveṣu daiteyā baleḥ saṃbandhibāndhavāḥ
nṛtyavādyādimuditā bubhujur viṣayān priyān
upagīyamāno bubhuje yatheṣṭaṃ viṣayān priyān
sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpūrṇā śrīr ivābjaṃ vināparā
na devī nāpi gandharvī nāpsarā na ca mānuṣī
tasyā rūpeṇa sadṛśī babhūva manujeśvara
sā tu pīnāyataśroṇī mṛdvaṅgī madhurasvarā
mṛdvalpapāṇipādābjā sumadhyā gajagāminī
sukeśī sumukhī śyāmā sarvair yoṣidguṇair yutā
tanayā merusāvarṇer dauhitrī mṛgamokinaḥ
vapuṣā rūpasaṃpadā pautanā mṛgalocanā
tīkṣṇāṃśur madhyamāṃ vīthīṃ yayau vaiṣuvatīṃ raviḥ
yadā yadā ca viṣuvaṃ bhāskaraḥ pratipadyate
tadā tadā hareś cakraṃ pātāle parivartate
sravanti yoṣitāṃ garbhās tasya dhārāṃśutāpitāḥ
sahasā daityapatnīnāṃ yāsu puṃsāṃ samudbhavaḥ
tad dṛṣṭvā sahasāyāntam ādityaśatatejasam
jvālāmālāsuduḥprekṣyaṃ viṣṇucakraṃ sudarśanam
hāhākṛtam abhūt sarvaṃ pātālam arisūdana
babhūvuḥ praṇatāś cānye siddhagandharvacāraṇāḥ
vaiklavyaṃ cāgatāḥ sarvāḥ striyaḥ parapuraṃjaya
tad dṛṣṭvā vyākulībhūtaṃ pātālam asurās tataḥ
ye tasthuḥ pauruṣaparās te hatāḥ śataneminā
bhrāmyatā tena cakreṇa saptalokavicāriṇā
śrutvā cakraṃ mahācakro niścakrāma gṛhād baliḥ
vimalaṃ khaḍgam ādāya śatacandraṃ ca bhānumat
vidhyāvalī nāma śubhā dadhāra dayitaṃ patim
uvāca ca pariṣvajya krodhatāmrekṣaṇaṃ balim
kalyāṇī guṇadoṣajñā praṇayān mṛdubhāṣiṇī
vimṛśya tajjñaḥ sāmādīn prayuñjīta balābalam
cakram itthaṃ vicārya tvaṃ krodhaṃ yāhi praśāmya vā
etat kila jagaddhātuś cakraṃ viṣṇoḥ sudarśanam
puṅgarbhān nikhilān etad dānavānāṃ mahāsura
vināśayaty anantarāṃ sarvaduṣṭanibarhaṇam
puruṣāṇāṃ na sarvatra saṃsthitā jagataḥ pateḥ
tasyaitac cakram āyāntaṃ puruṣaḥ ko na pūjayet
sadṛśe puruṣe krodhaṃ naraḥ kurvīta daityapa
śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ viṣṇuṃ yaṃ praṇamya na sīdati
bhraṣṭaś ca yadadhikṣepāt taṃ tvaṃ śaraṇam āvraja
śreyase sarvadharmajña śaraṇaṃ vraja keśavam
sa vyājahāra bhagavāṃs tavānugrahakāmyayā
saṃsmaryatāṃ mahābhāga sarvadharmabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
viṣṇubhakto mahābāhuḥ sa te śreyo 'bhidhāsyati
yayau tadārgham ādāya viṣṇoś cakrasya pūjakaḥ
sasmāra ca baliḥ sarvaṃ prahrādavacanaṃ nṛpa
tuṣṭāva vāsudevasya cakram avyaktamūrtinaḥ
jvālāmālākarālāntam udyadindusamaprabham
madhyāhnārkasamābhāsaṃ tejasaḥ piṇḍasaṃsthitam
taṃ dṛṣṭvā tejasā rāśim upasaṃgamya cā vibhum
uvāca daityaśārdūlaḥ praṇipatya kṛtāñjaliḥ
namāmi cakriṇaś cakraṃ karasaṅgi sudarśanam
kālāgnim iva yac cakraṃ
sahasram iva sūryāṇāṃ saṃghātaṃ vidyutām iva
tad viṣṇoḥ praṇamāmy aham
duṣṭarāhugalaccheda śoṇitāruṇatārakam
yasyārakeṣu śakrādyā lokapālā vyavasthitāḥ
tadantar vasavo rudrās tathaiva marutāṃ gaṇāḥ
dhārāyāṃ dvādaśādityāḥ samastāś ca hutāśanāḥ
dhārājāle 'bdhayaḥ sarve nābhimadhye prajāpatiḥ
samastanemiṣv akhilā yasya vidyāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ
yad bhramat surasaṅghānāṃ tejasaḥ paribṛṃhaṇam
daityaujasāṃ ca nāśāya tan namāmi sudarśanam
prasādasumukhe kṛṣṇe tasya cakraṃ sudarśanam
prasīda saṃyuge 'riṇāṃ sudarśanasudarśanam
vidyujjvālāmahākakṣaṃ dahāntar mama yat tamaḥ
visphoṭayākhilāṃ māyāṃ kuruṣva vimalāṃ matim
evaṃ saṃsthūyamānaṃ tad vahnipiṇḍopamaṃ mahat
dadarśa sa mahābāhuḥ prabhāmaṇḍaladurdṛśam
agnijvālāgataṃ tāmraṃ taptacakram ivāparam
trailokyam akhilaṃ daityo dṛṣṭavān bhūrbhuvādikam
mervādīn akhilāñ śailān gaṅgādyāḥ saritas tathā
kṣīrābdhipramukhāṃś cābdhīn dvīpāñ jambvādisaṃjñitān
vaimānikān sagandharvān sūryādīṃś ca tathā grahān
nakṣatratārakākāśaṃ śakrādīṃś ca divaukasaḥ
rudrādityāṃś ca marutāṃ sādhyānāṃ ca mahīpate
saṃnidhānaṃ nirīkṣyāsau daityānāṃ vismito 'bhavat
tataḥ praṇamyārtiharaṃ surāṇām apārasāraṃ paramāyudhaṃ hareḥ
yan no 'śubhaṃ cetasi vāyuvega yan no 'śubhaṃ vāci hutāśanottha
yac cāśubhaṃ kāyakṛtaṃ hares tad varāyudhaṃ tvaṃ praśamaṃ nayāśu
prasīda satkārakṛtaṃ mamāghaṃ prayātu te nāśam anantavīrya
satāṃ ca sanmārgavatāṃ manāṃsi sthirībhavantv acyutapādayugme
puṣpavṛṣṭir baler mūrdhni nipapātāntarikṣataḥ
tatas tad adbhutaṃ dṛṣṭvā cakrasyāgamanaṃ hareḥ
taṃ smariṣyāmi daityendraṃ sa naḥ śreyo 'bhidhāsyati
saṃsmṛtaś ca sa pātālam ājagāma mahāmatiḥ
cakrodyatakaraḥ sākṣād bhagavān iva keśavaḥ
tātāṃhridarśanād adya pāvito 'smy apakalmaṣaḥ
iti saṃstūya dattvā ca varāsanam udāradhīḥ
paryupāsata rājendro daityānāṃ svapitāmaham
tam upāsīnam anaghaḥ prahrādo daityapuṅgavaḥ
pratyuvāca mahātmānaṃ baliṃ vairocaniṃ nṛpa
tātenāhaṃ purā jñapto bhraṣṭarājyena te bale
saṃsmartavyo 'smy asaṃdigdhaṃ śreyo vakṣyāmy ahaṃ tadā
so 'haṃ rājyaparibhraṣṭo viṣayāsaktihṛṣitaḥ
indriyair avaśas tāta yat kāryaṃ tat praśādhi mām
taṃ devadevam anaghaṃ prayāhi śaraṇaṃ harim
śabdādiṣv anuraktāni tavākṣāṇy asurādhipa
gītakair gīyatāṃ viṣṇur manohāribhir ātmanaḥ
anyālambanataś cittam ākṛṣyādhatsva keśave
gandhān udārān bhakṣāṃś ca srajo vāsāṃsi cāsura
ātmānam acyutaṃ viddhi śatruṃ ca ripum ātmanaḥ
śabdādayo ye viṣayā viṣayī yaś ca puruṣaḥ
tad aśeṣaṃ vijānīhi svarūpaṃ paramātmanaḥ
paramātmā ca bhagavān viṣvakseno janārdanaḥ
bhagavān bhūtakṛd bhavyo bhūtānāṃ prabhavo hi yaḥ
prāpsyase paramāhlāda kāriṇīṃ paramāṃ gatim
tatra cittaṃ samāveṣṭuṃ na śaknoti bhavān yadi
tatrāpy asāmarthyavataḥ kriyāyogo mahātmanā
brahmaṇā yaḥ samākhyātas tanmanāḥ satataṃ bhava
kṣīṇakarmā mahābāho śubhāśubhavivarjitaḥ
niḥsaṃśayam avāpnoti dhundhumāro yathā nṛpaḥ
rājyam ārādhya govindaṃ kārtavīryas tathāptavān
dharmaṃ kṛṣṇaprasādena mudgalo jājaliḥ kuṇiḥ
prāpur anye tathā kāmān narendrā nahuṣādayaḥ
dharmadhvajas tathā muktiṃ keśavārādhanād gataḥ
tathānye munayo daitya rājānaś ca sahasraśaḥ
prāpur muktiṃ mahābhāgāḥ kṛtvā bhaktiṃ janārdane
śītahāniṃ tathānyeṣāṃ svedaṃ svedābhilāṣiṇām
karoti kṣudhitānāṃ ca bhojyapākaṃ tathotkaṭam
tathaiva kāmān bhūteśaḥ sa dadāti yathepsitān
tad etad akhilaṃ jñātvā yat taveṣṭaṃ śṛṇuṣva tat
etat prahrādavacanaṃ niśāmya ditijeśvaraḥ
pratyuvāca mahābhāgaṃ praṇipatya pitāmaham
saṃprāptasyāmṛtasyeva tava vākyasya nāsti me
tṛptir etad ahaṃ tāta śrotum icchāmi vistarāt
akṣīṇakarmā puruṣo maraṇe samupasthite
kīdṛśaṃ lokam āyāti yaḥ saṃsmarati keśavam
yathā ca vāsudevasya smaraṇaṃ tāta mānavaiḥ
mumūrṣubhiḥ prakartavyaṃ tan mamācakṣva vistarāt
kiṃ japyaṃ kīdṛśaṃ rūpaṃ smartavyaṃ ca hares tadā
sādhu vatsa tvayā praśnaḥ suguhyo 'yam udāhṛtaḥ
tapasāṃ tāta sarveṣāṃ tapo nānaśanāt param
kathyate ca mahābāho saṃvādo 'yaṃ purātanaḥ
bhagīrathasya rājarṣer brahmaṇaś ca prajāpateḥ
atītyāmaralokaṃ ca gavāṃ lokaṃ ca mānada
ṛṣilokaṃ ca yo 'gacchad bhagīratha iti śrutaḥ
taṃ dṛṣṭvā sa vacaḥ prāha brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ
kathaṃ bhagīrathāgās tvam imaṃ deśaṃ durāsadam
āyānty ataptatapasaḥ kathaṃ vai tvam ihāgataḥ
niḥśaṅkam annam adadaṃ brāhmaṇebhyaḥ śataṃ sahasrāṇi sadaiva dāyam
brāhmaṇaṃ vrataṃ nityam āsthāya vidvan na tv evāhaṃ tasya phalād ihāgām
daśaikarātrān daśa pañcarātrān ekādaśaikādaśakāṃs tathaiva
jyotiṣṭomānāṃ ca śataṃ yad iṣṭaṃ phalena tenāpi na cāgato 'ham
yac cāvasaṃ jāhnavītīranityaḥ śataṃ samās tapyamānas tapo 'ham
daśa dhenusahasrāṇi maṇiratnavibhūṣitāḥ
daśārbudāni cāśvānām ayutāni ca viṃśatiḥ
puṣkareṣu dvijātibhyaḥ prādāṃ gāś ca sahasraśaḥ
suvarṇacandrottamadhāriṇīnāṃ kanyottamānām adadaṃ sragviṇīnām
ṣaṣṭiṃ sahasrāṇi vibhūṣitānāṃ jāmbūnadair ābharaṇair na tena
daśārbudāny adadaṃ gosave yās tv ekaikaśo daśa gā lokanātha
samānavatsāḥ payasā samanvitāḥ suvarṇakāṃsyopaduhā na tena
gṛṣṭīnāṃ kṣīradātrīṇāṃ rohiṇīnāṃ śatāni ca
dogdhrīṇāṃ vai gavāṃ caiva prayutāni daśaiva tu
prādāṃ daśaguṇaṃ brahman na ca tenāham āgataḥ
koṭīś ca kāñcanasyāṣṭau prādāṃ brahman daśa tv aham
vājināṃ śyāmakarṇānāṃ haritānāṃ pitāmaha
prādāṃ hemasrajāṃ brahman koṭīr daśa ca sapta ca
īṣādantān mahākāyān kāñcanasragvibhūṣitān
patnīvataḥ sahasrāṇi prāyacchaṃ daśa sapta ca
alaṃkṛtānāṃ deveśa divyaiḥ kanakabhūṣaṇaiḥ
rathānāṃ kāñcanāṅgānāṃ sahasrāṇy adadaṃ daśa
sapta cānyāni yuktānāṃ vājibhiḥ samalaṃkṛtaiḥ
dakṣiṇāvayavāḥ kecid devair ye saṃprakīrtitāḥ
vājapeyeṣu daśasu prādāṃ tenāpi nāgataḥ
śakratulyaprabhāvānām ījyayā vikrameṇa ca
sahasraṃ niṣkakaṇṭhānāṃ pradadan dakṣiṇām aham
vijitya nṛpatīn sarvān makhair iṣṭvā pitāmaha
aṣṭābhyo rājasūyebhyo na ca tenāham āgataḥ
srotaś ca yāvad gaṅgāyāṃ chinnam āsīj jagatpate
dakṣiṇābhiḥ pravṛttābhir mama nāgaṃ ca tatkṛte
vājināṃ ca sahasre dve suvarṇamaṇibhūṣite
vāraṇānāṃ śataṃ cāham ekaikasya tridhādadam
varaṃ grāmaśataṃ cāham ekaikasya tridhādadam
tapasvī niyatāhāraḥ śamam āsthāya vāgyataḥ
dīrghakālaṃ himavati gaṅgāyāś ca durutsahām
mūrdhnā dhārāṃ mahādevaḥ śirasā yām adhārayat
śamyākṣepair ayajaṃ devadeva tathā kratūnām ayutaiś cāpi yattaḥ
trayodaśadvādaśāhaiś ca deva sapuṇḍarīkair na ca teṣāṃ phalena
aṣṭau sahasrāṇi kakudminām ahaṃ śuklarṣabhāṇām adaṃ brāhmaṇebhyaḥ
patnīś caiṣām adadaṃ niṣkakaṇṭhīs teṣāṃ phaleneha na cāgato 'smi
dhanadhānyasahasrāṃś ca grāmāñ śatasahasraśaḥ
śataṃ śatānāṃ gṛṣṭīnām adadaṃ cāpy atandritaḥ
iṣṭvānekair mahāyajñair brāhmaṇebhyo dhanena ca
ekādaśāhair ayajaṃ sudakṣiṇair dvir dvādaśāhair aśvamedhaiś ca deva
arkāyaṇaiḥ ṣoḍaśabhiś ca brahmaṃs teṣāṃ phaleneha na cāgato 'smi
bṛhadbhir dvādaśāhaiś ca aśvamedhaiḥ pitāmaha
niṣkrāmakaṃ cāpy adadaṃ yojanānāṃ dvir vistīrṇaṃ kāñcanapādapānām
vanaṃ cūtānāṃ ratnavibhūṣitānām na caiva teṣām āgato 'haṃ phalena
turāyaṇaṃ tu vratam apradhṛṣyam akrodhano 'karavaṃ triṃśato 'bdān
śataṃ gavām aṣṭa śatāni cāhaṃ dine dine prādadaṃ brāhmaṇebhyaḥ
payasvinīnāṃ atha rohiṇīnāṃ tathaiva cāpy anaḍuhāṃ lokanātha
prādām nityaṃ brāhmaṇebhyaḥ sureśa nehāgatas tena phalena cāham
triṃśataṃ vidhivad vahnīn ayajaṃ yac ca nityaśaḥ
aṣṭābhiḥ sarvamedhaiś ca nṛmedhair dviguṇais tathā
daśabhir viśvajidbhiś ca stobhair aṣṭādaśottaraiḥ
na caiva teṣāṃ deveśa phalenāham ihāgamam
saravyāṃ bāhudāyāṃ ca gayāyām atha naimiṣe
gavāṃ śatānām ayutam adadaṃ na ca tena vai
bhagīrathaṃ mahīpālaṃ puṇyalokanivāsinam
tad etad uktaṃ tapasāṃ samastānāṃ mahāmate
guṇair anaśanaṃ brahmā pradhānataram abravīt
sa yāti viṣṇusālokyaṃ yāvad indrāś caturdaśa
atītānāgatānīha kulāni puruṣarṣabha
ślokāś cātra mahābāho śrūyante yān bhagīrathaḥ
jagāda brahmaṇo lokam upetaḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ
brahma brahmamayaṃ viṣṇor yaḥ padaṃ paramātmanaḥ
saṃsmaraṃs tyajati prāṇān sa viṣṇuṃ praviśaty ajam
yaḥ kṣīṇakarmā bhogena tapasā vāpi saṃsmaran
akṣīṇakarmā maraṇe saṃsmaran devam acyutam
yathā tvam eva devānāṃ loke bhogān upāśnute
kṣutite 'pi kule kaścij jāyeyaṃ karmaṇaḥ kṣaye
taccintayādhunāśeṣa puṇyapāpavivarjitaḥ
ity etān āha rājarṣiḥ ślokān ādyo bhagīrathaḥ
viṣṇusaṃsmaraṇāt prāpya lokān anaśane mṛtaḥ
evam atyantaśastānāṃ karmaṇām asureśvara
nānyad utkṛṣṭam uddiṣṭaṃ tajjñair anaśanāt param
tasyāhaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ vakṣye yac ca japyaṃ mumūrṣubhiḥ
yādṛgrūpaś ca bhagavāṃś cintanīyo janārdanaḥ
āsannam ātmanaḥ kālaṃ jñātvā prājño mahāsura
nirdhūtamaladoṣaś ca snāto niyatamānasaḥ
samabhyarcya hṛṣīkeśaṃ puṣpadhūpādibhis tataḥ
praṇipātaiḥ stavaiḥ puṇyair dhyānayogaiś ca pūjayet
mitrān amitrān madhyasthān parān svāṃś ca punaḥ punaḥ
abhyarthanopacāreṇa kṣāmayet kukṛtaṃ svakam
śubhāśubhānāṃ daityendra vākyaṃ cedam udāharet
parityajāmy ahaṃ bhogāṃs tyajāmi suhṛdo 'khilān
bhojanādi mayotsṛṣṭam utsṛṣṭam anulepanam
sragbhūṣaṇādikaṃ geyaṃ dānam ādānam eva ca
homādayaḥ padārthā ye yāś ca nityakriyā mama
naimittikās tathā kāmyā varṇadharmās tathojjhitāḥ
guṇadharmādayo dharmā yāś ca kāścin mama kriyāḥ
kariṣye prāṇināṃ pīḍāṃ prāṇinaḥ santu nirbhayāḥ
kṣiter antaragā ye ca ye ca pāṣāṇasaṃpuṭe
ye dhānyādiṣu vastreṣu śayaneṣv āsaneṣu ca
na me 'sti bāndhavaḥ kaścid viṣṇuṃ muktvā jagadgurum
mitrapakṣe ca me viṣṇur adhaś cordhvaṃ tathāgrataḥ
pārśvato mūrdhni pṛṣṭhe ca hṛdaye vāci cakṣuṣi
śrotrādiṣu ca sarveṣu mama viṣṇuḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ
dakṣiṇāgreṣu darbheṣu śayīta prācchirās tataḥ
viṣṇuṃ jiṣṇuṃ hṛṣīkeśaṃ keśavaṃ madhusūdanam
nārāyaṇaṃ naraṃ kṛṣṇaṃ vāsudevaṃ janārdanam
vārāhaṃ yajñapuruṣaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣam acyutam
vāmanaṃ śrīdharaṃ śrīśaṃ nṛsiṃham aparājitam
sarveśvareśvaraṃ śuddham anantaṃ rāmam īśvaram
cakriṇaṃ gadinaṃ śārṅgiṃ śaṅkhinaṃ garuḍadhvajam
ayaṃ viṣṇur ayaṃ śaurir ayaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ puro mama
nīlotpaladalaśyāmaḥ padmapattropamekṣaṇaḥ
eṣa paśyatu mām īśaḥ paśyāmy aham adhokṣajam
āsīnaḥ sukhaduḥkheṣu samo mitrāhiteṣu ca
praśāntanetrabhrūvaktraṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharam
śrīvatsavakṣasaṃ caiva caturbāhuṃ kirīṭinam
pītāmbaradharaṃ viṣṇuṃ cārukeyūradhāriṇam
cintayec ca tadā rūpaṃ manaḥ kṛtvaikaniścayam
yādṛśe vā manaḥ sthairyaṃ rūpe badhnāti cakriṇaḥ
ā prāṇoparamād vīras taccittas tatparāyaṇaḥ
yathāgnis tṛṇajālāni dahaty anilasaṃgataḥ
tathānaśanasaṃkalpaḥ puṃsāṃ pāpam asaṃśayam
viṣṇoḥ saṃsmaraṇe prāpya lokam anaśane mṛtaḥ
evam atyantaśastānāṃ karmaṇām asureśvara
nāsti vidyāsamaṃ cakṣus tapo nānaśanāt param
nāsti jñānasamaṃ dānaṃ na saṃtoṣasamaṃ sukham
na caiverṣyāsamaṃ duḥkhaṃ tapo nānaśanāt param
nāsty arogasamaṃ dhanyaṃ nāsti gaṅgāsamā sarit
nāsti viṣṇusamaṃ dhyeyaṃ tapo nānaśanāt param
utkrāntikāle bhūtānāṃ muhyante cittavṛttayaḥ
jarāvyādhividhīnānāṃ kimu vyādhyādidoṣataḥ
atyantavayasā vṛddhyā vyādhinā cātipīḍitaḥ
nātra bhūmir na ca kuśāḥ saṃstaraś ca na kāraṇam
cittasyālambanībhūto viṣṇur evātra kāraṇam
bhuñjann abhuñjan gacchaṃś ca svapaṃs tiṣṭhann athāpi vā
kiṃ japaiḥ kiṃ bhuvā kṛtyaṃ kiṃ kuśair daityasattama
ity etat kathitaṃ sarvaṃ pṛṣṭo 'haṃ yat tvayā bale
utkrāntikāle smaraṇaṃ kiṃ bhūyaḥ kathayāmi te
kriyāyogas tvayā pūrvaṃ mamokto yaḥ pitāmaha
devārcāṃ devatāgāre tanmayatvena pūjayam
tapasā brahmacaryeṇa puṇyasvādhyāyasaṃstavaiḥ
kriyāyogaḥ sa vidvadbhir yogināṃ samudāhṛtaḥ
devārcāṃ kārayitvā vā yat puṇyaṃ puruṣo 'śnute
kāni mālyāni śastāni kāni nārhanti keśave
ke dhūpāḥ kṛṣṇadayitāḥ ke varjyāś ca jagatpateḥ
upahāre phalaṃ kīm syāt kiṃ phalaṃ gītavādite
ghṛtakṣīrādinā yac ca snāpite keśave phalam
vāsudevagṛhe sarvaṃ tad aśeṣaṃ vadasva me
śuśrūṣaṇavidhau puṇyaṃ tad ihaikamanāḥ śṛṇu
brahmaṇā kila devānām ṛṣīṇāṃ ca mahātmanām
śuśrūṣaṇaphalaṃ viṣṇoḥ proktaṃ daityapate purā
tebhyaḥ sakāśān manunā prāptaṃ svārociṣeṇa tu
svārociṣaḥ svaputrāya dattavān ṛtacakṣuṣe
ṛtacakṣuś ca bhargave śukras tasmād avāpa ca
mamākhyātaṃ ca śukreṇa yathāvat sumahātmanā
śuśrūṣave mahābhāga daityācāryeṇa dhīmatā
tad etac chrūyatāṃ tāta kriyāyogāśritaṃ phalam
jñānayogas tu saṃyogaś cittasyaivātmanā tu yaḥ
yas tu bāhyārthasāpekṣaḥ sa kriyāyoga ucyate
devālayādikaraṇe tad ihaikamanāḥ śṛṇu
yas tu devālayaṃ viṣṇor dārvaṃ śailamayaṃ tathā
kārayen mṛnmayaṃ vāpi śṛṇu tasya bale phalaṃ
kulānāṃ śatam āgāmi samatītaṃ tathā śatam
saptajanmakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ svalpaṃ vā yadi vā bahu
viṣṇor ālayavinyāsa prārambhād eva naśyati
pratiṣṭhāṃ samavāpnoti sa naraḥ saptalaukikīm
praśastadeśabhūbhāge yaḥ śastaṃ bhavanaṃ hareḥ
kārayaty akṣayāṃl lokān sa naraḥ pratipadyate
iṣṭakācayavinyāso yāvanty ṛkṣāṇi tiṣṭhati
pratimāṃ lakṣaṇavatīṃ yaḥ kārayati mānavaḥ
ṣaṣṭiṃ varṣasahasrāṇāṃ sahasrāṇi sa modate
pratiṣṭhāpya harer arcāṃ supraśaste niveśane
puruṣaḥ kṛtakṛtyatvān nainaṃ śvomaraṇaṃ tapet
ye bhaviṣyanti ye 'tītā ākalpāt puruṣāḥ kule
tāṃs tārayati saṃsthāpya devasya pratimāṃ hareḥ
anuśastāḥ kila purā yamena yamakiṃkarāḥ
pāśodyatāyudhā daitya prajāsaṃyamane ratāḥ
viharadhvaṃ yathānyāyaṃ niyogo me 'nupālyatām
nājñābhaṅgaṃ kariṣyanti bhavatāṃ jantavaḥ kvacit
kevalaṃ ye jagaddhātum anantaṃ samupāśritāḥ
bhavadbhiḥ parihartavyās teṣāṃ nāsty atra saṃsthitiḥ
ye tu bhāgavatā loke taccittās tatparāyaṇāḥ
pūjayanti sadā viṣṇuṃ te vas tyājyāḥ sudūrataḥ
saṃkīrtayati govindaṃ te vas tyājyāḥ sudūrataḥ
ye dhūpapuṣpavāsobhir bhūṣaṇaiś cāpi vallabhaiḥ
arcayanti na te grāhyā narāḥ kṛṣṇāśrayoddhatāḥ
upalepanakartāraḥ saṃmārjanaparāś ca ye
kṛṣṇālaye parityājyaṃ teṣāṃ tripuruṣaṃ kulam
yena cāyatanaṃ viṣṇoḥ kāritaṃ tatkulodbhavam
puṃsāṃ śataṃ nāvalokyaṃ bhavadbhir duṣṭacakṣuṣā
yenārcā bhagavadbhaktyā vāsudevasya kāritā
narāyutaṃ tatkulajaṃ bhavatāṃ śāsanātigam
bhavatāṃ bhramatām atra viṣṇusaṃśrayamudrayā
vinājñābhaṅgakṛn naiva bhaviṣyati naraḥ kvacit
vatsa vaivasvatasyaitāḥ śrutvā gāthā marīcinā
purukutsāya kathitāḥ pārthivendrāya dhīmate
etāṃ mahāphalāṃ yo 'rcāṃ viṣṇoh kārayate naraḥ
tavākhyātaṃ mahābāho gṛhakārayituś ca yat
yajñā narāṇāṃ pāpaugha kṣālakāḥ sarvakāmadāḥ
sthāpitāṃ pratimāṃ viṣṇoḥ samyak saṃpūjya mānavaḥ
yaṃ yaṃ prārthayate kāmaṃ taṃ tam āpnoty asaṃśayam
yaḥ snāpayati devasya ghṛtena pratimāṃ hareḥ
prasthe prasthe dvijāgryāṇāṃ sa dadāti gavāṃ śatam
gavāṃ śatasya viprāṇāṃ yad dattasya bhavet phalam
bhūridyumnena saṃprāptā saptadvīpā vasuṃdharā
ghṛtāḍhakena govinda pratimāsnāpanāt kila
pratimāsaṃ sitāṣṭamyāṃ ghṛtena jagataḥ patim
dvādaśyāṃ pañcadaśyāṃ ca gavyena haviṣā hareḥ
snāpanaṃ daityaśārdūla mahāpātakanāśanam
jñānato 'jñānato vāpi yat pāpaṃ kurute naraḥ
tat kṣālayati saṃdhyāyāṃ ghṛtena snāpayan harim
sarvayajñamayo viṣṇur havyānāṃ paramaṃ ghṛtam
tayor aśeṣapāpānāṃ kṣālakaḥ saṃgamo 'sura
yeṣu kṣīravahā nadyo hradāḥ pāyasakardamāḥ
tāṃl lokān puruṣā yānti kṣīrasnānakarā hareḥ
āhlādaṃ nirvṛtiṃ svāsthyam ārogyaṃ cārurūpatām
sapta janmāny avāpnoti kṣīrasnānakaro hareḥ
dadhyādīnāṃ vikārāṇāṃ kṣīrataḥ saṃbhavo yathā
tathaivāśeṣakāmānāṃ kṣīrasnāpanato hareḥ
yathā ca vimalaṃ jñānaṃ yathā nirvṛtikārakam
grahānukūlatāṃ puṣṭiṃ priyatvaṃ cākhile jane
karoti bhagavān viṣṇuḥ kṣīrasnāpanatoṣitaḥ
sarvo 'sya snigdhatām eti dṛṣṭamātraḥ prasīdati
ghṛtakṣīreṇa deveśe snāpite madhusūdane
atrāpy udāharantīmaṃ saṃvādaṃ keśavāśritam
śāṇḍilyā saha kaikeyyāḥ sumanāyāḥ surālaye
svarge 'tiśobhanāṃ dṛṣṭvā kaikeyīṃ patinā saha
brāhmaṇī śāṇḍilī nāma paryapṛcchata vismitā
śataśaḥ santi kaikeyi devāḥ svarganivāsinaḥ
devapatnyas tathaivaitāḥ siddhāḥ siddhāṅganās tathā
na teṣām īdṛśo gandho na kāntir na surūpatā
na vāsasāṃ ca śobheyaṃ yathā te patinā saha
naivābharaṇajātāni teṣāṃ bhrājanti vai tathā
śakrādyānām apīsānāṃ kṣayātiśayavarjitaḥ
tapaḥprabhāvo dānaṃ vā karma vā homasaṃjñitam
yajñair yajñeśvaro viṣṇur āvābhyāṃ yat tu toṣitaḥ
surūpatāṃ manaḥprīti paśyatāṃ cāruveṣatām
yat pṛcchasi mahābhāge tad apy eṣā vadāmi te
tīrthodakais tathā snānaiḥ snāpito 'yaṃ janārdanaḥ
tena kāntir atītyaitān devāṃs tribhuvaneśvarān
manaḥprasādaḥ saumyatvaṃ śārīrā yā ca nirvṛtiḥ
yāny abhīṣṭāni vāsāṃsi yac cābhīṣṭaṃ vibhūṣaṇam
ratnāni yāny abhīṣṭāni yat priyaṃ cānulepanam
ye dhūpā yāni mālyāni dayitāny abhavaṃs tadā
dattāni tatsamuttho 'yaṃ gandhabhūṣātmako guṇaḥ
āhārā dayitā ye ca pavitrāś ca niveditāḥ
te lokakartre kṣṛṇāya tṛptis tadguṇasaṃbhavā
kṛtam etad ato nābhūd āvayor bhavasaṃkṣayaḥ
ye tv akāmāṃ narāḥ samyag etat kurvanti śobhane
teṣāṃ dadāti viśveśo bhagavān muktim acyutaḥ
prāpnoty abhimatān kāmān daityāha sumanā yathā
candanāgarukarpūra kuṅkumośīrapadmakaiḥ
nRṇāṃ bhavanti rogāya dattāni puruṣottame
yāny ātmanaḥ sadeṣṭāni tāni śastāny upākuru
na śallakījaṃ nākṣaulaṃ na śuktāsavasaṃbhṛtam
dadyāt kṛṣṇāya dharmajño dhūpān ārādhanodyataḥ
mālatī mallikā caiva yūthikāthātimuktakā
pāṭalā karavīraś ca javā pārantir eva ca
kubjakas tagaraś caiva karṇikāraḥ kuraṇṭakaḥ
campako rotakaḥ kundo bāṇo varvaramālikāḥ
aśokatilakā rodhrās tathā caivāṭarūṣakaḥ
amī puṣpaprakārās tu śastāḥ keśavapūjane
bilvapatraṃ śamīpatraṃ patraṃ bhṛṅgārakasya ca
tulasīkālatulasī patraṃ bhṛṅgarajasya ca
ketakīpatrapuṣpaṃ ca sadyas tuṣṭikaraṃ hareḥ
sitotpalaṃ ca kṛṣṇasya dayitāni sadāsura
nārkaṃ nonmattakaṃ kāṃcit tathaiva girikarṇikām
na kaṇṭakārikāpuṣpam acyutāya nivedayet
kauṭajaṃ śālmalīpuṣpaṃ śairīṣaṃ ca janārdane
yeṣāṃ na pratiṣedho 'sti gandhavarṇānvitāni ca
tāni puṣpāṇi deyāni viṣṇave prabhaviṣṇave
sugandhaiś ca surāmāṃsī karpūrāgarucandanaiḥ
dukūlapaṭukauśeya vārkṣakarpāsikādibhiḥ
vāsobhiḥ pūjayed viṣṇuṃ daiteyendrātmanaḥ priyaiḥ
bhakṣyāṇi yāny abhīṣṭāni bhojyāny abhimatāni ca
ātmānaṃ keśavaṃ matvā yad yat tasyaiva rocate
cakravartī mahāvīryo māndhātā yuvanāśvajaḥ
śaśāsa sa mahābāhuḥ saptadvīpāṃ vasuṃdharām
agāyanta ca yā gāthā ye purāṇavido janāḥ
māndhātari mahābāho yauvanāśve samāśritāḥ
sarvaṃ tad yauvanāśvasya māndhātuḥ kṣetram ucyate
sa yauvanagataḥ saṃrāṭ saptadvīpavatīṃ mahīm
śaśāsa dharmeṇa purā cakravartī mahābalaḥ
nānyāyakṛn na cāśakto na daridro na kīkaṭaḥ
tasyābhūt puruṣo rājye samyagdharmānuśāsinaḥ
tasya bhaktir atīvābhūn nisargād eva bhūpateḥ
vāsudeve jagaddhāmni sarvakāraṇakāraṇe
sa cintayām āsa nṛpaḥ samṛddhyā vismitas tayā
evaṃ subahuśo rājā daityendra sumahābalaḥ
cintayann api tanmūlaṃ na cāsīn niścayānvitaḥ
yadā na niścayaṃ rājā sa yayau yuvanāśvajaḥ
praṇipatya mahābāhur gṛhītāsanasatkriyān
yadi sānugrahā buddhir bhavatāṃ mayi sattamāḥ
sametyākhilavijñānaṃ samyagdhautāntarātmabhiḥ
yad yathā tan mayā pṛṣṭā bhavanto matprasādhitāḥ
gadiṣyāmo yathānyāyaṃ yat te sāṃśayikaṃ hṛdi
vayaṃ hi naraśārdūla bhavatā paritoṣitāḥ
samyak prajāḥ pālayatā saptadvīpe mahītale
sutuṣṭo brāhmaṇo 'śnīyāc chindyād vā dharmasaṃśayam
vivakṣum atha bhūpālaṃ bhāryā tasyaiva dhīmataḥ
praṇāmapūrvam āhedaṃ vinayāt praṇayānvitam
na strīṇām avanīpāla vaktum īdṛg iheśyate
tathāpi bhūpate vakṣye saṃpad īdṛk sudurlabhā
bhūyo 'pi saṃśayaṃ praṣṭum alam īśa bhavān ṛṣīn
na tv ahaṃ puruṣavyāghra sadāntaḥpuracāriṇī
tan madīyam ṛṣīn praṣṭuṃ saṃśayaṃ pārthivārhasi
brūhi subhru mataṃ yat te praṣṭavyā yan mayā dvijāḥ
bhūyo 'ham ātmasaṃdehaṃ prakṣyāmy etān dvijottamān
śrūyante pṛthivīpāla nṛpa ye ca purātanāḥ
teṣāṃ na saṃpad bhūpāla yathā tava kilābhavat
tad īdṛksaṃpadāṃ dhāma tvam aśeṣakṣitīśvaraḥ
atīva karmaṇā yena tadvijñāne kutūhalam
nirastātiśayatvena nūnaṃ nālpena karmaṇā
munīn pṛcchatu yā cāhaṃ yan mayā ca purā kṛtam
sa tathoktas tayā rājā patnyā vismitamānasaḥ
munīnāṃ purato bhāryāṃ praśaṃsan vākyam abravīt
satyaṃ munivacaḥ puṃsām ardhaṃ vai gṛhiṇī yathā
mamāpy etad abhipretam imān praṣṭuṃ mahāmunīn
so 'ham etan mahābhāge prakṣyāmy etān mahāmunīn
naiṣām aviditaṃ kiṃcit triṣu lokeṣu vidyate
evam uktvā priyāṃ bhāryāṃ praṇipatya ca tān ṛṣīn
bhagavanto mamāśeṣaṃ prasādāhṛtacetasaḥ
kathayantu yathāvṛttaṃ yan mayā sukṛtaṃ kṛtam
ko 'ham āsaṃ purā viprāḥ kiṃ ca karma mayā kṛtam
kiṃ vānayā sucārvaṅgyā mama patnyā kṛtaṃ dvijāḥ
aśeṣā bhūbhṛto vaśyāḥ kośasyānto na vidyate
balaṃ caivāpratihataṃ śarīrārogyam uttamam
nijānuṣṭhānam akhilaṃ yasyāśeṣam idaṃ phalam
iti praṣṭā narendreṇa samastās te tapodhanāḥ
vasiṣṭhaṃ codayām āsuḥ kathyatām iti bhūbhṛtaḥ
yogam āsthāya suciraṃ yathāvad yatamānasaḥ
jñātavān nṛpates tasya pūrvadehaviceṣṭitam
māndhātāraṃ mahābuddhiṃ sapatnīkam idaṃ vacaḥ
śṛṇu bhūpāla sakalaṃ yasyedaṃ karmaṇaḥ phalam
tava rājyādikaṃ subhrūr yeyaṃ cāsīn mahīpate
tvam āsīḥ śūdrajātīyaḥ parahiṃsāparāyaṇaḥ
vākkrūro daṇḍapāruṣyo niḥsnehaḥ sarvajantuṣu
tatheyaṃ bhavato bhāryā pūrvam apy āyatekṣaṇā
dveṣyā babhūva taccittā tava śuśrūṣaṇe ratā
pativratā mahābhāgā bhartsyamānāpy aniṣṭhurā
kṣayaṃ jagāma yo 'rtho 'bhūt saṃcitaḥ prapitāmahaiḥ
tasmin kṣīṇe kṛṣiparas tvam āsīḥ pṛthivīpate
sāpi karmavipākena kṛṣir viphalatāṃ gatā
tato niḥsvaṃ parikṣīṇaṃ pareṣāṃ bhṛtyatāṃ gatam
tatyāja sādhvī veyaṃ tvāṃ tyajyamānāpi pārthiva
anayā ca samaṃ sādhvyā viṣṇor āvasathe tvayā
kṛtaṃ śuśrūṣaṇaṃ vīra parivrāḍbrahmacāriṇām
tadvṛttilipsuḥ śuśrūṣāṃ janarañjanahetukaḥ
kṛtavān yogināṃ vīra kṛṣṇasya jagataḥ pateḥ
vāsudevājire nityaṃ kṛtaṃ saṃmārjanaṃ tvayā
tathaivābhyukṣaṇaṃ vīra nityaṃ caivānulepanam
patnyānayā ca dharmajña yaṣmaccittānuvṛttayā
viṣṇoḥ kāryaṃ mayā kāryaṃ yogiśuśrūṣaṇaṃ tathā
bhṛtyāvasāyinaḥ samyag yathoktādhikakāriṇaḥ
smarataḥ puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ kāryeṇātidṛḍhātmanaḥ
niḥśeṣam upaśāntaṃ tat pāpaṃ yoginiṣevaṇāt
saṃmārjanaṃ ca bahuśaḥ sapatnikena te kṛtam
tatrāgataś ca sauvīraḥ purujin nāma bhūpatiḥ
mahāsainyaparīvāraḥ prabhūtagajavāhanaḥ
sarvasaṃpadupetaṃ taṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam
vṛtaṃ bhāryāsahasreṇa dṛṣṭvā srakcandanojjvalam
spṛhā kṛtā tvayā tatra cārumaulini pārthive
tatraivāvasathe dīpaḥ praśāntaḥ snehasaṃkṣayāt
anayā cottarīyānta cīravartyupavṛṃhitaḥ
tavāpy akhilabhūpāla manaḥkṣobhakaraṃ tataḥ
evaṃ narendra śūdratvād viṣṇukarmaparāyaṇaḥ
kiṃ punar yo naro bhaktyā viṣṇuśuśrūṣaṇādṛtaḥ
karoti satataṃ pūjāṃ niṣkāmo nānyamānasaḥ
pūjayācyutam īśeśaṃ tam ārādhya na sīdati
ārādhayācyutaṃ tadvad veśmasaṃmārjanādibhiḥ
tat tad dāttvā jagaddhātre vaikuṇṭhāya na sīdati
sugandhāgarukarpūra candanākṣodakuṃkumaiḥ
annopahārair vividhair ghṛtakṣīrābhiṣecanaiḥ
gītavāditanṛtyādyais toṣayasvācyutaṃ nṛpa
puṇyarātriṣu govindaṃ nṛtyagītaravojjvalaiḥ
evaṃ saṃtoṣyate bhaktyā bhagavān bhavabhaṅgakṛt
yeṣāṃ na vittaṃ tair bhaktyā mārjanādyupalepanaiḥ
devakarmāsamarthāṇāṃ prāṇināṃ smṛtisaṃstavaiḥ
toṣito 'bhimatān kāmān prayacchati janārdanaḥ
sadbhāvenaiva govindas toṣam āyāti saṃsmṛtaḥ
kṛtvālpam īdṛśaṃ prāptaṃ rājyam atyantadurlabham
tasmāt tvam anayā devyā sahātyantavinītayā
keśavārādhane yatnaṃ kuru dharmabhṛtāṃ vara
etan muner vasiṣṭhasya niśāmya vacanaṃ nṛpaḥ
bhāryāsahāyaḥ sa tadā saṃprahṛṣṭatanūruhaḥ
kṛtakāryam ivātmānaṃ manyamāno 'surottama
uvāca praṇato bhūtvā māndhātā vāruṇiṃ vacaḥ
yathāmaratvaṃ saṃprāpya yathā vā brahma śāśvatam
paraṃ nirvāṇam āpnoti tathāhaṃ vacasā tava
kṛtakṛtyaḥ sukhī cāsmi nirvṛtiṃ paramāṃ gataḥ
aham eṣā ca tanvaṅgī vibhūtibhraṃsabhīrukau
āḍhyāv āpāditau brahmann ihādya vacasā tava
saṃpadāṃ kathitaṃ bījam āvayor bhavatā mune
taduptāv udyatāv āvāṃ vijānīhi dvijottama
ārādhyate jagannātho bhāvaśūnyair janārdanaḥ
niḥsvair ārādhyate devo viṣṇuḥ sarveśvareśvaraḥ
sarvam etan mayā jñātaṃ yat tvam āttha mahāmune
kāni vratāni yair devo naraiḥ strībhiś ca keśavaḥ
toṣam ārādhito 'bhyeti kaiś ca dānair mahāmune
tāny aśeṣāṇi me brūhi kṛṣṇārādhanakāṅkṣiṇaḥ
śṛṇu bhūpāla yair viṣṇur narair ārādhyate vrataiḥ
nārībhiś cātighore 'smin patitābhir bhavārṇave
ekam aśnāti yo bhaktaṃ dvitīyaṃ brāhmaṇātmakam
karoti keśavaprītyai kārttikaṃ māsam ātmavān
pūrve vayasi yat tena jñānato 'jñānato 'pi vā
pāpam ācaritaṃ tasmān mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ
anenaiva vidhānena mārgaśīrṣe 'pi mādhavam
bhagavatprīṇanārthāya phalaṃ tasya śṛṇuṣva me
madhye vayasi yat pāpaṃ yoṣitā puruṣeṇa vā
kṛtaṃ tasmāc ca tenokto vimokṣaḥ paramātmanā
puṇḍarīkākṣam abhyarcya pauṣamāse mahīpate
tatprīṇanāya yat pāpaṃ vārddhike tena vai kṛtam
sa tasmān mucyate rājan pumān yoṣid athāpi vā
tadvat tṛtīye 'pi kṛtaṃ mahāpātakanāśanam
tribhiḥ saṃvatsarair eva pradadāti phalaṃ nṛṇām
trīṇi nāmāni devasya mocayanti trivārṣikaiḥ
sarvapāpapraśamanaṃ keśavārādhanaṃ param
śṛṇuṣva ca mahīpāla vrataṃ viṣṇupadatrayam
sarvapāpapraśamanaṃ yaj jagāda purā hariḥ
prācetasāya dakṣāya dakṣaś cāha vivasvate
asitena samākhyātam alpāyāsaṃ mahāphalam
tad idaṃ śrūyatāṃ samyag vrataṃ viṣṇupadatrayam
dakṣaḥ prajāpatiḥ pūrvaṃ viṣṇum ārādhya pṛṣṭavān
bahuśas tu vipannāyāṃ sṛṣṭāv arinisūdana
bhagavan sarvakaṛtvaṃ mamādiṣṭaṃ svayaṃbhuvā
brahmaṇā devadeveśa tavādeśena keśava
vipannā ca jagannātha mama sṛṣṭiḥ kṛtā kṛtā
pūrvakarmavipākena vyākulaś cāsmi cetasā
yathā ca deva mucyeya asmāt saṃsārasaṃkaṭāt
viṣayāsaṅgaviṣamāt tan mamājñāpayācyuta
ācaṣṭa duḥkhakṣayadaṃ vrataṃ viṣṇupadatrayam
sarvārambhaviniṣpatti kārakaṃ pāpanāśanam
saṃsārocchedakaṃ dhīrair ācīrṇaṃ sthirabuddhibhiḥ
kathayāmi samācaṣṭa yathā pūrvaṃ mamāsitaḥ
āṣāḍhe māsi pūrvāsu tathāṣāḍhāsu pārthiva
kṣīrasnehasthitaṃ tadvat paiṣṭaṃ viṣṇupadadvayam
yavāṃś ca dadyād viprāya bhūgatiḥ prīyatām iti
naktaṃ bhuñjīta rājendra haviṣyānnaṃ susaṃskṛtam
tathottarāsv āṣāḍhāsu śrāvaṇe māsi mānavaḥ
viprāya ca yavān dadyāt prīṇayitvā ca bhūgatim
naktaṃ bhūñjīta rājendra naro yoṣid athāpi vā
viprāya ca yavān dattvā prīṇayitvā bhuvogatim
bhuñjīta gorasaprāyaṃ naro yoṣid athāpi vā
padadvayasya pūjāṃ ca prīṇanaṃ ca bhuvogateḥ
strī vā rājendra pūrvāsu tathā bhadrapadāsu vai
phālgune phalgunī pūrvā bhavatī ha yadā nṛpa
hiraṇyaṃ dakṣiṇāṃ dattvā svargatiḥ prīyatām iti
eṣa evottarāyoge caitre māse vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ
etaj jagāda govindaḥ purā dakṣāya pṛcchate
sarvapāpaharaṃ puṇyaṃ vrataṃ viṣṇupadatrayam
samāgamaṃ proṣitaiś ca tathā prāpnoti bāndhavaiḥ
dravyam aiśvaryam ārogyaṃ saubhāgyaṃ cārurūpatām
yān yān kāmān naraḥ strī vā hṛdayenābhivāñchanti
tāṃs tāṃś cāpnoti niṣkāmo viṣṇulokaṃ ca gacchati
pūrvaṃ kṛtvāpi pāpāni naraḥ strī vā narādhipa
viṣṇor ārādhanārthāya yāni dānāni sattama
deyāni tāny aśeṣāṇi mamācakṣva dvijottama
yena caiva vidhānena dānaṃ puṃsaḥ sukhāvaham
prīṇanāya ca kṛṣṇasya tan mamākhyāhi vistarāt
kṛtopavāsaḥ saṃprāśya pañcagavyaṃ nareśvara
ghṛtakṣīrābhiṣekaṃ ca kṛtvā viṣṇoḥ samāhitaḥ
udaṅmukhīm arcayitvā tathā gṛṣṭiṃ payasvinīm
saputrāṃ vastrasaṃvītāṃ sitayajñopavītinīm
svarṇaśṛṅgīṃ śubhākārāṃ hiraṇyoparisaṃsthitām
hiraṇyaṃ vācayitvāgre brāhmaṇāyopapādayet
imāṃ tvaṃ pratigṛhṇīṣva govindaḥ prīyatām iti
govindaprīṇanād rājan viṣṇulokaṃ ca gacchati
saptāvarāṃs tathā pūrvān saptātmānaṃ ca mānavaḥ
sarveṣām eva pāpānāṃ kṛtānām avijānatā
prāyaścittam idaṃ śastam anutāpopavṛṃhitam
ikṣvākunaiṣā rājendra pūrvaṃ dattā mahātmanā
tataḥ sa lokān amalān prāptavān avanīpatiḥ
lokāḥ kāmadughāḥ prāptā dattvedṛgvidhinā nṛpa
tiladhenuṃ pravakṣyāmi keśavaprīṇanāya yā
yāṃ dattvā brahmahā goghnaḥ pitṛghno gurutalpagaḥ
āgāradāhī garadaḥ sarvapāparato 'pi vā
svanulipte mahīpṛṣṭe vastrājinasamāvṛte
dhenuṃ tilamayīṃ kṛtvā sarvaratnaiḥ samanvitām
suvarṇaśṛṅgīṃ raupyakhurāṃ gandhaghrāṇavatīṃ śubhām
mṛṣṭānnajihvāṃ kurvīta guḍāsyāṃ sūtrakambalām
ikṣupādāṃ tāmrapṛṣṭhāṃ kuryān muktāphalekṣaṇām
praśastapatraśravaṇāṃ phaladantavatīṃ śubhām
sragdāmapucchāṃ kurvīta navanītastanānvitām
īdṛksaṃsthānasaṃpannāṃ kṛtvā śrāddhasamanvitaḥ
kāṃsyopadohanāṃ dadyāt keśavaḥ prīyatām iti
prapitāmahaṃ tathā pūrvaṃ puruṣāṇāṃ catuṣṭayam
ātmānaṃ tanayaṃ pautraṃ tadadhas tu catuṣṭayam
yaś ca gṛhṇāti vidhivat tasyāpy evaṃvidhān kulān
caturdaśa tathā caiva dadataś cānumodakāḥ
dīyamānāṃ prapaśyanti tiladhenuṃ ca ye narāḥ
te 'py aśeṣāghanirmuktāḥ prayānti paramāṃ gatim
praśāntāya suśīlāya tathāmatsariṇe budhaḥ
cāndrāyaṇād abhyadhikaṃ śastaṃ tat tilabhakṣaṇam
tilābhāve tathā dadyād ghṛtadhenuṃ yatavrataḥ
yena bhūpa vidhānena tad ihaikamanāḥ śṛṇu
vāsudevaṃ jagannāthaṃ puruṣeśam ajaṃ vidhum
sarvapāpanihantāraṃ ghṛtakṣīrābhiṣecanāt
saṃpūjya pūrvavat puṣpa gandhadhūpādibhir naraḥ
ahorātroṣito bhūtvā tatparaḥ prayataḥ śuciḥ
parameśam atho nāmnā abhiṣṭūya ghṛtārciṣā
gavyasya sarpiṣaḥ kumbhaṃ puṣpamālyādibhūṣitam
ikṣuyaṣṭimayān pādān khurān raupyamayāṃs tathā
sauvarṇe cākṣiṇī kuryāc śṛṅge cāgarukāṣṭhaje
kuryāt turuṣkakarpūrau ghrāṇaṃ phalamayān stanān
maṇiratnasuvarṇānāṃ samyakkalpanayā kṛtām
tadvac charkarayā jihvāṃ guḍakṣīramayaṃ mukham
kṣaumasūtreṇa lāṅgūlaṃ romāṇi sitasarṣapaiḥ
tāmrapātramayaṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ kuryāc chraddhāsamanvitaḥ
īdṛksvarūpāṃ saṃkalpya ghṛtadhenuṃ narādhipa
taṃ ca vipraṃ mahābhāga manasaiva ghṛtārciṣam
etāṃ mamopakārāya ghṛhṇīṣva tvaṃ dvijottama
prīyatāṃ mama deveśo ghṛtāṛciḥ puruṣottamaḥ
maṇimuktāsuvarṇānāṃ samyakkalpanayā kṛtām
dattvaikarātraṃ sthitvā ca ghṛtāhāro narādhipa
mucyate sarvapāpebhyas tathā dānaphalaṃ śṛṇu
ghṛtakṣīravahā nadyo yatra pāyasakardamāḥ
teṣu lokeṣu lokeśa sa puṇyeṣūpajāyate
tāṃs teṣu nṛpa lokeṣu sa nayaty astakalmaṣaḥ
sakāmānām iyaṃ vyuṣṭiḥ kathitā nṛpasattama
viṣṇulokaṃ narā yānti niṣkāmā ghṛtadhenudāḥ
ghṛtam agnir ghṛtaṃ somas tanmayāḥ sarvadevatāḥ
jaladhenuṃ pravakṣyāmi prīyate dattayā yayā
devadevo hṛṣīkeśaḥ sarveśaḥ sarvabhāvanaḥ
kuṣṭhaṃ māṃsīm uśīraṃ ca vālakāmalakair yutam
caturbhiḥ saṃvṛtaṃ bhūpa tilapātraiś caturdiśam
puṣpadhūpopahārais tu yathāvibhavam ādṛtaḥ
evaṃ saṃpūjya govindaṃ jaladhenuṃ savatsakām
sitavastradharaḥ śānto vītarāgo vimatsaraḥ
dadyād viprāya rājendra prītyarthaṃ jalaśāyinaḥ
jalaśāyī jagadyoniḥ prīyatāṃ mama keśavaḥ
iti coccārya bhūnātha viprāya pratipādyatām
apakvānnāśinā stheyam ahorātram ataḥparam
sarvāhlādān avāpnoti ye divyā ye ca mānuṣāḥ
śarīrārogyam ābādhā praśamaḥ sārvakāmikaḥ
nṛṇāṃ bhavati dattāyāṃ jaladhenvāṃ na saṃśayaḥ
atrāpi śrūyate bhūpa pudgalena mahātmanā
dadarśa yātanā ghorāḥ pāpakarmakṛtāṃ kila
dīptāgnitīkṣṇaśastrotthāḥ kvāthatailagatās tathā
uṣṇakṣāranadīpātā bhairavāḥ puruṣarṣabha
vraṇāḥ kṣāranipātogrāḥ kumbhīpākamahābhayāḥ
tā dṛṣṭvā yātanā vipraś cakāra paramāṃ kṛpām
āhlādaṃ te tadā jagmuḥ pāpās tadanukampitāḥ
taṃ dṛṣṭvā nārakāḥ kecit kecit tadavalokinaḥ
dharmarājaṃ sa papraccha teṣāṃ praśamakāraṇam
tasmai cācaṣṭa rājendra tadā vaivasvato yamaḥ
āhlādahetuṃ viprāya pṛcchate pṛthivīpate
tavānubhāvād eteṣāṃ nārakāṇāṃ dvijottam
saṃpravṛtto 'yam āhlādaḥ kāraṇaṃ yac chṛṇuṣva tat
tvayābhyarcya jagannāthaṃ sarveśaṃ jalaśāyinam
tasya dānasya te vyuṣṭir iyam āhlādadāyinī
saṃprāpto 'si mahāprajña sarvaśāstraviśārada
ye tvāṃ paśyanti śṛṇvanti ye ca dhyāyanti pāpinaḥ
śṛṇoṣi yāṃs tvaṃ viprendra yāṃś ca dhyāyasi paśyasi
nirvṛtiḥ paramā teṣāṃ sarvāhlādapradāyinī
āhlādahetujananaṃ nāsti viprendra tādṛśam
jaladhenur yathā nRṇāṃ janmāny ekonasaptatiḥ
ekajanmakṛtaṃ vāñchā trijanmotthaṃ samāhṛtā
saptajanmakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ hanti dattāmbugaur nṛṇām
yeṣāṃ samāśrayaḥ kṛṣṇo na niyamyā hi te mayā
kṛṣṇaḥ saṃpūjito yais tu ye kṛṣṇārtham upoṣitāḥ
yaiś ca nityaṃ smṛtaḥ kṛṣṇo na te madviṣayopagāḥ
namaḥ kṛṣṇācyutānanta vāsudevety udīritam
yaiḥ saṃsmṛto dvijaśreṣṭha na te madviṣayopagāḥ
kṛṣṇety udīritaṃ yaiś ca na te madviṣayopagāḥ
sarvābādhāsu ye kṛṣṇaṃ smaranty uccārayanti ca
tadbhāvabhāvitā vipra na te madviṣayopagāḥ
ūcus te nārakāḥ sarve vahniśastrāstrabhīravaḥ
namaḥ kṛṣṇāya haraye viṣṇave jiṣṇave namaḥ
hṛṣīkeśāya devāya jagaddhātre 'cyutāya ca
namaḥ paṅkajanetrāya namaḥ paṅkajanābhaye
janārdanāya śrīśāya śrīpate pītavāsase
namaḥ karālavaktrāya nṛsiṃhāyātinādine
śārṅgiṇe sitakhaḍgāya śaṅkhacakragadādhṛte
varāharūpāya tathā namo yajñāṅgadhāriṇe
vyāptāśeṣadigantāya śāntāya paramātmane
śastrāṇi kuṇṭhatāṃ jagmur analaś cāpy aśīśamat
saṃśuṣkāḥ kṣārasaritaḥ patitaḥ kūṭaśālmaliḥ
prakāśatāmasītattvaṃ narakaś cāgatas tu saḥ
nirutsāhā jaḍadhiyo babhūvur yamakiṃkarāḥ
āsan gandhāmbuvāhinyaḥ pūyaśoṇitanimnagāḥ
veṇuvīṇāsvanayutān gītaśabdāṃś ca śuśruvuḥ
taṃ tādṛśam athālakṣya nṛpa vaivasvato yamaḥ
jājvalyamānāṃs tejobhir amalāmbaravāsasaḥ
namo namo 'stu kṛṣṇāya govindāyāvyayātmane
vāsudevāya devāya viṣṇave prabhaviṣṇave
kṣīṇapāpacayāṃs tāṃs tu pādyārghyādibhir arcayan
pūjayitvā ca tān āha sa kṛṣṇāya kṛtāñjaliḥ
samāhitamanā bhūtvā dharmarājo nareśvara
viṣṇor devātidevasya jagaddhātuḥ prajāpateḥ
praṇāmaṃ ye 'pi kurvanti teṣām api namo namaḥ
ye viṣṇoḥ praṇatās tebhyo namaḥ sadyaḥ punaḥ punaḥ
praṇāmaṃ ye 'pi kurvanti teṣām api namo namaḥ
evaṃ te saṃstutās tena dharmarājena nārakāḥ
vimānāni samārūḍhā nṛttagāndharvavanti vai
saṃsmṛtya yamavākyāni viṣṇor māhātmyam eva ca
jaladhenvāś ca māhātmyaṃ saṃsmṛtyaitad agāyata
jīvo vāñchati kīṭatvaṃ yūkāmatkuṇayonitaḥ
tasmāc ca śalabhādīnāṃ yoniṃ tasmāc ca pakṣiṇām
tataś ca paśutāṃ prāpya naratvam abhivāñchati
vimuktihetukī dhanyā narayoniḥ kṛtātmanām
jīvā mānuṣyatām anye janmanām ayutair api
viṣṇumāyāparītās te prāpyāpi na taranti ye
patanti bhūyaḥ saṃsāre viṣṇumāyāvimohitāḥ
dustarāpi tu sādhyāsau māyā kṛṣṇasya mohanī
chindanti vaiṣṇavīṃ māyāṃ keśavārpitamānasāḥ
avirodhena viṣayām bhuñjan viṣṇuvyapāśrayaḥ
kṛtvā manas taraty etāṃ viṣṇor māyāṃ sudustarām
īdṛgbahuphalāṃ bhaktiṃ sarvadhātari keśave
mudhaivoktaṃ mudhāyātaṃ mudhā tad vidhiceṣṭitam
ārādhito hi yaḥ puṃsām aihikāmuṣmikaṃ phalam
saṃvatsarās tathā māsā viphalā divasāś ca te
narāṇāṃ viṣayāndhānāṃ yeṣu nārādhito hariḥ
tuṣyate hṛdayenaiva kas tam īśaṃ na pūjayet
jaladhenvāś ca māhātmyaṃ niśāmyāpīdṛśaṃ narāḥ
tāṃ na yacchanti ye teṣāṃ vivekaḥ kutra tiṣṭhati
saṃprāpya tan na yair viṣṇus toṣito nāmbudhenukā
dattā ca samyak te muṣṭā janmani subahūni bhoḥ
ūrdhvabāhur viraumy eṣa dṛṣṭalokadvayo 'smi bhoḥ
duḥsaho nārako vahnir aviṣahyāś ca yātanāḥ
jñānaṃ mamaitad ālambya kṛṣṇe bhavata susthirāḥ
vimṛṣya satyam ity etan manaḥ kṛṣṇe niveśyatām
prātaḥ kṛṣṇeti deveti govindeti ca jalpatām
madhyāhne cāparāhne ca yo 'vasādaḥ sa ucyatām
mudhaiva jihvā kṛṣṇeti keśaveti ca vakṣyati
etāḥ pudgalagāthās te yamavākyaṃ tavoditam
jaladhenvāś ca māhātmyaṃ viṣṇusaṃpūjanasya ca
vratam anyan mahābhāga sarvakāmapradaṃ śṛṇu
bhaviṣyati śamīkasya śiṣyaḥ paramasaṃmataḥ
sa ca rājā jagaddhātur devadevasya śārṅginaḥ
prakṣyaty ārādhanārthāya devadevasya cakriṇaḥ
ārādhayitum icchāmi sarvecchāpūrakaṃ hariṃ
saṃkuruṣva mahābhāga prasādaṃ mama suvrata
kṛṣṇārādhanakāmasya manaso deśiko bhava
ārādhanena yeneśo jagatām īśvareśvaraḥ
viṣṇur ārādhyate puṃbhiḥ saṃsārābdhiparikṣataiḥ
kṛtvā sadaivārtimatāṃ śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ guruḥ
evaṃ sa tena bhūpāla bhūpālena rṣipuṅgavaḥ
keśavārādhanārthāya samyak pṛṣṭaḥ pravakṣyati
namaskṛtya jagaddhātre devadevāya śārṅgine
parameśasureśāya hṛṣīkeśāya vedhase
sarvakalyāṇabhūtāya śaṅkhacakragadādhṛte
varāsicarmāvitate krūraśāntātmamūrtaye
yadyadbhūtopakārāya tattadrūpavikāriṇe
paramāṇvantaparyanta sahasrāṃśāṇumūrtaye
jaṭharāntāyutāśānta sthitabrahmāṇḍadhāriṇe
śvetādidīrghahrasvādi kaṭhinādivikalpanā
tam ajaṃ śāśvataṃ nityaṃ pariṇāmavivarjitam
praṇamya jagatām īśam anantaṃ parataḥ param
paraṃ parāṇāṃ sraṣṭāraṃ purāṇaṃ puruṣaṃ prabhum
varaṃ vareṇyaṃ varadaṃ sthūlasūkṣmasvarūpiṇam
aśeṣajagatāṃ mūlam anādinidhanasthitim
jñānajñeyasya munibhir jñānavidbhir mahātmabhiḥ
śrūyatāṃ sa muniśreṣṭho yad vakṣyati parīkṣite
bhāryā sā vasudevasya satyadharmaparāyaṇā
na cātuṣyata govindas tatas tām āha bhārgavaḥ
aputrāhaṃ dvijaśreṣṭha patyur me nāsti saṃtatiḥ
tapas tāvat kariṣyāmi parameṇa samādhinā
yāvad ārādhito viṣṇur dāsyaty abhimataṃ mama
tad idaṃ vratam āsthāya toṣayāśu janārdanam
pañcagavyajalasnātaḥ pañcagavyakṛtāśanaḥ
ghṛtena vācayed vipraṃ gṛhṇīyāc ca tato vratam
adyaprabhṛty ahaṃ māsaṃ virataḥ prāṇināṃ vadhāt
asatyavacanāt stainyān madhumāṃsādibhakṣaṇāt
parāpavādapaiśūnyaṃ parapīḍākaraṃ tathā
kṛtvaivaṃ purato viṣṇor nivṛttiṃ pāpataḥ śubhe
naivedyaṃ svayam aśnīyān maunī nityam udaṅmukhaḥ
mārgaśīrṣe tathā māsi jātipuṣpair janārdanam
dattvā tathaiva gṛhṇīyān niyamaṃ cāsya rocate
sarveṣv eva tu māseṣu pañcagavyādikaṃ samam
puṣpadhūpopahāreṣu viśeṣo dakṣiṇāsu ca
snānaprāśanayoḥ sāmyaṃ tathā vai naktabhojane
arcayet pratimāsaṃ ca yaiḥ puṣpais tāni me śṛṇu
ye ca dhūpāḥ pradātavyā naivedyānnaṃ ca yad yadā
śvetais tato mālikayā tathā mallikayā tataḥ
kārttike mārgaśīrṣe ca dhūpaḥ pauṣe ca candanam
māghaphālgunacaitreṣu dadyād viṣṇos tathāgarum
vaiśākhādiṣu māseṣu triṣu devaki bhaktitaḥ
karpūraṃ devadevāya guggulaṃ śrāvaṇādiṣu
kārttikādiṣu māseṣu paramānnaṃ śubhe triṣu
kāsāraṃ māghapūrveṣu yavānnaṃ ca tatas triṣu
ghṛtaṃ tilāñ jalaghaṭān hiraṇyam athavājinam
pratimāsaṃ tathā dadyād brāhmaṇāya śubhavrate
yathoktaṃ niyamānāṃ ca grahaṇaṃ pratimāsikam
kurvañ jagatpatir viṣṇuḥ prīyatām iti mānavaḥ
vratenārādhito viṣṇur anena jagataḥ patiḥ
dadāty abhimatān kāmān alpakālena bhāmini
dhanyaṃ yaśasyam āyuṣyaṃ saubhāgyārogyadaṃ tathā
vratenānena śuddhānām abdenaikena keśavaḥ
sukhadṛśyo na saṃdeho dīpenaivāgrataḥ sthitaḥ
kāyavāṅmanaso śuddhiṃ karoty etan mahāvratam
śuddhānāṃ cāmalo devo dṛśya eva janārdanaḥ
tasminn ekāgracittānāṃ prāṇināṃ varavarṇini
śuddhivratam idaṃ tasmān mahāpātakanāśanam
ārādhanāya kṛṣṇasya kuru devaki pāvanam
tasmiṃś cīrṇe hṛṣīkeśas tubhyaṃ dāsyati darśanam
dṛṣṭe cābhimataṃ yat te tad aśeṣaṃ bhaviṣyati
devakī bhārgavasyaitac śrutvā vākyaṃ narādhipa
śuddhikāmā cacārātha sarvakāmapradaṃ vratam
vratenārādhitas tena tadā devyā janārdanaḥ
dadau darśanam īśeśaḥ śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ
dṛṣṭe tasminn aśeṣeśe jagaddhātari keśave
kṛtvā praṇāmam āhedaṃ bhaktinamrātha devakī
jagatām īśvareśeśa jñāna jñeya bhavāvyaya
pradhānapuṃsor ajayor yaḥ kāraṇam akāraṇam
tvaṃ pradhānaṃ pumāṃś caiva kāraṇākāraṇātmakaḥ
prasīda deva devānām ariśātana vāmana
aditis tvaṃ mahābhāge bhuvaṃ prāptā surāraṇi
tvām ahaṃ jagaddhātāram udāroruparākramam
dhārayiṣyāmi garbheṇa katham acyuta śaṃsa me
kurvatā vidhṛtāḥ sapta lokās tvaṃ cātmamāyayā
tathā sāṃpratam apy etāṃl lokān sasthāṇujaṅgamān
dhārayiṣyāmy athātmānaṃ tvāṃ ca devaki līlayā
ity evam uktvā tāṃ devīṃ devakīṃ bhagavān prabhuḥ
avāpa ca tato garbhaṃ ajāyata ca viśveśaḥ
svenāṅgena janārdanaḥ
devakī vasudevataḥ pratimāsaṃ ca te pūjām
aṣṭamyāṃ yaḥ kariṣyati mama caivākhilān kāmān
saṃprāpnoty apakalmaṣaḥ
nīlotpaladalaśyāmaṃ tāmrāyatavilocanam
caturbāhum udārāṅgaṃ śrīvatsāṅkitavakṣasam
taṃ jātaṃ devakī devaṃ nidhānaṃ sarvatejasām
praṇipatyābhituṣṭāva saṃprastutapayodharā
abālo bālarūpeṇa yeneśa tvam ihāsthitaḥ
namas te puṇḍarīkākṣa namas te 'stu janārdana
namas te śārṅgacakrāsi gadāparighapāṇaye
upendrāyāprameyāya hṛṣīkeśāya vai namaḥ
namo 'stu te 'ṇurūpāya bṛhadrūpāya vai namaḥ
aśeṣabhūtarūpāya tathārūpāya te namaḥ
anirdeśyaviśeṣāya tubhyaṃ sarvātmane namaḥ
sarveśvarāya sarvāya sarvabhūtāya te namaḥ
aśeṣabhūtarūpāya tathābhūtāya te namaḥ
namo 'stu te 'śvarūpāya tathārūpāya te namaḥ
anirdeśyaviśeṣāya tubhyaṃ sarvātmane namaḥ
viṣṇo namo 'stu te kṛṣṇa namas te puruṣottama
śrīśa śrīvatsa yogīśa śrīkānteśa namo 'stu te
nīlotpaladalaśyāma daṃṣṭroddhṛtavasuṃdhara
māyāvāmanarūpāya tubhyaṃ deva namo namaḥ
ṛgyajuḥsāmabhūtāya vedāharaṇakarmaṇe
praṇavodgītavacase mahāśvaśirase namaḥ
niḥkṣatriyorvīkaraṇa vikarālaparākrama
paulastyakulanāśāya sādhumārgavicāriṇe
sāṃprataṃ matprasannāya saṃbhūtāya mamodare
svamāyābālarūpāya namaḥ kṛṣṇāya vai hare
yāvanti tava rūpāṇi yāvatyaś ca vibhūtayaḥ
namāmi kṛṣṇa sarvebhyas tebhyas tābhyaś ca sarvadā
svarūpaceṣṭitaṃ yat te yad devatve viceṣṭitam
parameśa pareśeśa tiryagīśa nareśvara
evaṃ stutas tayā devyā devakyā madhusūdanaḥ
bālarūpī jagādaivaṃ vasudevasya śṛṇvataḥ
tat kṛtaṃ sakalaṃ bhūyo yad vṛṇoṣi dadāmi tat
avatāre tathaivāsmin varṣāṇām adhikaṃ śatam
sthāsyāmi naratāṃ prāpto duṣṭadaityanibarhaṇaḥ
vṛṇomi tad ahaṃ nityaṃ tava keśava darśanam
nālaṃ viyogaṃ saṃsoḍhuṃ tavāhaṃ madhusūdana
dākṣāyaṇī tvam aditiḥ saṃbhūtā vasudhātale
ṣaṣṭhe ṣaṣṭhe tadā pakṣe dine 'sminn eva bhāmini
tvaṃ māṃ drakṣyasy asaṃdigdhaṃ prasādas te kṛto mayā
anenaiva mahābhāge bālarūpeṇa saṃvṛtaḥ
tasmin kāle ca lokās tvāṃ pūjayiṣyanti devaki
saṃpūjito 'haṃ lokānāṃ tasmin kāle sutoṣitaḥ
aputrāṇāṃ varān putrān adhanānāṃ tathā dhanam
śubhān dārān adārāṇāṃ sarogāṇām arogatām
sugatiṃ gatikāmānāṃ vidyāṃ vidyārthinām api
pradāsyasi mahābhāge matprasādopavṛṃhitā
prasāditā hi martyānāṃ yat tvaṃ dāsyasi śobhane
tvām abhyarcyopacāreṇa snāpayitvā ghṛtena mām
sarvakāmān avāpsyanti kāle ṣaṭpakṣasaṃjñite
tvadaṅkasthaṃ ca māṃ bālaṃ saṃsmariṣyanti bhaktitaḥ
evaṃ pūrvaṃ hṛṣīkeśo devakyāḥ pradadau varam
tasmāt kṛṣṇāṣṭamī puṃsām aśeṣāghaughahāriṇī
tasyāṃ hi pūjitaḥ kṛṣṇo devakī ca samādhinā
tad eṣa puṣṭikāmānāṃ nRṇāṃ puṇyārthinām api
upavāso mahīpāla śastaḥ keśavatoṣadaḥ
śrāvaṇe śuklapakṣe tu dvādaśyāṃ prīyate nṛpa
pauṣaśukle tu tadvac ca dvādaśyāṃ ghṛtadhenukām
ghṛtārciḥ prīṇanāyālaṃ pradadyāt phaladāyinīm
tathaiva māghadvādaśyāṃ pradattā tilagaur nṛpa
keśavaṃ prīṇayaty āśu sarvakāmān prayacchati
jyaiṣṭhe māsi site pakṣe dvādaśyāṃ jaladhenukā
dattā yathāvad vidhinā prīṇayaty ambuśāyinam
lavaṇaṃ mārgaśīrṣe tu kṛṣṇam abhyarcya yo naraḥ
pauṣamāse tu yo dadyād ghṛtaṃ viprāya pārthiva
māghamāse tu saṃpūjya mādhavaṃ brāhmaṇāya yaḥ
prayacchati tilāṃl lokān saṃprāpnoty abhivāñchitān
phālgune puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ yaḥ samabhyarcya yacchati
jyaiṣṭhe 'bhyarcya hṛṣīkeśam udakumbhaprado hi yaḥ
sa parāṃ nirvṛtiṃ yāti sapta janmāntarāṇi vai
āṣāḍhamāse ca hariṃ yaḥ samabhyarcya yacchati
śrāvaṇe navanītaṃ tu sa svargaṃ sukṛtī vrajet
chattraṃ ca yo bhādrapade vāsudevābhipūjakaḥ
kāmyāny etāny aśeṣāṇi yaḥ saṃpūjya jagatpatim
dānāni yacchati naraḥ sa saṃpūrṇamanorathaḥ
sarvaśreṣṭhaḥ samastānāṃ bandhūnām āśrayo bhavet
evaṃ sarvāṇi dānāni prīṇanāyācyutasya yaḥ
prayacchati sa sarveṣāṃ phalānāṃ bhuvi bhājanam
yadīcchasi punaḥ prāptuṃ bhūtim abhraṃśanīṃ nṛpa
tadārādhaya govindaṃ nānyathā syur vibhūtayaḥ
evaṃ vasiṣṭhena tadā māndhātā nṛpa bodhitaḥ
saha patnyā mahīpālaḥ paritoṣaṃ paraṃ yayau
saha patnyā naraśreṣṭhaḥ samutthāya varāsanāt
anāsajya manaḥ kṛṣṇe viṣayāsaktacetasaḥ
tā niśās te ca divasās te rtavas te ca vatsarāḥ
narāṇāṃ saphalā yeṣu cintito bhagavān hariḥ
cintyamānaḥ samastānāṃ pāpānāṃ hāṇido hi saḥ
kaṣṭaṃ muṣṭo 'smi śiṣṭeṣu vidyamāneṣu mantriṣu
parāṅmukhānāṃ govinde yat prāptaṃ paramaṃ vayaḥ
evaṃ vinindya so 'tmānāṃ māndhātā pṛthivīpatiḥ
cakārārādhane yatnaṃ devadevasya śārṅgitiṇaḥ
prāpa siddhiṃ parāṃ pūrvaṃ dakṣaḥ prācetaso yathā
samārādhaya govindaṃ tam ārādhya na sīdati
puṣpopahārair dhūpaiś ca tathā caivānulepanaiḥ
vāsobhir bhūṣaṇaiḥ samyag brāhmaṇānāṃ ca tarpaṇaiḥ
bhagavaṃś cañcalaṃ cittaṃ manuṣyāṇām aharniśam
viṣayāsaṅgadurduṣṭaṃ pāpāyaiva pravartate
śārīram apy akaraṇāt sunivartyaṃ mataṃ mama
cañcalatvād dhi cittānāṃ mānasaṃ bahu pātakam
bhūmau tṛṇam asaṃkhyātaṃ yathā ca divi tārakāḥ
aharniśaṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ sātatyena pravartate
tan nāsti narakottāro varṣakoṭīśatair api
tad asya praśamāyālaṃ prāyaścittaṃ narādhipa
śṛṇuṣva yena cittotthaṃ sadyaḥ pāpaṃ vyapohati
oṃ namo vāsudevāya puruṣāya mahātmane
viṣṇave jiṣṇave nityaṃ śāntāyānagharūpiṇe
nārāyaṇāya viśvāya viśveśāyeśvarāya ca
keśavāyātisūkṣmāya brahmamūrtimate namaḥ
namaḥ paramakalyāṇa kalyāṇāyātmayonaye
janārdanāya devāya śrīdharāya sumedhase
mahātmane vareṇyāya namaḥ paṅkajanābhaye
smṛtamātrāghaghātāya kṛṣṇāyākliṣṭakarmaṇe
namo natāya namreśair aśeṣair vāsavādibhiḥ
hiraṇyagarbhagarbhāya jagataḥ kāraṇātmane
govindāyādibhūtāya śrādīnāṃ mahātmane
namo bhūtātmabhūtāya ātmane paramātmane
dāmodarāya śucaye yajñeśāya namo namaḥ
hṛṣīkeśāya ceśāya sarvabhūtātmarūpiṇe
saṃsārasāgarottāra jñānapotapradāyine
karālasaumyarūpāya vaikuṇṭhāya namo namaḥ
yathā na viṣṇubhakteṣu pāpam āpnoti saṃsthitim
smṛtamātro yathā viṣṇuḥ sarvaṃ pāpaṃ vyapohati
upayātu tathā nāśaṃ mamāghaṃ cittasaṃbhavam
pāpaṃ praṇāśaṃ mama saṃprayātu yan mānasaṃ yac ca karomi vācā
śārīram apy ācaritaṃ ca yan me smṛte jagaddhātari vāsudeve
prayāntu doṣā mama nāśam āśu rāgādayaḥ kāraṇakāraṇeśe
vijñānadīpāmalamārgadṛśye smṛte jagaddhātari vāsudeve
bhavantu bhadrāṇi samastadoṣāḥ prayāntu nāśaṃ jagato 'khilasya
ye bhūtale ye divi ye 'ntarikṣe rasātale prāṇigaṇāś ca kecit
ābrahmavṛkṣāntaragā mayādya smṛte jagaddhātari vāsudeve
te yāntu siddhiṃ paramāṃ mayādya smṛte jagaddhātari vāsudeve
ajñānino jñānavido bhavantu praśāntibhājaḥ satatogracittāḥ
paśvādayaḥ kīṭapipīlikāś ca bhavantu te 'py acyutayogabhājaḥ
tenāvivekopahatātmabodhā bhavantu puṃsāṃ matayaḥ suśīlāḥ
satyārjavādyās tv anṛtā vimāyā matsaṃstavārādhitakṛṣṇadṛṣṭāḥ
naśyantu duḥkhāni jagaty apaitu lobhādiko doṣaguṇaḥ prajābhyaḥ
saṃsāravaidye 'khiladoṣahāni vicakṣaṇe nirvṛtihetubhūte
saṃsārabandhāḥ śithilībhavantu hṛdi sthite sarvajanasya viṣṇau
uddiśya sattvāni ca yāni yāni stotraṃ paṭhante kṛpayā manuṣyāḥ
saṃkīrtanaṃ kāryam aśeṣapāpa vimokṣahetor abhavāya caiva
iti sakalajanopakārakārī haricaraṇābjaviniṣṭaśuddhabuddhiḥ
idaṃ ca śṛṇu bhūpāla naśyate durvicintitam
yenopāyena vai puṃsāṃ yoṣitāṃ vāpy asaṃśayam
viṣṇave viṣṇave nityaṃ viṣṇave viṣṇave namaḥ
jiṣṇave jiṣṇave sarvaṃ jiṣṇave jiṣṇave namaḥ
namāmi viṣṇuṃ buddhistham ahaṃkāragataṃ harim
viṣṇum īḍyam aśeṣeśam anādinidhanaṃ vibhum
yac cāhaṃkārago viṣṇur yad viṣṇur mayi saṃsthitaḥ
tat pāpaṃ nāśam āyātu tasminn eva vicintite
dhyāto harati yaḥ pāpaṃ svapne dṛṣṭaḥ śubhāvahaḥ
hastāvalambadaṃ viṣṇuṃ praṇato 'smi parātparam
hṛṣīkeśa hṛṣīkeśa hṛṣīkeśa namo 'stu te
nṛsiṃhānanta govinda bhūtabhāvana keśava
duruktaṃ duṣkṛtaṃ dhyātaṃ praśamāgrya namo 'stu te
yan mayā cintitaṃ duṣṭaṃ svacittavaśavartinā
jagannātha jagaddhātaḥ pāpaṃ praśamayācyuta
yac cāparāhne pūrvāhne madhyāhne ca tathā niśi
kāyena manasā vācā kṛtaṃ pāpam ajānatā
jānatā vā hṛṣīkeśa puṇḍarīkākṣa mādhava
śārīraṃ me hṛṣīkeśa puṇḍarīkākṣa mānasam
pāpaṃ praśamayādya tvaṃ vākkṛtaṃ mama mādhava
kṛtavāṃś cāpi yac cāhaṃ kāyena manasā girā
tad yātu praśamaṃ sarvaṃ vāsudevasya kīrtanāt
tasmin saṃkīrtite viṣṇoḥ pade pāpaṃ praṇaśyatu
sūrayo yat pravekṣyanti hy apunarbhavakāṅkṣiṇaḥ
mamākhilaṃ daha tvaṃ hi tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam
pāpaṃ praṇāśayatv adya tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam
praṇamāmi jagaddhāma tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam
śārīre mānase caiva pāpe vāgje ca pārthiva
mucyate sarvapāpebhyaḥ kṛṣṇanāmaprakīrtanāt
vilayaṃ pāpam āyāti bhāṇḍam āmam ivāmbhasi
saṃsārārṇavamagnena puruṣeṇa mahāmune
bhrāmyatāṃ saṃkaṭe durge saṃsāre viṣayaiṣiṇām
svakarmabhir manuṣyāṇām upakārakam ucyatām
kṣīpte manasy anāyatte vṛddhe lobhādike gaṇe
śaraṇaṃ yan manuṣyāṇāṃ tad ācakṣva mahāmune
namaskṛtya pravakṣyāmi narāṇām upakārakam
kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ prāha yac chiṣyāya sumantave
kṣatrabandhur abhūt pāpaḥ paramarmāvaghaṭṭakaḥ
mātāpitror aśuśrūṣur drogdhā bandhujanasya ca
gurudevadvijātīnāṃ nindāsu satatodyataḥ
moṣṭā viśvasatāṃ nityam aprītiḥ prītim icchatām
ṛjūnām anṛjuḥ kṣudraḥ parahiṃsāparāyaṇaḥ
avṛttimān aviśvāsyo mṛgayājīvano 'bhavat
ahany ahani cakrāṅgān eṇakādīṃs tathā mṛgān
hatvātmapoṣaṇaṃ cakre vyādhavṛttirato 'dhamaḥ
etayā tasya duṣṭasya kuvṛttyā pāpacetasaḥ
jagāma sumahān kālaḥ kurvato dārapoṣaṇam
mṛgayām aṭatā dṛṣṭo vartmanaḥ pracyutaḥ pathi
kṣutkṣāmakaṇṭhaḥ suśrāntaḥ śuṣkajihvāsyatālukaḥ
tṛṭparīto 'tivibhrāntaḥ kāṃdigbhūto 'lpacetanaḥ
śvāsāyāsaślathair aṅgaiḥ kṛcchrād ātmānam udvahan
sūryāṃśutāpāt pragalat svedārdracaraṇo nṛpa
kāruṇyaṃ dāruṇasyāpi vyādhavṛttiparigrahāt
naiṣa panthā dvijaśreṣṭha vipino 'yaṃ mahāṭaviḥ
niśāmya tad vacaḥ śrāntaḥ kṣatrabandhor mahānuniḥ
anuvavrāja rājendra jalāśājanitodyamaḥ
kiṃcid bhūbhāgam āsādya dadarśa ca mahāmuniḥ
haṃsakāraṇḍavākīrṇaṃ protphullanalinaṃ saraḥ
sārasābhirutaṃ ramyaṃ sūpatīrtham akardamam
padmotpalayutaṃ cāru pūrṇaṃ svacchena vāriṇā
suśītavanaṣaṇḍaiś ca samantāt pariveṣṭitam
tatkṣaṇāt tṛṭparītānāṃ cakṣuṣo hlādakāriṇam
dṛṣṭvaiva sa munis tatra tadāmalajalaṃ saraḥ
sūryāṃśutapto gharmārto nipapāta tadambhasi
tatrāśvāsya kṛtāhlādaḥ papau vāri narādhipa
ujjīvayan munivaro jihvātālu śanaiḥ śanaiḥ
so 'pi kṣatriyadāyādo munitrāṇaparāyaṇaḥ
vihāya saśaraṃ cāpam ujjahāra bisāny atha
yayau ca tṛptiṃ vipro 'pi bisanālāmbubhakṣaṇāt
tam āśvastaṃ kṛtāhāram upaviṣṭaṃ suśītale
nyagrodhaśākhāsaṃchanne niṣpaṅke sarasas taṭe
saṃvāhayām āsa ca taṃ kṣatrabandhuḥ śanaiḥ śanaiḥ
pādajaṅghorupṛṣṭeṣu tena saṃvāhito muniḥ
vibhraṣṭamārgo mūḍho 'haṃ kṣutpipāsāśramāturaḥ
kṣutpipāsāśramārtasya yas trāṇaṃ vipine vane
sa tvaṃ brūhi mahābhāga mamābhyuddhārakārakaḥ
yeṣāṃ prakhyātayaśasāṃ samutpannaḥ kule bhavān
vimatir nāma nāmnāhaṃ hantum abhyāgato mṛgān
pitrarthaṃ mṛgayeyaṃ te lakṣyārthaṃ vā mahāmate
āhārārtham utāho 'tra mṛgayā vyasanaṃ tu te
bhṛtyair anyaiś ca naṣṭe 'rthe nirdhanasyāmiṣāśinaḥ
pātakī kīkaṭaḥ kṣudrair upajaptaḥ pareṇa vā
ity uktaḥ so 'bhavan maunī paśyan doṣaṃ nṛpātmani
aduṣṭāṃś cātmano bhṛtyān vicintyātīva durmanāḥ
avekṣya taṃ sādhvasinaṃ kṣatrabandhuṃ mahāmuniḥ
dhyātvā ciram athāpaśyat kṣatrabandhuṃ svadoṣiṇam
kṛpāṃ cakāra sa muniḥ kṣatrabandhau dayāparaḥ
uvāca ca munir bhūyaḥ kṣatrabandhuṃ kṛpālukaḥ
upakāriṇam ugreṇa karmaṇā taṃ vidūṣitam
api śaknoṣi saṃyantum akāryaprasṛtaṃ manaḥ
prāṇi pīḍānivṛttiṃ ca kartuṃ krodhādisaṃyamam
api maitrīṃ jane kartuṃ śaknoṣi tvaṃ mudhaiva yā
aihikāmuṣmikī vīra kriyamāṇā mahāphalā
na śaknomi kṣamāṃ kartuṃ na maitrīṃ mama cetasi
prāṇinām avadhād brahman nāsti dārādipoṣaṇam
anāyattaṃ ca me cittaṃ viṣayān eva dhāvati
tadaprāptau ca sarveṣāṃ krodhādīnāṃ samudbhavaḥ
so 'haṃ na maitrīṃ na kṣāntiṃ na hiṃsādivivarjanam
tathāpy atikṛpālutvāt kṣatrabandhum abhāṣata
aśakyam uktaṃ bhavatā cañcalatvād dhi cetasaḥ
vākśarīraviniṣpādyaṃ yac chakyaṃ tad udīraya
uttiṣṭhatā prasvapatā prasthitena gamiṣyatā
govindeti sadā vācyaṃ kṣutapraskhalitādiṣu
kāryaṃ vartmani mūḍhānāṃ kṣemamārge 'vatāraṇam
hitaṃ ca vācyaṃ pṛṣṭena śatrūṇām api jānatā
udīrayann avāpāgryāṃ ratiṃ tatra śanaiḥ śanaiḥ
tasya saṃsmarato jātīḥ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
nirvedaḥ sumahāñ jajñe saṃsāre 'trātiduḥkhade
aham eko 'tra saṃjñāvān govindodīritaṃ hi yat
yac cādhvani vimūḍhānāṃ kṛtaṃ vartmāvatāraṇam
hitam uktaṃ ca pṛṣṭena tasya jātismṛtiḥ phalam
so 'haṃ jātismaro bhūyaḥ kariṣyāmy atisaṃkaṭe
yasyoccāraṇamātreṇa jātā jātismṛtir mama
tam evārādhayiṣyāmi jagatām īśvaraṃ harim
viṇmūtrapūyakalile garbhavāse 'tipīḍanāt
duḥkhaṃ ca jāyamānānāṃ gātrabhaṅgādipīḍanāt
vātena preryamāṇānāṃ mūrchākāry atibhītidam
bālatve nirvivekānāṃ bhūtadevātmasaṃbhavam
śītoṣṇatṛṣṇākṣudroga jvarādiparivāritaḥ
duḥkhātiśayabhūtaṃ hi yad ante vāsukhaṃ nṛṇām
tasyānumānaṃ naivāsti kāryeṇaivānumīyate
kṛṣyamāṇasya puruṣair yad yamasyātiduḥsaham
kālasūtre mahāyantre śūkare kūṭaśālmalau
śastrāgniyantravegeṣu śītoṣṇādiṣu dāruṇam
duḥkhāny etāny asahyāni saṃsārāntarvivartibhiḥ
saṃsārasaṃkaṭe tīvre upetānāṃ kadācana
viṣayāsaktacittānāṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ kadā matiḥ
saṃsārottāraṇe vāñchāṃ kariṣyati hi cañcalā
govindanāmnā satataṃ samuccāraṇasaṃbhavam
taccittas tanmayo bhūtvā toṣayiṣyāmi keśavam
ātmānam ātmanaivaṃ sa proktvā jātismaro dvijaḥ
tuṣṭāva vāgbhir iṣṭābhiḥ praṇataḥ puruṣottamam
praṇipatyākṣaraṃ viśvaṃ viśvahetuṃ nirañjanam
kartāram akṛtaṃ viṣṇuṃ sarvakāraṇakāraṇam
aṇor aṇīyāṃsam ajaṃ sarvavyāpinam īśvaram
taṃ praṇamyācyutaṃ devaṃ prārthayāmi yad astu tat
sarveśvarācyutānanta paramātmañ janārdana
saṃsārābdhimahāpota samuddhara mahārṇavāt
tadvad visṛṣṭer amarādibhinnair vikāśam āyāsi vibhūtibhedaiḥ
kiṃtv īśa māyā bhavato nijeyam āviṣkṛtāviṣkṛtalokasṛṣṭe
yayāham eṣo 'nyatamo mameti madīyam asyābhivadanti mūḍhāḥ
bhūmyambarāgnisalileṣu deva jāgratsuṣuptādiṣu duḥkhitena
na santi tāvanti jalāny apīḍya sarveṣu nāthābdhiṣu sarvakālam
stanyāni yāvanti mayātighore pītāni saṃsāramahāsamudre
saṃpac chilānāṃ himavanmahendra kailāsamervādiṣu naiva tādṛk
na santi te deva bhuvi pradeśā na yeṣu jāto 'smi tathā vinaṣṭaḥ
attā mayā yeṣu na jantavaś ca saṃbhakṣito yaiś ca na jantusaṃghaiḥ
siṃhena bhūtvā bahavo mayāttā vyāghreṇa bhūtvā bahavo mayāttāḥ
tathānyarūpair bahavo mayāttāḥ saṃbhakṣito 'haṃ bahubhis tataś ca
utkrāntiduḥkhāny atiduḥsahāni sahasraśo yāny anusaṃsmarāmi
taiḥ saṃsmṛtais tat kṣaṇam eva deva taḍid yathā me hṛdayaṃ prayāti
