tataś ca duḥkhāny anivāraṇāni yantrāgniśastraughasamudbhavāni
bhavanti yāny acyuta nārakānāṃ tāny eva teṣām upamānamātram
bhavanti yāni cyavataś ca garbhāt teṣāṃ svarūpaṃ gadituṃ na śakyam
duḥkhāni bāleṣu mahanti nātha kaumārake yauvaninaś ca puṃsaḥ
jvarātisārākṣirugādikāni samastaduḥkhālaya eva vṛddhaḥ
karoti karmācyuta tatkṣaṇena pāpaṃ naraḥ kāyamanovacobhiḥ
yasyābdalakṣair api nāntam eti śastrādiyantrāgninipīḍaneṣu
duḥkhāni yānīṣṭaviyogajāni bhavanti saṃsāravihārabhājām
pratyekaśas teṣu narā vināśam icchanty asūnāṃ mamatābhibhūtāḥ
śokābhibhūtasya mamāśru deva yāvatpramāṇaṃ na jalaṃ payodā
tāvatpramāṇaṃ na jalaṃ payodā muñcanty anekair api varṣalakṣaiḥ
manye dharitrī paramāṇusaṃkhyām upaiti pitror gaṇanāmaśeṣam
mitrāṇy amitrāṇy anujīvibandhūn saṃkhyātam īśo 'smi na devadeva
so 'haṃ bhṛśārtaḥ karuṇāṃ kuru tvaṃ saṃsāragātre patitasya viṣṇo
mām uddharāsmād uruduḥkhapaṅkāt saṃsāragartāt svaparigraheṇa
dharmātmanām avikalāṃ tvayi nātha bhaktiṃ śraddhāvatāṃ satatam udvahatāṃ vareṇya
jñātvā yayākhilam asāram asāram eva bhūtendriyādikam apāram amuktimūlam
brahmendrarudramarudaśvidivākarādyā jñātuṃ na yaṃ paramaguhyatamaṃ samarthāḥ
na tvām alaṃ stutipatheṣv aham īśitāraṃ stoṣyāmi mohakaluṣālpamatir manuṣyaḥ
itthaṃ kṛpāṃ kuru mayi praṇate kileśa tvāṃ stotum ambujabhavo 'pi hi deva neśaḥ
bhūmyambuvāyugaganaṃ jagatāṃ samuhāṃ stoṣyāmi taṃ stutipadaiḥ katamair bhavantam
yasyāgnirudrakamalodbhavavāsavādyaiḥ svāṃśāvatārakaraṇeṣu sadāṅghriyugmam
cittaṃ ca na tvayi samāhitam īśa doṣair ākṣipyate kathaya kiṃ nu karomi pāpaḥ
tat tvaṃ prasīda bhagavan kuru mayy anāthe viṣṇo kṛpāṃ paramakāruṇikaḥ kila tvam
saṃsārabandhabhītena kṛṣṇaḥ pratyakṣatāṃ yayau
sa taṃ pratyakṣam īśānam anantam aparājitam
śirasā dharaṇīṃ gatvā yatavākkāyamānasaḥ
parāpareśvaraṃ viṣṇuṃ jiṣṇum ādyam anopamam
varārthināṃ dvijaśreṣṭha nāphalaṃ mama darśanam
janmasaṃpaccitā deva pāpasaṃpan mamākhilā
prayātu nāśam īśeśa tvatprasādād adhokṣaja
yaḥ stuto 'smi kṣayaṃ pāpaṃ tenaivākhilam āgatam
yad akṣaraṃ yad acalaṃ vyāpi sūkṣmaṃ ca yat param
viśeṣāir aviśeṣaṃ ca gaccheyaṃ tat padaṃ tava
bhūpāla taṃ dvijaśreṣṭhaṃ gato 'ntardhānam īśvaraḥ
evam akṣīṇapāpo 'pi jagatām īśvareśvaram
vyapāśrito hariṃ yāti pāpamuktaḥ paraṃ padam
etat tvayā nāvratine na cāśuśrūṣave param
ākhyeyaṃ rājaśārdūla yaś ca nārcayate harim
viṣṇubhaktāya dāntāya vratine puṇyaśīline
kathanīyam idaṃ bhūpa rahasyaṃ paramaṃ hareḥ
bahuśo bhavatā proktaṃ sāṃprataṃ ca yad īritam
yatsvarūpaṃ yadādhāraṃ yatpramāṇaṃ yadātmakam
sādhv etad bhavatā pṛṣṭaṃ pṛṣṭam ātmajñānasamāśritam
tat kathyamānam ekāgraḥ śṛṇu viṣṇoḥ paraṃ padam
tatsvarūpaṃ ca rājendra śṛṇuṣveha samāhitaḥ
pradhānādiviśeṣāntaṃ yad etat paṭhyate jagat
janmasvapnādirūpādi duḥkhādirahitaṃ ca yat
kṣīṇakleśās tu saṃsāra vimuktipatham āśritāḥ
paśyatām apy anirdeśyaṃ yato vāgviṣaye na tat
brahma prakāśate teṣāṃ tad vareṇaiva sarvagam
pradhānādiviśeṣāntaṃ yatraitad akhilaṃ jagat
tasyānantasya kaḥ śaktaḥ pramāṇaṃ gadituṃ naraḥ
sūkṣmāṇāṃ tat paraṃ sūkṣmaṃ sthūlānāṃ tan mahattaram
parāṅmukhānāṃ govinde viṣayākrāntacetasām
teṣāṃ tat paramaṃ brahma dūrād dūratare sthitam
viṣayatyāginas teṣāṃ vijñeyaṃ ca tadantike
sarvataḥ pāṇipādāntaṃ sarvato 'kṣiśiromukham
sarvataḥ śrutimal loke sarvam āvṛtya tiṣṭhati
bhūtabhartṛ ca taj jñeyaṃ grasiṣṇu prabhaviṣṇu ca
jñānaṃ jñeyaṃ jñānagamyaṃ hṛdi sarvasy adhiṣṭhitam
tac cādyo jagatām īśaḥ pareśaḥ parameśvaraḥ
parāparasvarūpeṇa viṣṇuḥ sarvahṛdi sthitaḥ
kecid viṣṇuṃ hariṃ kecit kecit keśavasaṃjñitam
kecid govindanāmānaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣam acyutam
kecid viriñciṃ brāhmaṇam abjayoniṃ tathāpare
śarvam īśam ajaṃ rudraṃ śūlinaṃ cāpare nṛpa
hiraṇyagarbhaṃ kapilaṃ kṣetrajñaṃ kālam īśvaram
svabhāvam antarātmānam ātmānaṃ buddhirūpiṇam
vadanti nāmabhiś cānyair anāmānam arūpiṇam
śrūyatāṃ tu naravyāghra vedavedāntaniścayaḥ
yajñeśo yajñapuruṣo puṇḍarīkākṣasaṃjñitaḥ
tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ brahma yato nāvartate punaḥ
kṣetrajñākhyas tathaivānyāḥ saṃjñābhiḥ procyate budhaiḥ
saṃjñā tu tasya naivāsti na rūpaṃ nāpi kalpanā
sa sarvabhūtānugataḥ paramātmā sanātanaḥ
pariṇāmo na tasyāsti nirguṇaṃ sarvagaṃ yataḥ
sanātanāt sarvagatāt pariṇāmavivarjitāt
kathaṃ saṃjāyate kṛtsnaṃ tasmād apaguṇād api
nimittakāraṇaṃ pūrvaṃ dvitīyaṃ pariṇāmi ca
yathā kumbhasya karaṇe kulālaḥ prathamaṃ nṛpa
kāraṇaṃ pariṇāmākhyaṃ mṛddravyam aparaṃ smṛtam
kāraṇaṃ pariṇāmākhyaṃ nimittākhyaṃ tu tat param
kāraṇaṃ kālagagane yathā saṃnidhimātrataḥ
avikāritayā brahma tathā sṛṣṭer nareśvara
ajñānapaṭalācchanair ekadeśātmavṛttibhiḥ
yataḥ saṃbandhavān ebhir aśeṣaiḥ prāṇibhiḥ prabhuḥ
tayoḥ svarūpaṃ nṛpate śrūyatām ubhayor api
anādisaṃbandhavatyā kṣetrajñaḥ kṣetravidyayā
saṃkṣīnāśeṣakarmā tu paraṃ brahma prapaśyati
abhedenātmanaḥ śuddhaṃ śuddhatvād akṣayo 'kṣayam
karmiṇāṃ karmabhedena bhedād evādayo yataḥ
karmakṣayād aśeṣāṇāṃ bhedānāṃ saṃkṣayas tataḥ
avidyā tu kriyā sarvā vidyā jñānaṃ pracakṣate
abhedena tavākhyātaṃ yad etad brahma śāśvatam
jñānajñeyaikyasadbhāvaṃ tad evādvaitasaṃjñitam
manaso hy amatībhāve dvaitābhāvāt tad āpnuyāt
agrāhi tac ca vidhṛtaṃ yogināṃ viṣayaṃ prati
kṣīṇakleśās tu saṃsāra vimuktipatham āśritāḥ
ye 'pi karmāṇi kurvanti bhagavantam apāśritāḥ
kriyāyogaparā rājan kāmākāṅkṣāvivarjitāḥ
brahmaniṣṭhā dhyānaparā brahmaṇy eva vyavasthitāḥ
te 'pi tadbhāvam āyānti vimuktipatham āśritāḥ
karmaṇo bhāvanā yeyaṃ sā brahmaparipanthinī
tādṛg bhavato vijñaptir yādṛśī karmabhāvanā
kṣaye tasyāḥ paraṃ brahma svayam eva prakāśate
yathāvat karmaniṣṭhānāṃ tatprāptiḥ kathitaṃ tathā
vāsudevamayasyānyat kiṃ bhūyaḥ kathayāmi te
viṣṇur eva jagaddhātā yogināṃ vartate yataḥ
upāyas tasya yaḥ prāpto viṣṇor īśasya bhārgava
yena janmajarāmṛtyu mahāgrāhabhavārṇavam
tvadvākyanāvam āruhya muktitīram avāpnuyām
tasyāpagamane yatnaḥ kāryaḥ saṃsārabhīruṇā
suvarṇādimahādāna puṇyatīrthāvagāhanaiḥ
śārīraiś ca tathā kleśaiḥ śāstroktais tacchamo bhavet
devatāstutisacchāstra śravaṇaiḥ puṇyadarśanaiḥ
guruśuśrūṣaṇāc caiva pāpabandhaḥ praṇaśyati
prapākūpataḍāgāni devatāyatanāni ca
yoginām atha śuśrūṣāṃ tathaivāvasathān nṛpa
kurvan pūrtāśritaṃ cānyat pāpabandhāt pramucyate
viṣṇuḥ kṛṣṇo vāsudevo govindaḥ puṣkarekṣaṇaḥ
viśvo viśveśvaro viśva vidhātā dhāma śāśvatam
padmanābho hṛṣīkeśaḥ keśavo madhusūdanaḥ
nārāyaṇaś cakradharo viśvarūpas trivikramaḥ
viṣṇau pratiṣṭhitaṃ viśvaṃ viṣṇur viśve pratiṣṭhitaḥ
viṣṇur viśveśvaro viśvam iti bhāvāt pramucyate
evaṃ saṃśāntapāpasya puṇyavṛddhimato nṛpa
muktidāyīni karmāṇi niṣkāmena kṛtāni tu
nityanaimittikānīha karmāṇy uktāni yāni vai
teṣāṃ niṣkāmakāraṇāt puṇyabandhaḥ praśāmyati
anekajanmasaṃsāra citasyāpi dṛḍhātmanaḥ
karmabandhasya śaithilya kāraṇaṃ cāparaṃ śṛṇu
titikṣā samadarśitvaṃ maitryādau daṇḍasaṃyamaḥ
ṛjutvam indriyajayaḥ śaucam ācāryapūjanam
avivādas tathā mūḍhair amūḍhaiḥ praśnasatkathā
sadbhiḥ sahāsya satataṃ yogābhyāso mitoktitā
parayoṣidvilāsānāṃ kāvyālāpavivarjanam
gītavāditanṛtteṣu mṛdaṅgeṣv apareṣu ca
asṛṅmāṃsādibhūtatvān nijadehajugupsanam
sarvāṇy etāni bhūtāni viṣṇur ity acalā matiḥ
tatraivāśeṣabhūteśe bhaktir avyabhicāriṇī
ete guṇā mayākhyātā manonirvṛtikārakāḥ
ebhiḥ śāntiṃ gate citte dhyānākṛṣṭaḥ sthito hariḥ
śamaṃ nayati karmāṇi sitamiśrāsitāni vai
bhūyaś ca śṛṇu śāstrārthaṃ saṃkṣepād vadato mama
nityanaimittikānāṃ tu niṣkāmasya hi yā kriyā
nisiddhānāṃ sakāmānāṃ tathaivākaraṇaṃ nṛpa
prayacchati nṛṇāṃ muktiṃ mā te bhūd atra saṃśayaḥ
ākhyātam etad akhilaṃ yat pṛṣṭo 'si mayā dvija
jāyate śamakāmānāṃ praśamaḥ karmaṇāṃ yathā
kiṃtv atra bhavatā proktā praśāntiḥ sarvakarmaṇām
nātyantanāśaḥ śāntānām udbhavo bhavitā punaḥ
nijakāraṇam āsādya stokasyāgner yathā tṛṇam
na karmaṇāṃ kṣayo bhūpa janmanām ayutair api
karmakṣayam ṛte yogād yogāgniḥ kṣapayet param
taṃ yogaṃ mama viprarṣe praṇatasyābhiyācataḥ
tvam ācakṣva kṣayo yena jāyate 'khilakarmaṇām
pṛṣṭaḥ provāca yaṃ yogaṃ taṃ samāsena me śṛṇu
anādikālaprasṛtā yathā vidyā mahīpate
taṃ paraṃparayā śrutvā munayo 'tra dayālavaḥ
prakāśayanti bhūtānām upakāracikīrṣavaḥ
devā maharṣayo rājaṃs tathā rājarṣayo 'khilāḥ
śreyo'rthinaḥ purā jagmuḥ śaraṇaṃ kapilaṃ kila
te tam ūcur bhavān nityaṃ dayāluḥ sarvajantuṣu
so 'smān uddhara saṃmagnān itaḥ saṃsārakardamāt
yac chreyaḥ sarvavarṇānāṃ strīṇām apy upakārakam
ādāv ante ca madhye ca nRṇāṃ yad upakārakam
api kīṭapataṃgānāṃ tan naḥ śreyaḥ paraṃ vada
nāsti yogāt paraṃ śreyaḥ kiṃcid ity uktavān purā
yathā janmāyutaiḥ kleśāḥ sthairyaṃ cetasy upāgatāḥ
sa evābhyasatāṃ nRṇāṃ tīvrasaṃvegicetasām
āsannatāṃ prayāty āśu viṣṇuḥ saṃnyastakarmaṇām
brāhmaṇakṣatriyaviśāṃ strīśūdrasya ca pāvanam
śāntaye karmaṇāṃ nānyad yogād asti hi muktaye
yogasvarūpaṃ tat teṣāṃ strīśūdratve vyavasthitam
yogābhyāso nṛṇāṃ yeṣāṃ nāsti janmāntarāhṛtaḥ
yogasya prāptaye teṣāṃ śūdravaiśyādikaḥ kramaḥ
anūcānas tathā yajvī karmanyāsī tataḥ param
yeṣāṃ tu jātimātreṇa yogābhyāsas tirohitaḥ
yathā vāteritaḥ kakṣaṃ dahaty ūrdhvaśikho 'nalaḥ
yathā dagdhatuṣaṃ bījam abījatvān na jāyate
yogadagdhais tathā kleśair nātmā saṃjāyate punaḥ
adṛṣṭā dṛṣṭatattvānāṃ yogināṃ yogavicyutiḥ
yeṣāṃ bhavati yogitvaṃ prāpnuvantīha te punaḥ
sajjātiprāpakaṃ karma kṛtaṃ tena tadātmanā
jātiṃ prayānti viprādyā yogakarmānurañjitāḥ
tatrāpy anekajanmottha yogābhyāsānurañjitāḥ
jaigīṣavyo yathā vipro yathā caivāsitādayaḥ
hiraṇyanābho rājanyas tathā vai janakādayaḥ
pūrvābhyastena yogena tulādhārādayo viśaḥ
saṃprāptāḥ paramāṃ siddhiṃ śūdrāḥ pailavakādayaḥ
maitreyī sulabhā gārgī śāṇḍilī ca tapasvinī
strītve prāptāḥ parāṃ siddhim anyajanmasamādhitaḥ
varṇāvaratve saṃprāptāḥ saṃsiddhiṃ śravaṇī tathā
pūrvābhyastaṃ ca tat teṣāṃ yogajñānaṃ mahātmanām
tac chṛṇuṣva vadāmy eṣa vācyaṃ śuśrūṣatāṃ satām
yo dadyād bhagavajjñānaṃ kuryād vā dharmadeśanām
kṛtsnāṃ vā pṛthivīṃ dadyān na tattulyaṃ kathaṃcana
kṣayiṣṇūny aparāṇīha dānāni manujādhipa
ekam evākṣayaṃ śastaṃ jñānadānam anuttamam
dānāny ekaphalānīha trailokye dadatā satām
jñānaṃ prayacchatā samyak kiṃ na dattaṃ bhaven nṛpa
jñānāny anyāny asārāṇi śilpinīva nareśvara
ekam eva paraṃ jñānaṃ yad yogaprāptikārakam
ahaṃ vaktā bhavāñ śrotā vācyo yogo vimuktidaḥ
prāṇinām upakārāya saṃpad eṣā guṇādhikā
pareṇa brahmaṇā sārdham ekatvaṃ yan nṛpātmanaḥ
tayoḥ svarūpaṃ vakṣyāmi tad ihaikamanāḥ śṛṇu
sattāmātraṃ paraṃ brahma viṣṇvākhyam aviśeṣaṇam
vātālīcañcalaṃ cittam anālambanam asthiti
sūkṣmatvād brahmaṇo rājann agrāhy agrāhyadharmiṇaḥ
yady antarāya doṣeṇa nāpakarṣo narādhipa
yogino yogarūḍhasya tālāgrāt patanaṃ yathā
jñānaṃ prayacchatāṃ samyak kiṃ vadatu bhaven nṛpa
viṣṇvākhyaṃ brahma duṣprāpaṃ viṣayākṛṣṭacetasā
manuṣyeṇeti tatprāptāv upāyam aparaṃ śṛṇu
surūpāṃ pratimāṃ viṣṇoḥ prasannavadanekṣaṇām
kṛtvātmanaḥ prītikarīṃ suvarṇarajatādibhiḥ
tasyāś ca lakṣaṇaṃ bhūpa śṛṇuṣva gadato mama
suvarṇarūpyatāmrais tu ārakūṭamayīṃ tathā
śailadārumṛdā vāpi lekhyajāṃ vāpi kārayet
kāryas tu viṣṇur bhagavān saumyarūpaś caturbhujaḥ
salilādhmātameghābhaḥ śrīmāñ śrīvatsabhūṣitaḥ
ābaddhamakuṭaḥ sragvī hārabhārārpitodaraḥ
svakṣeṇa cārucipukaḥ sulalāṭena subhruṇā
kaṇṭhena śubhalekhena varābharaṇadhāriṇā
nānāratnānatārtābhyāṃ śravaṇābhyām alaṃkṛtaḥ
puṣṭaśliṣṭāyatabhujas tanutāmranakhāṅguliḥ
madhyena trivalībhaṅga bhūṣitena ca cāruṇā
supādaḥ sūruyugalaḥ sukaṭīgulphajānukaḥ
vāmapārśve gadādevī cakraṃ devasya dakṣiṇe
ūrdhvadṛṣṭim adhodṛṣṭiṃ tiryagdṛṣṭiṃ na kārayet
nimīlitākṣo bhagavān na praśasto janārdanaḥ
saumyā tu dṛṣṭiḥ kartavyā kiṃcit prahasiteva ca
kāryaś caraṇavinyāsaḥ sarvataḥ supratiṣṭhitaḥ
caraṇāntarasaṃsthā ca bibhratī rūpam uttamam
kāryā vasuṃdharā devī tatpādataladhāriṇī
yādṛgvidhā vā manasaḥ sthairyalambhopapādikā
nṛsiṃhavāmanādīnāṃ tādṛśīṃ kārayed budhaḥ
tām ārcayet tāṃ praṇamet tāṃ smaret tāṃ vicintayet
tām arcayaṃs tāṃ praṇamaṃs tāṃ smaraṃs tāṃ ca cintayan
viśaty apāstadoṣas tu tām eva brahmarūpiṇīm
saṃkalpanakriyārūḍhaḥ svarūpeṇa nṛpātmanaḥ
kurvīta bhāvanāṃ tatra tadbhāvotpattikāraṇāt
yamaiś ca niyamaiś caiva pūtātmā pṛthivīśvara
mūrtiṃ bhagavataḥ saṃyak pūjayet tanmayaḥ sadā
yamāṃś ca niyamāṃś caiva śrotum icchāmi bhārgava
yamās tavaite kathitā niyamān api me śṛṇu
saṃtoṣaśaucasvādhyāyās tapaś ceśvarabhāvanā
niyamāḥ kauravaśreṣṭha yogasaṃsiddhihetavaḥ
śraddadhānasya cānyāni yogāṅgāni nibodha me
madhyamaprāṇam acalaṃ sukhadāyi śubhaṃ śuci
yogasaṃsiddhaye bhūpa yoginām āsanaṃ smṛtam
prāṇāyāmas tridhā vāyoḥ prāṇasya hṛdi dhāraṇam
ete nibodha mātrās tu nālambanaguṇānvitāḥ
sālambanaś caturtho 'nyo bāhyāntarviṣayaḥ smṛtaḥ
indriyāṇāṃ svaviṣayād buddhiḥ pratyekaśas tu yat
karoty āharaṇaṃ jñeyaḥ pratyāhāraḥ sa paṇḍitaiḥ
dhyānākhyā labhate rājan samādhim api me śṛṇu
kathitāni tavaitāni yogāṅgāni kṛtais tu yaiḥ
yogāṅgāny aṅgabhūtāni dhyānasyaitāny aśeṣataḥ
dhyānam ekavratānāṃ tu kuśalākuśaleṣu tat
śubhāvyāvartitaṃ dhyānam avivekasya jāyate
saṃsāraduḥkhadaṃ rājann aśubhālambi tad yataḥ
tad evākṛṣya duṣṭebhyo viṣayebhyaḥ śubhāśubham
sarvasaṃsārakāntāra pāram abhyeti mānavaḥ
duḥkhadāghapraśamane yā cintāharniśaṃ nṛṇām
taddhyānam aviśuddhārthaṃ sukhadānām apālane
manovṛttir manuṣyāṇāṃ dhyānam etac chubhaṃ dvidhā
sukhābhilāṣo yanmuktau bandhuduḥkhādipīḍanāt
avāñchitaphalaṃ lobham alobhāṃśavivarjitam
śubhāśubhaphalaṃ dhyānam araktaṃ dviṣṭam iṣyate
dṛṣṭānumānāgamikaṃ dhyānasyālambanaṃ tridhā
na hi nirviṣayaṃ dhyānaṃ mūḍhavṛttir iveṣyate
prāk sthūleṣu padārtheṣu tataḥ sūkṣmeṣu paṇḍitaḥ
dhyānaṃ kurvīta tatpaścāt paramāṇau mahīpate
kurvītālambanaṃ kāle kasmiṃścid api pārthiva
prāṇinaḥ karmajanita saṃskāravaśavartinaḥ
yatas tato na te dhyāne dhyāninām upakārakāḥ
avidyāntargatāḥ sarve te hi saṃsāragocarāḥ
paścād udbhūtabodhāś ca dhyātā naivopakārakāḥ
dhyeyaṃ dhyānavidāṃ samyag yad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam
tac ca viṣṇoḥ paraṃ rūpam anirdeśyam ajaṃ sthiram
anidram ajam asvapnam arūpānāma śāśvatam
yoginas taṃ prapaśyanti jñānadṛśyaṃ sanātanam
nirdhūtapuṇyapāpā ye te viśanty evam īśvaram
tac ca sarvagataṃ brahma viṣṇuḥ sarveśvareśvaraḥ
paramātmā paraḥ proktaḥ sarvakāraṇakāraṇam
anantaśaktim īśeśaṃ svapratiṣṭham anopamam
yatra sarvaṃ yataḥ sarvaṃ yaḥ sarvaṃ sarvataś ca yaḥ
sargādikāraṇaṃ yasya svabhāvād eva śaktayaḥ
nirdhūtapuṇyapāpā yaṃ viśanty avyayam īśvaram
yad uktaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ tan me gadataḥ śrotum arhasi
nānyālambanasāpekṣaṃ yoginaḥ siddhikārakam
evam ekāgracittasya puṇyāpuṇyam aśeṣataḥ
prayāti saṃkṣayam ṛte dehārambhakare nṛpa
dehārambhakarasyāpi karmaṇaḥ saṃkṣayāvahaḥ
yo yogaḥ pṛthivīpāla śṛṇu tasyāpi lakṣaṇam
puruṣaḥ kāranābhāvād bhedaṃ naivānupaśyati
tadākhyas tanmayo bhūtvā gṛhyate na viśeṣataḥ
na bhedaḥ kalaśākāśa nabhasor iva jāyate
prakṣīṇāśeṣakarmā tu yadā brahmamayaḥ pumān
ghaṭadhvaṃse ghaṭākāśaṃ na bhinnaṃ nabhaso yathā
brahmaṇā heyavidhvaṃse viṣṇvākhyena pumāṃs tathā
bhinne dṛtau yathā vāyur naivānyaḥ saha vāyunā
kṣīṇapuṇyāghabandhas tu tathātmā brahmaṇā saha
āhlādam anyam atulaṃ kam apy āpnoti śāśvatam
ādarśasya malābhāvād vaimalyaṃ kāśate yathā
yathā na kriyate jyotsnā malaprakṣālanādinā
doṣaprahāṇaṃ na jñānam ātmanaḥ kriyate tathā
yathā heyagaṇadhvaṃsād avabodhādayo guṇāḥ
jñānavairāgyam aiśvaryaṃ dharmaś ca manujeśvara
punaś ca śrūyatām eṣa saṃkṣepād gadato mama
nānādvaikatvavijñāna svarūpam avanīpate
ātmā kṣetrajñasaṃjño 'yaṃ saṃyuktaḥ prākṛtair guṇaiḥ
dhyeyaṃ brahma pumān dhyātā upāyo dhyānasaṃjñitaḥ
yas tv etat karaṇeṣv āste tadvarge kā vibhāgatā
saṃkṣepād api bhūpāla saṃkṣepan aparaṃ śṛṇu
putrāya yat pitā brūyāt svaśiṣyāyāthavā guruḥ
saṃsārapāraṃ param īpsamānair ārādhanīyo harir eka eva
ārādhito 'rthān dhanakāṅkṣakānāṃ dharmārthināṃ dharmam aśeṣadharmī
dadāti kāmāṃś ca manoniviṣṭān mokṣārthināṃ muktida eva viṣṇuḥ
śūdro vaiśyatvam abhyeti kathaṃ vaiśyaś ca bhārgava
kṣatriyatvaṃ dvijaśreṣṭha brāhmaṇatvaṃ kathaṃ tataḥ
mayocyamānam akhilaṃ varṇānām upakārakam
śūdradharmān aśeṣeṇa kurvañ śūdro yathāvidhi
sarveṣām eva varṇānāṃ svadharmam anuvartatām
sadocchritir nyūnakṛto hāniś cotkṛṣṭakarmaṇaḥ
teṣāṃ ca brāhmaṇādīnāṃ varṇadharmān anukramāt
anasūyā dayā kṣāntiḥ śaucaṃ maṅgalam aspṛhā
akārpaṇyam anāyāsas tathānyaḥ sārvavarṇikaḥ
aṣṭāv ete guṇāḥ puṃsāṃ paratreha ca bhūtaye
bhavanti kuruśārdūla pṛthagdharmāṃś ca me śṛṇu
yajñādhyayanadānāni brahmakṣatraviśāṃ nṛpa
sādhāraṇāni teṣāṃ tu jīvikākarma kathyate
bhṛtyādibharaṇaṃ kuryād yajñāṃś ca vibhave sati
bhṛtyādibharaṇe nālaṃ svavṛttyā hi yadā dvijaḥ
tadā jīvet samālambya vṛttiṃ kṣatriyavaiśyayoḥ
saṃtyajeta samastāṃs tān na kuryād vṛttisaṃkaram
prajānāṃ pālanaṃ samyag vidhiḥ prathamakalpitaḥ
rājanyasya mahīpāla śastrājīvena vā bhṛtiḥ
tasyāpy āpadi vaiśyasya yā vṛttiḥ sā vidhīyate
vāṇijyaṃ vaiśyajātasya paśūnāṃ pālanaṃ kṛṣiḥ
dvijātijanaśuśrūṣāṃ krayavikrayajair dhanaiḥ
śūdro yajet pākayajñair dadyād iṣṭāni cārthinām
tasmai śuśrūṣave deyaṃ jīrṇavastram upānahau
caturṇām api varṇānāṃ dharmas te kathito mayā
śṛṇuṣva ca mahīpāla dharmam āśramiṇām ataḥ
kṛtopanayanaḥ pūrvaṃ brahmacārī guror gṛhe
guruśuśrūṣaṇaṃ kuryād bhaikṣānnakṛtabhojanaḥ
guror bhuktavataḥ paścān nātisvādumudāvatā
vahniśuśrūṣaṇaṃ kruyād vedāharaṇam eva ca
guror arthe sadā toyaṃ samidāharaṇaṃ tathā
puṣpādīnāṃ ca kurvīta supte tasmiñ śayīta ca
āhūtaś ca paṭhet tena tanmanā nānyatomukhaḥ
vratāni caratā saṃyag grāhyo vedo yatātmanā
daṇḍavatplavanaṃ snāne śastaṃ nāsyāṅgaśodhanam
adhītya vedān vedau vā vedaṃ vāpi yathākramam
yatheṣṭāṃ dakṣiṇāṃ dattvā gurave kurunandana
tato 'nujñāṃ samāsādya gṛhasthāśramam āvaset
tenaivāntaṃ vrajet prājñas tacchuśrūṣaṇatatparaḥ
vānaprasthāśramaṃ tasmāc caturthaṃ vāpi saṃśrayet
gṛhasthāśramavṛttyartham avyaṅgāṃ vidhinā nṛpa
ākhyātavarṇadharmeṇa dhanaṃ labdhvā mahīpate
kurvīta śraddhayā yukto nityanaimittikīḥ kriyāḥ
abhyāgatātithīn bandhūn bhṛtyādīn āturāṃs tathā
ṛtāv upagamaś caiva gṛhasthasyāpi śabditaḥ
dharmo dharmabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭha yajñocchiṣṭaṃ ca bhojanam
havyena prīṇayed devān pitṛn kavyena śaktitaḥ
manuṣyān annapānena svādhyāyena rṣitarpaṇam
kuryāc ca prīṇanaṃ nityaṃ bhūtānāṃ balikarmaṇā
śubhena karmaṇātmānam upadeśena cātmajān
anujīvijanaṃ vṛtyā gṛhasthas toṣayet sadā
tathaivāparamānebhyaḥ pradeyaṃ gṛhamedhinā
annaṃ bhikṣārthino ye ca parivrāḍbrahmacāriṇaḥ
evaṃ gṛhāśrame devāḥ pitaro munayas tathā
sarvakāmān prayacchanti manuṣyāś ca supūjitāḥ
gṛhasthas tu yadā paśyed valīpalitam ātmanaḥ
apatyasya tathāpatyaṃ tadāraṇyaṃ samāśrayet
pitṛdevātithīnāṃ tu smṛtaṃ tatrāpi pūjanam
tathaivāraṇyabhogaś ca tapobhiś cātmakarṣaṇam
brahmacaryaṃ mahīśayyā homas triṣavaṇāplutiḥ
maunādikaraṇaṃ śastaṃ jaṭāvalkaladhāraṇam
grīṣme pañcatapobhiś ca varṣāsv abhrāvakāśikaiḥ
iṅgudairaṇḍatailena gātrābhyaṅgāni ceṣyate
śyāmākanīvāramayaṃ phalamūlaiś ca bhojanam
apraveśas tathā grāme vānaprasthavidhiḥ smṛtaḥ
āśramaṇaṃ tv aparaṃ bhikṣoḥ śṛṇuṣva gadato mama
sarvasaṅgaparityāgaḥ kṣāntir indriyasaṃyamaḥ
vikālabhaikṣacaraṇam anārambhas tathā nṛpa
ātmajñānāvabodhecchā ātmāvalokanaṃ caiva
bhikṣoḥ śastāni pārthiva
kramād vimuktikāmānāṃ puruṣāṇām ayaṃ vidhiḥ
evaṃ tu varṇadharmeṇa tathā cāśramakarmanā
nijena saṃpūjya hariṃ siddhim āpnoti mānavaḥ
brahmacārī gṛhasthaś ca bhikṣur vaikhānasas tathā
yato hi devatāḥ sarvā brahmādyāḥ kurunandana
aṃśabhūtā jagaddhātur viṣṇor avyaktajanmanaḥ
viśve devā yato viṣṇur viṣṇuḥ pitṛgaṇo yataḥ
devā yajñabhujaś ceśo yataḥ pāpaharo hariḥ
viśve bhūtāni bhūtāni yato viṣṇus tatharṣayaḥ
tataḥ sarvāśramāṇāṃ hi pūjya eko janārdanaḥ
sarveśvaraṃ sarvamayaṃ samasta saṃsārahetukṣayakāraṇeśam
varaṃ vareṇyaṃ varadaṃ variṣṭhaṃ viṣṇuṃ kriyāvān yajate manuṣyaḥ
ārādhya yaṃ bhuvanabhāvanam acyutākhyam aiśvaryam īpsitam avāpa patiḥ surāṇām
kamalajaharasūryacandraśakraiḥ satatam abhiṣṭutam ādyam īśitāram
viṣṇor bhṛgukulaśreṣṭha yac ca dvaite mahātmanaḥ
vinivṛttirūpā yena teṣāṃ yena vader ha tam
sarveśvareśvareśasya yac ca rūpaṃ hareḥ param
devadevo jagaddhātā paramātmā janārdanaḥ
jagataḥ pālanārthāya durvṛttanidhanāya ca
svecchayā bhagavān viṣṇuḥ saṃbhavaty eva bhūtale
turīyāṃśena dharmasya bhagavān bhūtabhāvanaḥ
yadāvatāraṃ kṛtavāṃs tadā taccaritaṃ śṛṇu
naro nārāyaṇaś caiva hariḥ kṛṣṇas tathaiva ca
viṣṇor aṃśāṃśakā hy ete catvāro dharmasūnavaḥ
teṣāṃ nārāyaṇanarau gandhamādanaparvate
ātmany ātmānam ādhāya tepate paramaṃ tapaḥ
dhyāyamānāv anaupamyaṃ svakāraṇam akāraṇam
tayos tapaḥprabhāveṇa na tatāpa divākaraḥ
vavau cāśaṅkito vāyuḥ sukhasparśo hy asarkaraḥ
siṃhavyāghrādayaḥ saumyāś ceruḥ saha mṛgair girau
tayor gauravabhārārtā pṛthivī pṛthivīpate
cacāla bhūdharāś celuś cukṣubhuś ca mahābdhayaḥ
devāś ca sveṣu dhiṣṇyeṣu niṣprabheṣu hataprabhāḥ
babhūvur avanīpāla paramaṃ kṣobham āgatāḥ
yuyojāpsarasaḥ śubhrās tayor vighnacikīrṣayā
alambuṣe miśrakeśi puṇḍarīke varūthini
naranārāyaṇau tatra tapodīkṣānvitau dvijau
tāv asmākaṃ varārohāḥ kurvāṇau paramaṃ tapaḥ
karmātiśayaduḥkhārti pradāvayatināśakau
tad gacchata na bhīḥ kāryā bhavatībhir idaṃ vacaḥ
smaraḥ sahāyo bhavitā vasantaś ca varāṅganāḥ
rūpaṃ ca vaḥ samālokya madanoddīpanaṃ param
bhṛṅgamālārutaravair ramaṇīyam abhūd vanam
kiṃnaroragayakṣāṇāṃ babhūva ghrāṇatarpaṇaḥ
varāṅganāś ca tāḥ sarvā naranārāyaṇāv ṛṣī
jagur manoharaṃ kāścin nanṛtuś cātra cāparāḥ
avādayaṃs tathaivānyā manoharataraṃ nṛpa
hāvair bhāvaiḥ smitais trāsais tathānyā valgubhāṣitaiḥ
tayoḥ kṣobhāya tanvaṅgyaś cakrur udyamam aṅganāḥ
tathāpi na tayoḥ kaścin manasaḥ pṛthivīpate
vikāro 'bhavad adhyātma pārasaṃprāptacetasoḥ
nivātasthau yathā dīpāv akampau nṛpa tiṣṭhataḥ
pūryamāṇo 'pi cāmbhobhir bhuvam anyāṃ mahodadhiḥ
smaro 'pi na śaśākātha praveṣṭuṃ hṛdayaṃ tayoḥ
puṣpojjvalāṃs taruvarān vasantaṃ dakṣiṇānilam
tāś caivāpsarasaḥ sarvāḥ kandarpaṃ ca mahāmunī
yac cārabdhaṃ tapas tābhyām ātmānaṃ gandhamādanam
dadṛśāte 'khilaṃ rūpaṃ brahmaṇaḥ puruṣarṣabha
dāhāya nānalo vahner nāpaḥkledāya cāmbhasaḥ
tato vijñānavijñāta parabrahmasvarūpayoḥ
cakrāte tāś ca tanvaṅgyas tatkṣobhāya punaḥ punaḥ
atha nārāyaṇo dhairya gāmbhīryodāryamānasaḥ
ūror utpādayām āsa tāṃ varorubalāṃ tadā
guṇalāghavam abhyeti yasyāḥ saṃdarśanād anu
tāṃ vilokya mahīpāla cakampe mādhavānilam
vasanto vismayaṃ yātaḥ saṃyātaḥ saṃsmaraṃ smaraḥ
rambhātilottamādyāś ca vilakṣā devayoṣitaḥ
na rejur avanīpāla tallakṣahṛdayekṣaṇāḥ
tataḥ kāmo vasantaś ca pārthivāpsarasaś ca tāḥ
mohitāḥ sma vijānīmo nāntaraṃ vandyanindyayoḥ
dhāma bhūtasya lokānām anāder atra tiṣṭhati
naranārāyaṇau devau śārṅgacakrāyudhāv ubhau
āstāṃ prasādasumukhāv asmākam aparādhinām
nidhānaṃ sarvavidyānāṃ sarvapāpendhanānalaḥ
nārāyaṇo no bhagavān sarvapāpaṃ vyapohatu
śārṅgacakrāyudhaḥ śrīmān ātmajñānamayo 'naghaḥ
naraḥ samastapāpāni hatvātmā sarvadehinām
jaṭākalāpabandho 'yam anayor akṣayātmanoḥ
saumyā ca dṛṣṭiḥ pāpāni hantu sarvāṇi naḥ śubhā
prasīdatu naro 'smākaṃ tathā nārāyaṇo 'vyayaḥ
kva naḥ śarīrakāṇīdṛg miśrakarmacitāni vai
tathāpy avidyāduṣṭena manasā yaḥ kṛto hi vām
asmābhir aparādho 'yaṃ kṣamyatāṃ sumahādyutī
śaraṇaṃ ca prapannānāṃ tavāsmīti ca vādinām
prasādaṃ pitṛhantRṇām api kurvanti sādhavaḥ
eṣa eva varo 'smākam avivekāhṛto mahān
prasīda deva vijñāna ghanamūḍhadṛśām api
dṛṣṭvaitan naḥ samutpannaṃ yathā strīratnam īdṛśam
tvayi nārāyaṇotpannā śreṣṭhā pāravatī matiḥ
nārāyaṇa prasīdeti sarvalokaparāyaṇa
namasyāmo naraṃ devaṃ tathā nārāyaṇaṃ harim
namo narāya namyāya namo nārāyaṇāya ca
prasannānām anāthānām aparādhavatāṃ prabhuḥ
śaṃ karotu naro 'smākaṃ śaṃ nārāyaṇa dehi naḥ
prāheśaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ sādhyo nārāyaṇo nṛpa
yat kāryam āgatānāṃ va ihāsmābhis tad ucyatām
yūyaṃ saṃsiddhaye nūnam asmākaṃ valaśatruṇā
saṃpreṣitās tato 'smākaṃ nṛttageyādidarśitam
na vayaṃ nṛttagītena nāṅgaceṣṭādibhāṣitaiḥ
lubhyāmo viṣato manye viṣayā dāruṇātmakāḥ
śabdādisaṅgaduṣṭāni yadā nākṣāṇi naḥ śubhāḥ
tadā nṛttādayo bhāvāḥ kathaṃ lobhapradāyinaḥ
te siddhāḥ sma na vai sādhyā bhavatīnāṃ smarasya ca
mādhavasya ca śakro 'pi svāsthyaṃ yātv aviśaṅkitaḥ
yo 'sau parasmāt paramaḥ puruṣāt parameśvaraḥ
paramātmā hṛṣīkeśaḥ sthāvarasya carasya ca
sa sarvavāsidevatvād vāsudevety udāhṛtaḥ
vayam aṃśāṃśakās tasya caturvyūhasya māyinaḥ
taṃ sarvabhūtaṃ sarveśaṃ sarvatra samadarśinaḥ
paśyantaḥ kutra rāgādīn kariṣyāmo vibhedakān
yadā sa eva viśvātmā tadā dveṣādayaḥ katham
pṛthivy āpas tathā tejo vāyur ākāśam eva ca
tathendriyāṇy ahaṃkāro buddhiś ca na pṛthag yataḥ
samadṛṣṭir yataḥ kutra rāgadveṣau pravartataḥ
ātmā cāyam abhedena yataḥ sarveṣu jantuṣu
sarveśvareśvaro viṣṇuḥ kutra rāgādayas tataḥ
brahmāṇam indram īśānam ādityān maruto 'khilān
viśvedevān ṛṣīn sādhyān vasūn pitṛgaṇāṃs tathā
yakṣarākṣasabhūtādīn nāgasarpasarīsṛpān
makṣikāmaśakādaṃśāñ śalabhān alasān kṛmīn
gulmavṛkṣalatāvalli tvaksāratṛṇajātijān
yac ca kiṃcid adṛśyaṃ vā dṛśyaṃ vā tridaśāṅganāḥ
jānamānaḥ kathaṃ viṣṇum ātmānaṃ paramaṃ ca yat
rāgadveṣau tathā lobhaṃ kaḥ kuryād amarāṅganāḥ
nipātyatāṃ pṛthagbhūte kutra rāgādiko gaṇaḥ
evam asmāsu yuṣmāsu sarvabhūteṣu cābalāḥ
tanmayatvaikabhūteṣu rāgādyavasaraḥ kutaḥ
samyagdṛṣṭir iyaṃ proktā samastaikyāvalokinī
bhūtendriyāntaḥkaraṇa pradhānapuruṣātmakam
yathāgner arciṣaḥ pītāḥ piṅgalāruṇadhūsarāḥ
bhavatībhiś ca yat kṣobham asmākaṃ sa puraṃdaraḥ
bhavatyaḥ sa ca devendro lokāś ca sasurāsurāḥ
yatheyaṃ cārusarvāṅgī bhavatīnāṃ mayorutaḥ
darśitā darśayiṣyāmi tathātraivākhilaṃ jagat
yūyaṃ ca mā smayaṃ yāta santi rūpānvitāḥ striyaḥ
kiṃ surūpaṃ kurūpaṃ vā yadā bhedo na dṛśyate
tāratamyaṃ surūpatve satataṃ bhinnadarśinām
bhavatīnāṃ smayaṃ matvā rūpaudāryaguṇodbhavam
yasmān madūror udbhūtā iyam indīvarekṣaṇā
urvaśī nāma kalyāṇī bhaviṣyati tato 'psarāḥ
tad iyaṃ devarājāya nīyatāṃ varavarṇinī
bhavatyas tena cāsmākaṃ preṣitāḥ prītim icchatā
vaktavyaś ca sahasrākṣo nāsmākaṃ bhogakāraṇāt
tapaścaryā na cāprāpya phalaṃ prāptum abhīpsitam
yadi kaścit tavābādhāṃ karoti tridaśeśvara
tam ahaṃ vārayiṣyāmi nirvṛto bhava vāsava
kartāsi cet tvam ābādhām aduṣṭasyeha kasyacit
tavāpi śāstaitad ahaṃ pravartiṣyāmy asaṃśayam
etaj jñātvā na saṃtāpas tvayā kāryo hi māṃ prati
upakārāya jagatām avatīrṇo 'smi vāsava
yā ceyam urvaśī mattaḥ samudbhūtā puraṃdara
ity ukte 'psarasaḥ sarvāḥ praṇipatyātivismitāḥ
ūcur nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ taddarśanakutūhalāḥ
proktaḥ sa sarvo vijñāto māhātmyaṃ viditaṃ ca te
darśiteyaṃ viśālākṣī darśayiṣyāmi vo jagat
darśayātmānam akhilaṃ darśiteyaṃ yathorvaśī
yadi devāparāddheṣu nāsmāsu kupitaṃ tava
manas taj jagatam īśa darśayātmānam ātmanā
paśyatehākhilāṃl lokān mama dehe surāṅganāḥ
madhuṃ madanam ātmānaṃ yac cānyad draṣṭum icchatha
ity uktvā bhagavān devas tadā nārāyaṇo nṛpa
brahmā prajāpatiḥ śakraḥ saha rudraiḥ pinākadhṛk
ādityā vasavaḥ sādhyā viśvedevā maharṣayaḥ
nāsatyadasrāv anilāḥ sarve sarve tathāgnayaḥ
yakṣagandharvasiddhāś ca piśācāḥ kiṃnaroragāḥ
samastāpsaraso vidyāḥ sāṅgā vedās taduktayaḥ
manuṣyāḥ paśavaḥ kīṭāḥ pakṣiṇaḥ pādapās tathā
sarīsṛpāś ca ye sūkṣmā yac cānyaj jīvasaṃjñitam
samudrāḥ sakalāḥ śailāḥ saritaḥ kānanāni ca
dvīpāny aśeṣāṇi tathā nadāḥ sarvasarāṃsi ca
nagaragrāmapūrṇā ca medinī medinīpate
devāṅganābhir devasya dehe dṛṣṭaṃ mahātmanaḥ
dadṛśus tāḥ sucārvaṅgyas tasyāntar viśvarūpiṇaḥ
nordhvaṃ na tiryaṅ nādhaś ca yadāntas tasya dṛśyate
madanena samaṃ sarvā madhunā ca surāṅganāḥ
sasādhvasā bhaktimatyaḥ paraṃ vismayam āgatāḥ
paśyāma nādiṃ tava deva nāntam na madhyam avyākṛtarūpapāram
parāyaṇaṃ tvā jagatām anantam natāḥ sma nārāyaṇam ātmabhūtam
mahī divaṃ vāyujalāgnayas tvaṃ śabdādirūpaś ca parāparātman
draṣṭāsi rūpasya rasasya vettā śrotā ca śabdasya hare tvam ekaḥ
spraṣṭā bhavān spraśavato 'khilasya ghrātāsi gandhasya pṛthakśarīrī
rudrāntakādīni ca raudravatsu rūpeṣu rūpāṇi tavottamāni
kṣamādhaneṣu kṣitirūpam agryaṃ rūpaṃ tavāgryaṃ balavatsu vāyuḥ
manuṣyarūpaṃ tava rājaseṣu mūḍheṣu sarveśvara pādapo 'si
dṛśyasvarūpaś ca hutāśane tvaṃ sparśasvarūpo bhagavān samīre
paśyāma te nābhisarojamadhye brahmāṇam etaṃ ca haraṃ bhrukūṭyam
tatrāśvinau karṇagatau samastāṇ avasthitān bāhuṣu lokapālān
pādau dharitrīṃ jaṭharaṃ samastāṃl lokān hṛṣīkeśa vilokayāmaḥ
jaṅghe viyat pādakarāṅgulīṣu piśācarakṣoragasiddhasaṅghān
puṃstve prajānāṃ patir oṣṭhayugme pratiṣṭhitās te kratavaḥ samastāḥ
sarveṣṭayas te daśaneṣu deva daṃṣṭṛāsu vidyā bhavataś catasraḥ
romasv aśeṣās tava devasaṅghā vidyādharā nātha karāṅghrirekhāḥ
sāṅghāḥ samastās tava deva vedāḥ samāsthitā bahuṣu saṃdhibhūtāḥ
varāharūpaṃ dharaṇīdhṛtas te nṛsiṃharūpaṃ ca saṭākarālam
amī samudrās tava deva dehe mervādayaḥ śailavarās tavāmī
imāś ca gaṅgāpramukhāḥ sravatyo dvīpāny aśeṣāṇi vanāni caiva
tvām īśitāraṃ jagatām anantam yajñeśam arcanti ca yajvino 'mī
tvatto na śītaṃ na ca keśavoṣṇaṃ sarvasvarūpātiśayī tvam ekaḥ
kiṃ vāparāddhaṃ tava deva mūḍhair yan māyayā no hṛdayaṃ tathāpi
pāpāvaśaṃ kiṃ praṇatārtihārin mano hi no viṅkalatām upaiti
tat kṣamyatāṃ sṛṣṭikaras tavaiva devāparādhaṃ sṛjato vivekān
tvannāmasmaraṇāt pāpam aśeṣaṃ naḥ praṇaśyatu
tvannāmasmaraṇāt pāpam aśeṣaṃ naḥ praṇaśyatu
namo namas te vaikuṇṭha śrīvatsāṅkābjalocana
vareṇya yajñapuruṣa prajāpālaka vāmana
tvannāmasmaraṇāt pāpam aśeṣaṃ naḥ praṇaśyatu
saṃsārārṇavapotāya namas tubhyam adhokṣaja
tvannāmasmaraṇāt pāpam aśeṣaṃ naḥ praṇaśyatu
namaḥ parasmai śrīśāya vāsudevāya vedhase
upasaṃhāra viśvātman rūpam etat samantataḥ
vardhamānaṃ na no draṣṭuṃ samarthaṃ cakṣur īśvara
pramāṇena diśo bhūmir gaganaṃ ca samāvṛtam
sarvaṃ jagad ihaikasthaṃ piṇḍitaṃ lakṣayāmahe
kiṃ varṇayāmo rūpaṃ te kiṃ pramāṇam idaṃ hare
māhātmyaṃ kiṃtu te deva jihvāyā yan na gocaram
vaktrāṇām ayutenāpi buddhīnām ayutāyutaiḥ
guṇānāṃ varṇanaṃ nātha tava vaktuṃ na śakyate
tad etad darśitaṃ rūpaṃ prasādaḥ paramaḥ kṛtaḥ
divyajñānopapannānāṃ tāsāṃ pratyakṣam īśvaraḥ
viveśa sarvabhūtāni svair aṃśair bhūtabhāvanaḥ
taṃ dṛṣṭvā sarvabhūteṣu līyamānam adhokṣajam
vismayaṃ paramaṃ jagmuḥ samastā devayoṣitaḥ
sa ca sarveśvaraḥ śailān pādapān sāgarān bhuvam
jalam agniṃ tathā vāyum ākāśaṃ ca viveśa ha
kāle dikṣv atha sarvātmā manuṣyātmany athāpi ca
ātmarūpaḥ sthitaḥ svena mahimnā bhāvayañ jagat
devadānavarakṣāṃsi yakṣavidyādharoragān
manuṣyapaśukīṭādīn mṛgapakṣyantarikṣagān
ye 'ntarikṣe tathā bhūmau divi ye ye jalāśrayāḥ
tān praviśya sa viśvātmā punas tad rūpam āsthitaḥ
nareṇa sārchaṃ yat tābhir dṛṣṭapūrvam ariṃdama
tāḥ paraṃ vismayaṃ gatvā sarvās tridaśayoṣitaḥ
praṇemuḥ sādhyasāḥ pāṇḍu vadanā nṛpasattama
nārāyaṇo 'pi bhagavān āha tās tridaśāṅganāḥ
nīyatām urvaśī bhadrā yatrāste tridaśeśvaraḥ
bhavatīnāṃ hitārthāya sarvabhūteṣv asāv iti
jñānam utpāditaṃ bhūyo layaṃ bhūteṣu kurvatā
tam ajaṃ sarvabhūteśaṃ jānīta paramaṃ padam
ahaṃ bhavatyo devāś ca manuṣyāḥ paśavaś ca ye
devadevasya vistṛtiḥ etaj jñātvā samaṃ sargaṃ
sadevāsuramānuṣam sapaśvādigaṇaṃ caiva
draṣṭavyaṃ tridaśāṅganāḥ
praṇamya tau samadanāḥ savasantāś ca pārthiva
ādāya corvaśīṃ bhūyo devarājam upāgatāḥ
ācakhyuś ca yathāvṛttaṃ devarājāya tat tathā
jānann evam aśeṣeṣu bhūteṣu parameśvaram
vāsudevaṃ kathaṃ doṣāṃl lobhādīn na prahāsyasi
sarvabhūtāni govindād yadā nānyāni bhūpate
tadā vairādayo bhāvāḥ kriyatāṃ kutra pārthiva
iha paśyañ jagat sarvaṃ vāsudevātmakaṃ nṛpa
etad eva hi kṛṣṇena rūpam āviṣkṛtaṃ tadā
janmādibhāvarahitaṃ tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam
saṃkṣepeṇa ca bhūpāla śrūyatāṃ yad vadāmi te
yan matau puruṣaḥ kṛtvā paraṃ nirvāṇam ṛcchati
sarvaṃ viṣṇuḥ samastau hi bhāvābhāvau ca tanmayau
sadasat sarvam īśeśo vāsudevaḥ paraṃ padam
bhavajaladhigatānāṃ dvandvavātāhatānāṃ sutaduhitṛkalatratrāṇabhārārditānām
viṣamaviṣayatoye majjatām aplavānāṃ bhavati śaraṇam eko viṣṇupoto narāṇām
svarūpaṃ ca jagaddhātur ārādhanaviniścayaḥ
ārādhitāt phalaṃ yac ca keśavāt prāpyate naraiḥ
kathitaś ca mahābhāga dānānāṃ vistarād vidhiḥ
sa eṣa sarvapravaraḥ sarvabhūtaś ca mādhavaḥ
triyugaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣam apavargamahāhradam
triyugena tadā viṣṇoḥ kriyate kiṃ viśeṣaṇam
kṛtaṃ tretā dvāparaṃ ca kaliś ceti caturyugam
yadā jagati vikhyātaṃ tadā triyugatā kutaḥ
sādhu pṛṣṭo 'smi bhūpāla bhavatā triyugāśritam
kāṣṭhā pārthiva vijñeyā nimeṣā daśa pañca ca
kāṣṭhātriṃśat kalā jñeyā muhūrtaṃ tāvatīḥ kalāḥ
triṃśanmuhūrtā bhūpāla tathāhorātram ucyate
ayanaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ māsāḥ ṣaṇ māsāś ca tathottaram
ayanadvitayākhyaś ca kālaḥ saṃvatsaraḥ smṛtaḥ
dakṣiṇaṃ tv ayanaṃ rātrir devānām uttaraṃ dinam
śatatrayeṇa varṣāṇāṃ ṣaṣṭyā ca pṛthivīpate
manuṣyasaṃkhyayā varṣaṃ devānām api gaṇyate
catvāri tu sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ kṛtam ucyate
tasya tāvacchatī saṃdhyā saṃdhyāṃśaś ca tathāvidhaḥ
tretā trīṇi sahasrāṇi divyābdānāṃ nararṣabha
tasya tāvacchatī saṃdhyā saṃdhyāṃśaś ca tathāvidhaḥ
dvāparaṃ dve sahasre tu varṣāṇām abhidhīyate
tasya tāvacchatī saṃdhyā saṃdhyāṃśaś ca tathāvidhaḥ
kaliḥ sahasram ekaṃ tu divyābdānāṃ nararṣabha
tasya tāvacchatī saṃdhyā saṃdhyāṃśaś ca tathāvidhaḥ
kṛtaṃ nāmayugaṃ pūrvaṃ yatra dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ
na tatra dharmāḥ sīdanti na ca kṣīyanti vai prajāḥ
tataḥ kṛtayugaṃ nāma guṇataḥ procyate yugam
devadānavagandharvā yakṣarākṣasapannagāḥ
na sāmayajurṛgvarṇāḥ kriyā nāsīc ca mānavī
nāsūyā nāpi ruditaṃ na darpo nāpi paiśunam
na bhayaṃ nāpi saṃtāpo na cerṣyā nāpi matsaraḥ
tataḥ paramakaṃ brahma yā gatir yogināṃ parā
ātmā ca sarvabhūtānāṃ śuklo nārāyaṇas tadā
brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrāś ca kṛtalakṣaṇāḥ
kṛte yuge bhavantīha svakarmaniratāḥ prajāḥ
svam āśramaṃ svam ācāraṃ samyagjñānasamanvitam
caturāśramayuktena karmaṇā kālayoginā
akāmaphalasaṃyogāt prāpnuvanti parāṃ gatim
ātmayogasamāyukto dharmo 'yaṃ kṛtalakṣaṇaḥ
kṛte yuge catuṣpādaś caturvarṇyasya śāśvataḥ
tretām api nibodha tvaṃ yādṛgrūpaṃ pravartate
pādena hrasate dharmo raktatāṃ yāti cācyutaḥ
satyapravṛttāś ca narāḥ kriyādharmaparāyaṇāḥ
tato yajñāḥ pravartante dharmāś ca vividhāḥ kriyāḥ
tretāyāṃ bhāvasaṃkalpāḥ kriyādānaphalodayāḥ
pracaranti tato varṇās tapodānaparāyaṇāḥ
svakarmasthāḥ kriyāvantaḥ samatvād rajasānvitāḥ
dvivedāś caikavedāś ca anṛcaś ca tathāpare
evaṃ śāstreṣu bhinneṣu bahudhā nīyate kriyā
tapodānapravṛttā ca rājasī bhavati prajā
alpāyuṣo narā vedaḥ sumahāṃś ceti dustaraḥ
karoti bahudhā vedān vyāsarūpī tadā hariḥ
kāmāś copadravāś caiva tadā daivatakāritāḥ
yair ardyamānāḥ subhṛśaṃ tapas tapyanti mānavāḥ
dhanakāmāḥ svargakāmā yajñāṃs tanvanti cāpare
evaṃ dvāparam āsādya prajāḥ kṣīyanty adharmataḥ
tāmasaṃ yugam āsādya kṛṣṇo bhavati keśavaḥ
vratācārāḥ praśāmyanti dharmayajñakriyās tathā
ītayo vyādhayas tandrī doṣāḥ krodhādayas tathā
upadravāś ca vardhante manastāpāś ca saṃgatāḥ
yugeṣv āvartamāneṣu loko vyāvartate punaḥ
loke kṣīṇe kṣayaṃ yānti bhāvā lokapravartakāḥ
nātrāvatāraṃ kurute kṛṣṇāṃśena svarūpiṇā
kṛtādiṣu jagat pāti daityebhyo rūpadhṛd dhariḥ
kṛtādiṣv eva tenaiṣa triyugaḥ paripaṭhyate
pūrvotpanneṣu bhūteṣu teṣu teṣu kalau prabhuḥ
pīte ca pītatām asmin kṛṣṇe cātrāsitaṃ nṛpa
caturyugaṃ naḥ kathitaṃ saṃkṣepād bhavatākhilam
bhagavaty amale viṣṇau krīḍayā kṛṣṇatāṃ gate
kimāhārāḥ kimācārā bhaviṣyanti prajās tadā
brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrāś ca dvija kīdṛśāḥ
tapaḥ paraṃ kṛtayuge tretāyāṃ yajña eva hi
tapo niṣpādyate bhūpa yogasaṃsādhanaṃ param
rāgādidoṣaduṣṭena manasā yat tapo nṛpa
tretāyāṃ tu kriyāyajñān manoyajñāṃs tato narāḥ
tataḥ sthūlataraḥ panthā dānātmā kriyate naraiḥ
yathā satyaṃ tathā kṣāntir ahiṃsā ca kalau yuge
paropatāpād viratir narāṇām upakārikā
tasmin ghore yuge prāpte kṛṣṇe kṛṣṇatvam āgate
yādṛgrūpaṃ jagad idaṃ bhavatīha śṛṇuṣva tat
rājāno brāhmaṇā vaiśyāḥ śūdrāś ca manujeśvara
vyājadharmaparāś caiva dharmavaitaṃsikā janāḥ
satyaṃ saṃkṣipyate loke naraiḥ paṇḍitamānibhiḥ
satyahānyā tatas teṣāṃ svalpam āyur bhaviṣyati
āyuṣaḥ prakṣayād vidyāṃ na śakṣyanty upaśikṣitum
vidyāhīnān abuddhīṃs tāṃl lobho 'py abhibhaviṣyati
lobhakrodhaparā mūḍhāḥ kāmavaśyāś ca mānavāḥ
brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ saṃkīryantaḥ parasparam
śūdratulyā bhaviṣyanti tapaḥsatyavinākṛtāḥ
antyā madhyā bhaviṣyanti madhyāś cāntāvasāyinaḥ
īdṛśo bhavitā lokaḥ kṛṣṇe kṛṣṇatvam āgate
vastrāṇāṃ pravarā śāṇī dhānyānāṃ koradūṣakaḥ
bhāryāmitrāś ca puruṣā bhaviṣyanti kalau yuge
matsyāmiṣeṇa jīvanto duhantaś cāpy ajāvikāḥ
goṣu naṣṭāsu puruṣā bhaviṣyanti tadā nṛpa
sarittīreṣu kuddālair vāpayiṣyanti cauṣadhīḥ
tāś cāpy alpaphalās teṣāṃ bhaviṣyanti yugakṣaye
aniṣkrāntās tu saṃbandhāḥ svagotrāt puruṣarṣabha
aniṣkrāntāni śrāddhāni bhaviṣyanti ca gehataḥ
na vratāni cariṣyanti brāhmaṇā vedanindakāḥ
prāyaśaḥ kṛpaṇānāṃ ca tathā bandhimatām api
vidhavānāṃ ca vittāni hariṣyanti balānvitāḥ
anyāyopāttavitteṣu kariṣyanti narāḥ spṛhām
veśyālāvaṇyabhāveṣu spṛhāṃ yoṣit kariṣyati
kanyāṃ na yācitā kaścin na ca kanyāprado naraḥ
bhāryā na patiśuśrūṣāṃ tadā kācit kariṣyati
narā devadvijāṃs tyaktvā bhaviṣyanty anyatomukhāḥ
yajñabhāgabhujo devā ye vedapaṭhitā dvijāḥ
brahmādyās tān parityajya narāḥ kālabalātkṛtāḥ
hetuvādaparā devān kariṣyanty aparāṃs tadā
ye yavānnā janapadā godhūmānnās tathaiva ca
tān deśān saṃśrayiṣyanti narāḥ kaliyuge nṛpa
na śrāddhaiś ca pitRṃś cāpi tarpayiṣyanti mānavāḥ
bahu maṃsyanti te snānaṃ nāpi śaucaparā narāḥ
na viṣṇubhaktipravaṇaṃ narāṇāṃ nṛpa mānasam
bhavitā tu yuge prāpte kṛṣṇe kārṣṇyopalakṣite
vinindāṃ prathame pāde kariṣyanti harer narāḥ
yugānte tu harer nāma naiva kaścid gṛhīṣyati
dhanyās te puruṣavyāghra pāpāmbhodhāv apāpinaḥ
ye nāmāpi kalau viṣṇor gṛhīṣyanty akṣayātmanaḥ
bahupāṣaṇḍasaṃkīrṇe jagaty asmin kalau yuge
kṛṣṇāyeti namo 'stv atra sukṛtī yadi vakṣyati
pāṣaṇḍinaḥ kariṣyanti cāturāśramyadūṣakāḥ
pāṣaṇḍabhūtam atyarthaṃ jagad etad asatkṛtam
bhaviṣyati tadā bhūpa vṛthāpravrajitotkaṭam
na tu dvijātiśuśrūṣāṃ na svadharmānupālanam
kariṣyanti tadā śūdrāḥ pravrajyāliṅgino vṛthā
utkocāḥ saugatāś caiva mahāyānaratās tathā
bhaviṣyanty atha pāṣaṇḍāḥ kāpilā bhikṣavas tathā
vṛddhāḥ śrāvakanirgranthāḥ siddhaputrās tathāpare
bhaviṣyanti durātmānaḥ śūdrāḥ kaliyuge nṛpa
niḥśaucā vakramatayaḥ parapākānnabhojanāḥ
bhaviṣyanti durātmānaḥ śūdrāḥ pravrajitās tadā
ete cānye ca bahavaḥ pāṣaṇḍāḥ puruṣarṣabha
brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyā bhaviṣyanti tathā pare
rājaśulkaharāḥ kṣudrā gṛhasthaparimoṣakāḥ
muniveṣākṛticchannā vāṇijyam upajīvikāḥ
na dvijān na kalau devān pūjayiṣyanti mānavāḥ
mlecchabhāṣānibandhais tu hetuvādair vikūlitāḥ
evaṃ teṣv atiduṣṭeṣu vimārgapathivartinaḥ
bhaviṣyanty apare duṣṭās teṣāṃ mārgānuyāyinaḥ
asaṃskṛtoktivaktāro vedaśāstravinindakāḥ
jagadunmārgakartāro bhaviṣyanti tadā narāḥ
jagaty atra tadā nRṇāṃ svalpam āyur bhaviṣyati
paramāyuś ca bhavitā tadā varṣāṇi ṣoḍaśa
tataḥ prāṇān prahāsyanti kṛṣṇe kṛṣṇatvam āgate
pañcame vātha ṣaṣṭhe vā varṣe kanyā prasūyate
saptavarṣāṣṭavarṣā vā prajāsyanti narās tadā
alpadravyā vṛthāliṅgā hiṃsāratiparāyaṇāḥ
hartāro na tu dātāro bhaviṣyanti kalau narāḥ
śuklādānaparāḥ kṣudrāḥ parapākāśino dvijāḥ
vaiśyās tathā tu rājāno na tu kṣatriyavaṃśajāḥ
śūdrā bhikṣavatā viprāḥ śuśrūṣāvipaṇāśritāḥ
bhaviṣyanti nṛpaśreṣṭha kṛṣṇe kṛṣṇatvam āgate
na śiṣyo na guruḥ kaścin na putro na pitā tathā
etat kālasvarūpaṃ te śatānīka mayoditam
viṣṇubhaktān naraśreṣṭha na narān bādhate kaliḥ
ye tanmanaskās tiṣṭhanti prayāntaḥ saṃsthitās tathā
yasya bhāvo na taṃ bhūpa kadācid bādhate kaliḥ
kaliprabhāvo duṣṭoktiḥ pāṣaṇḍānāṃ tathoktayaḥ
aniṣṭvāpi mahāyajñair akṛtvāpi pitṛsvadhām
kṛṣṇam abhyarcya yad bhaktyā nainaṃ śvomaraṇaṃ tapet
yasyāgratas tathā pṛṣṭhe gacchatas tiṣṭhato 'pi vā
govinde niyataṃ cetaḥ kṛtakṛtyaḥ sadaiva saḥ
śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ gacchan govindaṃ nāvasīdati
kalikalmaṣakakṣāgniṃ nirvāṇaṃ padam avyayam
sarvakāraṇam avyaktaṃ viṣṇuṃ dhyāyan na sīdati
yatrārcite 'rcanīyaś ca jāyate taṃ namāmy aham
jagatsraṣṭāram iśeśam anādiṃ parataḥ param
aśeṣāghaharaṃ viṣṇuṃ harivarṇaṃ hariṃ namaḥ
yatkīrtanād aghaḥ śuddhaḥ smṛte yatrāśuciḥ suciḥ
tam ātmani sthitaṃ bhūpa puṇḍarīkekṣaṇaṃ namaḥ
yaḥ smaret puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ sa bāhyābhyantaraḥ śuciḥ
tathāpi saṃsmaran viṣṇuṃ sa bāhyābhyantaraḥ śuciḥ
kalāv atrātidoṣāḍhye viṣayāsaktamānasaḥ
kṛtvāpi pāpaṃ govindaṃ dhyāyan pāpair vimucyate
tad dhyānaṃ yatra govindaḥ sā kathā yatra keśavaḥ
naitat pitā tanūjāya na śiṣyāya gurur nṛpa
suhṛdaś ca tathivānye nopadeśo nṛpedṛśaḥ
upadeṣṭā paro bandhur īdṛśo yo vimuktaye
yo naikāgramanā viṣṇāv iti jñātvāpi pārthiva
upadeśapradānena saṃbhūtitraya āsuraḥ
naiva viṣṇuparo bhūpa bhavaty akṣīṇakalmaṣaḥ
hetuvādāśrito mūḍho dadāty uttaram akṣayam
āsurasyāpi tanmātrā jāyate nṛpate matiḥ
tvayācyutān matir bhūpa nāpaneyā kathaṃcana
aprāpya vāñchati ratiṃ sarvadaiva nṛṇāṃ manaḥ
sukhaprītikaraṃ nRṇāṃ patatāṃ nirvṛtipradam
yeṣāṃ gṛheṣu likhitam etat sthāsyati nityadā
na tadgṛhāṇi daivotthā bādhiṣyante hy upadravāḥ
kiṃ tīrthaiḥ kiṃ pradānair vā kiṃ yajñaiḥ kim upoṣitaiḥ
śṛṇoti ślokam ekaṃ ca dharmasyāsya samaṃ hi tat
adhyāyapāraṇaṃ cāsya gopradānāh viśiṣyate
śṛṇvaṃś cāsya daśādhyāyān sadyaḥ pāpaiḥ pramucyate
śrotuṃ vāñchā samastaṃ tat pārthivasya vyapohati
kapilānāṃ śate datte yad bhavej jyeṣṭhapuṣkare
narendra viṣṇudharmāṇāṃ tadāvāpnoti pāraṇe
nāsty anyad viṣṇudhamāṇāṃ sadṛśaṃ śāstram uttamam
paṭhann anudinaṃ dharmān etāñ śṛṇvaṃs tathāpi vā
bhaktyā matimatāṃ śreṣṭha sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate
na garbhahāriṇī bhītir na ca bālagrahā gṛhe
śṛṇvan vipro vedavit syāt kṣatriyaḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ
ṛddhiṃ prayāti vaiśyaś ca śūdraś cārogyam ṛcchati
viṣṇau manaḥ samāveśya sarvatra samadarśanaḥ
tasya pāpaṃ tathā rogān duḥsvapnādyābhicārukān
hemante ya imān dharmāñ śṛṇoti vasudhādhipa
śiśire ca naravyāghra yaḥ śṛṇoti yathāvidhi
puṇḍarīkasya yajñasya sa prāpnoti phalaṃ naraḥ
madhumādhavasaṃjñe tu yaḥ śṛṇoti naras tv imān
śṛṇvann etān nidāghe ca dharmān dharmabhṛtāṃ vara
varṣāsu cemān yo dharmān saṃśṛṇvan vasudhādhipa
rājasūyakratoḥ puṇyam akhilaṃ samavāpnuyāt
śaratkāle ca saṃśṛṇvan dharmān etān nararṣabha
ṛtuṣv eteṣv etad eva paṭhatām api pārthiva
phalaṃ bhavati duṣṭeṣu graheṣv ete śubhapradāḥ
kapilānāṃ śatasyoktaṃ yat phalaṃ jyeṣṭhapuṣkare
bhūyo bhūyas tad āpnoti pāraṇe pāraṇe gate
so 'rcayaty avanīpāla jñānayajñena keśavam
sarvābādhās tathā pāpam akhilaṃ manujeśvara
viṣṇudharmā vyapohanti saṃsmṛtāḥ paṭhitāḥ śrutāḥ
etat te sarvam ākhyātaṃ rahasyaṃ paramaṃ hareḥ
nātaḥ parataraṃ kiṃcic śrāvyaṃ śrutisukhāvaham
